# Question 51 — Hypertrophic Pulmonary Osteoarthropathy / 肥大性肺性骨关节病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>47-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>3-week history of moderate pain in her arms and legs</strong>. She states that her <strong>"bones ache" in all joints both at rest and with movement</strong>. She has hypertension, hyperlipidemia, and type 2 diabetes mellitus well controlled with diet. Current medications include hydrochlorothiazide and simvastatin. Her sister has Sjögren syndrome, and her mother has coronary artery disease. The patient does not smoke and drinks one glass of wine daily. Her blood pressure is 144/80 mm Hg. Cardiopulmonary examination shows no abnormalities. There is <strong>tenderness to palpation over the wrist, metacarpophalangeal, knee, and ankle joints</strong>. <strong>Clubbing of the fingers and toes</strong> is noted. A chest x-ray shows a <strong>left upper lobe mass with perihilar lymphadenopathy</strong>. X-rays of the tibia and fibula show <strong>periostosis</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bone metastases<br />
B) Hypertrophic pulmonary osteoarthropathy<br />
C) Neuropathic arthropathy (Charcot joint)<br />
D) Sarcoidosis<br />
E) Systemic sclerosis (scleroderma)</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Clubbing of the fingers and toes<br />
指趾杵状变</td>
<td>Classic component of the HOA triad; strongly points away from simple inflammatory arthritis<br />
HOA三联征的经典组成；强烈提示非单纯炎性关节炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Left upper lobe mass with perihilar lymphadenopathy<br />
左上叶肿块伴肺门淋巴结肿大</td>
<td>Suggests pulmonary malignancy — the most common underlying cause of secondary HOA<br />
提示肺部恶性肿瘤——继发性HOA最常见的潜在病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Periostosis of tibia and fibula on X-ray<br />
胫腓骨X线示骨膜增生</td>
<td>Pathognomonic imaging finding of HOA; distinguishes from bone metastases (lytic/sclerotic lesions)<br />
HOA特征性影像学表现；可与骨转移（溶骨/成骨病变）相鉴别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Bones ache" at rest and with movement<br />
静息和活动时均感"骨痛"</td>
<td>Diffuse arthralgia at rest is typical of HOA; distinguishes from mechanical/degenerative joint disease<br />
静息痛是HOA典型特征；可与机械性/退行性关节病相鉴别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Polyarticular tenderness (wrist, MCP, knee, ankle)<br />
多关节压痛（腕、掌指、膝、踝）</td>
<td>Large and small joint involvement mimics inflammatory arthritis, creating diagnostic confusion<br />
大小关节均受累，易误诊为炎性关节炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No smoking history despite lung mass<br />
无吸烟史但存在肺部肿块</td>
<td>Non-smoking lung cancer is possible; HOA functions as a paraneoplastic manifestation<br />
非吸烟者亦可患肺癌；HOA作为副肿瘤综合征表现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Hypertrophic pulmonary osteoarthropathy (HOA)** results from abnormal **fibrovascular proliferation** driven by underlying disease, most commonly **pulmonary malignancy**, through growth factor dysregulation:

**肥大性肺性骨关节病（HOA）**由潜在疾病（最常见为**肺部恶性肿瘤**）通过生长因子失调驱动的异常**纤维血管增生**所致：

- **Pulmonary malignancy** (or chronic lung disease) → tumor-derived VEGF/PDGF overproduction → periosteal endothelial activation\
  **肺部恶性肿瘤**（或慢性肺病）→ 肿瘤来源VEGF/PDGF过度产生 → 骨膜内皮细胞活化

- Periosteal activation → new bone deposition along long bone shafts (periostosis) → severe, deep bone pain\
  骨膜活化 → 长骨干新骨沉积（骨膜增生）→ 剧烈深部骨痛

- Vascular changes in distal extremities → soft tissue expansion beneath nail beds → **digital clubbing**\
  远端肢体血管改变 → 甲床下软组织增生 → **指趾杵状变**

- Synovial hypertrophy and effusion → polyarthralgia clinically indistinguishable from rheumatoid arthritis without imaging\
  滑膜增生和积液 → 不行影像学检查时临床上难以与类风湿关节炎区分的多关节痛

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Periostosis preferentially affects the distal long bones — tibia, fibula, radius, ulna — forming smooth, laminated periosteal new bone visible on plain X-ray.

**解剖小窍门:** 骨膜增生好发于远端长骨——胫骨、腓骨、桡骨、尺骨——平片可见光滑层状骨膜新骨形成。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Hypertrophic Pulmonary Osteoarthropathy / 正确答案 (B) — 肥大性肺性骨关节病

**Hypertrophic pulmonary osteoarthropathy (HOA)** is defined by the classic triad of digital clubbing, periostosis of long bones, and severe diffuse polyarthralgia — all three present in this patient:

**肥大性肺性骨关节病（HOA）**以经典三联征为定义：指趾杵状变、长骨骨膜增生和严重弥漫性多关节痛——本患者三项全备：

- Clubbing ✓ noted on examination; periostosis ✓ on tibia/fibula X-rays; diffuse polyarthralgia ✓ at rest and with movement\
  查体见杵状变✓；胫腓骨X线见骨膜增生✓；静息和活动时弥漫性多关节痛✓

- Left upper lobe mass with lymphadenopathy → most likely primary lung malignancy (e.g., NSCLC), the most common cause of secondary HOA\
  左上叶肿块伴淋巴结肿大 → 最可能为原发性肺部恶性肿瘤（如NSCLC），继发性HOA最常见病因

- HOA onset often precedes or coincides with lung cancer diagnosis — it is a paraneoplastic syndrome, not direct tumor invasion of bone\
  HOA发病常先于或与肺癌诊断同时——这是副肿瘤综合征，而非肿瘤直接侵犯骨骼

**Diagnosis:** Clinical triad plus periostosis on plain X-ray (smooth laminated periosteal new bone along long bone shafts) is sufficient; bone scan shows cortical "double stripe" sign; CT chest confirms lung mass.

**诊断:** 临床三联征加上平片骨膜增生（长骨干光滑层状骨膜新骨）即可确诊；骨扫描可见皮质"双条纹"征；胸部CT明确肺部肿块。

**Treatment:** Treat the underlying cause (lung malignancy resection or systemic therapy → rapid HOA symptom resolution); NSAIDs for symptomatic pain relief; bisphosphonates or octreotide for refractory cases.

**治疗:** 治疗根本病因（肺恶性肿瘤切除或系统治疗→HOA症状迅速缓解）；NSAIDs缓解症状；难治性病例可用双膦酸盐或奥曲肽。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Bone metastases<br />
A — 骨转移</td>
<td>Bone metastases cause lytic or sclerotic lesions on X-ray, not smooth periosteal new bone; digital clubbing is not a feature of metastatic disease<br />
骨转移X线表现为溶骨或成骨病变，非光滑骨膜新骨；杵状变不是转移性疾病的特征</td>
<td>X-ray shows periostosis (smooth periosteal new bone along shaft), not destructive lytic/blastic lesions<br />
X线示骨膜增生（沿骨干光滑骨膜新骨），非破坏性溶骨/成骨病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Hypertrophic pulmonary osteoarthropathy ✓<br />
B — 肥大性肺性骨关节病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — All three HOA triad elements present, with a lung mass as the underlying paraneoplastic trigger<br />
正确——三联征三项全备，肺部肿块为潜在副肿瘤触发因素</td>
<td>Classic triad + periostosis on imaging + lung mass = HOA until proven otherwise<br />
经典三联征+影像学骨膜增生+肺部肿块=首先考虑HOA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Neuropathic arthropathy (Charcot joint)<br />
C — 神经性关节病（Charcot关节）</td>
<td>Charcot joint requires afferent sensory neuropathy causing painless repetitive injury; leads to osteolysis and joint destruction, not periostosis; no clubbing; diabetes here is diet-controlled without noted neuropathy<br />
Charcot关节需传入感觉神经病变导致无痛性反复损伤；引起骨溶解和关节破坏，非骨膜增生；无杵状变；本题糖尿病饮食控制良好，未提及神经病变</td>
<td>Charcot = osteolysis + fragmentation + joint malalignment; HOA = smooth periosteal new bone<br />
Charcot=骨溶解+碎裂+关节移位；HOA=光滑骨膜新骨</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Sarcoidosis<br />
D — 结节病</td>
<td>Sarcoidosis causes bilateral (not unilateral) hilar lymphadenopathy without a mass; bone involvement shows periosteal resorption and cysts, not periostosis; clubbing is rare<br />
结节病致双侧（非单侧）肺门淋巴结肿大，无肿块；骨骼受累表现为骨膜吸收和囊肿，非骨膜增生；杵状变罕见</td>
<td>Unilateral lung mass + periostosis strongly favors malignancy-associated HOA over sarcoidosis<br />
单侧肺部肿块+骨膜增生强烈支持恶性肿瘤相关HOA而非结节病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Systemic sclerosis (scleroderma)<br />
E — 系统性硬化症（硬皮病）</td>
<td>Scleroderma causes progressive skin fibrosis, Raynaud's phenomenon, and esophageal dysmotility; no periostosis; lung mass is not a feature; arthralgia is not the dominant presentation<br />
硬皮病导致进行性皮肤纤维化、雷诺现象和食管运动障碍；无骨膜增生；肺部肿块非其特征；关节痛非主要表现</td>
<td>No skin thickening, no Raynaud's described; periostosis + lung mass clinches HOA<br />
无皮肤增厚、无雷诺现象描述；骨膜增生+肺部肿块确立HOA诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is sarcoidosis — both involve lung pathology and lymphadenopathy — but the unilateral mass (vs. bilateral hilar adenopathy) and periostosis (vs. periosteal resorption/cysts) decisively favor HOA from malignancy.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是结节病——两者均涉及肺部病变和淋巴结肿大——但单侧肺部肿块（而非双侧肺门腺病）和骨膜增生（而非骨膜吸收/囊肿）决定性地支持恶性肿瘤相关HOA。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — HOA vs. Bone Metastases vs. Sarcoidosis Bone Disease / 肥大性肺性骨关节病 vs. 骨转移 vs. 结节病骨病对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />

<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>HOA</strong><br />
<strong>肥大性肺性骨关节病</strong></th>
<th><strong>Bone Metastases</strong><br />
<strong>骨转移</strong></th>
<th><strong>Sarcoidosis Bone Disease</strong><br />
<strong>结节病骨病</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>X-ray finding<br />
X线表现</td>
<td>Smooth laminated periosteal new bone along shaft<br />
骨干光滑层状骨膜新骨</td>
<td>Lytic ± sclerotic lesions; cortical destruction<br />
溶骨性±成骨性病变；皮质破坏</td>
<td>Cysts; periosteal resorption<br />
囊肿；骨膜吸收</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Digital clubbing<br />
指趾杵状变</td>
<td>Yes — hallmark of triad<br />
有——三联征标志性特征</td>
<td>No<br />
无</td>
<td>Rare<br />
罕见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lung imaging pattern<br />
肺部影像模式</td>
<td>Unilateral mass (malignancy) or diffuse chronic lung disease<br />
单侧肿块（恶性肿瘤）或弥漫性慢性肺病</td>
<td>Primary tumor elsewhere; lung mets may be seen<br />
他处原发肿瘤；可见肺转移</td>
<td>Bilateral hilar lymphadenopathy (BHL)<br />
双侧肺门淋巴结肿大（BHL）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Arthralgia pattern<br />
关节痛类型</td>
<td>Diffuse polyarthralgia at rest AND with activity<br />
弥漫性多关节痛，静息和活动均有</td>
<td>Localized bone pain at metastatic sites<br />
转移部位局限性骨痛</td>
<td>Chronic oligoarticular, ankles most common<br />
慢性少关节受累，踝关节最常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pathology<br />
病理</td>
<td>Fibrovascular proliferation → periosteal new bone<br />
纤维血管增生→骨膜新骨</td>
<td>Tumor cell invasion of medullary cavity<br />
肿瘤细胞侵犯髓腔</td>
<td>Noncaseating granulomas in periosteum<br />
骨膜内非干酪样肉芽肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Response to treating underlying cause<br />
治疗根本病因后反应</td>
<td>Rapid symptom resolution after tumor resection<br />
切除肿瘤后症状迅速缓解</td>
<td>Depends on systemic cancer control<br />
取决于全身肿瘤控制情况</td>
<td>Responds to corticosteroids<br />
对皮质类固醇有反应</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a patient with a lung mass presents with the triad of digital clubbing, diffuse polyarthralgia, and periostosis on long bone X-rays, diagnose Hypertrophic Pulmonary Osteoarthropathy — a paraneoplastic syndrome of fibrovascular proliferation, not direct bone invasion.**

**当肺部肿块患者出现指趾杵状变、弥漫性多关节痛和长骨X线骨膜增生三联征时，诊断为肥大性肺性骨关节病——这是纤维血管增生性副肿瘤综合征，而非肿瘤直接侵犯骨骼。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — HOA Triad "C-P-A" / 记忆钩 — HOA三联征 "C-P-A":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>lubbing — digital clubbing (fingers and toes; nail angle lost) / 杵状变（指趾受累；甲角消失）<br />
• <strong>P</strong>eriostosis — smooth periosteal new bone on long bone X-rays (tibia, fibula, radius) / 骨膜增生（长骨X线光滑骨膜新骨：胫、腓、桡骨）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>rthralgia — diffuse polyarthralgia at REST and with activity; mimics RA / 关节痛（静息和活动均有的弥漫性多关节痛；类似RA）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Hypertrophic Osteoarthropathy (HOA) / 高频知识表 — 肥大性骨关节病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>HOA definition<br />
HOA定义</td>
<td>Syndrome of digital clubbing + periostosis of long bones + severe polyarthralgia; caused by abnormal fibrovascular proliferation<br />
指趾杵状变+长骨骨膜增生+严重多关节痛综合征；由异常纤维血管增生引起</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary vs. secondary HOA<br />
原发性vs.继发性HOA</td>
<td>Primary (pachydermoperiostosis) is rare and genetic (HPGD mutation); secondary accounts for &gt;95% of cases and is associated with pulmonary, cardiac, GI, or hepatic disease<br />
原发性（厚皮性骨膜病）罕见，遗传性（HPGD基因突变）；继发性占&gt;95%，与肺、心、消化道或肝脏疾病相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common causes of secondary HOA<br />
继发性HOA最常见病因</td>
<td>#1: Pulmonary malignancy (especially NSCLC, mesothelioma); also lung abscess, bronchiectasis, cystic fibrosis; non-pulmonary: cyanotic CHD, IBD, cirrhosis<br />
#1：肺部恶性肿瘤（尤其NSCLC、间皮瘤）；亦见于肺脓肿、支气管扩张、囊性纤维化；非肺部：紫绀型先心病、IBD、肝硬化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology<br />
病理生理</td>
<td>Hypoxemia and/or tumor-derived VEGF/PDGF → endothelial activation → periosteal fibrovascular proliferation → new bone formation; megakaryocytes bypassing pulmonary circulation may also release growth factors<br />
低氧血症和/或肿瘤来源VEGF/PDGF→内皮活化→骨膜纤维血管增生→新骨形成；绕过肺循环的巨核细胞亦可释放生长因子</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Imaging findings<br />
影像学表现</td>
<td>Plain X-ray: smooth, symmetric, laminated periosteal new bone along shafts (not epiphyses) of long bones; bone scan: "double stripe" sign (tracer uptake along cortical surface bilaterally)<br />
平片：长骨干（非骨骺）光滑对称层状骨膜新骨；骨扫描："双条纹"征（示踪剂沿双侧皮质表面摄取）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clinical mimics and key differentiator<br />
临床鉴别及关键鉴别点</td>
<td>Often misdiagnosed as seronegative RA or inflammatory arthritis; key differentiators: clubbing + periostosis on X-ray + identification of underlying lung/tumor pathology<br />
常被误诊为血清阴性RA或炎性关节炎；关键鉴别：杵状变+X线骨膜增生+发现潜在肺部/肿瘤病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment and prognosis<br />
治疗和预后</td>
<td>Treat underlying cause; lung tumor resection → rapid resolution of HOA symptoms within weeks; NSAIDs for pain; bisphosphonates or octreotide for refractory pain<br />
治疗根本病因；肺肿瘤切除→数周内HOA症状迅速缓解；NSAIDs止痛；难治性疼痛用双膦酸盐或奥曲肽</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Paraneoplastic syndrome context:** HOA is one of several paraneoplastic syndromes in lung cancer; others include SIADH (SCLC), hypercalcemia via PTHrP (squamous cell), ectopic ACTH/Cushing (SCLC), and Lambert-Eaton myasthenic syndrome (SCLC)\
  **副肿瘤综合征背景:** HOA是肺癌多种副肿瘤综合征之一；其他包括SIADH（SCLC）、PTHrP介导的高钙血症（鳞癌）、异位ACTH/库欣（SCLC）和Lambert-Eaton肌无力综合征（SCLC）

- **Differential of digital clubbing:** Pulmonary causes (lung cancer, CF, bronchiectasis, IPF, lung abscess); cardiac (cyanotic CHD, infective endocarditis); GI (IBD, cirrhosis, celiac disease); idiopathic — always investigate the underlying cause\
  **杵状变鉴别:** 肺部原因（肺癌、CF、支气管扩张、IPF、肺脓肿）；心脏（紫绀型先心病、感染性心内膜炎）；消化道（IBD、肝硬化、乳糜泻）；特发性——始终需明确潜在病因

- **Key complication of missed diagnosis:** Failure to recognize HOA delays evaluation of the underlying lung malignancy, directly reducing the window for curative surgical resection\
  **漏诊关键并发症:** 未能识别HOA会延误对潜在肺部恶性肿瘤的评估，直接缩短根治性手术切除的时间窗口

- **Variant — primary HOA (pachydermoperiostosis):** Autosomal dominant, presents in adolescent males; HOA triad PLUS pachydermia (skin thickening) and furrowing of face/scalp; no underlying lung disease; caused by HPGD or SLCO2A1 mutations affecting prostaglandin metabolism\
  **题目变式——原发性HOA（厚皮性骨膜病）:** 常染色体显性遗传，青春期男性发病；HOA三联征加上厚皮症（皮肤增厚）和面部/头皮皱褶；无潜在肺病；由影响前列腺素代谢的HPGD或SLCO2A1基因突变引起

# Question 52 — Seat Belt Use as the Greatest Mortality Reducer in Adolescents / 安全带使用——青少年最重要的死亡率降低措施

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>healthy 16-year-old girl</strong> comes to the physician for a school physical examination. She is <strong>sexually active with one partner</strong> and <strong>does not use contraception</strong>. She has <strong>smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 2 years</strong>. She is 163 cm (5 ft 4 in) tall and weighs 70 kg (156 lb); <strong>BMI is 27 kg/m²</strong>. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. Which of the following behavioral modifications is most likely to have the greatest impact on <strong>mortality in this patient during the next 10 years</strong>?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following behavioral modifications is most likely to have the greatest impact on mortality in this patient during the next 10 years?</strong></p>
<p>A) Condom use<br />
B) Monthly breast self-examination<br />
C) Seat belt use<br />
D) Smoking cessation<br />
E) Weight loss</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>16-year-old girl<br />
16岁女孩</td>
<td>Adolescents have a distinct mortality profile dominated by unintentional injury, not chronic disease<br />
青少年死亡原因以意外伤害为主，而非慢性病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Does not use contraception<br />
未使用避孕措施</td>
<td>Raises STI and unwanted pregnancy risk, but these cause death far less often than MVAs in this age group<br />
增加性传播感染和意外妊娠风险，但该年龄段中远不如机动车事故致命</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Smoked 1 PPD × 2 years<br />
每日1包，吸烟2年</td>
<td>Long-term cancer/COPD/CVD risk exists, but 10-year horizon is too short to manifest as mortality at age 16<br />
长期肺癌/COPD/心血管病风险存在，但在16岁时10年内尚不足以导致死亡</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 27 kg/m²<br />
BMI 27 kg/m²</td>
<td>Mild overweight only; metabolic complications (DM, HTN) require decades of persistent obesity<br />
仅为轻度超重；代谢并发症（糖尿病、高血压）需数十年持续肥胖才能显现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"During the next 10 years"<br />
"未来10年内"</td>
<td>Time constraint eliminates long-latency diseases and shifts focus to acute traumatic causes of death<br />
时间限制排除了长潜伏期疾病，将焦点转向急性创伤性死亡原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physical exam shows no abnormalities<br />
体格检查无异常</td>
<td>No current pathology; all mortality risk is behavioral and preventable, not disease-driven<br />
目前无病理改变；所有死亡风险均来自行为，属可预防范畴，而非已有疾病</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

In adolescents and young adults aged 15–24, **unintentional injuries** — overwhelmingly **motor vehicle collisions (MVCs)** — account for approximately 40% of all deaths, far exceeding any disease-based cause:

在15至24岁的青少年和年轻成人中，**意外伤害**——绝大多数为**机动车事故（MVC）**——约占全部死亡的40%，远超任何疾病相关原因：

- Unintentional injury (MVCs) → \#1 cause of death in ages 15–24, ~40% of all deaths\
  意外伤害（机动车事故）→ 15至24岁首要死亡原因，约占全部死亡40%

- Homicide → \#2 cause of death in this age group\
  他杀 → 该年龄段第二位死亡原因

- Suicide → \#3 cause of death; mental health is a key screening target\
  自杀 → 第三位死亡原因；心理健康是关键筛查方向

- Malignancy and heart disease → \#4 and \#5; rare at this age and not preventable by the listed behaviors\
  恶性肿瘤和心脏病 → 第四、第五位；该年龄段罕见，且无法通过所列行为预防

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Seat belts reduce MVA fatality by ~45% overall and ~60% in rollover crashes by preventing occupant ejection and distributing impact forces across the bony pelvis and sternum.

**解剖小窍门:** 安全带通过防止乘员飞出车外、将撞击力分散至骨盆和胸骨，可将机动车事故死亡率总体降低约45%，翻车事故中降低约60%。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Seat Belt Use / 正确答案 (C) — 安全带使用

**Seat belt use** is the single behavioral change most likely to reduce 10-year mortality in this patient because it directly targets the overwhelmingly dominant cause of death in her age group:

**安全带使用**是最有可能降低该患者10年死亡率的单一行为改变，因为它直接针对其年龄段压倒性的首要死亡原因：

- Seat belts reduce MVA fatality risk by ~45–60%; this translates to the largest absolute mortality reduction available\
  安全带可降低机动车事故死亡风险约45至60%；这对应着可获得的最大绝对死亡率降幅

- The 10-year time frame eliminates smoking and obesity as competitors; their mortality effects emerge after decades\
  10年时间框架排除了吸烟和肥胖的竞争力；其死亡率效应需数十年才能显现

- Condom use and BSE address risks that, while real, are orders of magnitude rarer than MVA death at age 16–26\
  避孕套使用和乳房自检所针对的风险虽然真实存在，但在16至26岁时其致死率比机动车事故低出数个数量级

**Diagnosis:** A healthy 16-year-old with multiple modifiable risk factors; the dominant short-term mortality threat is unintentional traumatic death from MVAs, not any chronic or infectious disease.

**诊断:** 一名健康16岁女孩，合并多种可改变的危险因素；短期内主要死亡威胁是机动车事故导致的意外创伤性死亡，而非任何慢性病或感染性疾病。

**Treatment:** Counsel on consistent seat belt use in every vehicle trip (driver or passenger); also advise helmets for bicycles/motorcycles — this constitutes the highest-priority injury prevention counseling per Bright Futures/USPSTF for adolescents.

**治疗:** 建议每次乘车（无论驾驶员还是乘客）均系安全带；同时建议骑自行车/摩托车时佩戴头盔——这是Bright Futures/USPSTF针对青少年优先级最高的伤害预防咨询内容。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Condom use<br />
A — 使用避孕套</td>
<td>STI complications and pregnancy-related death do occur but at far lower rates than MVA fatality in the 15–24 age group<br />
性传播感染并发症和妊娠相关死亡确实存在，但在15至24岁年龄段中其死亡率远低于机动车事故</td>
<td>MVA mortality dwarfs STI/pregnancy mortality in adolescents; time horizon does not change this<br />
青少年中机动车事故死亡率远超性传播感染/妊娠死亡率；时间跨度不改变此结论</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Monthly breast self-examination<br />
B — 每月乳房自检</td>
<td>Breast cancer is extremely rare in 16-year-olds without BRCA1/2 mutation or strong family history; BSE has no proven mortality benefit even in higher-risk adults<br />
无BRCA1/2突变或强阳性家族史的16岁女孩乳腺癌极为罕见；即便在高风险成年人中乳房自检也无经证实的死亡率获益</td>
<td>Breast cancer typically manifests at age 40–60s; not a 10-year mortality concern for a 16-year-old with no family history<br />
乳腺癌通常在40至60岁发病；对无家族史的16岁青少年而言不构成10年内死亡风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Seat belt use ✓<br />
C — 安全带使用 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Directly reduces risk of the #1 cause of teen/young adult death: MVA fatality<br />
正确——直接降低青少年/年轻成人首要死亡原因——机动车事故——的致死风险</td>
<td>Unintentional injury is the #1 killer at ages 15–24; seat belts reduce this by ~45–60%<br />
意外伤害是15至24岁首要死因；安全带可降低该风险约45至60%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Smoking cessation<br />
D — 戒烟</td>
<td>Tobacco causes COPD, lung cancer, and CVD, but these manifest after 20–40 pack-years of use — not within 10 years of starting at age 16<br />
烟草导致COPD、肺癌和心血管病，但需20至40包年的使用后才显现——而非在16岁开始吸烟后10年内</td>
<td>Tobacco mortality peaks at age 50+; the 10-year window makes this answer incorrect despite smoking being the #1 lifetime preventable killer<br />
烟草致死率高峰在50岁以上；尽管吸烟是终身最重要的可预防死亡原因，10年窗口使此选项错误</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Weight loss<br />
E — 减重</td>
<td>BMI 27 is only mildly overweight; DM, HTN, and CVD from obesity require decades to develop and cause death<br />
BMI 27仅为轻度超重；肥胖引发的糖尿病、高血压和心血管病需数十年才能发展并导致死亡</td>
<td>Mildly overweight at 16 carries negligible 10-year mortality risk; answer would differ if BMI were ≥35 or question asked about lifetime risk<br />
16岁轻度超重的10年死亡风险可忽略不计；若BMI≥35或问题关注终身风险则答案不同</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is D (smoking cessation) — USMLE tests whether you recognize that the \#1 lifetime preventable killer in the US loses to MVA when the time frame is restricted to 10 years in a 16-year-old.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是D（戒烟）——USMLE考查你是否意识到，当时间范围限定为16岁起的10年内时，美国终身最重要的可预防死亡原因（吸烟）败给了机动车事故。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a healthy 16-year-old, seat belt use is the highest-yield behavioral change for 10-year mortality because unintentional injury — especially MVAs — is the \#1 killer of young people aged 15–24, far outpacing tobacco, obesity, or STIs on this time horizon.**

**对于健康16岁青少年，系安全带是降低10年死亡率获益最高的行为改变，因为意外伤害——尤其是机动车事故——是15至24岁年轻人的首要死亡原因，在此时间跨度上远超烟草、肥胖或性传播感染。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — Teen Death Order "A-H-S-M-H" / 记忆钩 — 青少年死亡原因排序 "意-他-自-恶-心":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>ccidents (MVA) — #1; ~40% of teen deaths; seat belt is the fix / 意外伤害（机动车事故）——第一位；约占青少年死亡40%；安全带是解决方案<br />
• <strong>H</strong>omicide — #2; reflects violence exposure unique to adolescence / 他杀——第二位；反映青少年特有的暴力暴露<br />
• <strong>S</strong>uicide — #3; screen for depression at every well visit / 自杀——第三位；每次健康检查均需筛查抑郁<br />
• <strong>M</strong>alignancy — #4; leukemia/lymphoma in young adults, not solid tumors / 恶性肿瘤——第四位；年轻成人以白血病/淋巴瘤为主，非实体瘤<br />
• <strong>H</strong>eart disease — #5; congenital/arrhythmic, not atherosclerotic at this age / 心脏病——第五位；该年龄段以先天性/心律失常为主，而非动脉粥样硬化性</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Adolescent Preventive Counseling & Mortality Epidemiology / 高频知识表 — 青少年预防咨询与死亡率流行病学

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>#1 cause of death ages 15–24 in the US<br />
美国15至24岁首要死亡原因</td>
<td>Unintentional injury (predominantly MVA); ~40% of all deaths; seat belt use is the single most impactful preventive measure<br />
意外伤害（以机动车事故为主）；约占全部死亡40%；安全带使用是最有效的单一预防措施</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Seat belt efficacy data<br />
安全带效果数据</td>
<td>~45% fatality reduction in frontal crashes; ~60% in rollovers; applies equally to driver and all passengers<br />
正面碰撞中死亡率降低约45%；翻车事故中约60%；对驾驶员和所有乘客同等有效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why smoking doesn't win despite being #1 lifetime killer<br />
为何吸烟尽管是终身首要杀手却不是此题答案</td>
<td>Tobacco mortality requires 20–40 pack-years to manifest (COPD, lung cancer, CVD); at age 16 with 2 years of smoking, the 10-year window extends only to age 26 — insufficient exposure<br />
烟草死亡率需20至40包年才能显现（COPD、肺癌、心血管病）；在16岁吸烟2年时，10年窗口仅延伸至26岁——暴露量不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bright Futures / USPSTF for adolescents<br />
青少年Bright Futures/USPSTF建议</td>
<td>Priority counseling: seat belts/helmets, tobacco cessation (long-term), HPV vaccine, STI/depression/substance use screening<br />
优先咨询内容：安全带/头盔、戒烟（长期获益）、HPV疫苗、性传播感染/抑郁/物质使用筛查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Breast cancer risk in adolescents<br />
青少年乳腺癌风险</td>
<td>Extremely rare without BRCA1/2 mutation or first-degree relative with early-onset breast cancer; USPSTF recommends mammography starting at age 40; no role for BSE in routine adolescent care<br />
无BRCA1/2突变或早发乳腺癌一级亲属时极为罕见；USPSTF建议40岁起乳腺X线筛查；乳房自检不纳入常规青少年保健</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 27 in adolescents vs. adults<br />
青少年vs成人BMI 27的意义</td>
<td>In a 16-year-old, BMI 27 (mild overweight) carries negligible 10-year mortality risk; in a 50-year-old with decades of obesity, the same BMI would contribute meaningfully to CVD/DM mortality<br />
对16岁青少年而言，BMI 27（轻度超重）的10年死亡风险可忽略不计；对已有数十年肥胖史的50岁成人而言，相同BMI将对心血管病/糖尿病死亡率产生显著贡献</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Most common cause of death" question pattern<br />
"最常见死亡原因"题型规律</td>
<td>USMLE frequently asks this by age group; memorize: infants (congenital anomalies), 1–14 (unintentional injury), 15–44 (unintentional injury), 45–64 (cancer), 65+ (heart disease)<br />
USMLE频繁按年龄段考查此知识；记忆：婴儿（先天性畸形）、1至14岁（意外伤害）、15至44岁（意外伤害）、45至64岁（癌症）、65岁以上（心脏病）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of "best preventive intervention" by time horizon:** For lifetime impact → smoking cessation (#1 preventable killer in US, 480,000 deaths/year); for 10-year impact in adolescent → seat belt use; time constraint is the pivotal qualifier in this question type\
  **按时间跨度区分"最佳预防干预":** 终身影响→戒烟（美国最重要可预防死亡原因，每年48万人死亡）；青少年10年影响→安全带使用；时间限制是此类题型的关键限定词

- **Variant — if patient were 50 years old with same risk factors:** Smoking cessation would become the top priority, as decades of tobacco use would now represent sufficient cumulative exposure to cause near-term cancer/CVD mortality\
  **题目变式——若患者为50岁且具有相同危险因素:** 戒烟将成为最优先事项，因为数十年烟草使用已积累足够暴露量，可在近期导致癌症/心血管病死亡

- **Key complication of not counseling on seat belts:** Traumatic brain injury, spinal cord injury, and internal hemorrhage are the dominant mechanisms of MVA death in adolescents — all preventable with restraint systems\
  **未进行安全带咨询的关键并发症:** 创伤性脑损伤、脊髓损伤和内出血是青少年机动车事故死亡的主要机制——均可通过约束系统预防

- **Additional counseling for this specific patient:** HPV vaccination series (if not completed), chlamydia/gonorrhea screening (sexually active female \<25 years, USPSTF Grade B), depression screening (USPSTF Grade B for ages 12–18), and tobacco cessation counseling for long-term benefit\
  **针对该患者的额外咨询建议:** HPV疫苗系列接种（若未完成）、衣原体/淋球菌筛查（性活跃女性\<25岁，USPSTF B级推荐）、抑郁筛查（USPSTF B级推荐，适用于12至18岁）及长期获益的戒烟咨询

# Question 53 — Acute Suppurative Parotitis / 急性化脓性腮腺炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>82-year-old woman</strong> who resides in a skilled nursing care facility is transferred to the hospital because of a <strong>2-day history of fever and cellulitis of the left side of her face</strong>. She is hemiparetic, aphasic, and <strong>unable to swallow. She is fed through a gastrostomy tube.</strong> She has congestive heart failure, type 2 diabetes mellitus, hypertension, hyperlipidemia, major depressive disorder, and osteoporosis. Her medications are furosemide, metoprolol, digoxin, glyburide, lisinopril, carvedilol, atorvastatin, amitriptyline, alendronate, and 81-mg aspirin. She appears ill and moans frequently. Her temperature is <strong>39.1°C (102.4°F)</strong>, pulse is 84/min, respirations are 24/min, and blood pressure is 112/72 mm Hg. A <strong>firm, exquisitely tender mass is palpated from the left cheek to the angle of the mandible; this area is also erythematous and edematous.</strong> The left pinna appears normal, and the otic canal is not inflamed. The <strong>mouth is dry.</strong> Bilateral basilar crackles are heard. Cardiac examination shows no abnormalities. The abdomen is soft and nontender. The gastrostomy tube is in place with no inflammation. Her <strong>leukocyte count is 28,000/mm³ (78% segmented neutrophils, 18% bands,</strong> and 4% lymphocytes), and serum glucose concentration is 168 mg/dL. A chest x-ray shows cardiomegaly; there are bilateral basilar increased markings and atelectasis in the left lung base but <strong>no focal infiltrates.</strong> Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's fever?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely cause of this patient's fever?</strong></p>
<p>A) Acute suppurative parotitis<br />
B) Aspiration pneumonia<br />
C) Mandibular osteomyelitis<br />
D) Osteonecrosis of the jaw<br />
E) Urinary tract infection</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>82-year-old, skilled nursing facility resident<br />
82岁，住于专业护理机构</td>
<td>Elderly, institutionalized patients are at highest risk for suppurative parotitis due to debilitation and poor oral care<br />
老年、入住机构的患者因体质虚弱和口腔护理不足，是化脓性腮腺炎的最高危人群</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Unable to swallow; fed via gastrostomy tube<br />
无法吞咽，经胃造口管喂养</td>
<td>Absent oral intake → no chewing stimulation → ↓ salivary flow → bacterial stasis in Stensen's duct<br />
无口服摄入→无咀嚼刺激→唾液分泌减少→Stensen 导管内细菌淤滞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dry mouth<br />
口腔干燥</td>
<td>Xerostomia removes the mechanical flushing defense of the parotid duct; anticholinergic amitriptyline compounds this<br />
口腔干燥去除了腮腺导管的机械冲刷防御；抗胆碱能药阿米替林进一步加剧此效应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Firm, exquisitely tender mass from left cheek to angle of mandible; erythematous and edematous<br />
左颊至下颌角的硬性极度触痛肿块；红肿</td>
<td>Anatomically corresponds to parotid gland; classic triad of suppurative parotitis<br />
解剖位置精确对应腮腺；是化脓性腮腺炎的经典三联征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocyte count 28,000/mm³ with 18% bands<br />
白细胞 28,000/mm³，18% 杆状核粒细胞</td>
<td>Pronounced leukocytosis with marked left shift indicates severe acute bacterial infection<br />
显著白细胞增多伴明显核左移，提示严重急性细菌感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No focal infiltrates on chest x-ray<br />
胸片无局灶性浸润</td>
<td>Definitively excludes aspiration pneumonia as the primary fever source despite dysphagia risk factors<br />
尽管存在吞咽困难等危险因素，仍决定性地排除吸入性肺炎作为发热主要来源</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Alendronate (bisphosphonate) use<br />
服用阿仑膦酸钠（双膦酸盐）</td>
<td>Raises osteonecrosis of the jaw as a differential, but ONJ does not cause fever, erythema, or soft-tissue swelling — a deliberate distractor<br />
提示需鉴别颌骨骨坏死，但ONJ通常不引起发热、红肿及软组织肿胀——是一个刻意设置的干扰</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Decreased salivary flow** creates a stagnant, nutrient-rich environment within **Stensen's duct**, permitting oral flora and *Staphylococcus aureus* to migrate **retrogradely** into the **parotid gland parenchyma**, triggering **suppurative inflammation** and abscess formation:

**唾液流量减少**在 **Stensen 导管**内形成淤滞、富营养环境，使口腔菌群和\*金黄色葡萄球菌**\*逆行**迁移至**腮腺实质**，引发**化脓性炎症**及脓肿形成：

- Absent mastication + NPO state → ↓ parasympathetic stimulation of acinar cells → ↓ salivary secretion\
  缺乏咀嚼+禁食状态→腺泡细胞副交感神经刺激减少→唾液分泌减少

- Systemic dehydration + anticholinergic drugs (amitriptyline) → inspissated, thickened saliva → further ductal obstruction\
  全身脱水+抗胆碱能药物（阿米替林）→唾液浓缩变稠→导管进一步阻塞

- Bacterial retrograde seeding of stagnant duct → glandular parenchymal infection → neutrophilic infiltrate → pus\
  细菌逆行播种于淤滞导管→腺体实质感染→中性粒细胞浸润→化脓

- Dominant pathogen: *S. aureus* (most common); mixed oral anaerobes; gram-negative rods in severely debilitated patients\
  主要病原体：金黄色葡萄球菌（最常见）；混合口腔厌氧菌；重度体弱患者中可见革兰氏阴性杆菌

- Gland edema and purulent content expand the parotid capsule → overlying skin erythema, induration, and exquisite tenderness\
  腺体水肿及脓液使腮腺包膜膨胀→上覆皮肤出现红斑、硬结和极度触痛

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The parotid gland wraps around the angle of the mandible, so parotitis swelling characteristically spans from the anterior cheek to the inferoposterior jaw angle — this distribution distinguishes it from dental abscesses (more inferior, near tooth roots) or masticator space infections.

**解剖小窍门:** 腮腺包绕下颌角，因此腮腺炎肿胀特征性地从前方颊部延伸至后下方下颌角——此分布可与牙源性脓肿（位置偏下，近牙根）或咬肌间隙感染相鉴别。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Acute Suppurative Parotitis / 正确答案 (A) — 急性化脓性腮腺炎

**Acute suppurative parotitis** is a bacterial infection of the parotid gland that arises when salivary stasis allows retrograde ductal bacterial invasion, classically in elderly, debilitated, dehydrated, or NPO patients:

**急性化脓性腮腺炎**是腮腺的细菌性感染，由唾液淤滞导致细菌逆行侵入导管所致，经典地见于老年、体弱、脱水或禁食患者：

- Unilateral indurated, erythematous, exquisitely tender swelling spanning the cheek to the angle of the mandible\
  单侧硬结性、红肿、极度触痛肿块，从颊部延伸至下颌角

- High fever, leukocytosis with bandemia (WBC 28,000 + 18% bands here) indicating severe bacterial infection\
  高热，白细胞增多伴核左移（本例 WBC 28,000，18% 杆状核）提示严重细菌感染

- Risk factors present: elderly, NPO/tube feeds, xerostomia, anticholinergic drug (amitriptyline), debilitation, dehydration\
  存在危险因素：老年、禁食/管饲、口腔干燥、抗胆碱能药物（阿米替林）、体质虚弱、脱水

- Most common pathogen: *S. aureus*; consider MRSA in healthcare-associated cases\
  最常见病原体：金黄色葡萄球菌；医疗相关病例应考虑MRSA

- Pus expressible from Stensen's duct orifice on bimanual massage is pathognomonic when present\
  双手按摩腮腺时 Stensen 导管开口可挤出脓液，具有诊断意义

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis (fever + unilateral parotid swelling + tenderness + xerostomia); ultrasound or CT with contrast to evaluate for abscess and delineate extent; Gram stain and culture of pus if expressible.

**诊断:** 临床诊断（发热+单侧腮腺肿胀+触痛+口腔干燥）；超声或增强CT评估脓肿并明确累及范围；若能挤出脓液则行革兰染色和培养。

**Treatment:** IV antistaphylococcal antibiotics (nafcillin/oxacillin; vancomycin if MRSA suspected); aggressive IV hydration; oral hygiene; surgical incision and drainage if abscess develops.

**治疗:** 静脉抗葡萄球菌抗生素（奈夫西林/苯唑西林；若怀疑MRSA则用万古霉素）；积极静脉补液；口腔护理；若形成脓肿则切开引流。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Acute suppurative parotitis ✓<br />
A — 急性化脓性腮腺炎 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Unilateral tender erythematous mass at angle of mandible + xerostomia + NPO + leukocytosis with bandemia all converge on suppurative parotitis<br />
正确——下颌角单侧触痛红肿肿块+口腔干燥+禁食+白细胞增多伴核左移，均汇聚指向化脓性腮腺炎</td>
<td>Parotid anatomy + complete risk factor profile (NPO, dry mouth, elderly, amitriptyline, debilitated)<br />
腮腺解剖位置+完整危险因素组合（禁食、口干、老年、阿米替林、体弱）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Aspiration pneumonia<br />
B — 吸入性肺炎</td>
<td>Although at risk (dysphagia, tube feeds), chest x-ray shows NO focal infiltrates — definitively ruling out pneumonia as the fever source; bilateral crackles reflect CHF/atelectasis<br />
虽存在高危因素（吞咽困难、管饲），但胸片无局灶性浸润——决定性地排除肺炎作为发热来源；双肺啰音反映心力衰竭/肺不张</td>
<td>Aspiration pneumonia requires radiographic infiltrate to explain fever; no infiltrate here<br />
吸入性肺炎需有影像学浸润才能解释发热；本例无浸润影</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Mandibular osteomyelitis<br />
C — 下颌骨骨髓炎</td>
<td>Can cause jaw pain but typically presents insidiously without acute erythema, prominent soft-tissue swelling, or high-grade fever unless far advanced; no dental infection source described<br />
可引起颌骨疼痛，但通常起病隐匿，无急性红肿或显著软组织肿胀及高热（除非进展严重）；无牙源性感染来源的描述</td>
<td>Acute soft-tissue inflammatory signs (erythema, edema, indurated tender mass) and acute 2-day onset favor parotitis<br />
急性软组织炎症体征（红肿、水肿、硬结性触痛肿块）和2天急性起病更支持腮腺炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Osteonecrosis of the jaw<br />
D — 颌骨骨坏死</td>
<td>Patient takes alendronate, but BRONJ presents as exposed necrotic bone without fever, erythema, or fluctuant soft-tissue swelling; bisphosphonate use is a deliberate red herring<br />
患者服用阿仑膦酸盐，但BRONJ表现为暴露坏死骨，无发热、红肿或波动性软组织肿胀；双膦酸盐使用是刻意设置的干扰</td>
<td>ONJ is afebrile and lacks soft-tissue inflammatory signs; fever + erythema + leukocytosis rule it out<br />
ONJ无发热且缺乏软组织炎症体征；发热+红肿+白细胞增多可排除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Urinary tract infection<br />
E — 尿路感染</td>
<td>UTI is a common fever source in nursing home patients but cannot explain the localized facial mass, erythema, and tenderness — the facial finding demands a facial diagnosis<br />
UTI是养老院患者常见发热来源，但无法解释局部面部肿块、红肿和触痛——面部体征需要面部诊断</td>
<td>UTI causes systemic fever but no focal facial examination finding; always explain the localizing sign<br />
UTI可引起全身发热但无局部面部体征；始终需解释定位体征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is aspiration pneumonia given the dysphagia and tube feeds, but the absence of chest x-ray infiltrates is the decisive clue that eliminates it — never accept a diagnosis that cannot explain the localizing physical finding.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是吸入性肺炎（因吞咽困难和管饲的存在），但胸片无浸润影是排除它的决定性线索——永远不要接受一个无法解释局部体征的诊断。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Suppurative Parotitis vs. Mandibular Osteomyelitis vs. Jaw Osteonecrosis (BRONJ) / 化脓性腮腺炎 vs. 下颌骨骨髓炎 vs. 颌骨骨坏死（BRONJ）对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Suppurative Parotitis</strong><br />
<strong>化脓性腮腺炎</strong></th>
<th><strong>Mandibular Osteomyelitis</strong><br />
<strong>下颌骨骨髓炎</strong></th>
<th><strong>Jaw Osteonecrosis (BRONJ)</strong><br />
<strong>颌骨骨坏死（BRONJ）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Key risk factors<br />
主要危险因素</td>
<td>Elderly, NPO/tube feeds, dehydration, anticholinergic meds, debilitation<br />
老年、禁食/管饲、脱水、抗胆碱能药物、体弱</td>
<td>Dental infection/trauma, immunosuppression, diabetes<br />
牙源性感染/外伤、免疫抑制、糖尿病</td>
<td>Bisphosphonates/denosumab, radiation, dental procedures, steroids<br />
双膦酸盐/地舒单抗、放疗、口腔操作、激素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever<br />
发热</td>
<td>Yes — high-grade, acute onset<br />
是——高热、急性起病</td>
<td>Possible if severe/advanced<br />
严重/进展期时可出现</td>
<td>No (unless secondarily infected)<br />
无（除非继发感染）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Soft tissue erythema &amp; swelling<br />
软组织红肿</td>
<td>Yes — hallmark finding<br />
是——标志性表现</td>
<td>Minimal unless severe<br />
轻微，除非严重</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Exposed necrotic bone<br />
坏死骨暴露</td>
<td>No<br />
无</td>
<td>Possible in advanced cases<br />
晚期可能出现</td>
<td>Yes — pathognomonic<br />
是——特征性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocytosis with bandemia<br />
白细胞增多伴核左移</td>
<td>Marked (WBC &gt;15,000, bands prominent)<br />
明显（WBC&gt;15,000，杆状核突出）</td>
<td>Moderate<br />
中度</td>
<td>Typically absent<br />
通常无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anatomic location<br />
解剖位置</td>
<td>Cheek to angle of mandible (parotid gland)<br />
颊部至下颌角（腮腺）</td>
<td>Mandibular body/ramus<br />
下颌骨体/升支</td>
<td>Alveolar ridge, mandible/maxilla<br />
牙槽嵴、下颌骨/上颌骨</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management<br />
治疗</td>
<td>IV antistaphylococcal antibiotics ± surgical drainage<br />
静脉抗葡萄球菌抗生素±手术引流</td>
<td>IV antibiotics + surgical debridement<br />
静脉抗生素+手术清创</td>
<td>Discontinue offending agent; debridement; hyperbaric O₂ in refractory cases<br />
停用致病药物；清创；难治性病例可用高压氧</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An elderly, debilitated, NPO patient with dry mouth and a unilateral tender erythematous mass at the angle of the mandible most likely has acute suppurative parotitis caused by salivary stasis and retrograde bacterial ductal invasion.**

**老年体弱、禁食、口腔干燥、下颌角单侧触痛红肿肿块的患者，最可能是由唾液淤滞和细菌逆行侵入导管引起的急性化脓性腮腺炎。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — FEAST for Suppurative Parotitis / 记忆钩 — FEAST 记化脓性腮腺炎:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>F</strong>ever + Facial mass at angle of mandible — cardinal presentation of parotitis / 发热+下颌角面部肿块——腮腺炎的主要表现<br />
• <strong>E</strong>lderly and debilitated — highest-risk demographic / 老年体弱——最高风险人群<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bsent oral intake (NPO/tube feed) — removes salivary flow stimulation / 无口服摄入（禁食/管饲）——去除唾液分泌刺激<br />
• <strong>S</strong>taph aureus — dominant causative pathogen / 金黄色葡萄球菌——主要致病菌<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hick dried saliva from dehydration — stagnant duct enables retrograde infection / 脱水致唾液浓稠——导管淤滞使细菌逆行感染成为可能</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Acute Suppurative Parotitis / 高频知识表 — 急性化脓性腮腺炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Epidemiology &amp; risk factors<br />
流行病学及危险因素</td>
<td>Elderly, hospitalized, institutionalized, NPO/tube-fed, post-surgical, dehydrated; also salivary duct calculi or tumor obstruction<br />
老年、住院、入住机构、禁食/管饲、术后、脱水；也见于唾液腺导管结石或肿瘤梗阻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Causative organisms<br />
致病菌</td>
<td><em>S. aureus</em> most common; mixed oral anaerobes; gram-negative rods (Pseudomonas, E. coli) in severely debilitated; consider MRSA in healthcare settings<br />
金黄色葡萄球菌最常见；混合口腔厌氧菌；重度体弱者中可见革兰氏阴性杆菌（铜绿假单胞菌、大肠杆菌）；医疗机构中应考虑MRSA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clinical diagnosis<br />
临床诊断</td>
<td>Unilateral painful parotid swelling + fever + leukocytosis; pus from Stensen's duct orifice on massage = pathognomonic; dry mouth supports diagnosis<br />
单侧腮腺区疼痛性肿胀+发热+白细胞增多；按摩腮腺时Stensen导管口流脓具有诊断意义；口腔干燥支持诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anticholinergic drug contribution<br />
抗胆碱能药物的作用</td>
<td>Drugs blocking muscarinic M3 receptors (amitriptyline, antihistamines, antipsychotics) reduce salivary secretion, contributing to xerostomia and parotitis risk<br />
阻断毒蕈碱M3受体的药物（阿米替林、抗组胺药、抗精神病药）减少唾液分泌，导致口腔干燥并增加腮腺炎风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Imaging<br />
影像学检查</td>
<td>Ultrasound (first-line): delineates gland extent, detects abscess, guides drainage; CT with contrast: better for deep neck space involvement or unclear diagnosis<br />
超声（首选）：显示腺体范围、检测脓肿、引导引流；增强CT：更适用于颈深间隙受累或诊断不明确时</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>IV antistaphylococcal antibiotics (nafcillin; vancomycin if MRSA risk); aggressive IV hydration; oral hygiene; surgical incision and drainage for abscess<br />
静脉抗葡萄球菌抗生素（奈夫西林；有MRSA风险时用万古霉素）；积极静脉补液；口腔卫生护理；脓肿形成时切开引流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Suppurative vs. viral parotitis<br />
化脓性 vs. 病毒性腮腺炎的鉴别</td>
<td>Viral (mumps): bilateral, younger patients, less toxic, no pus, elevated amylase; suppurative: unilateral, older/debilitated, toxic appearance, purulent, marked leukocytosis<br />
病毒性（腮腺炎）：双侧、较年轻、中毒表现轻、无脓液、淀粉酶升高；化脓性：单侧、老年/体弱、中毒表现明显、化脓、白细胞显著增多</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of unilateral facial swelling + fever:** Suppurative parotitis, masticator space abscess (dental origin, more lateral/buccal), Ludwig's angina (sublingual/submandibular floor-of-mouth, life-threatening airway risk), peritonsillar abscess (more posterior/uvular deviation) — location of the mass is the key anatomic discriminator\
  **单侧面部肿胀+发热的鉴别诊断:** 化脓性腮腺炎、咬肌间隙脓肿（牙源性，位置偏侧/颊部）、Ludwig 咽峡炎（舌下/颌下口底，有致命性气道风险）、扁桃体旁脓肿（位置偏后/悬雍垂偏斜）——肿块位置是关键解剖鉴别点

- **Bisphosphonate red herring strategy:** NBME frequently pairs a bisphosphonate (alendronate, zoledronate) with jaw symptoms to test whether you can distinguish BRONJ (exposed bone, afebrile, no soft-tissue inflammation) from infectious parotitis; recognize the deliberate distractor\
  **双膦酸盐干扰项策略:** NBME常将双膦酸盐（阿仑膦酸盐、唑来膦酸）与颌骨症状配对，考查能否鉴别BRONJ（骨质暴露、无发热、无软组织炎症）和感染性腮腺炎；识别这一刻意设置的干扰

- **Aspiration pneumonia trap:** Dysphagia + tube feeds reflexively suggest aspiration pneumonia, but always require a chest x-ray infiltrate before accepting it as the fever source; crackles alone (from CHF/atelectasis) are insufficient\
  **吸入性肺炎陷阱:** 吞咽困难+管饲会本能地联想到吸入性肺炎，但在接受其作为发热来源前，始终需要胸片浸润影；仅有啰音（源于心力衰竭/肺不张）不足以支持诊断

- **Key complication to know:** Untreated suppurative parotitis can extend into the deep neck spaces (parapharyngeal, retropharyngeal), causing necrotizing fasciitis or septic thrombophlebitis of the internal jugular vein (Lemierre's syndrome analog) — early IV antibiotics are essential\
  **需掌握的关键并发症:** 未治疗的化脓性腮腺炎可向颈深间隙（咽旁、咽后）扩散，引起坏死性筋膜炎或颈内静脉化脓性血栓性静脉炎（类似 Lemierre 综合征）——早期静脉抗生素治疗至关重要

# Question 54 — Febrile Nonhemolytic Transfusion Reaction / 发热性非溶血性输血反应

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>hospitalized 42-year-old man</strong> has <strong>chills</strong> and a <strong>temperature of 38.3°C (101°F)</strong> <strong>1 hour after transfusion of packed red blood cells</strong> for treatment of <strong>anemia secondary to a bleeding duodenal ulcer</strong>. He has <strong>never received a blood transfusion</strong> in the past. He has <strong>no known allergies</strong>. He is pale and flushed. He is 178 cm (5 ft 10 in) tall and weighs 79 kg (175 lb); BMI is 25 kg/m². His pulse is <strong>98/min</strong> and regular, and blood pressure is 128/82 mm Hg. Examination shows <strong>no abnormalities</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: The most appropriate next step in management is administration of which of the following?</strong></p>
<p>A) Oral acetaminophen<br />
B) Oral ibuprofen<br />
C) Subcutaneous epinephrine<br />
D) Intravenous diphenhydramine<br />
E) Intravenous methylprednisolone</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Fever (38.3°C) 1 hour after transfusion<br />
输血后 1 小时出现发热（38.3°C）</td>
<td>Timing during or shortly after transfusion is classic for FNHTR; fever is the hallmark symptom<br />
输血中或输血后短时间内出现发热是 FNHTR 的典型时间特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chills/rigors present<br />
寒战存在</td>
<td>Common accompanying symptom of FNHTR alongside fever; does NOT indicate severity<br />
寒战是 FNHTR 的常见伴随症状，并不代表病情危重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Never received a blood transfusion before<br />
从未输过血</td>
<td>Reduces likelihood of alloantibody-mediated hemolytic reaction from prior sensitization<br />
降低了既往致敏所致同种异体抗体介导溶血反应的可能性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No known allergies<br />
无已知过敏史</td>
<td>Makes anaphylactic or allergic transfusion reaction less likely<br />
降低过敏性或变态反应性输血反应的可能性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hemodynamically stable (BP 128/82, HR 98)<br />
血流动力学稳定（血压 128/82，心率 98）</td>
<td>Rules out anaphylaxis (hypotension) and acute hemolytic reaction (shock)<br />
排除过敏反应（低血压）和急性溶血性反应（休克）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Examination shows no abnormalities<br />
体格检查无异常</td>
<td>No bronchospasm, no urticaria, no back pain — rules out anaphylaxis and hemolytic reaction<br />
无支气管痉挛、无荨麻疹、无腰背痛——排除过敏反应和溶血反应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Underlying bleeding duodenal ulcer<br />
基础病为出血性十二指肠溃疡</td>
<td>Specifically contraindicates NSAIDs (risk of worsening GI bleeding); steers toward acetaminophen<br />
特别禁用 NSAIDs（加重消化道出血风险），提示应选择对乙酰氨基酚</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Febrile nonhemolytic transfusion reactions (FNHTRs)** are mediated by **cytokines** (IL-1, IL-6, TNF-α) that accumulate in blood products during storage, released by **donor leukocytes** undergoing apoptosis:

**发热性非溶血性输血反应（FNHTR）**由储存血液制品过程中积累的**细胞因子**（IL-1、IL-6、TNF-α）介导，这些细胞因子由**供体白细胞**凋亡时释放：

- Donor leukocytes in stored packed RBCs release pro-inflammatory cytokines throughout the storage period\
  储存红细胞中的供体白细胞在整个保存期间持续释放促炎细胞因子

- These cytokines trigger the hypothalamic thermostat upon infusion → fever and rigors in the recipient\
  输注时这些细胞因子激活下丘脑体温调节中枢 → 受者出现发热和寒战

- No antibody–RBC interaction occurs; therefore no hemolysis, no hemoglobinuria, no renal injury\
  无抗体–红细胞相互作用，因此无溶血、无血红蛋白尿、无肾损伤

- Prestorage leukoreduction (removing WBCs before storage) significantly reduces cytokine accumulation and FNHTR incidence\
  预存白细胞滤除（储存前去除白细胞）显著减少细胞因子积累，降低 FNHTR 发生率

**Prevention pearl:** Prestorage leukoreduction filters donor WBCs before storage, preventing cytokine buildup in the blood product — the most effective FNHTR prevention strategy.

**预防要点:** 预存白细胞滤除在储存前过滤供体白细胞，阻止细胞因子在血液制品中积累——是最有效的 FNHTR 预防策略。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Oral Acetaminophen / 正确答案 (A) — 口服对乙酰氨基酚

**Oral acetaminophen** is the antipyretic of choice for FNHTR — centrally inhibiting hypothalamic prostaglandin synthesis to reduce fever without the GI mucosal risks of NSAIDs:

**口服对乙酰氨基酚**是 FNHTR 的首选退热药——通过中枢抑制下丘脑前列腺素合成退热，且无 NSAIDs 的消化道黏膜损伤风险：

- Stop the transfusion immediately upon recognizing a febrile reaction — this is always the first step\
  识别发热反应后立即停止输血——这永远是第一步

- Administer oral acetaminophen for fever control; it is safe in patients with active peptic ulcer disease\
  给予口服对乙酰氨基酚控制发热；对活动性消化性溃疡患者安全

- Evaluate for other causes of fever including acute hemolytic reaction and bacterial contamination before resuming or discarding the unit\
  在继续输血或废弃血袋之前，评估其他发热原因，包括急性溶血反应和细菌污染

**Diagnosis:** Isolated fever ± rigors during or shortly after transfusion, with stable vitals, no urticaria, no dyspnea, no flank pain, no hemoglobinuria.

**诊断:** 输血中或输血后短时间内出现孤立性发热±寒战，生命体征稳定，无荨麻疹、无呼吸困难、无腰痛、无血红蛋白尿。

**Treatment:** Stop transfusion → administer oral acetaminophen → rule out hemolytic reaction and septic transfusion reaction before restarting.

**治疗:** 停止输血 → 给予口服对乙酰氨基酚 → 排除溶血反应和败血症性输血反应后方可重新开始输血。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Oral acetaminophen ✓<br />
A — 口服对乙酰氨基酚 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Antipyretic of choice; no GI mucosal risk; safe with active duodenal ulcer<br />
正确——首选退热药；无消化道黏膜损伤风险；活动性十二指肠溃疡患者安全</td>
<td>Treats fever without exacerbating underlying GI disease<br />
退热同时不加重基础消化道疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Oral ibuprofen<br />
B — 口服布洛芬</td>
<td>NSAID that treats fever but inhibits prostaglandin-mediated mucosal protection — specifically contraindicated with active duodenal ulcer and GI bleeding<br />
NSAIDs 可退热但抑制前列腺素介导的黏膜保护——活动性十二指肠溃疡及消化道出血时明确禁用</td>
<td>Same antipyretic efficacy as acetaminophen but unsafe GI profile in this patient<br />
退热效果与对乙酰氨基酚相当，但本患者消化道安全性差</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Subcutaneous epinephrine<br />
C — 皮下注射肾上腺素</td>
<td>First-line for anaphylaxis (bronchospasm, urticaria, hypotension, angioedema) — none of which are present here<br />
过敏反应的一线治疗（支气管痉挛、荨麻疹、低血压、血管性水肿）——本患者均无上述表现</td>
<td>Anaphylaxis: hypotension + urticaria + bronchospasm; here only isolated fever<br />
过敏反应：低血压+荨麻疹+支气管痉挛；本例仅有孤立性发热</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Intravenous diphenhydramine<br />
D — 静脉注射苯海拉明</td>
<td>Used for anaphylaxis or isolated transfusion-associated urticaria — no hives or allergic symptoms present; antihistamines do not treat cytokine-mediated FNHTR<br />
用于过敏反应或输血相关孤立性荨麻疹——本患者无荨麻疹或过敏症状；抗组胺药不能治疗细胞因子介导的 FNHTR</td>
<td>FNHTR is cytokine-mediated, not histamine-mediated<br />
FNHTR 由细胞因子介导，而非组胺介导</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Intravenous methylprednisolone<br />
E — 静脉注射甲泼尼龙</td>
<td>Corticosteroid used as adjunct in severe anaphylaxis — grossly excessive for isolated FNHTR with stable vitals<br />
皮质类固醇作为严重过敏反应的辅助治疗——对生命体征稳定的孤立性 FNHTR 明显过度</td>
<td>Steroids reserved for severe allergic reactions; cytokine-mediated fever does not require immunosuppression<br />
激素保留用于严重过敏反应；细胞因子介导的发热不需要免疫抑制治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is B (oral ibuprofen) — it would effectively treat the fever, and many test-takers forget the patient's duodenal ulcer when focusing on the transfusion reaction. The question specifically embeds a contraindication to NSAIDs to reward complete clinical synthesis over partial diagnosis.*

最容易错的干扰项是 B（口服布洛芬）——它确实能有效退热，但很多考生在关注输血反应时忘记了患者的十二指肠溃疡病史。本题特意嵌入 NSAIDs 禁忌证，以奖励完整临床综合分析而非片面诊断。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — FNHTR vs. Acute Hemolytic vs. Anaphylaxis vs. Septic Transfusion Reaction / 四类输血反应鉴别对比

<table>
<colgroup>

<th><strong>Acute Hemolytic</strong><br />
<strong>急性溶血性</strong></th>
<th><strong>Anaphylaxis</strong><br />
<strong>过敏性</strong></th>
<th><strong>Septic Reaction</strong><br />
<strong>败血症性</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
机制</td>
<td>Cytokines from donor leukocytes<br />
供体白细胞细胞因子</td>
<td>ABO mismatch → complement → RBC lysis<br />
ABO 不相容→补体→红细胞溶解</td>
<td>IgE or anti-IgA antibodies → mast cell degranulation<br />
IgE 或抗 IgA 抗体→肥大细胞脱颗粒</td>

不典型</td>

荨麻疹/支气管痉挛</td>

<td>No<br />

<td>Unstable — shock possible<br />
不稳定——可能休克</td>
<td>Unstable — hypotension<br />
不稳定——低血压</td>
<td>Unstable — septic shock<br />

<tr>
<td>Labs<br />

<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
<td>↑LDH, ↑bilirubin, ↓haptoglobin, hemoglobinuria<br />
LDH↑、胆红素↑、触珠蛋白↓、血红蛋白尿</td>
<td>Normal (↑tryptase possible)<br />
正常（类胰蛋白酶可能升高）</td>
<td>↑WBC, positive blood cultures<br />
白细胞升高，血培养阳性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Stop transfusion + acetaminophen<br />
停止输血+对乙酰氨基酚</td>
<td>Stop transfusion + IV fluids + renal monitoring<br />
停止输血+静脉补液+监测肾功能</td>
<td>Epinephrine ± diphenhydramine ± methylprednisolone<br />
肾上腺素±苯海拉明±甲泼尼龙</td>
<td>Stop transfusion + broad-spectrum antibiotics<br />
停止输血+广谱抗生素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prevention<br />
预防</td>
<td>Prestorage leukoreduction<br />
预存白细胞滤除</td>
<td>Strict ABO crossmatch<br />
严格 ABO 交叉配血</td>
<td>Washed RBCs (for IgA deficiency)<br />
洗涤红细胞（IgA 缺乏症）</td>
<td>Proper blood storage protocols<br />
规范血液储存流程</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Febrile nonhemolytic transfusion reaction = isolated fever ± rigors from stored cytokines in donor leukocytes; treat by stopping the transfusion and giving oral acetaminophen — not NSAIDs when the patient has a GI ulcer.**

**发热性非溶血性输血反应 = 供体白细胞储存细胞因子所致孤立性发热±寒战；治疗为停止输血并给予口服对乙酰氨基酚——当患者有消化道溃疡时不用 NSAIDs。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "STOP the C.A.R." for FNHTR / 记忆钩 — FNHTR 用 "STOP C.A.R." 记忆:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>top the transfusion first — always step 1 / 首先停止输血——永远是第一步<br />
• <strong>T</strong>emperature isolated — fever alone (no urticaria, no shock) = FNHTR / 孤立性体温升高——仅发热（无荨麻疹、无休克）= FNHTR<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ral acetaminophen — NOT ibuprofen (ulcer risk!) / 口服对乙酰氨基酚——不用布洛芬（溃疡风险！）<br />
• <strong>P</strong>restorage leukoreduction — the prevention / 预存白细胞滤除——预防措施<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ytokines — the culprit mechanism / 细胞因子——致病机制<br />
• <strong>A</strong>BO mismatch ruled out — hemolysis absent / 排除 ABO 不匹配——无溶血<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ule out septic reaction — cultures if high fever / 排除败血症性反应——高热时送血培养</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Transfusion Reactions / 高频知识表 — 输血反应

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>FNHTR definition and incidence<br />
FNHTR 定义与发生率</td>
<td>Fever rise ≥1°C ± rigors during/after transfusion; most common transfusion reaction; benign and self-limited<br />
输血中/后体温升高≥1°C±寒战；最常见的输血反应；良性、自限性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>FNHTR pathophysiology<br />
FNHTR 病理生理</td>
<td>IL-1, IL-6, TNF-α from donor leukocytes accumulate during storage; activate recipient hypothalamus<br />
储存期间供体白细胞产生的 IL-1、IL-6、TNF-α积累；激活受者下丘脑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prestorage leukoreduction<br />
预存白细胞滤除</td>
<td>Removes WBCs from blood product before storage → less cytokine accumulation → reduced FNHTR; also reduces CMV transmission and alloimmunization<br />
储存前去除白细胞→细胞因子积累减少→FNHTR 降低；同时减少 CMV 传播和同种异体免疫</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute hemolytic transfusion reaction<br />
急性溶血性输血反应</td>
<td>ABO incompatibility (clerical error most common cause); fever + flank/back pain + hemoglobinuria + DIC + shock; must stop transfusion immediately<br />
ABO 不相容（文书错误最常见）；发热+腰背痛+血红蛋白尿+DIC+休克；必须立即停止输血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Delayed hemolytic transfusion reaction<br />
迟发性溶血性输血反应</td>
<td>Occurs 3-10 days post-transfusion; anamnestic antibody response (non-ABO); extravascular hemolysis; less severe than acute<br />
输血后 3-10 天发生；回忆性抗体反应（非 ABO）；血管外溶血；较急性溶血轻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Transfusion-related anaphylaxis<br />
输血相关过敏反应</td>
<td>Most common in IgA-deficient patients with anti-IgA antibodies; urticaria + bronchospasm + hypotension; treat with epinephrine; use IgA-deficient or washed blood products for prevention<br />
最常见于有抗 IgA 抗体的 IgA 缺乏患者；荨麻疹+支气管痉挛+低血压；肾上腺素治疗；预防用 IgA 缺乏或洗涤血液制品</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Transfusion-associated circulatory overload (TACO)<br />
输血相关循环超负荷</td>
<td>Pulmonary edema + hypertension + respiratory distress within 6 hours; most common in elderly and cardiac patients; treat with diuretics and oxygen<br />
6 小时内出现肺水肿+高血压+呼吸困难；最常见于老年和心脏病患者；利尿剂和吸氧治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Transfusion-related acute lung injury (TRALI)<br />
输血相关急性肺损伤</td>
<td>Non-cardiogenic pulmonary edema within 6 hours; donor anti-HLA or anti-HNA antibodies attack recipient neutrophils; fever + hypoxia + bilateral infiltrates; supportive care<br />
6 小时内非心源性肺水肿；供体抗 HLA 或抗 HNA 抗体攻击受者中性粒细胞；发热+低氧血症+双侧浸润影；支持治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of post-transfusion fever:** Stop transfusion first, then distinguish FNHTR (isolated fever, stable), acute hemolytic reaction (fever + back pain + hemoglobinuria), septic reaction (high fever, shock, from platelet contamination most often), and TRALI (fever + respiratory failure)\
  **输血后发热鉴别诊断:** 先停止输血，再区分 FNHTR（孤立性发热，稳定）、急性溶血反应（发热+腰背痛+血红蛋白尿）、败血症性反应（高热、休克，最常来自血小板污染）和 TRALI（发热+呼吸衰竭）

- **Variant — premedication controversy:** Some protocols premedicate with acetaminophen ± diphenhydramine before transfusion in patients with prior FNHTR; current evidence does not support routine premedication but it is practiced widely\
  **题目变式——预用药争议:** 部分医院对既往有 FNHTR 史的患者输血前预防性给予对乙酰氨基酚±苯海拉明；目前证据不支持常规预用药，但临床广泛使用

- **Key NSAID contraindication:** NSAIDs inhibit COX-1 → reduced prostaglandin E2 and prostacyclin → loss of gastric/duodenal mucosal protection + impaired platelet aggregation → exacerbated GI ulceration and bleeding; this makes acetaminophen the only safe antipyretic choice here\
  **NSAIDs 关键禁忌证:** NSAIDs 抑制 COX-1 → 前列腺素 E2 和前列环素减少 → 胃/十二指肠黏膜保护丧失+血小板聚集受损 → 加重消化道溃疡和出血；这使对乙酰氨基酚成为本例唯一安全的退热药选择

- **Risk factors for FNHTR:** Platelet transfusions (higher leukocyte content) \> packed RBCs; longer storage time; prior transfusions or pregnancies (sensitization); children receiving large-volume transfusions\
  **FNHTR 危险因素:** 血小板输注（白细胞含量更高）\> 浓缩红细胞；储存时间越长风险越高；既往输血或妊娠史（致敏）；接受大容量输血的儿童

# Question 55 — Neurogenic Bladder (Diabetic Overflow Incontinence) / 神经源性膀胱（糖尿病充溢性尿失禁）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>A 77-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>1-year history of frequent urinary incontinence during the day and at night</strong>. The incontinence is <strong>not associated with coughing or sneezing</strong>, and she <strong>does not have urinary urgency before the episodes</strong>. She has not had pain with urination or vaginal discharge. She has a <strong>10-year history of type 2 diabetes mellitus</strong> well controlled with metformin. Her other medications are atorvastatin and lisinopril. Examination shows some wetting of an absorbent pad that she is wearing. Results of laboratory studies are shown: Hemoglobin A1c 6.2%; Serum Na+ 138 mEq/L, K+ 3.7 mEq/L, Cl- 98 mEq/L, HCO3- 26 mEq/L, Urea nitrogen 12 mg/dL, <strong>Glucose 180 mg/dL</strong>, Creatinine 1.1 mg/dL; Urine pH normal, Glucose 1+, <strong>Protein 2+</strong>, RBC none, WBC 3/hpf, Casts none.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's urinary incontinence?</strong></p>
<p>A) Hyperglycemia<br />
B) Interstitial cystitis<br />
C) Medication adverse effect<br />
D) Neurogenic bladder<br />
E) Stress incontinence</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>77-year-old woman with 10-year T2DM<br />
77岁女性，T2DM病史10年</td>
<td>Long-standing diabetes is the strongest risk factor for autonomic neuropathy; duration correlates with neuropathy severity<br />
长期糖尿病是自主神经病变的最强危险因素；病程越长，神经病变越重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Incontinence not associated with coughing or sneezing<br />
尿失禁与咳嗽/打喷嚏无关</td>
<td>Explicitly excludes stress incontinence, which requires increased intra-abdominal pressure as the trigger<br />
明确排除压力性尿失禁，后者需腹压增加作为诱因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No urinary urgency before episodes<br />
漏尿前无尿急感</td>
<td>Excludes urge incontinence; in neurogenic overflow, afferent sensation is impaired so there is no warning urgency<br />
排除急迫性尿失禁；神经源性充溢中传入感觉受损，无预警性尿急</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Incontinence occurs both day and night<br />
昼夜均有尿失禁</td>
<td>Continuous passive leakage pattern points to overflow incontinence rather than situational or urgency-driven loss<br />
持续被动漏尿模式指向充溢性尿失禁，而非情境性或急迫性尿失禁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum glucose 180 mg/dL with HbA1c only 6.2%<br />
血糖180 mg/dL但HbA1c仅6.2%</td>
<td>Good overall control does NOT exclude established neuropathy — prior years of suboptimal control may have already caused irreversible nerve damage<br />
整体控制良好并不排除已发生的神经病变——既往血糖控制不佳可能已造成不可逆神经损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urine protein 2+<br />
尿蛋白2+</td>
<td>Suggests concurrent diabetic nephropathy — a marker of generalized diabetic microvascular complications including neuropathy<br />
提示合并糖尿病肾病——全身性糖尿病微血管并发症（含神经病变）的标志</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Diabetic autonomic neuropathy** damages **unmyelinated autonomic fibers** innervating the detrusor muscle and bladder neck, progressively impairing the afferent limb of the micturition reflex:

**糖尿病自主神经病变**损伤支配**逼尿肌**和膀胱颈的**无髓鞘自主神经纤维**，逐渐损害排尿反射的传入弧：

- Loss of afferent stretch sensation → patient is unaware the bladder is filling or full\
  传入牵张感觉丧失→患者感知不到膀胱正在充盈或已充满

- Detrusor becomes hypotonic/acontractile → bladder gradually overdistends with large residual volume\
  逼尿肌变为低张力/无收缩→膀胱逐渐过度膨胀，积聚大量残余尿

- Once intravesical hydrostatic pressure exceeds internal and external sphincter closing pressure → passive overflow leakage occurs without any urgency warning\
  一旦膀胱内静水压超过内外括约肌关闭压→发生被动充溢性漏尿，无任何尿急预警

- Clinical result: infrequent voiding, weak stream, incomplete emptying, continuous dribbling day and night\
  临床结果：排尿次数减少、尿流细弱、排空不完全、昼夜持续滴尿

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Neurogenic bladder = "full but can't feel it" → bladder silently overdistends until hydrostatic overflow defeats the sphincter

**解剖小窍门:** 神经源性膀胱="满了但感觉不到"→膀胱无声过度充盈，直至静水压充溢突破括约肌

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Neurogenic Bladder / 正确答案 (D) — 神经源性膀胱

**Neurogenic bladder** from diabetic autonomic neuropathy disrupts both the efferent (detrusor contraction) and afferent (stretch sensation) arcs of bladder control, producing the classic overflow incontinence pattern seen in this patient:

**神经源性膀胱**由糖尿病自主神经病变破坏膀胱控制的传出弧（逼尿肌收缩）和传入弧（牵张感觉），产生该患者典型的充溢性尿失禁表现：

- Absent urgency sensation + passive continuous leakage = hallmark of overflow/neurogenic incontinence\
  无尿急感+被动持续漏尿=充溢性/神经源性尿失禁的标志

- Elevated postvoid residual (PVR \>300 mL) on bladder ultrasound is the key confirmatory finding\
  膀胱超声残余尿增多（PVR \>300 mL）是关键确认性发现

- Concurrent urine protein 2+ supports generalized diabetic microvascular disease affecting multiple organ systems\
  尿蛋白2+支持影响多器官系统的全身性糖尿病微血管病变

**Diagnosis:** Bladder ultrasound for postvoid residual; urodynamic studies confirm acontractile detrusor; cystometry if needed

**诊断:** 膀胱超声测量残余尿；尿动力学检查证实逼尿肌无收缩；必要时行膀胱测压

**Treatment:** Timed voiding, clean intermittent self-catheterization (CIC) as first-line; alpha-blockers (tamsulosin) reduce bladder neck resistance; bethanechol (muscarinic agonist) occasionally used to enhance detrusor contractility

**治疗:** 定时排尿、清洁间歇性自我导尿（CIC）为一线治疗；α受体阻滞剂（坦索罗辛）降低膀胱颈阻力；贝坦尼克（毒蕈碱激动剂）偶尔用于增强逼尿肌收缩力

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Hyperglycemia<br />
A — 高血糖</td>
<td>Osmotic diuresis causes polyuria with urinary frequency and urgency — but NOT passive overflow incontinence without any urgency sensation<br />
渗透性利尿引起多尿伴尿频和尿急——但不会引起无尿急感的被动充溢性尿失禁</td>
<td>HbA1c 6.2% shows well-controlled overall glycemia; current glucose 180 is insufficient to drive symptomatic osmotic diuresis causing incontinence<br />
HbA1c 6.2%提示整体血糖控制良好；当前血糖180不足以引起导致尿失禁的症状性渗透性利尿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Interstitial cystitis<br />
B — 间质性膀胱炎</td>
<td>IC presents with urinary frequency, urgency, chronic suprapubic pain, and dyspareunia — this patient has none of these features<br />
IC表现为尿频、尿急、慢性耻骨上疼痛和性交痛——该患者均无上述特征</td>
<td>No pain, no urgency, no pelvic symptoms; IC is an inflammatory condition, not an overflow disorder<br />
无疼痛、无尿急、无盆腔症状；IC是炎症性疾病，而非充溢性疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Medication adverse effect<br />
C — 药物不良反应</td>
<td>Metformin, atorvastatin, and lisinopril do not cause incontinence; diuretics can cause urgency/frequency, but no diuretic is prescribed here<br />
二甲双胍、阿托伐他汀、赖诺普利均不导致尿失禁；利尿剂可引起尿急/尿频，但该患者未用利尿剂</td>
<td>None of the three listed medications carry incontinence as a recognized adverse effect; ACE inhibitor cough is unrelated to bladder<br />
三种药物均无尿失禁作为公认不良反应；ACE抑制剂干咳与膀胱功能无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Neurogenic bladder ✓<br />
D — 神经源性膀胱 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Long-standing T2DM + incontinence without urgency + no exertional trigger = classic overflow incontinence from diabetic autonomic neuropathy<br />
正确——长期T2DM+无尿急的尿失禁+无用力诱因=糖尿病自主神经病变典型充溢性尿失禁</td>
<td>Passive continuous leakage day and night without warning is the defining pattern of neurogenic overflow incontinence<br />
昼夜无预警的被动持续漏尿是神经源性充溢性尿失禁的定义性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Stress incontinence<br />
E — 压力性尿失禁</td>
<td>Stress incontinence is triggered by increased intra-abdominal pressure (cough, sneeze, Valsalva) — the stem explicitly states this is absent<br />
压力性尿失禁由腹压增加（咳嗽、打喷嚏、Valsalva动作）诱发——题干明确指出不存在此诱因</td>
<td>Single stem clue "not associated with coughing or sneezing" is sufficient to eliminate Choice E with certainty<br />
"与咳嗽或打喷嚏无关"这一题干线索足以确定地排除E选项</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is A (Hyperglycemia) because this patient has diabetes with an elevated glucose; however, osmotic diuresis produces urgency and frequency with awareness, not silent passive overflow without any warning sensation.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是A（高血糖），因为患者有糖尿病且血糖升高；但渗透性利尿产生有自觉意识的尿急和尿频，而非毫无预警感觉的被动充溢性漏尿。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Types of Urinary Incontinence / 尿失禁类型鉴别

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />

<strong>压力性</strong></th>
<th><strong>Urge</strong><br />
<strong>急迫性</strong></th>
</tr>
