</tr>
<tr>
<td>Scope of Universal Protocol<br />
通用规程的适用范围</td>
<td>ALL invasive procedures — operating rooms, bedside, endoscopy suites, interventional radiology, not only ORs<br />
所有侵入性操作——手术室、床边、内镜室、介入放射，不仅限于手术室</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wrong-site surgery as sentinel event<br />
手术部位错误作为哨兵事件</td>
<td>Wrong-site surgery is a Joint Commission "sentinel event" — requires immediate investigation and root cause analysis<br />
手术部位错误是联合委员会的"哨兵事件"——需要立即调查和根本原因分析</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **WHO Surgical Safety Checklist:** Broader international equivalent with three phases — Sign In (before anesthesia induction), Time Out (before skin incision), Sign Out (before patient leaves OR); validated to reduce surgical mortality\
  **WHO手术安全核查表:** 更广泛的国际同类规程，分三阶段——签入（麻醉诱导前）、暂停（切皮前）、签出（患者离开手术室前）；已验证可降低手术死亡率

- **Quality improvement tools:** Universal Protocol is one of many QI tools; others include PDSA cycles, root cause analysis (RCA), failure mode and effects analysis (FMEA), and lean/Six Sigma\
  **质量改进工具:** 通用规程是众多质量改进工具之一；其他工具包括PDSA循环、根本原因分析（RCA）、失效模式与影响分析（FMEA）和精益/六西格玛

- **Site marking exceptions:** Procedures involving teeth, premature infants (skin marking not appropriate), or single-organ cases (e.g., Cesarean section) may have modified or waived marking requirements\
  **部位标记例外情况:** 涉及牙齿、早产儿（皮肤标记不适用）或单器官手术（如剖宫产）的操作可能有修改或豁免的标记要求

- **Discrepancy resolution:** Any discrepancy identified during verification must be resolved before proceeding — the procedure should be paused until all team members are in agreement\
  **差异处理:** 核查过程中发现的任何差异必须在继续前解决——手术应暂停直至所有团队成员达成一致

# Question 65 — Bilateral Recurrent Laryngeal Nerve Paralysis / 双侧喉返神经麻痹

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Immediately after extubation</strong> following a <strong>total thyroidectomy</strong>, a <strong>72-year-old woman</strong> has <strong>stridor</strong> and <strong>shortness of breath</strong>. She has a history of transient ischemic attacks and coronary artery disease. Her only medication is aspirin. She appears to be in distress and is gasping for air. Her pulse is <strong>100/min</strong>, respirations are <strong>35/min</strong>, and blood pressure is 170/100 mm Hg. Examination shows an <strong>intact surgical incision</strong> and <strong>no ecchymosis</strong>. <strong>Breath sounds are decreased bilaterally</strong>. Arterial blood gas analysis on 40% oxygen by face mask shows: <strong>pH 7.3</strong>, <strong>PCO2 60 mm Hg</strong>, PO2 200 mm Hg, O2 saturation 99%.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cerebral infarction<br />
B) Extrinsic tracheal compression<br />
C) Laryngeal nerve paralysis<br />
D) Pulmonary embolism<br />
E) Tension pneumothorax</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Immediately after extubation post-total thyroidectomy<br />
全甲状腺切除术后即刻拔管</td>
<td>Timing points to a surgical complication, not a delayed process like PE or hematoma<br />
时间节点提示术中并发症，排除 PE 或迟发血肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Stridor<br />
喘鸣音</td>
<td>Indicates upper airway obstruction (larynx/trachea level), not lower airway or parenchymal disease<br />
提示上气道梗阻（喉/气管水平），非下气道或肺实质病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Decreased breath sounds bilaterally<br />
双侧呼吸音减弱</td>
<td>Suggests poor airflow through a central obstruction, not unilateral pathology like pneumothorax<br />
提示中央性气流减少，而非单侧病变如气胸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Intact incision, no ecchymosis<br />
切口完整，无瘀斑</td>
<td>Rules out expanding hematoma causing extrinsic tracheal compression<br />
排除血肿扩张压迫气管的可能</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PCO2 60, pH 7.3<br />
PCO2 60，pH 7.3</td>
<td>Respiratory acidosis from hypoventilation — hallmark of upper airway obstruction with CO2 retention<br />
通气不足所致呼吸性酸中毒，是上气道梗阻伴 CO2 潴留的标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PO2 200 on 40% O2<br />
40% 吸氧下 PO2 200</td>
<td>Oxygenation is maintained by supplemental O2; the problem is ventilation (CO2 clearance), not diffusion<br />
氧合靠补充 O2 维持；问题在通气（清除 CO2），而非弥散</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **recurrent laryngeal nerves (RLNs)** run in the tracheoesophageal groove posterior to each thyroid lobe and provide **motor innervation to nearly all intrinsic laryngeal muscles**, including the **posterior cricoarytenoid** (the sole abductor of the vocal cords):

**喉返神经（RLN）**走行于甲状腺两叶后方的气管食管沟内，支配**几乎所有喉内肌**，包括**环杓后肌**（声带唯一的外展肌）：

- Unilateral RLN injury → ipsilateral cord paralysis in adducted/paramedian position → hoarseness only\
  单侧 RLN 损伤 → 同侧声带固定于内收/旁正中位 → 仅声音嘶哑

- Bilateral RLN injury → both cords fixed medially → glottic aperture nearly closed → **severe upper airway obstruction**\
  双侧 RLN 损伤 → 双侧声带固定于正中位 → 声门裂几乎关闭 → **严重上气道梗阻**

- CO2 rises because ventilation is obstructed; O2 saturation can remain high if supplemental O2 overcomes diffusion capacity\
  CO2 升高是因通气受阻；若补充 O2 足够，弥散尚可，氧饱和度仍可维持

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The RLN on the right loops around the right subclavian artery; on the left it loops around the aortic arch — both ascend medially into the tracheoesophageal groove directly behind the thyroid, making them vulnerable during dissection.

**解剖小窍门:** 右侧喉返神经绕右锁骨下动脉，左侧绕主动脉弓——两侧均沿气管食管沟上行，紧贴甲状腺后方，手术分离时极易误伤。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Bilateral Recurrent Laryngeal Nerve Paralysis / 正确答案 (C) — 双侧喉返神经麻痹

**Bilateral recurrent laryngeal nerve paralysis** is the classic catastrophic complication of total thyroidectomy that presents immediately after extubation with stridor and respiratory failure:

**双侧喉返神经麻痹**是全甲状腺切除术后最典型的灾难性并发症，在拔管后即刻以喘鸣和呼吸衰竭起病：

- Both vocal cords are denervated and assume the adducted midline position, leaving only a narrow glottic chink\
  双侧声带失神经支配，固定于内收正中位，声门裂极为狭窄

- Inspiratory stridor results from turbulent airflow forced through the near-closed glottis\
  吸气性喘鸣源于气流被迫通过近乎关闭的声门时产生的湍流

- Bilateral decreased breath sounds reflect globally reduced air entry, not pneumothorax or effusion\
  双侧呼吸音减弱反映整体进气减少，而非气胸或积液

- ABG shows hypercapnic (type 2) respiratory failure: ↑PCO2, ↓pH, normal-to-high PO2 on supplemental O2\
  血气提示高碳酸血症（Ⅱ型）呼吸衰竭：PCO2↑、pH↓、吸氧下 PO2 正常偏高

- Intraoperative nerve monitoring is used to identify RLNs and reduce this risk\
  术中神经监测用于识别喉返神经，降低此风险

**Diagnosis:** Immediate post-thyroidectomy stridor + bilateral decreased breath sounds + intact wound with no hematoma + hypercapnic respiratory failure = bilateral RLN injury until proven otherwise.

**诊断:** 甲状腺切除术后即刻喘鸣 + 双侧呼吸音减弱 + 切口完整无血肿 + 高碳酸血症性呼吸衰竭 = 除外其他原因前首先考虑双侧 RLN 损伤。

**Treatment:** Immediate reintubation to secure airway; tracheotomy may be required if intubation fails; long-term management depends on whether paralysis is neuropraxic (transient) or permanent.

**治疗:** 立即重新插管以保证气道安全；插管失败则行气管切开；远期处理取决于麻痹是神经失用（暂时性）还是永久性。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cerebral infarction<br />
A — 脑梗死</td>
<td>Wrong — would cause focal motor/sensory deficits or dysarthria, not stridor; no mechanism for bilateral upper airway obstruction<br />
错——导致局灶性运动/感觉障碍或构音障碍，不产生喘鸣；无双侧上气道梗阻机制</td>
<td>Cerebral infarction does not affect glottic patency<br />
脑梗死不影响声门通畅性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Extrinsic tracheal compression<br />
B — 气管外压性梗阻</td>
<td>Wrong — caused by post-op hematoma, but this patient has intact incision and NO ecchymosis/swelling; hematoma excluded<br />
错——由术后血肿引起，但此患者切口完整，无瘀斑/肿胀；血肿已排除</td>
<td>No ecchymosis + intact wound = no hematoma<br />
无瘀斑 + 切口完整 = 排除血肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Laryngeal nerve paralysis ✓<br />
C — 喉返神经麻痹 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — bilateral RLN injury during total thyroidectomy causes immediate post-extubation stridor from bilateral vocal cord adduction<br />
正确——全甲状腺切除术中双侧 RLN 损伤，拔管后即刻因双侧声带内收引起喘鸣</td>
<td>Timing + stridor + intact wound + bilat. decreased BS + hypercapnia<br />
时间 + 喘鸣 + 完整切口 + 双侧呼吸音减弱 + 高碳酸血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Pulmonary embolism<br />
D — 肺栓塞</td>
<td>Wrong — PE typically presents days after surgery; causes hypoxia (↓PO2) not hypercarbia; no stridor with PE<br />
错——PE 通常术后数天出现；导致低氧（PO2↓）而非高碳酸血症；PE 不产生喘鸣</td>
<td>PE onset: days post-op; ABG shows ↓PO2 not ↑PCO2; no stridor<br />
PE 发生在术后数天；血气示 PO2↓ 而非 PCO2↑；无喘鸣</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Tension pneumothorax<br />
E — 张力性气胸</td>
<td>Wrong — tension PTX causes UNILATERAL absent breath sounds, tracheal deviation, and HYPOTENSION; this patient is hypertensive with bilateral decreased sounds<br />
错——张力性气胸导致单侧呼吸音消失、气管偏移和低血压；此患者血压高且双侧减弱</td>
<td>Tension PTX = unilateral absent BS + hypotension + tracheal deviation; this case = bilateral ↓BS + hypertension<br />
张力性气胸 = 单侧消失 + 低血压 + 气管偏移；此案例 = 双侧减弱 + 高血压</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) extrinsic tracheal compression — both cause post-thyroidectomy stridor — but the absence of hematoma on exam (no ecchymosis, intact incision) firmly excludes it.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是 (B) 气管外压性梗阻——两者均可引起甲状腺切除术后喘鸣——但体格检查无血肿表现（无瘀斑、切口完整）可将其明确排除。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Bilateral recurrent laryngeal nerve injury during total thyroidectomy causes immediate post-extubation stridor and hypercapnic respiratory failure from bilateral vocal cord adduction at the midline.**

**全甲状腺切除术中双侧喉返神经损伤，导致双侧声带内收固定于正中位，拔管后即刻出现喘鸣及高碳酸血症性呼吸衰竭。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "VOCAL CORDS CLOSE" After Total Thyroidectomy / 记忆钩 — 全甲状腺切除后「声带关闭」:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>ilateral RLN cut → cords stuck <strong>B</strong>oth in midline — no abduction possible / 双侧 RLN 切断 → 双侧声带固定正中——无法外展<br />
• <strong>I</strong>mmediate stridor on extubation = upper airway hallmark / 拔管即刻喘鸣 = 上气道梗阻标志<br />
• <strong>N</strong>o hematoma (intact wound) rules out compression / 无血肿（切口完整）排除外压性梗阻<br />
• <strong>D</strong>ual injury needed for obstruction; unilateral = hoarseness only / 需双侧损伤方致梗阻；单侧仅声嘶</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Recurrent Laryngeal Nerve Anatomy & Thyroid Surgery Complications / 高频知识表 — 喉返神经解剖及甲状腺手术并发症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>RLN anatomical course<br />
喉返神经解剖走行</td>
<td>Right RLN loops around right subclavian artery; left loops around aortic arch; both ascend in tracheoesophageal groove posterior to thyroid lobes<br />
右侧绕右锁骨下动脉，左侧绕主动脉弓；两侧均沿气管食管沟上行，位于甲状腺叶后方</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RLN motor function<br />
喉返神经运动功能</td>
<td>Innervates all intrinsic laryngeal muscles except cricothyroid; posterior cricoarytenoid is the sole vocal cord abductor<br />
支配除环甲肌外所有喉内肌；环杓后肌是声带唯一外展肌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Unilateral RLN injury<br />
单侧喉返神经损伤</td>
<td>Hoarseness; cord paralyzed in paramedian position; contralateral cord compensates; no airway emergency<br />
声音嘶哑；声带麻痹于旁正中位；对侧代偿；无气道急症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bilateral RLN injury<br />
双侧喉返神经损伤</td>
<td>Both cords adducted at midline; severe upper airway obstruction; stridor; requires immediate reintubation or tracheotomy<br />
双侧声带内收于正中位；严重上气道梗阻；喘鸣；须立即重新插管或气管切开</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-thyroidectomy hematoma<br />
甲状腺切除术后血肿</td>
<td>Presents hours post-op; wound swelling + ecchymosis; extrinsic tracheal compression; immediate bedside wound opening<br />
术后数小时出现；切口肿胀 + 瘀斑；气管外压性梗阻；立即床旁开放伤口</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypoparathyroidism post-thyroidectomy<br />
甲状腺切除术后甲状旁腺功能减退</td>
<td>Inadvertent parathyroid removal/devascularization; presents 24-72 h post-op with hypocalcemia → perioral tingling, Chvostek, Trousseau signs<br />
甲状旁腺意外切除或去血管化；术后 24-72 h 出现低钙血症 → 口周麻木、Chvostek 征、Trousseau 征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Superior laryngeal nerve injury<br />
喉上神经损伤</td>
<td>External branch: cricothyroid muscle; injury → loss of high-pitched phonation (less dramatic than RLN); internal branch: sensation above glottis<br />
外支支配环甲肌；损伤 → 丧失高音调发声（影响不如 RLN 严重）；内支负责声门上方感觉</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Intraoperative nerve monitoring (IONM):** Electromyographic endotracheal tube monitors RLN integrity in real time during thyroidectomy, reducing but not eliminating bilateral injury risk\
  **术中神经监测（IONM）:** 电肌图气管插管实时监测甲状腺切除术中喉返神经完整性，可降低但不能完全消除双侧损伤风险

- **ABG interpretation pearl:** High PO2 (200) + low pH + high PCO2 = type 2 (hypercapnic) respiratory failure; oxygenation maintained by O2 mask, but ventilation (CO2 removal) is impaired — classic obstructive pattern\
  **血气解读要点:** PO2 高（200）+ pH 低 + PCO2 高 = Ⅱ型（高碳酸血症性）呼吸衰竭；面罩吸氧维持氧合，但通气（CO2 清除）受损——经典梗阻性表现

- **Differential for post-thyroidectomy stridor:** RLN paralysis (immediate, intact wound) vs. hematoma (hours later, swollen wound) vs. laryngospasm (immediate, responds to Ca2+ if hypocalcemia) vs. tracheomalacia (rare, tracheal softening from chronic goiter compression)\
  **甲状腺切除术后喘鸣鉴别:** 喉返神经麻痹（即刻，切口完整）vs. 血肿（数小时，切口肿胀）vs. 喉痉挛（即刻，低钙时补钙有效）vs. 气管软化（罕见，慢性甲状腺肿压迫致气管软化）

- **Unilateral RLN injury management:** Voice therapy first; if persistent \> 6–12 months, medialization laryngoplasty or vocal cord injection to restore glottic closure for phonation\
  **单侧喉返神经损伤处理:** 首选嗓音训练；持续 \> 6–12 个月则行声带内移喉成形术或声带注射以恢复声门闭合改善发音

# Question 66 — Schizotypal Personality Disorder / 分裂型人格障碍

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>46-year-old man</strong> with hypertension comes to the physician for a routine examination. When the physician enters the room, the patient says <strong>the office staff were talking about him</strong> in the waiting room. The patient has declined antihypertensive therapy in the past; today, he declines it again, saying <strong>"it does not matter because the world is going to end soon."</strong> He does not drink alcohol or use illicit drugs. He <strong>lives alone and has minimal contact with his family.</strong> He says he has <strong>one friend</strong> and spends his free time playing video games. He works at home for an accounting firm. He appears fearful and older than his stated age. He wears <strong>an overcoat and woolen hat</strong> although the <strong>outside temperature is 80°F.</strong> His pulse is 80/min and regular, and blood pressure is 140/98 mm Hg. Limited physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, he has a euthymic mood and <strong>odd affect.</strong> He makes <strong>minimal eye contact</strong> with the physician and appears <strong>anxious when questioned.</strong> He says he has not had anxiety or changes in mood. Cognition is intact, and answers to questions are appropriate. His <strong>thought process is linear.</strong> He reports <strong>no hallucinations.</strong> Results of laboratory studies are within the reference ranges.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Autism spectrum disorder<br />
B) Delusional disorder<br />
C) Oppositional defiant disorder<br />
D) Schizophrenia<br />
E) Schizotypal personality disorder</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Schizotypal personality disorder** is a **Cluster A** ("odd and eccentric") personality disorder in DSM-5, representing a pervasive pattern of **social and interpersonal deficits** coupled with **cognitive/perceptual distortions** and **eccentric behavior** beginning by early adulthood:

**分裂型人格障碍**是DSM-5中**A群**（"奇怪且古怪"）人格障碍，代表从早期成年期开始的普遍**社交和人际缺陷**，伴有**认知/感知扭曲**和**古怪行为**：

- Patients experience **ideas of reference** and **magical thinking** (e.g., superstitions, belief in clairvoyance or telepathy), but the conviction behind these beliefs fluctuates — they are not the fixed, unshakeable quality of true delusions\
  患者经历**关系意念**和**魔法性思维**（如迷信、相信千里眼或心灵感应），但这些信念背后的确信程度可变——不具有真正妄想固定、不可动摇的特质

- **Social anxiety** in schizotypal PD is paranoid in nature and does **not diminish with familiarity** — unlike social anxiety disorder, where anxiety stems from fear of embarrassment and typically improves as the patient becomes comfortable\
  分裂型人格障碍中的**社交焦虑**本质上是偏执性的，**不随熟悉度降低**——不同于社交焦虑障碍，后者源于对尴尬的恐惧，通常随患者变得舒适而改善

- **Eccentric appearance** (inappropriate dress, unusual mannerisms) and **odd speech** (vague, over-elaborate, metaphorical) reflect persistent detachment from mainstream social norms throughout adulthood\
  **古怪外表**（不适当着装、不寻常举止）和**奇异言语**（模糊、过度精细、隐喻性）反映了成年期对主流社会规范的持续疏离

- Unlike schizophrenia, schizotypal PD produces **no frank psychosis** — no hallucinations, no disorganized speech, and no disorganized behavior meeting psychotic episode criteria\
  与精神分裂症不同，分裂型人格障碍不产生**明显精神病症状**——无幻觉、无言语混乱、无满足精神病发作标准的行为混乱

**Diagnostic rule of thumb:** Schizotypal PD = Schizophrenia "lite" — odd beliefs + eccentric appearance + social isolation, but NO fixed delusions, NO hallucinations, NO disorganized speech/behavior.

**诊断小窍门:** 分裂型人格障碍 = "轻版"精神分裂症——奇异信念+古怪外表+社交孤立，但无固定妄想、无幻觉、无言语/行为混乱。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Schizotypal Personality Disorder / 正确答案 (E) — 分裂型人格障碍

**Schizotypal personality disorder** is a Cluster A personality disorder defined by a pervasive, enduring pattern (present from early adulthood, across multiple contexts) of social/interpersonal deficits, cognitive or perceptual distortions, and eccentric behavior. DSM-5 requires ≥5 of 9 criteria:

**分裂型人格障碍**是A群人格障碍，由从早期成年期开始、存在于多种情境中的普遍、持久的社交/人际缺陷、认知或感知扭曲及古怪行为模式定义。DSM-5要求满足9条标准中的≥5条：

- Ideas of reference (not delusions of reference)\
  关系意念（不是关系妄想）

- Odd beliefs or magical thinking inconsistent with subcultural norms\
  与亚文化规范不一致的奇异信念或魔法性思维

- Unusual perceptual experiences including bodily illusions (not true hallucinations)\
  异常感知体验，包括躯体错觉（非真正幻觉）

- Odd thinking and speech (vague, circumstantial, metaphorical, or stereotyped)\
  奇异思维和言语（模糊、迂回、隐喻性或刻板化）

- Suspiciousness or paranoid ideation\
  多疑或偏执意念

- Inappropriate or constricted affect\
  不适当或受限情感

- Odd, eccentric, or peculiar behavior or appearance\
  奇异、古怪或特殊的行为或外表

- Lack of close friends or confidants other than first-degree relatives\
  除一级亲属外缺乏亲密朋友或知己

- Excessive social anxiety with paranoid fears that does not diminish with familiarity\
  伴有偏执恐惧、不随熟悉度降低的过度社交焦虑

**Diagnosis:** This patient meets at least 5 criteria: ideas of reference (office staff talking about him), magical thinking ("world is going to end"), suspiciousness/paranoid ideation, odd affect on exam, eccentric appearance (overcoat in 80°F weather), and lack of close relationships (one friend, minimal family contact).

**诊断:** 该患者满足至少5条标准：关系意念（工作人员在谈论他）、魔法性思维（"世界将终结"）、多疑/偏执意念、检查时奇异情感、古怪外表（80°F高温下穿大衣）以及缺乏亲密关系（只有一个朋友、与家人联系极少）。

**Treatment:** Psychotherapy (supportive therapy, CBT) is first-line; low-dose antipsychotics (e.g., risperidone) may target psychotic-like symptoms or severe social anxiety; SSRIs for comorbid depression or anxiety.

**治疗:** 心理治疗（支持性治疗、CBT）是一线治疗；低剂量抗精神病药（如利培酮）可针对类精神病症状或严重社交焦虑；SSRIs用于共病抑郁或焦虑。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Autism spectrum disorder<br />
A — 自闭症谱系障碍</td>
<td>Neurodevelopmental disorder that typically manifests by age 1–2; this 46-year-old has no stated childhood history; ASD features restricted/repetitive behaviors and communication deficits, not paranoid eccentric beliefs<br />
神经发育障碍，通常在1–2岁出现；该46岁患者无儿童期病史；ASD以局限重复行为和沟通缺陷为特征，而非偏执古怪信念</td>
<td>Age of onset (childhood vs. adulthood); ASD = communication/repetitive behavior deficits; Schizotypal = paranoid-eccentric beliefs with social anxiety<br />
发病年龄（儿童期vs成年期）；ASD=沟通/重复行为缺陷；分裂型=伴社交焦虑的偏执古怪信念</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Delusional disorder<br />
B — 妄想障碍</td>
<td>Features one or more fixed, non-bizarre delusions ≥1 month; critically lacks eccentric appearance, social indifference, and odd affect; patient's beliefs fluctuate in conviction and he displays multiple schizotypal features delusional disorder does not cause<br />
以一个或多个固定、非荒诞妄想（≥1个月）为特征；关键性地缺乏古怪外表、社交冷漠和奇异情感；患者信念的确信程度可变，且他表现出妄想障碍不会引起的多种分裂型特征</td>
<td>Fixed vs. variable conviction; eccentric appearance + social isolation present (schizotypal) vs. absent (delusional disorder); functioning preserved in delusional disorder<br />
固定vs可变的确信程度；有古怪外表+社交孤立（分裂型）vs无（妄想障碍）；妄想障碍中社会功能保留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Oppositional defiant disorder<br />
C — 对立违抗性障碍</td>
<td>A childhood-onset disorder (persistent angry mood, defiant behavior, vindictiveness causing impairment); entirely inapplicable to a 46-year-old adult<br />
儿童期发病障碍（持续愤怒情绪、对立行为、报复心导致损害）；完全不适用于46岁成年人</td>
<td>Age alone excludes this; patient's medication refusal stems from eccentric magical beliefs, not defiance<br />
年龄本身即可排除；患者拒绝服药源于古怪魔法性信念，而非对立行为</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Schizophrenia<br />
D — 精神分裂症</td>
<td>Requires ≥2 of: delusions, hallucinations, disorganized speech, disorganized behavior, or negative symptoms for ≥6 months; this patient has NO hallucinations, NO disorganized speech, and a linear thought process — he does not meet criteria<br />
需要≥6个月内出现≥2项：妄想、幻觉、言语混乱、行为混乱或阴性症状；该患者无幻觉、无言语混乱、思维线性——不满足标准</td>
<td>No hallucinations (patient explicitly denies); linear thought process; odd beliefs with variable conviction (not fixed delusions); personality disorder (lifelong) not psychotic episode<br />
无幻觉（患者明确否认）；思维线性；奇异信念确信程度可变（非固定妄想）；人格障碍（终身）而非精神病发作</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Schizotypal personality disorder ✓<br />
E — 分裂型人格障碍 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — patient meets ≥5 DSM-5 criteria: ideas of reference, magical thinking, suspiciousness, odd affect, eccentric appearance, social isolation; no frank psychosis<br />
正确——患者满足≥5条DSM-5标准：关系意念、魔法性思维、多疑、奇异情感、古怪外表、社交孤立；无明显精神病症状</td>
<td>Cluster A personality disorder with psychotic-like but not psychotic features; lifelong pattern not an acute episode<br />
A群人格障碍，具有类精神病但非精神病性特征；终身模式而非急性发作</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Delusional Disorder (B) — the "world ending" belief sounds like a delusion, but the key differentiator is that schizotypal beliefs fluctuate in conviction and are accompanied by eccentric appearance and social isolation, features that are conspicuously absent in delusional disorder.*

最容易误选的干扰项是妄想障碍（B）——"世界终结"的信念听起来像妄想，但关键鉴别在于分裂型的信念确信程度可变，且伴有古怪外表和社交孤立，这些特征在妄想障碍中显著缺失。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Schizotypal PD vs. Schizophrenia vs. Delusional Disorder / 分裂型人格障碍 vs. 精神分裂症 vs. 妄想障碍

社交孤立</td>

精神病性障碍；发作性或慢性；≥6个月</td>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Schizotypal personality disorder is a lifelong Cluster A pattern of odd beliefs, eccentric appearance, social isolation, and paranoid social anxiety — producing psychotic-like features without true hallucinations or fixed delusions.**

**分裂型人格障碍是终身A群模式，表现为奇异信念、古怪外表、社交孤立和带偏执色彩的社交焦虑——产生类精神病特征，但无真正幻觉或固定妄想。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — STOMPED (Schizotypal's 9 DSM Criteria) / 记忆钩 — STOMPED（分裂型9条DSM标准）:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>uspiciousness / paranoid ideation — 多疑/偏执意念 / 关系意念<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hinking odd (magical thinking, odd beliefs) — 奇异思维（魔法性思维、奇异信念）<br />
• <strong>O</strong>dd perceptual experiences (illusions, not hallucinations) — 奇异感知体验（错觉，非幻觉）<br />
• <strong>M</strong>inimal close friends (social isolation) — 亲密朋友极少（社交孤立）<br />
• <strong>P</strong>eculiar appearance and behavior (eccentric) — 古怪外表和行为（奇特）<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ccentric speech (vague, metaphorical, circumstantial) — 古怪言语（模糊、隐喻、迂回）<br />
• <strong>D</strong>oesn't have fixed delusions or true hallucinations — 无固定妄想或真正幻觉（区别于精神分裂症）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Cluster A Personality Disorders / 高频知识表 — A群人格障碍

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Three Cluster A disorders<br />
三种A群障碍</td>
<td>Paranoid PD (pervasive distrust/suspicion, no eccentricity), Schizoid PD (social detachment + flat affect, no paranoia, no eccentricity), Schizotypal PD (eccentricity + paranoid ideas + psychotic-like features)<br />
偏执型PD（普遍不信任/多疑，无古怪性）、分裂样PD（社交疏离+情感平淡，无偏执，无古怪性）、分裂型PD（古怪性+偏执意念+类精神病特征）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 criteria for schizotypal<br />
分裂型DSM-5标准</td>
<td>Must meet ≥5 of 9 criteria; lifelong pattern beginning by early adulthood; present across multiple contexts (not situational)<br />
必须满足9条中≥5条；从早期成年期开始的终身模式；存在于多种情境中（非情境性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Social anxiety distinguisher<br />
社交焦虑鉴别要点</td>
<td>Schizotypal PD: anxiety is paranoid-driven (fear of others' intentions/harm); does NOT improve with familiarity; Social anxiety disorder: anxiety is embarrassment-driven; DOES improve as patient becomes comfortable<br />
分裂型PD：焦虑由偏执驱动（对他人意图/伤害的恐惧）；不随熟悉度改善；社交焦虑障碍：焦虑由尴尬恐惧驱动；随患者变得舒适而改善</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ideas of reference vs. delusions of reference<br />
关系意念vs关系妄想</td>
<td>Ideas of reference: variable conviction, can be challenged — schizotypal PD; Delusions of reference: fixed, unshakeable, cannot be reasoned away — schizophrenia or delusional disorder<br />
关系意念：确信程度可变，可被质疑——分裂型PD；关系妄想：固定、不可动摇、无法被说服——精神分裂症或妄想障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Schizoid vs. Schizotypal (classic distinction)<br />
分裂样vs分裂型（经典鉴别）</td>
<td>Schizoid PD: flat/restricted affect, voluntarily detached from relationships, NO odd beliefs, NO magical thinking, NO paranoia, NO eccentric appearance; Schizotypal PD: adds odd beliefs, magical thinking, paranoia, eccentric appearance, and social anxiety<br />
分裂样PD：情感平淡/受限、主动与关系疏离、无奇异信念、无魔法性思维、无偏执、无古怪外表；分裂型PD：增加奇异信念、魔法性思维、偏执、古怪外表和社交焦虑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 classification nuance<br />
DSM-5分类细节</td>
<td>Schizotypal PD is listed BOTH under Personality Disorders (Chapter 17) AND under Schizophrenia Spectrum Disorders (Chapter 2) in DSM-5, reflecting its genetic and phenomenological link to schizophrenia<br />
分裂型人格障碍在DSM-5中同时列于人格障碍（第17章）和精神分裂症谱系障碍（第2章），反映其与精神分裂症的遗传和现象学关联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment approach<br />
治疗方法</td>
<td>Psychotherapy (supportive, CBT) first-line for social skills and reality testing; low-dose antipsychotics (risperidone, olanzapine) for psychotic-like or severe anxiety symptoms; SSRIs for comorbid depression<br />
心理治疗（支持性、CBT）为一线，用于社交技能和现实检验；低剂量抗精神病药（利培酮、奥氮平）用于类精神病或严重焦虑症状；SSRIs用于共病抑郁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk of conversion to schizophrenia<br />
转化为精神分裂症的风险</td>
<td>~10% lifetime risk of developing schizophrenia or another psychotic disorder; schizotypal PD is more common in first-degree relatives of patients with schizophrenia<br />
约10%的终身风险发展为精神分裂症或其他精神病性障碍；分裂型PD在精神分裂症患者的一级亲属中更常见</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Eccentric dress as USMLE trigger:** Wearing weather-inappropriate clothing (heavy coat in summer heat) is a classic schizotypal PD cue on NBME exams — always confirm by looking for co-occurring ideas of reference, magical thinking, and social isolation\
  **USMLE古怪着装触发线索:** 穿着与天气不符的衣物（夏日酷暑穿厚重外套）是NBME考题中分裂型人格障碍的经典提示——始终通过寻找共存的关系意念、魔法性思维和社交孤立来确认

- **Differential for "world is ending" belief:** Grandiose delusion (bipolar mania) — associated with elevated mood, decreased sleep, pressured speech; Nihilistic delusion (psychotic depression) — associated with depressed mood; Schizotypal magical thinking — euthymic mood, odd affect, no other psychotic features\
  **"世界终结"信念的鉴别:** 夸大妄想（双相躁狂）——与情绪高涨、睡眠减少、语速加快相关；虚无妄想（精神病性抑郁）——与抑郁情绪相关；分裂型魔法性思维——情绪正常、奇异情感、无其他精神病特征

- **Key complication:** Patients with schizotypal PD have elevated lifetime rates of major depressive episodes (~50%), schizophrenia conversion (~10%), and suicidal ideation — monitoring is essential\
  **主要并发症:** 分裂型人格障碍患者终身重性抑郁发作（约50%）、转化为精神分裂症（约10%）和自杀意念的发生率升高——监测至关重要

- **Variant — prodromal schizophrenia:** Schizotypal PD may represent the premorbid state before schizophrenia onset; patients who later develop schizophrenia may have had unrecognized schizotypal features for years prior to their first psychotic break\
  **题目变式——精神分裂症前驱期:** 分裂型人格障碍可能代表精神分裂症发病前的病前状态；后来发展为精神分裂症的患者可能在首次精神病发作前数年就有未被识别的分裂型特征

# Question 67 — Nonspecific Prepubertal Vulvovaginitis / 青春期前非特异性外阴阴道炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>4-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the office by her mother because of a <strong>1-week history of vaginal itching</strong>. The mother says her daughter is scratching her vaginal area frequently and the area appears irritated. The patient has not had <strong>fever, pain with urination, or urinary frequency</strong>. She has been <strong>toilet-trained for 1 year</strong>. The mother is not concerned about sexual abuse. When questioned alone, the patient says that no one has touched her inappropriately. Examination shows <strong>erythema of the vaginal area</strong>. There is <strong>no vaginal discharge, foul odor, bleeding, tears, or ecchymoses</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Begin antibiotic therapy<br />
B) Begin antifungal therapy<br />
C) Order evaluation by child protective services<br />
D) Recommend that the patient switch to cotton underwear and avoid bubble baths<br />
E) Schedule gynecologic examination</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>4-year-old prepubertal girl<br />
4岁青春期前女孩</td>
<td>Low estrogen → thin, atrophic, non-keratinized vaginal epithelium → heightened susceptibility to irritants<br />
雌激素水平低→阴道上皮薄、萎缩、角化程度低→对刺激物高度敏感</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1-week vaginal itching + erythema only<br />
1周外阴瘙痒+仅见红斑</td>
<td>Classic presentation of nonspecific irritant vulvovaginitis; localized to external genitalia without systemic signs<br />
非特异性刺激性外阴阴道炎的典型表现；局限于外阴，无全身症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, no dysuria, no urinary frequency<br />
无发热、无排尿疼痛、无尿频</td>
<td>Argues strongly against urinary tract infection; symptom pattern is localized vulvovaginal irritation<br />
强烈反对尿路感染诊断；症状模式为局限性外阴阴道刺激</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No discharge, no foul odor, no bleeding<br />
无阴道分泌物、无异味、无出血</td>
<td>Absence of these signs effectively excludes bacterial infection (Strep A, E. coli) and vaginal foreign body<br />
这些征象的缺失有效排除细菌感染（A族链球菌、大肠杆菌）及阴道异物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No signs of physical or sexual abuse; child denied abuse when questioned alone<br />
无身体或性虐待迹象；单独询问时患者否认</td>
<td>Abuse must always be evaluated in prepubertal vulvovaginitis; negative history and absent physical findings argue against CPS referral at this stage<br />
青春期前外阴阴道炎必须常规排查虐待；阴性病史及无体征不支持此阶段转介保护服务</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Toilet-trained for 1 year<br />
如厕训练已1年</td>
<td>Children recently toilet-trained often have suboptimal front-to-back wiping technique, facilitating fecal contamination of the vulva<br />
近期完成如厕训练的儿童常缺乏正确由前向后的擦拭习惯，易导致粪便污染外阴</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

In prepubertal girls, **low circulating estrogen** produces a **thin, atrophic, non-keratinized vaginal epithelium** and a **neutral-to-alkaline vaginal pH**, creating a mucosal surface highly vulnerable to chemical and mechanical insults:

青春期前女孩体内**雌激素水平低**，导致**阴道上皮薄、萎缩、角化程度低**，阴道**pH值接近中性至碱性**，形成对化学和机械刺激高度敏感的黏膜表面：

- Bubble baths and scented soaps contain surfactants and fragrances that strip protective lipids from the vulvar epithelium, triggering direct chemical inflammation\
  泡泡浴和香皂含有表面活性剂及香精，剥脱外阴上皮的保护性脂质，引发直接化学性炎症

- Synthetic (nylon/polyester) underwear traps moisture and heat, creating a warm, macerated microenvironment that perpetuates irritation\
  合成纤维（尼龙/聚酯）内裤闷热潮湿，形成温暖、浸渍的微环境，持续加重刺激

- The short anatomic distance between the vaginal introitus and the anus in prepubertal girls facilitates fecal bacterial contamination when wiping is performed incorrectly (back-to-front)\
  青春期前女孩阴道口与肛门解剖距离短，由后向前擦拭时易造成粪便细菌污染

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Prepubertal = low estrogen = thin epithelium = nonspecific irritant vulvovaginitis is the default diagnosis when discharge and odor are absent; their presence mandates culture.

**解剖小窍门:** 青春期前=雌激素低=上皮薄=无分泌物及异味时首先考虑非特异性刺激性外阴阴道炎；若出现上述症状则须行阴道培养。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Conservative Hygiene Measures / 正确答案 (D) — 保守卫生干预措施

**Nonspecific vulvovaginitis** is the diagnosis when there is no discharge, no odor, no bleeding, and no evidence of abuse — and the first-line management is removal of the offending irritants:

**非特异性外阴阴道炎**在无分泌物、无异味、无出血、无虐待证据时确诊——一线处理是去除致病刺激物：

- Switching to breathable cotton underwear eliminates the moisture-trapping, friction-inducing effect of synthetic fabrics\
  换用透气棉质内裤，消除合成纤维闷热潮湿和摩擦刺激的影响

- Avoiding bubble baths removes the primary chemical irritant; plain warm water sitz baths are soothing and acceptable\
  避免泡泡浴可去除主要化学刺激物；普通温水坐浴舒缓且可接受

- Additional guidance includes front-to-back wiping, avoiding prolonged wet bathing suits, and loose-fitting clothing\
  其他指导包括由前向后擦拭、避免长时间穿着湿泳衣及穿着宽松衣物

**Diagnosis:** Nonspecific vulvovaginitis is a clinical diagnosis of exclusion — no infection signs (discharge/odor), no foreign body, no abuse evidence.

**诊断:** 非特异性外阴阴道炎是排除性临床诊断——无感染征象（分泌物/异味）、无异物、无虐待证据。

**Treatment:** First-line is conservative hygiene measures; if recurrent or unresponsive after 2–4 weeks, obtain vaginal cultures and consider topical low-potency estrogen cream to thicken the atrophic epithelium.

**治疗:** 一线治疗为保守卫生措施；若2~4周后复发或无效，行阴道培养，考虑局部低效价雌激素软膏以增厚萎缩上皮。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Begin antibiotic therapy<br />
A — 开始抗生素治疗</td>
<td>No signs of bacterial infection: no purulent discharge, no foul odor, no fever — antibiotics are unwarranted before conservative measures<br />
无细菌感染征象：无脓性分泌物、无异味、无发热——在保守措施之前使用抗生素无依据</td>
<td>Bacterial vulvovaginitis (e.g., Group A Strep) features mucopurulent discharge and characteristic odor<br />
细菌性外阴阴道炎（如A族链球菌）表现为黏脓性分泌物和特征性异味</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Begin antifungal therapy<br />
B — 开始抗真菌治疗</td>
<td>Candidal vulvovaginitis is rare in prepubertal girls due to the low-estrogen environment; no cottage-cheese discharge or predisposing factors present<br />
念珠菌性外阴阴道炎在低雌激素的青春期前女孩中罕见；无典型豆腐渣样分泌物及易感因素</td>
<td>Candida requires estrogen-rich environment (post-menarche) or predisposing factors (antibiotic use, diabetes, immunosuppression)<br />
念珠菌需富雌激素环境（初潮后）或易感因素（抗生素使用、糖尿病、免疫抑制）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Order evaluation by child protective services<br />
C — 转介儿童保护服务</td>
<td>Sexual abuse must be considered but there is no clinical evidence: no physical trauma, no STI signs, no behavioral red flags, child denied abuse when questioned alone<br />
性虐待须纳入考虑，但无临床证据：无躯体创伤、无性传播感染征象、无行为危险信号、单独询问时患者否认</td>
<td>CPS referral requires actual clinical evidence (unexplained trauma, STI, ecchymoses, concerning disclosure) — not mere possibility<br />
转介保护服务需要实际临床证据（无法解释的创伤、性传播感染、瘀斑、令人担忧的陈述）——而非仅凭可能性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Recommend cotton underwear and avoid bubble baths ✓<br />
D — 建议棉质内裤并避免泡泡浴 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — removes the chemical and physical irritants (surfactants, synthetic fabrics) that caused the nonspecific vulvovaginitis<br />
正确——去除了导致非特异性外阴阴道炎的化学和物理刺激物（表面活性剂、合成纤维）</td>
<td>First-line management for nonspecific prepubertal vulvovaginitis before any further diagnostic workup<br />
青春期前非特异性外阴阴道炎在任何进一步检查之前的一线处理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Schedule gynecologic examination<br />
E — 安排妇科检查</td>
<td>Not necessary at this stage; diagnosis is clear from history and external inspection alone; invasive pelvic examination is distressing and unwarranted without diagnostic uncertainty<br />
此阶段无必要；仅凭病史和外部检查已可明确诊断；在诊断明确时对儿童行侵入性盆腔检查造成不必要痛苦</td>
<td>Gynecologic exam is reserved for recurrent/persistent vulvovaginitis not responding to conservative therapy, or when foreign body is suspected<br />
妇科检查仅用于保守治疗无效的复发/持续性外阴阴道炎，或怀疑阴道异物时</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Choice C (CPS referral) is the most tempting distractor because sexual abuse evaluation is part of the standard workup — the key distinction is that referral requires actual clinical evidence of abuse, not the possibility alone; this patient has a negative disclosure, no physical findings, and no red flags.*

选项C（转介保护服务）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，因为性虐待评估本属于标准诊疗流程——关键区别在于转介需要虐待的实际临床证据，而非仅凭可能性；本例患者否认受虐、无相关体征、无危险信号。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a prepubertal girl with vulvar itching and erythema but no discharge, odor, bleeding, or abuse evidence, the diagnosis is nonspecific vulvovaginitis and the first-line step is conservative hygiene measures — cotton underwear and no bubble baths.**

**青春期前女孩出现外阴瘙痒和红斑，但无分泌物、异味、出血或虐待证据时，诊断为非特异性外阴阴道炎，一线措施为保守卫生干预——棉质内裤并避免泡泡浴。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CHIPS Causes of Prepubertal Vulvovaginitis / 记忆钩 — "CHIPS"记忆青春期前外阴阴道炎病因:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>hemical irritants (bubble baths, scented soaps) — most common; first-line: remove the irritant / 化学刺激物（泡泡浴、香皂）——最常见；一线：去除刺激物<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ygiene (poor front-to-back wiping) — fecal contamination → irritation / 卫生习惯差（错误擦拭方向）——粪便污染→刺激<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfection (Group A Strep, E. coli, pinworms) — discharge + odor present → culture + antibiotics / 感染（A族链球菌、大肠杆菌、蛲虫）——有分泌物+异味→培养+抗生素<br />
• <strong>P</strong>hysical/sexual abuse (STI, genital trauma) — always exclude; refer to CPS only if red flags present / 身体/性虐待（性传播感染、生殖器创伤）——必须排查；仅有危险信号时转介保护服务<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ynthetic clothing (nylon, polyester) — traps moisture and heat → switch to cotton / 合成纤维衣物（尼龙、聚酯）——闷热潮湿→换棉质内裤</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Prepubertal Vulvovaginitis / 高频知识表 — 青春期前外阴阴道炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Why prepubertal girls are uniquely vulnerable<br />
为何青春期前女孩特别易感</td>
<td>Low estrogen → thin atrophic epithelium, neutral/alkaline vaginal pH, no Lactobacillus colonization, short vagina-to-anus distance, immature hygiene habits<br />
雌激素低→上皮薄而萎缩、阴道pH中性/碱性、无乳酸杆菌定植、阴道口至肛门距离短、卫生习惯未成熟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common cause overall<br />
最常见总体病因</td>
<td>Nonspecific (irritant/hygiene-related) — no pathogen identified; accounts for the majority of cases<br />
非特异性（刺激物/卫生相关）——无病原体；占大多数病例</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Infectious causes to know for boards<br />
考试必掌握的感染性病因</td>
<td>Group A Streptococcus (purulent discharge, perianal erythema); pinworms/Enterobius (nocturnal perianal itching, scotch-tape test); Candida is rare pre-puberty<br />
A族链球菌（脓性分泌物、肛周红斑）；蛲虫（夜间肛周瘙痒，透明胶带试验）；念珠菌在青春期前罕见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to suspect sexual abuse<br />
何时怀疑性虐待</td>
<td>STI in a prepubertal child (gonorrhea, chlamydia, trichomonas, syphilis); unexplained genital trauma, ecchymoses, or tears; behavioral changes; concerning or inconsistent disclosures<br />
青春期前儿童出现性传播感染（淋病、衣原体、滴虫、梅毒）；无法解释的生殖器创伤、瘀斑或裂伤；行为改变；令人担忧或前后矛盾的陈述</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Workup escalation pathway<br />
检查升级路径</td>
<td>Conservative measures first → if recurrent/persistent (&gt;2–4 weeks): vaginal culture → if foreign body suspected: examination under anesthesia<br />
首先保守措施→若复发/持续（&gt;2~4周）：阴道培养→若怀疑异物：麻醉下检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pinworm-associated vulvovaginitis pearl<br />
蛲虫相关外阴阴道炎要点</td>
<td>Enterobius vermicularis migrates from perianal area to vagina at night → nocturnal perianal and vulvar itching; diagnose with scotch-tape test applied perianally in the morning; treat with mebendazole or albendazole (single dose, repeat in 2 weeks)<br />
蛲虫夜间从肛周迁移至阴道→夜间肛周和外阴瘙痒；晨起肛周透明胶带试验确诊；甲苯达唑或阿苯达唑单剂治疗（2周后重复）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential for bloody vaginal discharge in prepubertal girls:** Foreign body (most common cause of bloody discharge in this age group), vaginal trauma, urethral prolapse, sarcoma botryoides (rare rhabdomyosarcoma — grape-like mass), precocious puberty, sexual abuse\
  **青春期前女孩血性阴道分泌物鉴别:** 异物（该年龄组血性分泌物最常见病因）、阴道创伤、尿道脱垂、葡萄状肉瘤（罕见横纹肌肉瘤——葡萄串样肿块）、性早熟、性虐待

- **When conservative measures fail:** If symptoms persist beyond 2–4 weeks despite hygiene optimization, obtain vaginal cultures; Group A Strep → amoxicillin; E. coli → trimethoprim-sulfamethoxazole; consider a short course of topical low-potency estrogen to thicken the atrophic epithelium\
  **保守措施无效时:** 卫生优化后症状仍持续超过2~4周，行阴道培养；A族链球菌→阿莫西林；大肠杆菌→甲氧苄啶-磺胺甲噁唑；考虑短期局部低效价雌激素增厚萎缩上皮

- **Sexual abuse interview protocol:** Always interview the child alone (as done correctly in this case) using open-ended, non-leading questions; document physical findings meticulously; do not perform invasive examination without a clear clinical indication — the examination itself can be traumatic\
  **性虐待面谈规范:** 始终单独面谈儿童（本题已正确执行），使用开放性、非诱导性问题；详细记录体格检查结果；无明确临床指征不行侵入性检查——检查本身可造成创伤

- **USMLE exam trap:** Do not jump to antibiotics for vulvar erythema without discharge or odor — the test rewards the step of conservative management first, then escalating only if signs of true infection are present; similarly, CPS requires evidence, not just the theoretical possibility of abuse\
  **USMLE考试陷阱:** 外阴红斑而无分泌物或异味时不可直接使用抗生素——考试考查先进行保守处理再升级的思路；同样，转介保护服务需要证据，而非虐待的理论可能性

# Question 68 — Age-Related Macular Degeneration (AMD) / 年龄相关性黄斑变性

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>87-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-day history of visual changes</strong> in his right eye. He notices that the <strong>lines of his daily crossword puzzle look curved</strong>, and the <strong>blinds in his apartment appear wavy</strong>. He wears magnifying lenses for reading. There is <strong>no pain</strong> in his eye, <strong>no photophobia</strong>, and no history of trauma to the area. He had <strong>cataract removal from the right eye 5 years ago</strong>. There is no history of serious illness. On examination, <strong>visual acuity is 20/200 in his right eye</strong> and 20/100 in his left eye. The right pupil is irregular, but it is reactive to light. The left pupil is round and reactive. This examination finding is unchanged since his cataract operation. Palpation of both globes through closed eyelids shows no abnormalities. His lenses appear clear. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Dilated funduscopic examination<br />
B) Slit-lamp examination<br />
C) Visual field testing<br />
D) CT scan of the head<br />
E) Temporal artery biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />

<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>87-year-old man<br />
87 岁男性</td>
<td>Age is the strongest risk factor for AMD; incidence rises sharply after age 65<br />
年龄是 AMD 最强的危险因素；65 岁后发病率急剧上升</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lines look curved / blinds appear wavy<br />
线条弯曲/百叶窗呈波浪形</td>
<td>Classic metamorphopsia — hallmark symptom of macular pathology, especially wet AMD<br />
典型视物变形——黄斑病变的标志性症状，尤其是湿性 AMD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No pain, no photophobia<br />
无疼痛，无畏光</td>
<td>Rules out angle-closure glaucoma, uveitis, and keratitis as causes<br />
排除闭角型青光眼、葡萄膜炎和角膜炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>

右侧瞳孔不规则自白内障手术后未改变</td>
<td>Post-surgical artifact, NOT new pathology; prevents misdiagnosis as CN III palsy or Horner syndrome<br />
手术后改变，非新发病理；防止误诊为动眼神经麻痹或 Horner 综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>

右眼视力 20/200</td>
<td>Significant central vision loss mandates urgent retinal evaluation<br />
显著中心视力丧失需要紧急视网膜评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>

晶体透明</td>
<td>Eliminates cataract as the cause of acute visual decline<br />
排除白内障作为急性视力下降的原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Magnifying lenses for reading<br />
阅读需用放大镜</td>
<td>Suggests pre-existing reduced central vision, consistent with chronic underlying AMD<br />
提示预先存在的中心视力减退，符合慢性潜在 AMD</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Age-Related Macular Degeneration (AMD)** is caused by progressive dysfunction of the **retinal pigment epithelium (RPE)** and photoreceptors in the **macula** — the central retinal zone responsible for high-acuity, color, and fine-detail vision:

**年龄相关性黄斑变性（AMD）**是由**视网膜色素上皮（RPE）**和**黄斑区**光感受器进行性功能障碍所致——黄斑是负责高分辨率、彩色和精细细节视力的视网膜中央区域：

- **Drusen** (yellow lipoproteinaceous deposits under RPE) accumulate, impairing metabolic exchange between RPE and choriocapillaris\
  **玻璃膜疣**（RPE 下方黄色脂蛋白沉积物）积聚，损害 RPE 与脉络膜毛细血管层之间的代谢交换

- In **dry AMD**: progressive RPE and photoreceptor atrophy → geographic atrophy → slow, insidious central vision loss over years\
  在**干性 AMD** 中：进行性 RPE 和光感受器萎缩→地图样萎缩→数年内缓慢隐匿的中心视力丧失

- In **wet AMD**: **choroidal neovascularization (CNV)** breaks through Bruch's membrane → subretinal fluid, hemorrhage, acute metamorphopsia, and rapid vision loss\
  在**湿性 AMD** 中：**脉络膜新生血管（CNV）**穿破 Bruch 膜→视网膜下液体、出血、急性视物变形和迅速视力丧失

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The macula (5 mm diameter) houses the fovea centralis, responsible for the central 20° of vision; damage here causes a central scotoma, not peripheral field loss.

**解剖小窍门:** 黄斑区（直径 5 mm）含有中央凹，负责中央 20° 的视力；此处损伤导致中心暗点，而非周边视野丧失。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Dilated Funduscopic Examination / 正确答案 (A) — 扩瞳眼底镜检查

**Dilated funduscopic examination** is the gold-standard method for directly visualizing the retina, macula, and optic disc, and is the established diagnostic modality for AMD:

**扩瞳眼底镜检查**是直接观察视网膜、黄斑和视神经盘的金标准方法，是 AMD 公认的诊断手段：

- Mydriatic drops (e.g., tropicamide) dilate the pupil, allowing a full 360° retinal view impossible through an undilated pupil\
  散瞳药（如托品酰胺）扩大瞳孔，实现未散瞳时无法完成的全视网膜 360° 观察

- Directly visualizes drusen, RPE atrophy, geographic atrophy, subretinal hemorrhage, or exudate confirming AMD type\
  直接观察玻璃膜疣、RPE 萎缩、地图样萎缩、视网膜下出血或渗出，确认 AMD 类型

- This patient's metamorphopsia + acute VA drop + advanced age + clear lens together mandate retinal examination as the first step\
  该患者的视物变形+急性视力下降+高龄+透明晶体共同要求将视网膜检查作为第一步

**Diagnosis:** AMD confirmed by drusen ≥125 μm (intermediate/advanced AMD), geographic atrophy, or CNV-associated findings (wet AMD); optical coherence tomography (OCT) is the modern adjunct for detailed cross-sectional retinal imaging.

**诊断:** AMD 通过玻璃膜疣 ≥125 μm（中/进展期 AMD）、地图样萎缩或 CNV 相关改变（湿性 AMD）确认；光学相干断层扫描（OCT）是现代辅助手段，用于详细的视网膜横断面成像。

**Treatment:** Dry AMD: AREDS2 supplements (vitamins C, E + zinc + copper + lutein + zeaxanthin) reduce progression by ~25%. Wet AMD: intravitreal anti-VEGF injections (ranibizumab, bevacizumab, aflibercept) are first-line.

**治疗:** 干性 AMD：AREDS2 补充剂（维生素 C、E+锌+铜+叶黄素+玉米黄质）可将进展风险降低约 25%。湿性 AMD：玻璃体腔内抗 VEGF 注射（雷珠单抗、贝伐单抗、阿柏西普）为一线治疗。

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Dilated funduscopic examination ✓<br />
A — 扩瞳眼底镜检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — gold-standard test for visualizing the retina and diagnosing AMD<br />
正确——观察视网膜、诊断 AMD 的金标准检查</td>
<td>Metamorphopsia + age + acute VA loss + clear lens → macular pathology → direct retinal exam needed<br />
视物变形+高龄+急性视力丧失+透明晶体→黄斑病变→需要直接视网膜检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Slit-lamp examination<br />
B — 裂隙灯检查</td>
<td>Evaluates anterior segment (cornea, iris, lens); lenses already documented as clear; not the primary tool for macular diagnosis<br />
评估眼前段（角膜、虹膜、晶状体）；晶状体已记录为透明；非黄斑诊断的主要工具</td>
<td>Anterior segment is unremarkable here; posterior retinal segment requires fundoscopy<br />
此处眼前段无异常；需要眼底镜检查眼后段视网膜</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Visual field testing<br />
C — 视野检查</td>
<td>Best for glaucoma and optic nerve disorders (arcuate/peripheral scotomas); AMD causes central scotoma not captured well on standard perimetry<br />
最适用于青光眼和视神经疾病（弓形/周边暗点）；AMD 导致中心暗点，标准视野检查不能很好地捕捉</td>
<td>AMD → central vision loss (Amsler grid more appropriate); glaucoma → peripheral/arcuate field defects<br />
AMD→中心视力丧失（Amsler 方格更合适）；青光眼→周边/弓形视野缺损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — CT scan of the head<br />
D — 头部 CT 扫描</td>
<td>For orbital masses or fractures; irregular pupil is explicitly stated as unchanged since cataract surgery — not new pathology; no proptosis, diplopia, or ptosis present<br />
用于眶内肿块或骨折；不规则瞳孔明确说明自白内障手术后未改变——非新发病理；无眼球突出、复视或上睑下垂</td>
<td>"Unchanged since cataract surgery" eliminates acute orbital/intracranial pathology; CT has no role in AMD diagnosis<br />
"白内障手术以来未改变"排除急性眶内/颅内病理；CT 在 AMD 诊断中无作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Temporal artery biopsy<br />
E — 颞动脉活检</td>
<td>For giant cell arteritis (GCA); requires headache, scalp tenderness, jaw claudication, ESR &gt;50, constitutional symptoms — none present in this patient<br />
用于巨细胞动脉炎（GCA）；需要头痛、头皮触痛、颌痛、ESR &gt;50、全身症状——该患者均无</td>
<td>Metamorphopsia is not a GCA feature; GCA causes sudden, complete, painless monocular vision loss without distortion<br />
视物变形不是 GCA 特征；GCA 导致突发、完全、无痛的单眼视力丧失，无变形</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (E) temporal artery biopsy — this elderly patient with acute vision loss could raise suspicion for GCA, but the characteristic absence of headache, jaw claudication, and constitutional symptoms, combined with metamorphopsia (a specifically macular symptom), firmly directs toward AMD.*

颞动脉活检（E）是最具迷惑性的干扰选项——这位老年患者急性视力丧失可能引发 GCA 考虑，但特征性缺乏头痛、颌痛和全身症状，加上视物变形（特异性黄斑症状），明确指向 AMD。

地图样萎缩（进展较慢）</td>
<td>Responsible for ~90% of severe AMD-related vision loss<br />
导致约 90% 的严重 AMD 相关视力丧失</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An elderly patient with acute metamorphopsia (wavy/curved lines), significant central vision loss, and no pain or systemic symptoms should undergo dilated funduscopic examination to diagnose age-related macular degeneration.**

**老年患者出现急性视物变形（波浪/弯曲线条）、显著中心视力丧失且无疼痛或全身症状，应行扩瞳眼底镜检查以诊断年龄相关性黄斑变性。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — AMD "WAVES" / 记忆钩 — AMD「波浪」口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>W</strong>avy lines = metamorphopsia — hallmark presenting symptom of wet AMD / 波浪线=视物变形——湿性 AMD 的标志性症状<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ge &gt;65 — strongest non-modifiable risk factor / 年龄 &gt;65 岁——最强的不可干预危险因素<br />
• <strong>V</strong>EGF inhibitors (anti-VEGF) — intravitreal treatment for wet AMD / VEGF 抑制剂（抗 VEGF）——湿性 AMD 的玻璃体腔治疗<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xamine with dilated fundus — the diagnostic gold standard / 扩瞳眼底检查——诊断金标准<br />
• <strong>S</strong>moking — the major modifiable risk factor to counsel against / 吸烟——需要劝告戒除的主要可干预危险因素</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Age-Related Macular Degeneration / 高频知识表 — 年龄相关性黄斑变性

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Age (strongest), smoking (2–4× risk), family history, light iris color, hypertension, cardiovascular disease, obesity<br />
年龄（最强）、吸烟（风险增加 2–4 倍）、家族史、浅色虹膜、高血压、心血管病、肥胖</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Drusen classification<br />
玻璃膜疣分级</td>
<td>Small (&lt;63 μm) = normal aging; Medium (63–124 μm) = intermediate AMD; Large (≥125 μm) = advanced AMD risk<br />
小（&lt;63 μm）=正常老化；中（63–124 μm）=中期 AMD；大（≥125 μm）=进展期 AMD 风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Amsler grid test<br />
Amsler 方格表检查</td>
<td>Patient covers one eye and views central dot on grid; wavy/distorted lines = positive metamorphopsia; used for home monitoring<br />
患者遮一眼注视方格表中心点；波浪/扭曲线条=阳性视物变形；用于家庭监测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AREDS2 supplement formula<br />
AREDS2 补充剂配方</td>
<td>Vitamins C + E + zinc + copper + lutein + zeaxanthin; reduces AMD progression risk ~25% in intermediate/advanced dry AMD<br />
维生素 C+E+锌+铜+叶黄素+玉米黄质；将中/进展期干性 AMD 进展风险降低约 25%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anti-VEGF mechanism<br />
抗 VEGF 机制</td>
<td>Ranibizumab / bevacizumab / aflibercept block VEGF-A → halt CNV growth and reduce subretinal leakage in wet AMD<br />
雷珠单抗/贝伐单抗/阿柏西普阻断 VEGF-A→抑制 CNV 生长并减少湿性 AMD 视网膜下渗漏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Differentiating from GCA<br />
与 GCA 鉴别</td>
<td>GCA: sudden complete painless monocular vision loss + headache + jaw claudication + ESR &gt;50 + CRP↑; start steroids immediately before biopsy<br />
GCA：突发完全无痛性单眼视力丧失+头痛+颌痛+ESR &gt;50+CRP↑；活检前立即开始激素治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Genetics<br />
遗传学</td>
<td>CFH (complement factor H) and ARMS2/HTRA1 gene variants most strongly associated with AMD; complement dysregulation is central to pathogenesis<br />
CFH（补体因子 H）和 ARMS2/HTRA1 基因变异与 AMD 关联最强；补体失调是发病机制的核心</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of acute painless vision loss:** Central retinal artery occlusion (sudden severe loss, cherry-red spot, relative afferent pupillary defect), central retinal vein occlusion (flame hemorrhages in all quadrants), vitreous hemorrhage, retinal detachment — all require urgent dilated funduscopic exam\
  **急性无痛性视力丧失鉴别:** 视网膜中央动脉阻塞（突发严重丧失、樱桃红斑、相对性传入性瞳孔障碍）、视网膜中央静脉阻塞（全象限火焰状出血）、玻璃体积血、视网膜脱离——均需紧急扩瞳眼底镜检查

- **Exam trap — post-surgical irregular pupil:** Cataract surgery commonly distorts the pupil; the explicit clue "unchanged since surgery" is the examiner's signal to rule out new CN III palsy, Adie's tonic pupil, or Horner syndrome, and to focus on the visual complaint instead\
  **考试陷阱——术后不规则瞳孔:** 白内障手术常使瞳孔变形；"手术以来未改变"这一明确线索是出题者排除新发动眼神经麻痹、Adie 强直瞳孔或 Horner 综合征的信号，应将注意力集中于视觉主诉

- **GCA urgency rule:** If temporal arteritis is clinically suspected, initiate high-dose prednisone (1 mg/kg/day, up to 60 mg) immediately — delay pending biopsy risks irreversible bilateral blindness; biopsy remains valid up to 2 weeks after steroid initiation\
  **GCA 紧迫性规则:** 若临床怀疑颞动脉炎，立即开始大剂量泼尼松（1 mg/kg/天，最高 60 mg）——等待活检会有永久性双侧失明的风险；激素开始后 2 周内活检仍有效

- **OCT as modern adjunct:** Optical coherence tomography (OCT) provides high-resolution cross-sectional retinal imaging and has become the standard for quantifying drusen burden, geographic atrophy extent, and subretinal fluid in CNV; often performed alongside or after fundoscopy\
  **OCT 作为现代辅助手段:** 光学相干断层扫描（OCT）提供高分辨率视网膜横断面成像，已成为量化玻璃膜疣负担、地图样萎缩范围和 CNV 视网膜下液体的标准；通常在眼底镜检查期间或之后进行

# Question 69 — Solitary Thyroid Nodule: Fine-Needle Aspiration Biopsy Indication / 孤立性甲状腺结节：细针穿刺活检指征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>27-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office for a health maintenance examination. She says she feels well. She has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. Vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows <strong>no lymphadenopathy</strong>. A <strong>2-cm nodule</strong> is palpated in the <strong>left lobe of the thyroid gland</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Results of laboratory studies, including measurement of <strong>serum thyroid-stimulating hormone concentration, are within the reference ranges</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) 131I scintigraphy<br />
B) Levothyroxine therapy and reexamination in 6 weeks<br />
C) Reexamination of the thyroid gland in 6 months<br />
D) Repeat measurement of serum thyroid-stimulating hormone concentration in 6 weeks<br />
E) Ultrasonography-guided fine-needle aspiration biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>27-year-old woman<br />
27 岁女性</td>
<td>Young age is a risk factor for thyroid malignancy; prevalence of benign nodules increases with age, so younger patients carry higher relative cancer risk<br />
年龄年轻是甲状腺恶性肿瘤的风险因素；良性结节随年龄增长更为常见，因此年轻患者的相对恶性风险更高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2-cm palpable thyroid nodule<br />
2 cm 可触及甲状腺结节</td>
<td>Palpable nodule ≥1 cm warrants workup to exclude malignancy regardless of symptoms<br />
可触及且 ≥1 cm 的结节无论有无症状均需评估以排除恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TSH within reference range<br />
TSH 在正常范围内</td>
<td>Normal TSH excludes primary hyperthyroidism; hyperfunctioning (hot) nodules — which rarely require FNA — present with low TSH; normal TSH directs workup to FNA<br />
TSH 正常排除原发性甲亢；功能亢进（热）结节——极少需要 FNA——表现为 TSH 偏低；TSH 正常则指向 FNA 评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No lymphadenopathy<br />
无淋巴结肿大</td>
<td>Absence of cervical lymphadenopathy does not exclude early thyroid malignancy, particularly papillary carcinoma which spreads lymphatically<br />
颈部淋巴结无肿大不能排除早期甲状腺恶性肿瘤，尤其是经淋巴道转移的乳头状癌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No medications or serious illness<br />
无用药史或严重疾病史</td>
<td>Establishes a clean baseline; no prior thyroid treatment or competing diagnoses that might alter the workup<br />
确立干净基线；无既往甲状腺治疗或可能影响评估的其他诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Health maintenance examination context<br />
健康体检中偶然发现</td>
<td>Incidentally discovered nodule; emphasizes that even asymptomatic patients need systematic cytologic workup<br />
偶然发现的结节；强调即使无症状患者也需系统性细胞学评估</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The evaluation of a newly discovered thyroid nodule is driven by the need to **exclude malignancy**, with the **serum TSH** serving as the critical branch point that directs the entire workup:

甲状腺结节的评估核心在于**排除恶性肿瘤**，**血清 TSH** 是决定整个评估流程走向的关键分支点：

- **Low TSH** → nodule is likely hyperfunctioning (hot) → 131I scintigraphy to confirm; hot nodules are rarely malignant and do not require FNA\
  **TSH 偏低** → 结节很可能是功能亢进（热结节）→ 放射性碘核素扫描证实；热结节极少恶变，不需要 FNA

- **Normal or elevated TSH** → nodule is not autonomously functioning (cold or indeterminate) → thyroid ultrasound + FNA biopsy to assess malignancy risk\
  **TSH 正常或升高** → 结节无自主功能（冷结节或不确定）→ 甲状腺超声 + FNA 活检评估恶性风险

- **Ultrasound-guided FNA** provides cytologic material classified by the Bethesda System (I–VI), which directly guides the decision between surveillance, repeat biopsy, molecular testing, or surgery\
  **超声引导 FNA** 提供按 Bethesda 系统（I–VI 类）分类的细胞学标本，直接指导随访、重复活检、分子检测或手术的决策

**Key principle:** TSH is normal in this patient → scintigraphy is NOT appropriate → proceed directly to ultrasound + FNA biopsy.

**关键原则:** 本患者 TSH 正常 → 核素扫描不适用 → 直接进行超声 + FNA 活检。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Ultrasonography-Guided Fine-Needle Aspiration Biopsy / 正确答案 (E) — 超声引导细针穿刺活检

**Ultrasonography-guided FNA biopsy** is the standard of care for thyroid nodules with normal or elevated TSH, particularly when risk factors for malignancy (young age, radiation history, family history) are present:

**超声引导细针穿刺活检**是 TSH 正常或升高的甲状腺结节的标准处理方案，尤其当存在恶性风险因素（年龄年轻、放射线暴露史、家族史）时：

- FNA is indicated for nodules ≥1 cm with normal/elevated TSH, for nodules of any size with concerning ultrasound features (microcalcifications, irregular margins, hypoechogenicity, taller-than-wide shape), or when risk factors exist\
  FNA 适用于 TSH 正常/升高且 ≥1 cm 的结节、任何大小但超声有可疑特征（微钙化、边缘不规则、低回声、纵横比 \>1）的结节、或存在风险因素时

- Ultrasound guidance improves sampling accuracy over palpation alone, reducing the rate of non-diagnostic (Bethesda I) specimens\
  超声引导比单纯触诊取样准确性更高，降低无法诊断（Bethesda I 类）标本的比例

- Bethesda classification guides next steps: II (benign, ~5% malignancy) → surveillance; III/IV (indeterminate, 10–40%) → molecular testing or repeat FNA; V/VI (suspicious/malignant, 60–99%) → surgery\
  Bethesda 分类指导后续步骤：II 类（良性，~5% 恶性）→ 随访；III/IV 类（不确定，10–40%）→ 分子检测或重复 FNA；V/VI 类（可疑/恶性，60–99%）→ 手术

**Diagnosis:** This 27-year-old woman with a 2-cm thyroid nodule and normal TSH meets standard criteria for FNA — the priority is cytologic characterization to rule out papillary thyroid carcinoma, the most common thyroid malignancy in young women.

**诊断:** 这位 27 岁女性有 2 cm 甲状腺结节且 TSH 正常，符合 FNA 活检的标准适应症——重点是通过细胞学检查排除乳头状甲状腺癌，这是年轻女性中最常见的甲状腺恶性肿瘤。

**Treatment:** Depends on FNA results — benign (Bethesda II): surveillance ultrasound at 6–18 months; indeterminate (III/IV): molecular testing (ThyroSeq, Afirma) or diagnostic lobectomy; suspicious/malignant (V/VI): hemithyroidectomy or total thyroidectomy.

**治疗:** 取决于 FNA 结果——良性（Bethesda II 类）：6–18 个月超声随访；不确定（III/IV 类）：分子检测（ThyroSeq、Afirma）或诊断性腺叶切除；可疑/恶性（V/VI 类）：甲状腺半切或全切。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — 131I scintigraphy<br />
A — 放射性碘核素扫描</td>
<td>Wrong — scintigraphy is indicated only when TSH is low (suggesting an autonomously functioning hot nodule); this patient has a normal TSH<br />
错误——核素扫描仅适用于 TSH 偏低时（提示自主功能性热结节）；本患者 TSH 正常</td>
<td>Low TSH → scintigraphy; Normal TSH → ultrasound + FNA. Never use scintigraphy as the first step when TSH is normal<br />
TSH 偏低 → 核素扫描；TSH 正常 → 超声 + FNA。TSH 正常时绝不应将核素扫描作为第一步</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Levothyroxine therapy and reexamination in 6 weeks<br />
B — 左甲状腺素治疗并 6 周后复查</td>
<td>Wrong — TSH suppression therapy with levothyroxine is no longer recommended for thyroid nodules; it does not address the risk of malignancy and carries cardiac and bone risks<br />
错误——用左甲状腺素抑制 TSH 的治疗方案不再推荐用于甲状腺结节；不能解决恶性风险，且有心脏和骨骼副作用</td>
<td>This was an old management strategy now abandoned; cytologic diagnosis always takes priority<br />
此为已废弃的旧方案；细胞学诊断始终是优先事项</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Reexamination of the thyroid gland in 6 months<br />
C — 6 个月后复查甲状腺</td>
<td>Wrong — watchful waiting without cytologic evaluation is inappropriate for a new 2-cm nodule in a young patient where malignancy must be excluded promptly<br />
错误——对于需要尽快排除恶性肿瘤的年轻患者新发 2 cm 结节，在无细胞学评估的情况下单纯观察等待是不适当的</td>
<td>Surveillance is appropriate only after a benign FNA result, not as the initial step<br />
随访仅适用于 FNA 结果已证实为良性之后，而非初始步骤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Repeat measurement of serum TSH in 6 weeks<br />
D — 6 周后复测血清 TSH</td>
<td>Wrong — TSH is already within normal limits; repeating it adds no diagnostic information and unnecessarily delays cytologic workup<br />
错误——TSH 已在正常范围内；重复检测无额外诊断价值，且不必要地延误了细胞学评估</td>
<td>Repeat TSH is only useful if the initial result was borderline or clinical status has changed; normal TSH is already actionable<br />
仅当初始结果处于临界值或临床状态改变时才需复测 TSH；正常 TSH 已足以指导下一步行动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Ultrasonography-guided fine-needle aspiration biopsy ✓<br />
E — 超声引导细针穿刺活检 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — normal TSH + 2-cm nodule in a 27-year-old woman → proceed directly to FNA for cytologic diagnosis and malignancy exclusion<br />
正确——TSH 正常 + 27 岁女性 2 cm 结节 → 直接进行 FNA 细胞学诊断，排除恶性肿瘤</td>
<td>Standard of care: normal TSH → ultrasound + FNA; FNA is both diagnostic and guides definitive management<br />
标准方案：TSH 正常 → 超声 + FNA；FNA 既有诊断价值又指导最终处理</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice A (131I scintigraphy) — examinees who confuse the workup algorithm may select scintigraphy automatically for any thyroid nodule, but it is only appropriate when TSH is suppressed, not normal.*

最危险的干扰项是 A 选项（放射性碘核素扫描）——混淆评估流程的考生可能对任何甲状腺结节自动选择核素扫描，但该检查仅适用于 TSH 被抑制而非正常的情况。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Cold vs. Hot Thyroid Nodule: Workup Algorithm / 冷结节 vs. 热结节：甲状腺结节评估流程对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />

<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Cold/Indeterminate Nodule (Normal or High TSH)</strong><br />

<th><strong>Hot Nodule (Low/Suppressed TSH)</strong><br />
<strong>热结节（TSH 偏低/被抑制）</strong></th>
</tr>

<tr>
<td>TSH level<br />
TSH 水平</td>
<td>Normal or elevated<br />
正常或升高</td>

偏低（被自主功能抑制）</td>

恶性风险</td>
<td>Higher — requires cytologic evaluation<br />

极低——功能亢进结节极少恶变</td>

下一步诊断措施</td>

是否需要 FNA？</td>
<td>Yes — cytology guides surveillance vs. surgery<br />
是——细胞学指导随访或手术决策</td>
<td>No — hot nodules are not biopsied<br />
否——热结节不需要活检</td>

胶质结节、滤泡腺瘤、乳头状癌</td>

毒性腺瘤、毒性多结节性甲状腺肿</td>

<td>Definitive treatment if benign<br />
确认良性后的处理</td>
<td>Surveillance ultrasound at 6–18 months<br />
6–18 个月超声随访</td>
<td>Radioactive iodine ablation or surgical resection<br />
放射性碘消融或手术切除</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For any thyroid nodule, check TSH first: normal TSH → ultrasound + FNA biopsy; low TSH → 131I scintigraphy — never skip to scintigraphy when TSH is normal.**

**对于任何甲状腺结节，先查 TSH：TSH 正常 → 超声 + FNA 活检；TSH 偏低 → 放射性碘核素扫描——TSH 正常时绝不可直接跳到核素扫描。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — TSH as the Traffic Light for Thyroid Nodule Workup / 记忆钩 — TSH 是甲状腺结节评估的"交通灯":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>G</strong>reen light (Normal TSH) — <strong>G</strong>o straight to ultrasound + FNA / <strong>绿灯</strong>（TSH 正常）——直接进行超声 + FNA<br />
• <strong>R</strong>ed light (Low TSH) — <strong>R</strong>adioactive iodine scan first (hot nodule suspected) / <strong>红灯</strong>（TSH 偏低）——先做放射性碘扫描（疑热结节）<br />
• <strong>Y</strong>oung patient — <strong>Y</strong>ield for cancer is higher → lower threshold for biopsy / <strong>年轻患者</strong>——癌症检出率更高 → 降低活检门槛<br />
• <strong>F</strong>NA result → <strong>F</strong>ollow Bethesda: II = follow, V/VI = operate / <strong>FNA 结果</strong> → <strong>遵循 Bethesda</strong>：II 类随访，V/VI 类手术</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Thyroid Nodule Evaluation / 高频知识表 — 甲状腺结节评估

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Universal first steps for any thyroid nodule<br />
任何甲状腺结节的通用初始步骤</td>
<td>TSH measurement + thyroid ultrasonography; TSH result determines whether to proceed with FNA or scintigraphy<br />
TSH 检测 + 甲状腺超声；TSH 结果决定后续是进行 FNA 还是核素扫描</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>FNA indications (normal/elevated TSH)<br />
FNA 适应症（TSH 正常/升高时）</td>
<td>Nodule ≥1 cm; any nodule with suspicious ultrasound features (microcalcifications, hypoechoic, irregular margins, taller-than-wide, extrathyroidal extension); risk factors present (young age, radiation exposure, family history of thyroid cancer/MEN2)<br />
结节 ≥1 cm；任何有超声可疑特征的结节（微钙化、低回声、边缘不规则、纵横比 &gt;1、腺外浸润）；存在风险因素（年轻、放射线暴露、甲状腺癌/MEN2 家族史）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bethesda System for FNA cytology<br />
FNA 细胞学的 Bethesda 分类系统</td>
<td>I: Non-diagnostic (repeat FNA); II: Benign (~5% malignancy, surveillance); III: AUS/FLUS (10–30%); IV: Follicular neoplasm (25–40%); V: Suspicious for malignancy (60–75%); VI: Malignant (97–99%, → surgery)<br />
I 类：无法诊断（重复 FNA）；II 类：良性（~5% 恶性，随访）；III 类：意义不明（10–30%）；IV 类：滤泡性肿瘤（25–40%）；V 类：可疑恶性（60–75%）；VI 类：恶性（97–99%，→ 手术）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common thyroid malignancy<br />
最常见的甲状腺恶性肿瘤</td>
<td>Papillary thyroid carcinoma (80%): young women, psammoma bodies, "Orphan Annie eye" nuclei, nuclear grooves; spreads to cervical lymph nodes; excellent prognosis; treatment: hemithyroidectomy or total thyroidectomy ± RAI<br />
乳头状甲状腺癌（80%）：年轻女性，砂砾体，"孤儿安妮眼"核，核沟；颈部淋巴结转移；预后极佳；治疗：甲状腺半切或全切 ± 放射性碘</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors for thyroid malignancy<br />
甲状腺恶性肿瘤的风险因素</td>
<td>Young age, male sex, childhood radiation to head/neck, family history of thyroid cancer, MEN2A/2B (medullary carcinoma), FAP/Gardner syndrome (papillary carcinoma); clinical red flags: rapid nodule growth, hoarseness (RLN invasion), fixation, lymphadenopathy<br />
年龄年轻、男性、儿童期头颈部放射线暴露、甲状腺癌家族史、MEN2A/2B（髓样癌）、FAP/Gardner 综合征（乳头状癌）；临床红旗征：结节快速增大、声嘶（喉返神经受侵）、固定、淋巴结肿大</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When scintigraphy IS appropriate<br />
核素扫描适用情形</td>
<td>Only when serum TSH is low — confirms hyperfunctioning (hot) nodule; hot nodule uptake pattern → treat with RAI or surgery for hyperthyroidism; warm/cold pattern on scan → still requires FNA if no prior biopsy<br />
仅当血清 TSH 偏低时——证实功能亢进（热）结节；热结节摄取模式 → 用放射性碘或手术治疗甲亢；扫描显示温/冷结节 → 若无既往活检仍需 FNA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surveillance after benign FNA<br />
良性 FNA 后的随访方案</td>
<td>Repeat ultrasound at 6–18 months; FNA should be repeated if nodule grows &gt;20% in two dimensions or develops new suspicious features; stable nodule may extend surveillance intervals<br />
6–18 个月后复查超声；若结节两径增大 &gt;20% 或出现新的可疑特征则重复 FNA；稳定结节可延长随访间隔</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of solitary thyroid nodule:** Colloid nodule (most common, benign), follicular adenoma, Hashimoto thyroiditis (may present as dominant nodule), simple thyroid cyst, papillary carcinoma, follicular carcinoma, medullary carcinoma (check calcitonin; associated with MEN2), anaplastic carcinoma (elderly, rapidly growing, poor prognosis)\
  **孤立性甲状腺结节的鉴别诊断:** 胶质结节（最常见，良性）、滤泡腺瘤、桥本甲状腺炎（可表现为优势结节）、单纯甲状腺囊肿、乳头状癌、滤泡癌、髓样癌（检测降钙素；与 MEN2 相关）、未分化癌（老年人，快速增大，预后极差）

- **Variant — incidentally found nodule on cross-sectional imaging:** Same workup applies (TSH → ultrasound → FNA if indicated); PET-avid thyroid nodules carry ~30% malignancy risk and always warrant further evaluation regardless of size\
  **题目变式——影像学偶然发现结节:** 适用相同评估流程（TSH → 超声 → 必要时 FNA）；PET 摄取增高的甲状腺结节恶性风险约 30%，无论大小均需进一步评估

- **Key complication of delayed or missed diagnosis:** Papillary carcinoma may invade the recurrent laryngeal nerve (→ hoarseness) or trachea if allowed to progress; follicular carcinoma metastasizes hematogenously to lung and bone; anaplastic carcinoma has median survival of 3–5 months\
  **延误或漏诊的关键并发症:** 乳头状癌进展后可侵犯喉返神经（→ 声嘶）或气管；滤泡癌经血行转移至肺和骨；未分化癌中位生存期仅 3–5 个月

- **Mnemonic for suspicious ultrasound features ("MATCH"):** Microcalcifications, Absent halo, Taller-than-wide shape, Central vascularity (on Doppler), Hypoechoic compared to surrounding thyroid — each feature lowers the size threshold at which FNA is recommended\
  **超声可疑特征记忆口诀（"MATCH"）:** 微钙化（Microcalcifications）、无晕环（Absent halo）、纵横比 \>1（Taller-than-wide）、中央血流（Central vascularity，多普勒）、低回声（Hypoechoic）——每项特征均降低推荐 FNA 的结节大小门槛

# Question 70 — Paroxysmal Supraventricular Tachycardia / 阵发性室上性心动过速

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>17-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the emergency department by his mother because of a <strong>20-minute episode of severe chest pain and sweating</strong> that started 1 hour ago while he was watching television. On arrival, he is alert and repeatedly expresses concern that something is 'very wrong.' He reports that during the episode, his <strong>heart was 'pounding,'</strong> he felt <strong>short of breath,</strong> and he was sure he was having a heart attack and was going to die. One month ago, he had a <strong>similar episode</strong> that occurred in the evening 30 minutes after his high school football practice. At that time, <strong>results of laboratory studies and an ECG obtained in the emergency department showed no abnormalities.</strong> After the initial episode, he quit the football team, and he has continued to <strong>limit his physical activity</strong> because he is afraid of bringing on another episode. He reports no insomnia or changes in appetite. His mother states that he was diagnosed with an innocent heart murmur at the age of 6 months, but it has not been noted on examinations since the age of 1 year. His paternal grandfather died of a myocardial infarction 3 years ago at the age of 68 years. The patient takes no medications. He does not smoke cigarettes, drink alcohol, or use illicit drugs. He performs well in school. He is 180 cm (5 ft 11 in) tall and weighs 73 kg (161 lb); BMI is 23 kg/m2. His temperature is 37.0°C (98.6°F), and blood pressure is 130/83 mm Hg. No murmurs are heard on cardiac examination. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. <strong>ECG is shown.</strong></p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Acute stress disorder<br />
B) Delusional disorder<br />
C) Generalized anxiety disorder<br />
D) Hypertrophic cardiomyopathy<br />
E) Idiopathic recurrent pericarditis<br />
F) Panic disorder<br />
G) Paroxysmal supraventricular tachycardia</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: G</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<tr>
<td>17-year-old boy, recurrent paroxysmal episodes<br />
17岁男孩，反复阵发性发作</td>
<td>PSVT most commonly affects young patients with structurally normal hearts; "paroxysmal" (abrupt onset/offset) is the hallmark<br />
