目前无杂音；婴儿期功能性杂音已消失</td>
<td>Structurally normal heart at time of episode; rules out HCM (which produces a characteristic systolic murmur)<br />
发作时心脏结构正常；排除 HCM（HCM 可产生特征性收缩期杂音）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

A **re-entrant circuit** forms above the ventricles when two conducting pathways with differing **refractory periods** and conduction velocities are present. The most common subtype is **atrioventricular nodal re-entrant tachycardia (AVNRT)**, in which dual AV nodal pathways create a self-sustaining electrical loop:

当两条**不应期**和传导速度不同的传导通路并存时，心室以上形成**折返环**。最常见亚型是**房室结折返性心动过速（AVNRT）**，其双通路在房室结内形成自我维持的电折返环：

- Anterograde conduction down the slow pathway and retrograde up the fast pathway creates a circular current, producing the classic "short RP" tachycardia\
  前向经慢通路下传、逆向经快通路上传形成环形电流，产生经典"短 RP"心动过速

- Wolff-Parkinson-White (WPW) syndrome adds an **accessory bypass tract (Bundle of Kent)**, creating **orthodromic AVRT** with delta waves visible on resting ECG between episodes\
  Wolff-Parkinson-White（WPW）综合征存在**旁道（Kent 束）**，形成**顺向型 AVRT**，发作间期静息 ECG 可见 delta 波

- A premature atrial contraction (PAC) initiates the re-entry loop by encountering one pathway during its refractory period\
  房性早搏（PAC）遭遇一条处于不应期的通路时触发折返

- Result: abrupt-onset, rapid, regular tachycardia with **narrow QRS complex** because ventricular activation proceeds normally through the His-Purkinje system\
  结果：突然发作的快速规则心动过速，**窄 QRS 波群**，因心室经正常 His-Purkinje 系统激动

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Any tachycardia with a narrow QRS (\< 120 ms) is almost certainly supraventricular — narrow width proves both ventricles are activated simultaneously through normal conduction.

**解剖小窍门:** 窄 QRS（\< 120 ms）心动过速几乎必然是室上性——窄 QRS 证明两心室经正常传导系统同时激动。

## 3. Correct Answer (G) — Paroxysmal Supraventricular Tachycardia / 正确答案 (G) — 阵发性室上性心动过速

**Paroxysmal supraventricular tachycardia (PSVT)** is a generic term for episodic, rapid, regular tachycardias originating above the bundle of His, most commonly AVNRT (60%), followed by AVRT (30%), and atrial tachycardia (10%):

**阵发性室上性心动过速（PSVT）**是一类起源于 His 束以上的发作性快速规则心动过速的统称，最常见为 AVNRT（60%），其次为 AVRT（30%）和房性心动过速（10%）：

- Rate typically 150–250 bpm with truly abrupt onset and abrupt termination (the "paroxysmal" qualifier)\
  心率通常 150–250 次/分，突发突止（"阵发性"的精确含义）

- Narrow QRS complex (\< 120 ms) because ventricular activation uses the normal His-Purkinje system\
  窄 QRS 波群（\< 120 ms），因心室经正常 His-Purkinje 系统激动

- Symptoms — palpitations, chest tightness, dyspnea, diaphoresis, near-syncope — arise from reduced diastolic filling time at high rates\
  症状包括心悸、胸闷、气短、大汗、近晕厥，均因高心率时舒张充盈时间缩短所致

- ECG between episodes is often entirely normal; the diagnostic ECG must be obtained during an active episode\
  发作间期 ECG 通常完全正常；必须在发作期获取有诊断意义的 ECG

**Diagnosis:** The ECG obtained during this episode showing narrow complex tachycardia at a rate far exceeding normal sinus is the definitive finding. The history of identical recurrent paroxysmal episodes with complete return to baseline confirms chronicity.

**诊断:** 本次发作期 ECG 显示窄 QRS 心动过速，心率远超正常窦性，是决定性依据。完全相同的反复阵发性发作史伴发作间期完全恢复正常，确认了慢性病程。

**Treatment:** Hemodynamically stable — vagal maneuvers (Valsalva, carotid sinus massage, ice water to face) first, then IV adenosine 6 mg rapid push (repeat 12 mg if needed), then IV diltiazem or metoprolol. Hemodynamically unstable — synchronized DC cardioversion immediately. Long-term: catheter ablation of the re-entrant pathway (\> 95% cure rate).

**治疗:** 血流动力学稳定——先行迷走神经操作（Valsalva、颈动脉窦按摩、冰水敷面），再静脉腺苷 6 mg 快速推注（必要时重复 12 mg），再静脉地尔硫䓬或美托洛尔。血流动力学不稳定——立即同步直流电复律。长期：导管消融折返通路（治愈率 \> 95%）。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Acute stress disorder<br />
A — 急性应激障碍</td>
<td>Requires a qualifying traumatic event (e.g., life-threatening collision); chest pain while watching TV does not constitute trauma; symptoms must include intrusive thoughts, dissociation, or avoidance of trauma reminders<br />
需要符合条件的创伤性事件（如威胁生命的车祸）；看电视时出现胸痛不构成创伤；症状须包括侵入性思维、解离或对创伤提示的回避</td>
<td>No traumatic precipitant; no intrusive thoughts or dissociation; episodic cardiac symptoms<br />
无创伤性诱因；无侵入性思维或解离；发作性心脏症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Delusional disorder<br />
B — 妄想性障碍</td>
<td>Requires one or more fixed delusions lasting ≥ 1 month with no other psychotic features; fear of having a heart attack during an episode is reactive and situational, not a fixed false belief<br />
需要 ≥ 1 个月的固定妄想且无其他精神病性特征；发作时对心脏病发作的恐惧是反应性情境性的，非固定错误信念</td>
<td>No persistent false belief independent of episodes; normal school performance and social functioning<br />
发作之外无持续性错误信念；学习表现及社会功能正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Generalized anxiety disorder<br />
C — 广泛性焦虑障碍</td>
<td>GAD requires pervasive, excessive, difficult-to-control worry on most days for ≥ 6 months across multiple domains; no insomnia or appetite change reported here<br />
GAD 需要 ≥ 6 个月内大多数时间对多个领域存在弥漫性、难以控制的过度担忧；本例无失眠或食欲改变</td>
<td>Anxiety is episode-specific, not generalized; complete interepisodic normalcy; no somatic complaints between attacks<br />
焦虑局限于发作，非弥漫性；发作间期完全正常；发作外无躯体不适</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Hypertrophic cardiomyopathy<br />
D — 肥厚型心肌病</td>
<td>HCM classically causes exertional syncope/dyspnea with a systolic murmur loudest at the lower left sternal border; no murmur on exam; ECG would show LVH voltage criteria and septal Q waves, not narrow complex tachycardia<br />
HCM 经典表现为劳力性晕厥/气短伴胸骨左缘下段收缩期杂音；查体无杂音；ECG 应显示左室肥大电压标准和室间隔 Q 波，而非窄 QRS 心动过速</td>
<td>No murmur; ECG during episode shows tachycardia, not LVH; episodes occur at rest as well as with exertion<br />
无杂音；发作期 ECG 示心动过速而非左室肥大；静息亦可发作</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Idiopathic recurrent pericarditis<br />
E — 特发性复发性心包炎</td>
<td>Pericarditis pain is pleuritic (sharp, worsens lying down, improves leaning forward); physical exam reveals a pericardial friction rub; ECG shows diffuse saddle-shaped ST elevation and PR depression<br />
心包炎疼痛为胸膜炎性（锐痛，平卧加重，前倾减轻）；查体有心包摩擦音；ECG 示弥漫鞍形 ST 段抬高和 PR 段压低</td>
<td>No friction rub; no positional chest pain; ECG shows tachycardia, not diffuse ST changes<br />
无摩擦音；无体位性胸痛；ECG 示心动过速而非弥漫 ST 改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Panic disorder<br />
F — 惊恐障碍</td>
<td>Panic disorder produces an identical somatic symptom profile and avoidance behavior, but ECG during a panic attack shows only modest sinus tachycardia (100–120 bpm), never a narrow complex tachycardia at 150–250 bpm<br />
惊恐障碍可产生完全相同的躯体症状和回避行为，但发作时 ECG 仅显示轻度窦性心动过速（100–120 次/分），绝不会出现 150–250 次/分的窄 QRS 心动过速</td>
<td>ECG during this episode shows narrow complex tachycardia — impossible in a pure panic attack; abrupt flip-switch termination also favors arrhythmia<br />
本次发作 ECG 示窄 QRS 心动过速——单纯惊恐发作不可能出现；突然终止也更符合心律失常特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>G — Paroxysmal supraventricular tachycardia ✓<br />
G — 阵发性室上性心动过速 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — ECG during the episode demonstrates narrow complex tachycardia at 150–250 bpm; recurrent identical paroxysmal episodes; normal ECG and labs between attacks<br />
正确——发作期 ECG 显示 150–250 次/分窄 QRS 心动过速；反复完全相同的阵发性发作；发作间期 ECG 及化验正常</td>
<td>Narrow QRS tachycardia on the in-episode ECG is pathognomonic for SVT and cannot be explained by any psychiatric diagnosis<br />
发作期 ECG 窄 QRS 心动过速是 SVT 的特征表现，任何精神科诊断均无法解释</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The hardest distractor is Panic Disorder (F): both produce identical somatic symptoms — palpitations, chest pain, dyspnea, diaphoresis — in young patients with avoidance behavior, but the ECG obtained during the episode is the decisive differentiator: SVT yields a narrow complex tachycardia at 150–250 bpm, whereas panic attack produces only sinus tachycardia at 100–120 bpm.*

最难排除的干扰项是惊恐障碍（F）：两者在年轻患者中均可产生完全相同的躯体症状——心悸、胸痛、气短、大汗——且均可出现回避行为，但发作期 ECG 是决定性鉴别依据：SVT 呈 150–250 次/分窄 QRS 心动过速，而惊恐发作仅引起 100–120 次/分的窦性心动过速。

<td>Absent (fear is secondary to physical symptoms)<br />
缺乏（恐惧继发于躯体症状）</td>

<td>Catheter ablation of re-entrant pathway (&gt; 95% cure)<br />
导管消融折返通路（治愈率 &gt; 95%）</td>
<td>CBT + SSRIs; no ablation<br />
认知行为疗法 + SSRI；无需消融</td>
</tr>
</tbody>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a young patient with recurrent paroxysmal palpitations and chest pain, the ECG obtained during the episode revealing narrow complex tachycardia at 150–250 bpm is the single finding that clinches PSVT and rules out panic disorder.**

**在年轻患者出现反复阵发性心悸和胸痛时，发作期 ECG 显示 150–250 次/分窄 QRS 心动过速是确诊 PSVT 并排除惊恐障碍的唯一决定性依据。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SNAP" for PSVT Features / 记忆钩 — "SNAP" 记忆 PSVT 核心特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>udden onset/offset — the hallmark paroxysmal "flip-switch" start and end / 突发突止——标志性"电灯开关"式发作与终止<br />
• <strong>N</strong>arrow QRS complex on ECG (&lt; 120 ms) — supraventricular origin confirmed / ECG 窄 QRS 波群（&lt; 120 ms）——室上性起源的证明<br />
• <strong>A</strong>denosine terminates stable PSVT — vagal maneuvers first, adenosine second / 腺苷终止稳定期 PSVT——迷走神经操作优先，腺苷次之<br />
• <strong>P</strong>alpitations + diaphoresis + dyspnea — all from decreased cardiac output during tachycardia / 心悸 + 大汗 + 气短——均源于心动过速时心输出量下降</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — PSVT: Mechanism, ECG, and Management / 高频知识表 — PSVT：机制、ECG 及处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>PSVT subtypes and prevalence<br />
PSVT 亚型及发生率</td>
<td>AVNRT 60% (most common, dual AV nodal pathways); AVRT 30% (accessory pathway, includes WPW); atrial tachycardia 10% (ectopic focus)<br />
AVNRT 60%（最常见，房室结双通路）；AVRT 30%（旁道，含 WPW）；房性心动过速 10%（异位兴奋灶）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG during PSVT episode<br />
PSVT 发作期 ECG 特征</td>
<td>Narrow QRS (&lt; 120 ms), regular rate 150–250 bpm; P waves absent, buried in QRS (AVNRT), or retrograde negative in II/III/aVF (AVRT)<br />
窄 QRS（&lt; 120 ms），规则心率 150–250 次/分；P 波消失或埋入 QRS（AVNRT），或在 II/III/aVF 逆行倒置（AVRT）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>WPW syndrome ECG findings<br />
WPW 综合征 ECG 表现</td>
<td>Short PR (&lt; 120 ms) + delta wave (slurred QRS upstroke) on resting ECG; wide QRS due to ventricular pre-excitation; can degenerate to life-threatening AF with rapid conduction<br />
静息 ECG 短 PR（&lt; 120 ms）+ delta 波（QRS 起始部粗钝）；心室预激导致宽 QRS；可退化为快速传导的致命性房颤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute management — hemodynamically stable<br />
急性处理——血流动力学稳定</td>
<td>Step 1: vagal maneuvers (Valsalva, carotid sinus massage, ice water to face); Step 2: IV adenosine 6 mg rapid push → repeat 12 mg; Step 3: IV diltiazem or metoprolol<br />
第一步：迷走神经操作；第二步：腺苷 6 mg 快速静推 → 重复 12 mg；第三步：静脉地尔硫䓬或美托洛尔</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute management — hemodynamically unstable<br />
急性处理——血流动力学不稳定</td>
<td>Immediate synchronized DC cardioversion; instability signs: hypotension, altered mental status, angina, pulmonary edema<br />
立即同步直流电复律；不稳定征象：低血压、意识改变、心绞痛、肺水肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long-term management<br />
长期处理</td>
<td>Catheter ablation of the re-entrant pathway is curative (&gt; 95% success rate, low recurrence); drugs (beta-blocker or CCB) for patients who decline or are not candidates for ablation<br />
导管消融折返通路可根治（成功率 &gt; 95%，复发率低）；拒绝或不适合消融者可选 β 受体阻滞剂或钙通道阻滞剂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PSVT vs. VT: the critical distinction<br />
PSVT vs. 室速：关键鉴别</td>
<td>PSVT: narrow QRS, usually hemodynamically stable; VT: wide QRS (&gt; 120 ms), AV dissociation, fusion beats, cannon A waves; clinical rule — any wide complex tachycardia = VT until proven otherwise<br />
PSVT：窄 QRS，通常血流动力学稳定；VT：宽 QRS（&gt; 120 ms），房室分离，融合波，大炮 A 波；临床法则——任何宽 QRS 心动过速均视为 VT 直至排除</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Caution with adenosine in WPW + AF:** If WPW coexists with atrial fibrillation, adenosine blocks the AV node and forces all conduction through the accessory pathway, risking ventricular fibrillation — never give AV nodal blockers in pre-excited AF\
  **WPW 合并房颤时腺苷禁忌:** WPW 合并房颤时，腺苷阻断房室结可迫使所有传导经旁道下传，诱发室颤——预激合并房颤时禁用房室结阻滞剂

- **Variant — antidromic AVRT:** In WPW, anterograde conduction via the accessory pathway and retrograde via the AV node produces wide QRS tachycardia that mimics VT on ECG — treat with cardioversion, never adenosine or diltiazem\
  **变式——逆向型 AVRT:** WPW 中前向经旁道、逆向经房室结传导可产生宽 QRS 心动过速，ECG 酷似室速——应电复律，禁用腺苷或地尔硫䓬

- **Differential of narrow complex tachycardia:** Sinus tachycardia (gradual onset, rate \< 150) vs. AVNRT/AVRT (abrupt, 150–250) vs. atrial flutter (sawtooth flutter waves in II/III/aVF, rate ~150 with 2:1 block) vs. atrial fibrillation (irregularly irregular, no distinct P waves)\
  **窄 QRS 心动过速鉴别:** 窦性心动过速（逐渐加速，\< 150 次/分）vs. AVNRT/AVRT（突发，150–250 次/分）vs. 心房扑动（II/III/aVF 锯齿波，2:1 阻滞约 150 次/分）vs. 心房颤动（绝对不规则，无明确 P 波）

- **Key complication — tachycardia-induced cardiomyopathy:** Persistent or very frequent PSVT over months can produce a reversible dilated cardiomyopathy; EF normalizes after rate control or ablation\
  **关键并发症——心动过速性心肌病:** 持续或频繁 PSVT 发作数月可导致可逆性扩张型心肌病；控制心率或消融后射血分数可恢复正常

# Question 71 — Abdominal Aortic Aneurysm Rupture Mortality Calculation / 腹主动脉瘤破裂死亡率计算

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>72-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician for a routine health maintenance examination. Abdominal examination shows a <strong>nontender, pulsatile mass in the epigastrium</strong>. Abdominal ultrasonography shows a <strong>7.2-cm aneurysm</strong>. The physician reviews several studies of patients with abdominal aneurysms that are greater than 7 cm in size. The rupture rate is estimated to be <strong>20% per year</strong>. Following rupture of an abdominal aneurysm, <strong>one half of patients die before reaching a hospital</strong>. For patients who do reach a hospital, the <strong>perioperative mortality rate is approximately 50%</strong>. The mortality rate for patients who undergo elective repair of an aneurysm is <strong>5%</strong>. After discussing the risks and benefits of surgical repair of the aneurysm, the patient decides not to undergo an operation.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following best represents this patient's risk for mortality from rupture of the aneurysm during the next year?</strong></p>
<p>A) 5%<br />
B) 10%<br />
C) 15%<br />
D) 20%<br />
E) 50%</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>72-year-old man<br />
72岁男性</td>
<td>AAA predominantly affects elderly men; risk increases sharply with age and male sex<br />
腹主动脉瘤主要影响老年男性；风险随年龄和男性性别显著增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nontender, pulsatile epigastric mass<br />
无痛性搏动性上腹部包块</td>
<td>Classic presentation of AAA; painless until expansion or rupture<br />
腹主动脉瘤经典表现；在扩张或破裂前无痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>7.2-cm aneurysm<br />
7.2cm动脉瘤</td>
<td>&gt;5.5 cm triggers repair; &gt;7 cm carries very high annual rupture risk (~20-40%/yr)<br />
&gt;5.5cm为修复指征；&gt;7cm年破裂风险极高（约20-40%/年）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>20% annual rupture rate<br />
20%年破裂率</td>
<td>The baseline probability P(rupture) — the outer multiplier in the final calculation<br />
基础破裂概率P(破裂)——最终计算中的外乘因子</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>One half die before reaching hospital<br />
到达医院前一半患者死亡</td>
<td>First mortality filter in the sequential probability chain (0.50)<br />
序贯概率链中的第一个死亡筛选因子（0.50）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Perioperative mortality rate ~50% (post-rupture)<br />
围手术期死亡率约50%（破裂后）</td>
<td>Second mortality filter applied only to hospital survivors (0.50 × 0.50 = 0.25 of all ruptures)<br />
第二个死亡筛选因子，仅适用于到院生存者（0.50 × 0.50 = 破裂总数的0.25）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Elective repair mortality 5%<br />
择期修复死亡率5%</td>
<td>Comparator that frames the decision: 5% surgical risk vs. 15% annual rupture mortality<br />
决策框架的比较数据：5%手术风险 vs. 15%年破裂死亡率</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

This question tests **sequential probability calculation** applied to a patient with a large **abdominal aortic aneurysm (AAA)**. The key insight is that mortality from rupture involves **two independent death filters** occurring after the rupture event — they must be summed before being multiplied by the rupture rate:

本题考查大型**腹主动脉瘤（AAA）**患者的**序贯概率计算**。核心要点在于破裂后死亡涉及**两个独立的死亡筛选因子**——必须先将两者相加，再乘以破裂率：

- **Step 1:** Annual rupture probability = 20% → P(rupture) = 0.20\
  **第一步：** 年破裂概率 = 20% → P(破裂) = 0.20

- **Step 2:** Of those who rupture, 50% die pre-hospital → P(pre-hospital death \| rupture) = 0.50\
  **第二步：** 破裂者中50%院前死亡 → P(院前死亡\|破裂) = 0.50

- **Step 3:** Of the 50% who reach hospital, 50% die perioperatively → P(peri-op death \| hospital arrival) = 0.50\
  **第三步：** 到达医院的50%中，50%围手术期死亡 → P(围手术期死亡\|到达医院) = 0.50

- **Step 4:** Combined mortality if ruptured = 0.50 + (0.50 × 0.50) = 0.50 + 0.25 = **0.75 (75%)**\
  **第四步：** 破裂后综合死亡率 = 0.50 + (0.50 × 0.50) = 0.50 + 0.25 = **0.75（75%）**

- **Step 5:** Overall 1-year mortality = P(rupture) × P(death \| rupture) = 0.20 × 0.75 = **0.15 = 15%**\
  **第五步：** 1年总死亡率 = P(破裂) × P(破裂后死亡) = 0.20 × 0.75 = **0.15 = 15%**

**Statistical rule of thumb:** When two sequential events must both occur, multiply their probabilities — but first sum all death pathways within the conditional event (pre-hospital + peri-op) before applying the outer probability.

**统计小窍门:** 当两个序贯事件都必须发生时，将其概率相乘——但在应用外部概率之前，先将条件事件内的所有死亡途径（院前 + 围手术期）相加。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Sequential Probability Calculation / 正确答案 (C) — 序贯概率计算

**15% annual mortality from rupture** is derived by combining both death pathways for a ruptured AAA, then multiplying by the annual rupture probability:

**破裂致15%年死亡率**通过合并破裂后两条死亡途径，再乘以年破裂概率得出：

- If AAA ruptures: 50% die before reaching hospital (0.50), and of the 50% who arrive, 50% die perioperatively (0.50 × 0.50 = 0.25)\
  若发生破裂：50%到达医院前死亡（0.50），到达医院的50%中有50%围手术期死亡（0.50 × 0.50 = 0.25）

- Combined mortality if ruptured = 0.50 + 0.25 = 0.75 → 75% of rupture patients die\
  破裂后综合死亡率 = 0.50 + 0.25 = 0.75 → 75%的破裂患者死亡

- Annual mortality risk = rupture rate × death-if-ruptured = 0.20 × 0.75 = **0.15 = 15%**\
  年死亡风险 = 破裂率 × 破裂后死亡率 = 0.20 × 0.75 = **0.15 = 15%**

**Diagnosis:** 7.2-cm AAA clearly exceeds the 5.5-cm repair threshold; patient's refusal of surgery means accepting a 15%/year mortality from rupture versus the one-time 5% risk of elective repair

**诊断:** 7.2cm腹主动脉瘤明显超过5.5cm修复阈值；患者拒绝手术意味着接受15%/年的破裂死亡率，而择期修复仅有一次性5%风险

**Treatment:** Elective open or endovascular (EVAR) repair; urgency is clear given 15% annual rupture mortality far exceeds 5% elective mortality

**治疗:** 择期开放手术或腔内修复（EVAR）；鉴于15%年破裂死亡率远超5%择期手术死亡率，手术紧迫性明确

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — 5%<br />
A — 5%</td>
<td>Incorrect calculation: 0.20 × 0.50 × 0.50 = 0.05; multiplies all three values in series, which treats the two death pathways as purely multiplicative rather than combining them first<br />
计算错误：0.20 × 0.50 × 0.50 = 0.05；将三个数值连乘，错误地将两条死亡途径视为纯乘法关系而非先相加</td>
<td>Pre-hospital and peri-op mortality are additive pathways, not sequential multiplicative filters<br />
院前死亡和围手术期死亡是相加的并行途径，而非序贯相乘的筛选因子</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — 10%<br />
B — 10%</td>
<td>Incorrect calculation: 0.20 × 0.50 = 0.10; accounts only for pre-hospital mortality, ignoring perioperative mortality entirely<br />
计算错误：0.20 × 0.50 = 0.10；仅计入院前死亡率，完全忽略围手术期死亡率</td>
<td>Must include both death pathways: pre-hospital AND in-hospital perioperative for complete calculation<br />
完整计算必须纳入两条死亡途径：院前死亡和院内围手术期死亡</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — 15% ✓<br />
C — 15% ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — 0.20 × (0.50 + 0.25) = 0.20 × 0.75 = 0.15; correctly sums both death pathways then multiplies by rupture rate<br />
正确——0.20 × (0.50 + 0.25) = 0.20 × 0.75 = 0.15；正确合并两条死亡途径后乘以破裂率</td>
<td>Sequential two-step: calculate P(death if ruptured) = 75% first, then multiply by P(rupture) = 20%<br />
序贯两步法：先算P(破裂后死亡) = 75%，再乘以P(破裂) = 20%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — 20%<br />
D — 20%</td>
<td>This is the annual rupture rate alone, not the annual mortality rate; rupture ≠ death (25% of rupture patients survive)<br />
这是年破裂率，而非年死亡率；破裂≠死亡（25%的破裂患者存活）</td>
<td>Rupture rate and mortality rate are distinct; must account for the 25% survival after rupture<br />
破裂率和死亡率是不同概念；必须考虑破裂后25%的存活率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — 50%<br />
E — 50%</td>
<td>This is the pre-hospital conditional mortality (among those who rupture), not the overall annual mortality risk; confuses a conditional probability with an absolute annual risk<br />
这是院前条件死亡率（破裂者中），而非年总死亡风险；将条件概率与绝对年风险混淆</td>
<td>Must multiply conditional mortality by the probability of rupture (20%), not use the raw conditional figure directly<br />
必须将条件死亡率乘以破裂概率（20%），不能直接使用原始条件死亡率</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most common trap is D (20%), which confuses the annual rupture rate with annual mortality — remember that 25% of ruptured AAA patients survive, so true mortality is 0.20 × 0.75 = 15%, not 20%.*

最常见的陷阱是D（20%），将年破裂率与年死亡率混淆——请记住25%的腹主动脉瘤破裂患者存活，因此真实死亡率为0.20 × 0.75 = 15%，而非20%。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For a \>7-cm AAA with 20%/year rupture rate, annual mortality = 20% × 75% = 15%, because rupture carries 75% mortality (50% pre-hospital + 50% of hospital arrivals), not 100%.**

**对于破裂率20%/年的\>7cm腹主动脉瘤，年死亡率 = 20% × 75% = 15%，因为破裂死亡率为75%（50%院前 + 到院者中50%），而非100%。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — R.I.P. Formula / 记忆钩 — R.I.P. 公式:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>R</strong>upture rate = 20%/year — start here as the outer multiplier / 破裂率 = 20%/年——以此作为外乘因子的起点<br />
• <strong>I</strong>n-route (pre-hospital): 50% of rupture patients die = 0.50 / 途中（院前）：50%破裂患者死亡 = 0.50<br />
• <strong>P</strong>erioperative: 50% of hospital arrivals die = 0.50 × 0.50 = 0.25 of all ruptures / 围手术期：50%到院者死亡 = 0.50 × 0.50 = 0.25（占破裂总数）<br />
• <strong>Total</strong> if ruptured = I + P = 0.50 + 0.25 = 0.75; Annual mortality = <strong>R</strong> × 0.75 = 20% × 75% = <strong>15%</strong> / 破裂后总死亡 = I + P = 0.75；年死亡率 = <strong>R</strong> × 0.75 = 20% × 75% = <strong>15%</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

<td>Repair Indications<br />
修复指征</td>
<td>≥5.5 cm diameter; rapid growth (&gt;0.5 cm/6 months or &gt;1 cm/year); symptomatic (pain, tenderness); embolic complications<br />
直径≥5.5cm；快速增长（&gt;0.5cm/6个月或&gt;1cm/年）；有症状（疼痛、压痛）；栓塞并发症</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rupture Risk by Size<br />
按尺寸的破裂风险</td>
<td>&lt;4 cm: ~0%/yr; 4–5 cm: ~1%/yr; 5–6 cm: ~5–10%/yr; 6–7 cm: ~10–20%/yr; &gt;7 cm: ~20–40%/yr<br />
&lt;4cm：约0%/年；4–5cm：约1%/年；5–6cm：约5–10%/年；6–7cm：约10–20%/年；&gt;7cm：约20–40%/年</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>EVAR vs. Open Repair<br />
腔内修复 vs. 开放手术</td>
<td>EVAR: lower short-term mortality (~1.5%), faster recovery, requires surveillance for endoleak; Open: more durable, higher peri-op risk (~3–5%), but fewer late complications<br />
EVAR：短期死亡率更低（约1.5%），恢复更快，需监测内漏；开放手术：更持久，围手术期风险更高（约3–5%），但晚期并发症较少</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic Rupture Triad<br />
经典破裂三联征</td>
<td>Hypotension + severe back/flank pain + pulsatile abdominal mass → emergent OR without waiting for imaging; high mortality even with immediate surgery<br />
低血压 + 严重背部/侧腹痛 + 搏动性腹部包块 → 紧急手术，不等待影像学；即使立即手术死亡率仍高</td>
<td></td>
<td></td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sequential Probability Calculation Rule<br />
序贯概率计算规则</td>
<td>P(A and B) = P(A) × P(B</td>
<td>A); when B has parallel pathways, sum all pathways first: P(death if ruptured) = P(pre-hospital death) + P(survive to hospital) × P(peri-op death)<br />
P(A且B) = P(A) × P(B</td>
<td>A)；当B有并行途径时，先将所有途径相加：P(破裂后死亡) = P(院前死亡) + P(存活到院) × P(围手术期死亡)</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of Pulsatile Abdominal Mass:** Para-aortic lymphadenopathy (transmitted pulsation, non-expansile), retroperitoneal tumor, horseshoe kidney — true expansile pulsatile mass almost always means AAA, confirmed by ultrasound\
  **搏动性腹部包块的鉴别诊断:** 腹主动脉旁淋巴结肿大（传导性搏动，无扩张性）、腹膜后肿瘤、马蹄肾——真正的扩张性搏动包块几乎总是腹主动脉瘤，超声可确诊

- **Screening Mnemonic:** "65–75, Male, Ever-Smoked = One Ultrasound" — catches asymptomatic AAA before rupture; most AAAs are found incidentally on imaging\
  **筛查记忆法:** "65–75岁、男性、曾吸烟 = 一次超声"——在破裂前发现无症状腹主动脉瘤；大多数腹主动脉瘤在影像学检查中偶然发现

- **Key Complication of EVAR:** Endoleak (persistent flow into aneurysm sac outside the graft) — requires surveillance CT at 1 month, 12 months, then annually; Type II endoleak (from collateral vessels) most common\
  **EVAR的关键并发症:** 内漏（支架外持续血流进入动脉瘤囊）——需在术后1个月、12个月及此后每年行CT随访；II型内漏（来自侧支血管）最常见

- **Statistical Principle Applied Broadly:** This same two-filter probability framework appears in NBME questions on cancer screening (sensitivity × prevalence), diagnostic test cascades, and multi-step procedural mortality — always identify all conditional pathways, sum them, then multiply by the trigger probability\
  **统计原理广泛应用:** 相同的双筛选因子概率框架出现在肿瘤筛查（灵敏度×患病率）、诊断检测级联和多步骤手术死亡率等NBME题目中——始终识别所有条件途径，相加后再乘以触发概率

# Question 72 — Medication-Induced Parkinsonism / 药物性帕金森综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>58-year-old man</strong> with an 8-year history of <strong>schizoaffective disorder, manic type</strong>, is brought to the clinic for a follow-up examination. Two weeks ago, he was hospitalized for a manic episode. <strong>Risperidone</strong> was added to his medication regimen; <strong>the dosage was increased to the maximum recommended</strong> prior to discharge. At that time, neurologic examination showed <strong>mild cogwheel rigidity</strong>. There was no evidence of tremors. Muscle strength was 5/5. He has no other history of serious medical or psychiatric illness. His other medications are valproic acid and clonazepam. Today, examination shows <strong>drooling, masked facies, and decreased blinking</strong>. He has a <strong>slow, shuffling gait with decreased arm swing</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Mental status examination shows normal speech and a mildly anxious mood. There is no evidence of psychosis. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Addition of diphenhydramine to the medication regimen<br />
B) Addition of lithium carbonate to the medication regimen<br />
C) Cognitive behavioral therapy<br />
D) Decreasing the dosage of risperidone<br />
E) Increasing the dosage of clonazepam<br />
F) Psychotherapy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Risperidone increased to maximum recommended dose<br />
利培酮加至最大推荐剂量</td>
<td>Higher doses of antipsychotics cause greater D2 blockade in the nigrostriatal pathway, proportionally increasing EPS risk<br />
抗精神病药剂量越高，黑质纹状体通路D2阻断越强，EPS风险成比例增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cogwheel rigidity noted 2 weeks ago<br />
2周前已出现齿轮样强直</td>
<td>Early warning sign of drug-induced parkinsonism that progressed because the dose was not adjusted at discharge<br />
药物性帕金森综合征的早期预警信号，出院时未调整剂量导致症状进展</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Drooling, masked facies, decreased blinking<br />
流涎、面具脸、眨眼减少</td>
<td>Cardinal signs of parkinsonism: autonomic (drooling) and motor (hypomimia) features of dopaminergic deficiency in basal ganglia<br />
帕金森综合征的经典体征：基底节多巴胺能缺乏的自主神经（流涎）和运动（表情减少）特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Slow, shuffling gait with decreased arm swing<br />
缓慢拖曳步态伴手臂摆动减少</td>
<td>Classic parkinsonian gait reflecting bradykinesia and impaired postural reflexes<br />
经典帕金森步态，反映运动迟缓和姿势反射受损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No evidence of psychosis<br />
无精神病症状</td>
<td>Psychotic symptoms are controlled; the clinical problem is now purely pharmacological side effects, not undertreated illness<br />
精神症状已控制；当前临床问题纯粹是药物副作用，而非疾病控制不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Subacute onset over weeks<br />
数周内亚急性起病</td>
<td>Onset timeline (weeks after dose increase) distinguishes drug-induced parkinsonism from acute dystonia (hours) and tardive dyskinesia (months)<br />
发病时间线（增量后数周）可区分药物性帕金森综合征、急性肌张力障碍（数小时）和迟发性运动障碍（数月）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Risperidone**, a second-generation antipsychotic, is a potent **D2 receptor antagonist** that non-selectively blocks dopamine signaling across multiple brain pathways simultaneously:

**利培酮**是一种二代抗精神病药，是强效的 **D2受体拮抗剂**，可同时在多条脑通路中非选择性阻断多巴胺信号传导：

- **Mesolimbic pathway** blockade → reduced dopamine activity in limbic system → antipsychotic effect (controls hallucinations and delusions)\
  **中脑边缘通路**阻断 → 边缘系统多巴胺活性降低 → 抗精神病效果（控制幻觉和妄想）

- **Nigrostriatal pathway** blockade → loss of dopaminergic tone in basal ganglia → drug-induced parkinsonism (bradykinesia, cogwheel rigidity, masked facies, shuffling gait)\
  **黑质纹状体通路**阻断 → 基底节多巴胺调控丧失 → 药物性帕金森综合征（运动迟缓、齿轮样强直、面具脸、拖曳步态）

- **Tuberoinfundibular pathway** blockade → elevated prolactin → galactorrhea, amenorrhea, gynecomastia\
  **结节漏斗通路**阻断 → 催乳素升高 → 溢乳、闭经、男性乳房发育

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The mesolimbic and nigrostriatal pathways cannot be pharmacologically separated — at higher doses, the drug that controls psychosis inevitably spills into the motor control circuitry.

**解剖小窍门:** 中脑边缘通路和黑质纹状体通路在药理上无法分离——剂量越高，控制精神症状的药物不可避免地会影响运动控制回路。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Dose Reduction of Offending Antipsychotic / 正确答案 (D) — 减少致病抗精神病药剂量

**Medication-induced parkinsonism** is a dose-dependent extrapyramidal side effect of dopamine antagonists that is best managed by reducing or discontinuing the causative agent:

**药物性帕金森综合征**是多巴胺拮抗剂的剂量依赖性锥体外系副作用，最佳处理是减少或停用致病药物：

- Drug-induced parkinsonism appears subacutely (weeks after starting or dose-escalating an antipsychotic) and is reversible upon dose reduction\
  药物性帕金森综合征亚急性出现（启用或增加抗精神病药剂量后数周），减量后可逆

- Since risperidone was already titrated to the maximum recommended dose, reduction directly addresses the root cause (excessive nigrostriatal D2 blockade)\
  由于利培酮已加至最大推荐剂量，减量可直接解决根本原因（过度的黑质纹状体D2阻断）

- If dose reduction alone is insufficient, switching to a lower-EPS-risk antipsychotic (quetiapine, clozapine) is the next step\
  若单纯减量效果不足，下一步是改用EPS风险更低的抗精神病药（喹硫平、氯氮平）

**Diagnosis:** Drug-induced parkinsonism is clinical — bradykinesia + rigidity + hypomimia + shuffling gait developing weeks after initiating or increasing a dopamine antagonist, with no prior parkinsonian history.

**诊断:** 药物性帕金森综合征为临床诊断——在启用或增加多巴胺拮抗剂数周后出现运动迟缓+强直+表情减少+拖曳步态，且无既往帕金森病史。

**Treatment:** Decrease or discontinue risperidone as first step; if needed, switch to quetiapine or clozapine; anticholinergics (benztropine, diphenhydramine) may transiently help acute EPS but are not first-line for subacute drug-induced parkinsonism.

**治疗:** 首先减少或停用利培酮；如需要，改用喹硫平或氯氮平；抗胆碱能药（苯甲托品、苯海拉明）可短暂缓解急性EPS，但不是亚急性药物性帕金森综合征的一线用药。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Addition of diphenhydramine<br />
A — 加用苯海拉明</td>
<td>Diphenhydramine (anticholinergic) is effective for acute dystonia and akathisia but offers only transient benefit for subacute drug-induced parkinsonism; it does not remove the underlying D2 blockade<br />
苯海拉明（抗胆碱能药）对急性肌张力障碍和静坐不能有效，但对亚急性药物性帕金森综合征只有短暂效益；不能消除根本的D2阻断</td>
<td>Anticholinergics are best for early-onset EPS (hours to days); subacute parkinsonism (weeks) requires dose reduction<br />
抗胆碱能药最适合早发型EPS（数小时至数天）；亚急性帕金森综合征（数周）需要减量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Addition of lithium carbonate<br />
B — 加用碳酸锂</td>
<td>Lithium treats active manic or bipolar episodes; this patient's current symptoms are entirely motor/autonomic EPS with no evidence of active psychosis or mania<br />
锂盐治疗活动性躁狂或双相发作；该患者当前症状完全是运动/自主神经EPS，无活动性精神病或躁狂证据</td>
<td>No active psychiatric decompensation — the problem is pharmacological side effects, not undertreated mood disorder<br />
无活动性精神科失代偿——问题是药物副作用，而非心境障碍控制不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cognitive behavioral therapy<br />
C — 认知行为治疗</td>
<td>CBT addresses psychological conditions (depression, anxiety, phobias); it has no mechanism to reverse dopamine receptor blockade or reduce motor EPS<br />
认知行为治疗针对心理问题（抑郁、焦虑、恐惧症）；对逆转多巴胺受体阻断或减少运动性EPS无效</td>
<td>The pathology is pharmacological (D2 blockade in nigrostriatal pathway), not psychological — behavioral interventions are irrelevant<br />
病理机制是药理性（黑质纹状体D2阻断），而非心理性——行为干预无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Decreasing the dosage of risperidone ✓<br />
D — 减少利培酮剂量 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — directly reduces nigrostriatal dopamine blockade, addressing the root cause of subacute drug-induced parkinsonism<br />
正确——直接减少黑质纹状体多巴胺阻断，解决亚急性药物性帕金森综合征的根本原因</td>
<td>Dose reduction targets the mechanism; cogwheel rigidity was already present 2 weeks ago and untreated, making dose reduction overdue<br />
减量针对机制；2周前齿轮样强直已存在但未处理，减量早已应当进行</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Increasing the dosage of clonazepam<br />
E — 增加氯硝西泮剂量</td>
<td>Benzodiazepines sedate and have GABA-ergic activity but do not antagonize D2 blockade or treat parkinsonian motor features<br />
苯二氮䓬类药物有镇静和GABA能活性，但不能拮抗D2阻断或治疗帕金森样运动特征</td>
<td>Clonazepam is already in the regimen for mood/seizure prophylaxis; escalating it adds sedation without addressing EPS<br />
氯硝西泮已在方案中用于情绪/癫痫预防；增量只加重镇静，不解决EPS</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Psychotherapy<br />
F — 心理治疗</td>
<td>Psychotherapy has no pharmacological mechanism to treat EPS; the patient's complaint is motor (gait, rigidity, masked facies), not psychological<br />
心理治疗无治疗EPS的药理机制；患者问题是运动性的（步态、强直、面具脸），而非心理性</td>
<td>Same reasoning as CBT — motor extrapyramidal side effects require pharmacological, not behavioral, management<br />
与认知行为治疗理由相同——运动性锥体外系副作用需要药理干预，而非行为管理</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice A (diphenhydramine) — students who know "anticholinergics treat EPS" often select it without distinguishing EPS type; the critical distinction is that anticholinergics work best for acute dystonia (onset: hours) while subacute drug-induced parkinsonism (onset: weeks) is best treated by reducing the offending drug.*

苯海拉明（选项A）是最大干扰项——知道"抗胆碱能药治疗EPS"的学生常在未区分EPS类型的情况下选择它；关键区别在于抗胆碱能药对急性肌张力障碍（数小时起病）效果最佳，而亚急性药物性帕金森综合征（数周起病）应首选减少致病药物。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Drug-Induced Parkinsonism vs. Idiopathic Parkinson's Disease / 药物性帕金森综合征 vs. 特发性帕金森病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Drug-Induced Parkinsonism</strong><br />
<strong>药物性帕金森综合征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Idiopathic Parkinson's Disease</strong><br />
<strong>特发性帕金森病</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Onset<br />
起病方式</td>
<td>Subacute — weeks after starting or increasing offending drug<br />
亚急性——启用或增加致病药物后数周</td>
<td>Insidious, progressive over years<br />
隐匿起病，多年内缓慢进展</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cause<br />
病因</td>
<td>D2 receptor blockade (antipsychotics, metoclopramide, prochlorperazine)<br />
D2受体阻断（抗精神病药、甲氧氯普胺、丙氯拉嗪）</td>
<td>Degeneration of dopaminergic neurons in substantia nigra (Lewy body pathology)<br />
黑质多巴胺能神经元变性（路易体病理）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symmetry<br />
对称性</td>
<td>Symmetric and bilateral from onset<br />
从起病即双侧对称</td>
<td>Asymmetric onset (unilateral tremor/rigidity initially)<br />
非对称起病（初期单侧震颤/强直）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Resting tremor<br />
静止性震颤</td>
<td>Less prominent or absent<br />
不明显或缺乏</td>
<td>Hallmark pill-rolling resting tremor<br />
标志性搓丸样静止性震颤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reversibility<br />
可逆性</td>
<td>Reversible upon dose reduction or drug discontinuation<br />
减量或停药后可逆</td>
<td>Progressive and irreversible<br />
进行性且不可逆</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Reduce/stop offending agent; switch to low-EPS antipsychotic (quetiapine, clozapine)<br />
减量/停用致病药物；改用低EPS风险药（喹硫平、氯氮平）</td>
<td>Levodopa/carbidopa, dopamine agonists (pramipexole), MAO-B inhibitors (selegiline)<br />
左旋多巴/卡比多巴，多巴胺激动剂（普拉克索），MAO-B抑制剂（司来吉兰）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a patient on maximum-dose risperidone develops masked facies, drooling, and shuffling gait (drug-induced parkinsonism), decrease the dose of the antipsychotic — this removes the nigrostriatal D2 blockade at the source.**

**当使用最大剂量利培酮的患者出现面具脸、流涎和拖曳步态（药物性帕金森综合征）时，应减少抗精神病药剂量——这可从源头消除黑质纹状体D2阻断。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — DAPT Timeline for Antipsychotic EPS / 记忆钩 — 抗精神病药EPS时间线 "DAPT":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>D</strong>ystonia — hours to days; treat with diphenhydramine or benztropine / 肌张力障碍——数小时至数天；苯海拉明或苯甲托品治疗<br />
• <strong>A</strong>kathisia — days to weeks; inner restlessness; treat with propranolol (first-line) / 静坐不能——数天至数周；内在坐立不安感；普萘洛尔一线治疗<br />
• <strong>P</strong>arkinsonism — weeks to months; shuffling gait + rigidity; treat by decreasing dose or switching agent / 帕金森综合征——数周至数月；拖曳步态+强直；减量或换药治疗<br />
• <strong>T</strong>ardive dyskinesia — months to years; orofacial choreoathetosis; treat with VMAT2 inhibitors; may be irreversible / 迟发性运动障碍——数月至数年；口面部手足徐动；VMAT2抑制剂治疗；可能不可逆</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Extrapyramidal Side Effects of Antipsychotics / 高频知识表 — 抗精神病药锥体外系副作用

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Highest EPS risk antipsychotics<br />
EPS风险最高的抗精神病药</td>
<td>First-generation (typical): haloperidol, fluphenazine, chlorpromazine; high D2 affinity proportionally increases nigrostriatal side effects<br />
第一代（典型）：氟哌啶醇、氟奋乃静、氯丙嗪；高D2亲和力成比例增加黑质纹状体副作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lowest EPS risk antipsychotics<br />
EPS风险最低的抗精神病药</td>
<td>Clozapine (lowest), quetiapine; low D2 affinity combined with high 5-HT2A antagonism confers EPS protection<br />
氯氮平（最低）、喹硫平；低D2亲和力联合高5-HT2A拮抗提供EPS保护</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute dystonia features and treatment<br />
急性肌张力障碍特征与治疗</td>
<td>Sustained involuntary muscle contractions (oculogyric crisis, torticollis, opisthotonus); onset hours after first dose; treat with IV/IM diphenhydramine or benztropine<br />
持续性不自主肌肉收缩（动眼危象、斜颈、角弓反张）；首次给药后数小时起病；静脉/肌注苯海拉明或苯甲托品治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Akathisia features and treatment<br />
静坐不能特征与治疗</td>
<td>Subjective sense of restlessness and compulsion to move; may be misinterpreted as anxiety; treat with propranolol (first-line) or low-dose benzodiazepines<br />
主观坐立不安感和运动冲动；可被误判为焦虑；普萘洛尔一线治疗或低剂量苯二氮䓬类</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tardive dyskinesia features and treatment<br />
迟发性运动障碍特征与治疗</td>
<td>Repetitive involuntary orofacial/limb movements (lip smacking, tongue protrusion, choreoathetosis) after months to years of antipsychotic use; treat with valbenazine or deutetrabenazine (VMAT2 inhibitors); may be irreversible<br />
使用抗精神病药数月至数年后出现重复性不自主口面部/肢体动作（吸唇、伸舌、手足徐动）；用缬苯那嗪或氘代丁苯那嗪（VMAT2抑制剂）治疗；可能不可逆</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neuroleptic malignant syndrome vs. drug-induced parkinsonism<br />
神经阻滞剂恶性综合征 vs. 药物性帕金森综合征</td>
<td>NMS: hyperthermia + "lead-pipe" rigidity + autonomic instability + altered consciousness; medical emergency — discontinue antipsychotic immediately, treat with dantrolene and bromocriptine; drug-induced parkinsonism lacks fever and autonomic crisis<br />
NMS：高热+"铅管样"强直+自主神经不稳定+意识改变；医疗急症——立即停用抗精神病药，丹曲林和溴隐亭治疗；药物性帕金森综合征无发热和自主神经危象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clozapine monitoring requirements<br />
氯氮平监测要求</td>
<td>Clozapine carries 1-2% risk of agranulocytosis — requires absolute neutrophil count (ANC) monitoring: weekly for first 6 months, then biweekly; hold if ANC &lt;1500/μL<br />
氯氮平有1-2%粒细胞缺乏症风险——需要绝对中性粒细胞计数（ANC）监测：前6个月每周，之后每两周；ANC &lt;1500/μL时停药</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Non-antipsychotic causes of drug-induced parkinsonism:** metoclopramide (a prokinetic antiemetic), prochlorperazine, and reserpine can all cause the same syndrome through nigrostriatal D2 blockade — always take a full medication history when evaluating parkinsonism\
  **非抗精神病药引起药物性帕金森综合征:** 甲氧氯普胺（促动力止吐药）、丙氯拉嗪和利血平均可通过黑质纹状体D2阻断引起相同综合征——评估帕金森综合征时务必完整采集用药史

- **Timing of anticholinergics vs. dose reduction:** Benztropine or diphenhydramine is appropriate acutely (dystonia, first 24–48 hours); for subacute drug-induced parkinsonism presenting over weeks, removing the offending stimulus (dose reduction or agent switch) is mechanistically superior and should be pursued first\
  **抗胆碱能药 vs. 减量的时机:** 苯甲托品或苯海拉明适用于急性情况（肌张力障碍，前24-48小时）；对数周内出现的亚急性药物性帕金森综合征，消除致病刺激（减量或换药）在机制上更优，应首先尝试

- **Schizoaffective disorder manic type management:** Requires dual coverage — antipsychotic for psychosis component and mood stabilizer for manic component; if risperidone must be reduced, optimizing valproic acid dosing or adding quetiapine (which also has mood-stabilizing properties) preserves psychiatric control\
  **精神分裂情感障碍躁狂型的管理:** 需要双重覆盖——抗精神病药控制精神症状，心境稳定剂控制躁狂；如需减少利培酮，优化丙戊酸剂量或加用喹硫平（也具有心境稳定作用）可维持精神症状控制

- **VMAT2 inhibitors for tardive dyskinesia:** Valbenazine (Ingrezza) and deutetrabenazine (Austedo) are FDA-approved for tardive dyskinesia; they deplete presynaptic dopamine stores rather than blocking receptors — a mechanistically distinct strategy from antipsychotic dose reduction\
  **VMAT2抑制剂治疗迟发性运动障碍:** 缬苯那嗪（Ingrezza）和氘代丁苯那嗪（Austedo）已获FDA批准用于迟发性运动障碍；它们耗竭突触前多巴胺储存而非阻断受体——与抗精神病药减量机制上截然不同的策略

# Question 73 — Hypercalcemia of Malignancy (PTHrP-Mediated) / 恶性肿瘤相关高钙血症（PTHrP 介导）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>67-year-old man</strong> with <strong>metastatic lung cancer</strong> comes to the physician because of <strong>malaise and lethargy</strong> during the past 3 days. Medications are ibuprofen and lisinopril. He appears cachectic but is oriented to person, place, and time. His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is <strong>102/min</strong>, respirations are 13/min, and blood pressure is <strong>105/75 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows <strong>decreased skin turgor</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 10.6 g/dL, Hematocrit 36%, Leukocyte count 11,100/mm³, Platelet count 226,000/mm³, Serum Na⁺ 136 mEq/L, K⁺ 3.6 mEq/L, Cl⁻ 96 mEq/L, HCO₃⁻ 28 mEq/L, <strong>Ca²⁺ 11.8 mg/dL</strong>, Urea nitrogen 22 mg/dL, Glucose 98 mg/dL, Creatinine 0.9 mg/dL, Phosphorus 2.5 mg/dL, <strong>Albumin 2.9 g/dL</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate initial pharmacotherapy?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate initial pharmacotherapy?</strong></p>
<p>A) Calcitonin<br />
B) Hydrocortisone<br />
C) Plicamycin<br />
D) 0.9% Saline<br />
E) Zoledronic acid</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Metastatic lung cancer<br />
转移性肺癌</td>
<td>Squamous cell lung cancer is the classic PTHrP-secreting tumor; PTHrP drives osteoclast-mediated hypercalcemia<br />
鳞状细胞肺癌是经典 PTHrP 分泌肿瘤；PTHrP 激活破骨细胞引起高钙血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ca²⁺ 11.8 + Albumin 2.9 g/dL<br />
钙 11.8 + 白蛋白 2.9</td>
<td>Corrected Ca = 11.8 + 0.8 × (4 − 2.9) ≈ 12.7 mg/dL; true hypercalcemia exceeds 12 mg/dL threshold requiring treatment<br />
校正钙约 12.7 mg/dL，超过需要治疗的 12 mg/dL 阈值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Malaise and lethargy<br />
乏力和嗜睡</td>
<td>Neuropsychiatric manifestations of hypercalcemia ("psychic moans"); confirm symptomatic disease requiring intervention<br />
高钙血症神经精神表现（"精神症状"），确认有症状的疾病需要干预</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Decreased skin turgor, HR 102, BP 105/75<br />
皮肤弹性降低、心率 102、血压 105/75</td>
<td>Signs of volume depletion; hypercalcemia causes DI-like polyuria → dehydration → decreased GFR → further Ca rise<br />
容量不足的体征；高钙血症致肾源性多尿→脱水→GFR 下降→钙进一步升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HCO₃⁻ 28 mEq/L<br />
碳酸氢根 28</td>
<td>Mild contraction alkalosis from volume depletion; further supports hypovolemia as the immediate problem<br />
容量收缩性轻度代谢性碱中毒，进一步支持血容量不足是最紧迫问题</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Phosphorus 2.5 mg/dL (low-normal)<br />
磷 2.5 mg/dL（偏低）</td>
<td>PTHrP promotes renal phosphate wasting; hypophosphatemia distinguishes PTHrP-mediated from other hypercalcemia causes<br />
PTHrP 促进肾脏排磷；低磷血症将 PTHrP 介导与其他高钙血症原因区分开</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Parathyroid hormone-related peptide (PTHrP)** secreted by malignant lung cells binds **PTH receptors** system-wide, producing effects that mimic **primary hyperparathyroidism** at far greater magnitude:

**甲状旁腺激素相关肽（PTHrP）**由恶性肺细胞分泌，全身结合 **PTH 受体**，产生的效应大规模模拟**原发性甲旁亢**：

- PTHrP activates osteoclasts via G-protein coupled receptors → massive bone resorption → Ca²⁺ floods into bloodstream\
  PTHrP 通过 G 蛋白偶联受体激活破骨细胞→大规模骨溶解→大量 Ca²⁺ 进入血液

- PTHrP increases renal tubular Ca²⁺ reabsorption → urinary Ca loss paradoxically reduced despite high serum Ca\
  PTHrP 增加肾小管 Ca²⁺ 重吸收→尽管血钙高，但尿钙排泄反常地减少

- Elevated Ca²⁺ impairs renal concentrating ability (nephrogenic DI-like) → polyuria → volume depletion → ↓ GFR → ↑ Ca²⁺ (vicious cycle that IV saline breaks)\
  高钙血症损害肾脏浓缩功能→多尿→容量不足→GFR 下降→钙进一步升高（IV 生理盐水打破此恶性循环）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The kidney is the only organ that acutely excretes calcium — restoring renal perfusion with IV saline is mechanistically the first intervention because it opens the only exit route for excess calcium.

**解剖小窍门:** 肾脏是唯一能急性排出钙的器官——用 IV 生理盐水恢复肾灌注在机制上是第一干预措施，因为它打开了多余钙的唯一出口。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Intravenous Normal Saline / 正确答案 (D) — 静脉输注生理盐水

**0.9% Saline (IV Normal Saline)** is the universal first step in symptomatic or severe hypercalcemia because it addresses the immediate hemodynamic crisis and enables calciuresis:

**0.9% 生理盐水（静脉注射）**是有症状或严重高钙血症的通用第一步，因为它解决即时的血流动力学危机并促进尿钙排泄：

- Expands intravascular volume → ↑ GFR → ↑ filtered Ca load → ↑ renal calcium excretion\
  扩充血容量→↑ GFR→↑ 滤过钙负荷→↑ 肾脏钙排泄

- Can acutely reduce serum calcium by 1–3 mg/dL through dilution and calciuresis\
  通过稀释和尿钙排泄可急性降低血清钙 1–3 mg/dL

- Provides safe hemodynamic foundation before adding calcitonin and bisphosphonates, which are nephrotoxic when given to dehydrated patients\
  在加用降钙素和双膦酸盐前提供安全的血流动力学基础，后两者给脱水患者时有肾毒性

**Diagnosis:** Hypercalcemia of malignancy (PTHrP-mediated); corrected Ca ≈ 12.7 mg/dL with neuropsychiatric symptoms (lethargy, malaise) and volume depletion (tachycardia, hypotension, decreased turgor) — treatment required.

**诊断:** 恶性肿瘤性高钙血症（PTHrP 介导）；校正钙约 12.7 mg/dL 伴神经精神症状（嗜睡、乏力）和容量不足（心动过速、低血压、皮肤弹性下降）——需要治疗。

**Treatment:** Step 1: IV 0.9% NS (200–500 mL/hr initially); Step 2: Calcitonin 4 IU/kg SC/IM q12h (fast onset, tachyphylaxis in 24–48h); Step 3: Zoledronic acid 4 mg IV over 15 min (durable, full effect in 2–4 days); treat underlying malignancy.

**治疗:** 第 1 步：IV 0.9% 生理盐水（初始 200–500 mL/hr）；第 2 步：降钙素 4 IU/kg SC/IM q12h（起效快，24–48h 快速抗药）；第 3 步：唑来膦酸 4 mg IV 15 分钟输注（持久，2–4 天完全起效）；治疗基础恶性肿瘤。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Calcitonin<br />
A — 降钙素</td>
<td>Useful adjunct but must follow IV fluid resuscitation; giving calcitonin first ignores volume depletion and risks worsening renal function<br />
有效辅助药物，但必须跟在 IV 补液之后；先用降钙素忽略了容量不足，有损害肾功能的风险</td>
<td>Onset is fast (4–6h) but tachyphylaxis develops in 24–48h; fluids address the more immediate hemodynamic problem<br />
起效快（4–6h）但 24–48h 后快速抗药；补液解决的是更紧迫的血流动力学问题</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Hydrocortisone<br />
B — 氢化可的松</td>
<td>Glucocorticoids reduce Ca only in lymphoma and vitamin D toxicity (blocks 1α-hydroxylase); has no mechanism of action against PTHrP-mediated hypercalcemia<br />
糖皮质激素只在淋巴瘤和维生素 D 中毒时降钙（抑制 1α-羟化酶）；对 PTHrP 介导的高钙血症无作用机制</td>
<td>Mechanism mismatch: PTHrP does not involve 1,25-dihydroxyvitamin D; steroids would be wrong choice regardless of severity<br />
机制不符：PTHrP 不涉及 1,25-二羟维生素 D；无论严重程度如何，激素都是错误选择</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Plicamycin<br />
C — 光辉霉素</td>
<td>RNA synthesis inhibitor that blocks osteoclasts and lowers Ca effectively but has severe dose-limiting toxicity: thrombocytopenia, hepatotoxicity, nephrotoxicity<br />
抑制 RNA 合成从而抑制破骨细胞，有效降钙但有严重剂量限制性毒性：血小板减少、肝毒性、肾毒性</td>
<td>Obsolete: superseded entirely by bisphosphonates; its presence here tests recognition of a historically relevant but abandoned agent<br />
已废弃：已被双膦酸盐完全取代；此选项考查对历史相关但已弃用药物的识别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — 0.9% Saline ✓<br />
D — 0.9% 生理盐水 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — First-line; restores intravascular volume, ↑ GFR, promotes calciuresis, and provides safe hemodynamic foundation for all subsequent Ca-lowering pharmacotherapy<br />
正确——一线治疗；恢复血容量、↑ GFR、促进尿钙排泄，为所有后续降钙药物治疗提供安全的血流动力学基础</td>
<td>Directly addresses both the hypovolemia and opens the renal excretion pathway for calcium; must always come first<br />
直接解决血容量不足并开放钙的肾脏排泄通道；必须永远第一步</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Zoledronic acid<br />
E — 唑来膦酸</td>
<td>Most potent bisphosphonate for malignancy hypercalcemia but requires 2–4 days for full effect; also nephrotoxic when infused before adequate hydration<br />
最强效的双膦酸盐用于恶性高钙血症，但需 2–4 天完全起效；在充分补液前输注还有肾毒性</td>
<td>Delayed onset makes it unsuitable as sole initial therapy; correct to use after fluids — but not before<br />
起效延迟使其不适合作为唯一初始治疗；正确做法是在补液后使用——但不能先于补液</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most common trap is choosing Calcitonin (A) because it rapidly lowers calcium — but the NBME specifically tests whether students recognize that volume resuscitation must precede all pharmacologic calcium-lowering agents.*

最常见的陷阱是选降钙素（A），因为它确实能快速降钙——但本题考点恰恰是识别容量复苏必须先于所有药物性降钙治疗。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In PTHrP-mediated hypercalcemia of malignancy with volume depletion, intravenous normal saline is always the first intervention — restore perfusion before any pharmacologic calcium-lowering agent.**

**PTHrP 介导的恶性肿瘤性高钙血症伴容量不足时，静脉生理盐水永远是第一干预——在任何药物降钙之前先恢复灌注。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "Saline → Calcitonin → Bisphosphonate" / 记忆钩 — "盐水→降钙素→双膦酸盐" 三步顺序:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>aline IV first — volume expansion opens the renal Ca excretion door / 盐水 IV 第一——扩容打开肾脏排钙的门<br />
• <strong>C</strong>alcitonin second — fast bridge (4–6h), but clock is ticking on tachyphylaxis / 降钙素第二——快速桥梁（4–6h），但快速抗药性在倒计时<br />
• <strong>B</strong>isphosphonate third — durable definitive control (2–4 days), requires hydration to be safe / 双膦酸盐第三——持久最终控制（2–4天），需要水化才安全<br />
• <strong>P</strong>ThrP mimic — acts like PTH: ↑ bone resorption, ↑ renal Ca reabsorption, ↓ phosphate / PTHrP 模拟——作用似 PTH：↑ 骨吸收、↑ 肾脏钙重吸收、↓ 磷酸盐</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Hypercalcemia of Malignancy / 高频知识表 — 恶性肿瘤性高钙血症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic PTHrP-secreting tumors<br />
经典 PTHrP 分泌肿瘤</td>
<td>Squamous cell lung cancer #1; also squamous cell of head/neck, breast cancer, renal cell carcinoma<br />
鳞状细胞肺癌第一；还有头颈部鳞癌、乳腺癌、肾细胞癌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Albumin-corrected calcium formula<br />
白蛋白校正钙公式</td>
<td>Corrected Ca = Measured Ca + 0.8 × (4 − albumin g/dL); this patient: 11.8 + 0.8 × 1.1 = 12.68 mg/dL<br />
校正钙 = 实测钙 + 0.8 × (4 − 白蛋白 g/dL)；本例：11.8 + 0.88 = 12.68 mg/dL</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypercalcemia symptoms mnemonic<br />
高钙血症症状记忆法</td>
<td>"Stones, Bones, Groans, Thrones, Psychic Moans": nephrolithiasis, bone pain, abdominal pain, polyuria/constipation, neuropsychiatric<br />
"石、骨、痛、尿、神"：肾结石、骨痛、腹痛、多尿/便秘、神经精神症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment threshold<br />
治疗阈值</td>
<td>Treat if symptomatic OR corrected Ca &gt; 12 mg/dL; mild asymptomatic (&lt;12 mg/dL) may be observed<br />
有症状或校正钙 &gt; 12 mg/dL 需治疗；轻度无症状（&lt; 12 mg/dL）可观察</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PTHrP vs. intact PTH labs<br />
PTHrP 与完整 PTH 实验室鉴别</td>
<td>Malignancy: PTHrP elevated, intact PTH suppressed (feedback), phosphate low; Primary hyperparathyroidism: intact PTH elevated, PTHrP undetectable<br />
恶性肿瘤：PTHrP 升高、完整 PTH 受负反馈抑制、磷偏低；原发性甲旁亢：完整 PTH 升高、PTHrP 检测不到</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why loop diuretics are no longer first-line<br />
为什么袢利尿剂不再是一线</td>
<td>Historical: furosemide was used to force calciuresis; modern evidence shows this worsens dehydration if given before adequate hydration; use only if volume overloaded<br />
历史上：呋塞米用于强制尿钙排泄；现代证据显示若在充分补液前使用会加重脱水；仅在容量超负荷时使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG finding in hypercalcemia<br />
高钙血症心电图表现</td>
<td>Shortened QT interval (hypercalcemia accelerates ventricular repolarization); inverse of QT prolongation seen in hypocalcemia<br />
QT 间期缩短（高钙血症加速心室复极）；与低钙血症 QT 延长相反</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Other mechanisms of malignancy hypercalcemia:** Osteolytic bone metastases (breast cancer, multiple myeloma release local osteoclast-activating cytokines); ectopic 1,25-dihydroxyvitamin D overproduction (lymphomas, granulomatous tissue); ectopic PTH secretion (very rare)\
  **恶性肿瘤高钙血症的其他机制:** 溶骨性骨转移（乳腺癌、多发性骨髓瘤释放局部破骨细胞活化细胞因子）；异位 1,25-二羟维生素 D 过度产生（淋巴瘤、肉芽肿组织）；异位 PTH 分泌（极罕见）

- **Glucocorticoid exception rule:** Hydrocortisone/prednisone effectively lowers calcium ONLY in lymphoma and vitamin D toxicity by blocking 1α-hydroxylase; absolutely no role in PTHrP-mediated hypercalcemia regardless of severity\
  **糖皮质激素例外规则:** 氢化可的松/泼尼松仅在淋巴瘤和维生素 D 中毒时有效，通过抑制 1α-羟化酶降钙；对 PTHrP 介导的高钙血症无论严重程度如何均无效

- **Denosumab as renal-sparing alternative:** RANK-L inhibitor that inhibits osteoclast differentiation; preferred over bisphosphonates when CrCl \< 30 mL/min because it does not require renal dose adjustment\
  **地诺单抗作为保肾替代方案:** RANK-L 抑制剂，抑制破骨细胞分化；当 CrCl \< 30 mL/min 时优于双膦酸盐，因为无需根据肾功能调整剂量

- **Ibuprofen caution in this patient:** NSAIDs impair renal prostaglandin synthesis → ↓ GFR → reduces the kidney's ability to excrete calcium; stopping ibuprofen is a supportive measure alongside IV saline\
  **本例使用布洛芬的注意事项:** NSAIDs 抑制肾脏前列腺素合成→↓ GFR→降低肾脏排钙能力；停用布洛芬是 IV 生理盐水之外的辅助措施

# Question 74 — Occult Hip Fracture in Corticosteroid-Induced Osteoporosis / 皮质类固醇诱发骨质疏松致隐匿性髋部骨折

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>47-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department because of <strong>severe left groin pain</strong> since <strong>he fell 2 hours ago</strong>. He is <strong>unable to walk</strong> because of the pain. He does not have pain in other joints. He has a <strong>20-year history of ulcerative colitis</strong>. His only medication is <strong>daily prednisone</strong>. On examination, any attempts at range of motion of the left hip <strong>elicit pain</strong>. Muscle strength is intact distally and in the right lower extremity. Distal pulses are 2+. An x-ray of the pelvis and left lower hip shows <strong>moderate loss of joint space</strong> and <strong>diffuse osteopenia</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Observation only<br />
B) DEXA scan<br />
C) MRI of the hip<br />
D) Nonsteroidal anti-inflammatory drug therapy<br />
E) Aspiration of the hip joint<br />
F) Total hip arthroplasty</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Daily prednisone (chronic corticosteroid use)<br />
长期每日口服泼尼松（慢性皮质类固醇使用）</td>
<td>Chronic corticosteroids suppress osteoblast function and stimulate osteoclast activity → bone loss → osteoporosis/osteopenia<br />
长期皮质类固醇抑制成骨细胞、激活破骨细胞 → 骨量丢失 → 骨质疏松/骨质减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>20-year history of ulcerative colitis<br />
20年溃疡性结肠炎病史</td>
<td>Chronic inflammatory disease is an independent risk factor for osteoporosis; combined with steroids, risk compounds significantly<br />
慢性炎症性疾病是骨质疏松的独立危险因素，与类固醇叠加后风险成倍增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fell 2 hours ago + unable to walk<br />
2小时前跌倒 + 无法行走</td>
<td>Low-energy trauma causing inability to ambulate in an osteopenic patient strongly suggests an occult fracture<br />
骨质减少患者因低能量外伤无法行走，强烈提示隐匿性骨折</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diffuse osteopenia on x-ray<br />
X线示弥漫性骨质减少</td>
<td>Osteopenia reduces radiodensity and can mask occult fractures on plain films — a negative x-ray does NOT rule out fracture<br />
骨质减少降低X线密度，可遮蔽隐匿性骨折——X线阴性不能排除骨折</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain with any range of motion of left hip<br />
左髋任何方向活动均引发疼痛</td>
<td>Diffuse pain on ROM suggests intra-articular or peri-articular pathology, consistent with fracture rather than soft tissue injury<br />
全方向活动时疼痛提示关节内或关节周围病变，符合骨折而非软组织损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Severe left groin pain<br />
严重左侧腹股沟疼痛</td>
<td>Groin pain is the classic presentation of hip pathology; femoral neck fractures characteristically cause groin and anterior thigh pain<br />
腹股沟痛是髋关节病变的经典表现；股骨颈骨折特征性地引起腹股沟和大腿前侧疼痛</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Corticosteroid-induced osteoporosis** leads to diffuse bone loss that impairs the structural integrity of trabecular and cortical bone, predisposing to **fragility fractures** even with minimal trauma:

**皮质类固醇诱发的骨质疏松**导致骨小梁和皮质骨弥漫性骨量丢失，即使轻微外伤也容易发生**脆性骨折**：

- Glucocorticoids inhibit osteoblast proliferation and differentiation → reduced bone formation\
  糖皮质激素抑制成骨细胞增殖与分化 → 骨形成减少

- Glucocorticoids increase osteoclast activity and lifespan → accelerated bone resorption\
  糖皮质激素增加破骨细胞活性与寿命 → 骨吸收加速

- Glucocorticoids decrease intestinal calcium absorption and increase renal calcium excretion → secondary hyperparathyroidism → further bone loss\
  糖皮质激素减少肠道钙吸收、增加肾脏钙排泄 → 继发性甲状旁腺功能亢进 → 进一步骨量丢失

- Diffuse osteopenia on plain x-ray reduces contrast needed to visualize subtle cortical breaks → occult fractures are missed on plain films\
  X线平片上的弥漫性骨质减少降低了显示细微皮质断裂所需的对比度 → 平片上隐匿性骨折被漏诊

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The femoral neck is the most vulnerable site for fragility fractures in osteoporosis because it is composed primarily of trabecular bone and bears high mechanical stress with ambulation.

**解剖小窍门:** 股骨颈是骨质疏松性脆性骨折最易发生的部位，因为它主要由松质骨构成且行走时承受较高的机械应力。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — MRI of the Hip / 正确答案 (C) — 髋关节MRI

**MRI of the hip** is the imaging modality of choice when an occult fracture is suspected but plain x-rays are non-diagnostic or equivocal due to underlying osteopenia:

**髋关节MRI** 是当怀疑隐匿性骨折而普通X线因基础骨质减少无法诊断或结果不确定时的首选影像学检查：

- MRI detects bone marrow edema (increased T2/STIR signal) at fracture sites that are invisible on plain x-ray\
  MRI可检测到普通X线上不可见的骨折部位骨髓水肿（T2/STIR信号增高）

- Sensitivity of MRI for occult hip fractures approaches 100%, far superior to plain x-ray (~50–80%)\
  MRI对隐匿性髋部骨折的灵敏度接近100%，远优于普通X线（约50–80%）

- CT is an acceptable alternative when MRI is unavailable or contraindicated (pacemaker, metallic implants), but delivers radiation without detecting marrow edema\
  CT在MRI不可用或禁忌时（起搏器、金属植入物）是可接受的替代方案，但有辐射且无法显示骨髓水肿

- If hip fracture is confirmed, urgent orthopedic consultation and surgical management are required\
  若确诊髋部骨折，需紧急骨科会诊并进行手术处理

**Diagnosis:** Occult hip fracture (likely femoral neck) in the setting of corticosteroid-induced osteoporosis; x-ray shows osteopenia and joint space loss but cannot exclude fracture — MRI is required to confirm.

**诊断:** 皮质类固醇诱发骨质疏松背景下的隐匿性髋部骨折（可能为股骨颈）；X线示骨质减少和关节间隙丢失但不能排除骨折——需行MRI确诊。

**Treatment:** Once fracture is confirmed: urgent orthopedic consultation; non-displaced fracture → ORIF; displaced femoral neck fracture → hemiarthroplasty or THA; address underlying osteoporosis with calcium, vitamin D, and bisphosphonates.

**治疗:** 骨折确诊后：紧急骨科会诊；无移位骨折→切开复位内固定；移位股骨颈骨折→半髋或全髋置换；同时治疗基础骨质疏松（钙剂、维生素D、双膦酸盐）。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Observation only<br />
A — 仅观察</td>
<td>Wrong — patient has severe pain, inability to walk, and high suspicion for fracture; observation delays diagnosis of a potential surgical emergency<br />
错误——患者剧烈疼痛、无法行走、高度怀疑骨折；观察会延误潜在手术急症的诊断</td>
<td>Inability to bear weight after trauma = fracture until proven otherwise<br />
外伤后无法负重 = 除外骨折前视为骨折</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — DEXA scan<br />
B — DEXA扫描</td>
<td>Wrong — DEXA measures bone mineral density for osteoporosis screening and monitoring; it does NOT diagnose acute fractures and is inappropriate in the acute trauma setting<br />
错误——DEXA测量骨密度用于骨质疏松筛查与监测；不能诊断急性骨折，急性外伤时不适用</td>
<td>DEXA = outpatient osteoporosis screening; MRI = acute occult fracture diagnosis<br />
DEXA = 门诊骨质疏松筛查；MRI = 急性隐匿性骨折诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — MRI of the hip ✓<br />
C — 髋关节MRI ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — gold standard for detecting occult hip fractures that are invisible on plain x-ray due to osteopenia; highest sensitivity approaching 100%<br />
正确——检测因骨质减少在X线上不可见的隐匿性髋部骨折的金标准；灵敏度最高，接近100%</td>
<td>Osteopenia + low-energy trauma + equivocal x-ray → MRI mandatory<br />
骨质减少 + 低能量外伤 + X线不明确 → 必须行MRI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — NSAID therapy<br />
D — 非甾体抗炎药治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — NSAIDs are appropriate for soft tissue injury (strain/sprain); this patient's traumatic hip pain with inability to walk in an osteopenic host is far more likely a fracture requiring surgery, not anti-inflammatory therapy<br />
错误——NSAIDs适用于软组织损伤（拉伤/扭伤）；骨质减少患者外伤性髋部疼痛且无法行走，骨折可能性远大于软组织损伤，需手术而非抗炎治疗</td>
<td>NSAIDs treat sprains; fractures require operative fixation<br />
NSAIDs治疗扭伤；骨折需手术固定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Aspiration of the hip joint<br />
E — 髋关节穿刺抽液</td>
<td>Wrong — joint aspiration is indicated for suspected septic arthritis; septic arthritis presents with atraumatic onset, fever, and elevated inflammatory markers; this patient has traumatic pain without systemic signs of infection<br />
错误——关节穿刺用于疑似化脓性关节炎；化脓性关节炎无外伤史、有发热和炎症指标升高；该患者为外伤性疼痛，无感染全身症状</td>
<td>Trauma history differentiates fracture from septic arthritis<br />
外伤史将骨折与化脓性关节炎区分开来</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Total hip arthroplasty<br />
F — 全髋关节置换</td>
<td>Wrong — THA may ultimately be indicated if a displaced femoral neck fracture is confirmed, but it is premature to proceed directly to surgery before imaging confirms the diagnosis and fracture pattern<br />
错误——若确认移位股骨颈骨折最终可能需要THA，但在影像学确认诊断和骨折类型之前直接手术为时过早</td>
<td>Diagnose first with MRI, then choose the appropriate surgical procedure<br />
先用MRI确诊，再选择相应手术方案</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice F (THA) — while surgery is likely necessary, jumping to arthroplasty without first confirming the fracture type (displaced vs. non-displaced) would lead to inappropriate management, as non-displaced fractures are treated with ORIF, not arthroplasty.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是选项F（全髋置换）——虽然手术很可能是必要的，但在影像学确认骨折类型（有移位/无移位）之前直接选择关节置换会导致不恰当的处理，因为无移位骨折应行内固定而非关节置换。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In an osteopenic patient with low-energy trauma and hip pain, a normal x-ray does NOT rule out an occult hip fracture — MRI of the hip is the mandatory next step.**

**骨质减少患者因低能量外伤出现髋部疼痛时，X线正常不能排除隐匿性髋部骨折——髋关节MRI是必须执行的下一步检查。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — STEROID Hip = Hidden Fracture / 记忆钩 — 类固醇髋关节 = 隐匿性骨折:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>teroids cause bone loss → osteoporosis risk / 类固醇致骨量丢失 → 骨质疏松风险<br />
• <strong>T</strong>rauma + inability to walk = suspect fracture / 外伤 + 无法行走 = 怀疑骨折<br />
• <strong>E</strong>quivocal x-ray in osteopenia ≠ rule out fracture / 骨质减少时X线不明确 ≠ 排除骨折<br />
• <strong>R</strong>each for MRI — highest sensitivity for occult fractures / 选择MRI——对隐匿性骨折灵敏度最高<br />
• <strong>O</strong>rthopedic surgery follows confirmed diagnosis / 确诊后再行骨科手术</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Corticosteroid-Induced Osteoporosis & Occult Fractures / 高频知识表 — 皮质类固醇性骨质疏松与隐匿性骨折

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism of steroid-induced bone loss<br />
类固醇致骨量丢失的机制</td>
<td>Inhibit osteoblasts, stimulate osteoclasts, reduce intestinal Ca absorption, increase renal Ca excretion → secondary hyperparathyroidism → further resorption<br />
抑制成骨细胞、激活破骨细胞、减少肠道钙吸收、增加肾脏钙排泄 → 继发性甲状旁腺功能亢进 → 进一步骨吸收</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DEXA scan T-score interpretation<br />
DEXA扫描T值判读</td>
<td>T-score ≥ −1.0: normal; −1.0 to −2.5: osteopenia; ≤ −2.5: osteoporosis; Z-score compares to age-matched peers (used in premenopausal women and men &lt;50)<br />
T值 ≥ −1.0：正常；−1.0至−2.5：骨质减少；≤ −2.5：骨质疏松；Z值与同年龄人群比较（用于绝经前女性和50岁以下男性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Occult fracture imaging algorithm<br />
隐匿性骨折影像学流程</td>
<td>X-ray first (fast, cheap); if negative but suspicion remains → MRI (gold standard); if MRI contraindicated → CT or technetium bone scan<br />
先行X线（快速、廉价）；若阴性但仍高度怀疑→MRI（金标准）；若MRI禁忌→CT或锝骨扫描</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common osteoporotic fracture sites<br />
骨质疏松性骨折最常见部位</td>
<td>Hip (proximal femur) &gt; vertebrae (compression fractures) &gt; distal radius (Colles' fracture) — "Hip, Spine, Wrist"<br />
髋部（股骨近端）&gt; 椎体（压缩性骨折）&gt; 桡骨远端（Colles骨折）——"髋、脊、腕"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prevention and treatment of steroid-induced osteoporosis<br />
类固醇性骨质疏松的预防与治疗</td>
<td>Any systemic steroid &gt;3 months: calcium + vitamin D; dose &gt;7.5 mg/day prednisone equivalent &gt;3 months: add bisphosphonate (alendronate first-line)<br />
任何全身类固醇使用&gt;3个月：补充钙剂+维生素D；泼尼松等效剂量&gt;7.5 mg/天且&gt;3个月：加用双膦酸盐（阿仑膦酸为一线）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bisphosphonate mechanism<br />
双膦酸盐机制</td>
<td>Bind to hydroxyapatite on bone surface → taken up by osteoclasts → induce osteoclast apoptosis → reduce bone resorption; reduce vertebral fracture risk ~50%, hip fracture risk ~25%<br />
与骨表面羟基磷灰石结合→被破骨细胞摄取→诱导破骨细胞凋亡→减少骨吸收；椎骨骨折风险降低约50%，髋部骨折风险降低约25%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Septic arthritis vs. occult hip fracture<br />
化脓性关节炎与隐匿性髋部骨折鉴别</td>
<td>Septic arthritis: atraumatic onset, fever, elevated WBC/ESR/CRP, aspiration yields purulent fluid; Hip fracture: traumatic mechanism, osteoporosis risk factors, pain on passive ROM, imaging confirms<br />
化脓性关节炎：无外伤、发热、WBC/ESR/CRP升高，穿刺见脓液；髋部骨折：外伤机制、骨质疏松危险因素、被动活动时疼痛、影像确认</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Surgical decision for hip fractures:** Non-displaced femoral neck fracture → ORIF (cannulated screws); displaced femoral neck fracture → hemiarthroplasty (low-demand elderly) or THA (active patients with pre-existing arthritis); intertrochanteric fracture → cephalomedullary nail\
  **髋部骨折手术决策:** 无移位股骨颈骨折→切开复位内固定（空心螺钉）；移位股骨颈骨折→半髋置换（低需求老年人）或全髋置换（有基础关节炎的活跃患者）；股骨粗隆间骨折→髓内钉固定

- **IBD and bone health:** Ulcerative colitis and Crohn's disease both increase osteoporosis risk through chronic inflammation (IL-6, TNF-α promote osteoclastogenesis), malabsorption of Ca/Vit D, and frequent steroid use; DEXA screening is recommended in IBD patients on long-term steroids\
  **炎症性肠病与骨健康:** 溃疡性结肠炎和克罗恩病均通过慢性炎症（IL-6、TNF-α促进破骨细胞生成）、Ca/维生素D吸收不良和频繁类固醇使用增加骨质疏松风险；建议长期使用类固醇的IBD患者行DEXA筛查

- **Avascular necrosis (AVN) as a mimic:** Chronic steroid use also causes AVN of the femoral head (disrupted blood supply → bone death); x-ray shows subchondral collapse ("crescent sign") in later stages; MRI detects early AVN before x-ray changes appear\
  **股骨头坏死（AVN）作为鉴别:** 长期类固醇使用还可导致股骨头坏死（血供中断→骨坏死）；X线晚期见软骨下塌陷（"新月征"）；MRI可在X线改变出现前检测早期AVN

- **Differential of acute hip pain:** Fracture (trauma + osteoporosis), AVN (steroid use, sickle cell), septic arthritis (fever + atraumatic), transient osteoporosis of pregnancy, slipped capital femoral epiphysis (obese adolescent), Perthes disease (child 4–8 years)\
  **急性髋部疼痛的鉴别:** 骨折（外伤+骨质疏松）、股骨头坏死（类固醇、镰刀细胞贫血）、化脓性关节炎（发热+无外伤）、妊娠一过性骨质疏松、股骨头骺滑脱（肥胖青少年）、Perthes病（4–8岁儿童）

# Question 75 — Wernicke-Korsakoff Syndrome / Wernicke-Korsakoff 综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>74-year-old woman</strong> is brought to the clinic by her family because of a <strong>7-month history of progressive confusion</strong> and <strong>urinary incontinence</strong>. During the past year, she has had <strong>multiple falls</strong>; she sustained wrist fractures 1 year ago and a left tibia fracture 3 months ago. She has hypertension, osteoporosis, and depression. She is <strong>evasive when asked how much alcohol she drinks</strong>. She appears frail. Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination shows a <strong>wide-based gait and marked ataxia</strong>. She is unable to attempt the Romberg test. Cranial nerve examination shows <strong>nystagmus and an inability to move her eyes horizontally</strong>. On cognitive testing, she recalls <strong>zero of three objects after 5 minutes</strong>. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 10 g/dL, <strong>Mean corpuscular volume 102 μm³</strong>, Serum Vitamin B12 (cobalamin) <strong>980 pg/mL (N=160–950)</strong>, Folate <strong>3.1 ng/mL (N=2.7–17)</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Folic acid deficiency<br />
B) Lewy body dementia<br />
C) Normal-pressure hydrocephalus<br />
D) Progressive supranuclear palsy<br />
E) Wernicke-Korsakoff syndrome</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Evasive about alcohol intake<br />
对饮酒量含糊其辞</td>
<td>Strongly implies alcohol use disorder — the #1 cause of thiamine deficiency in developed countries<br />
强烈提示酒精使用障碍——发达国家维生素 B1 缺乏的首要病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wide-based gait + marked ataxia<br />
宽基步态 + 明显共济失调</td>
<td>Reflects cerebellar vermis dysfunction from thiamine deficiency; classic Wernicke component<br />
反映小脑蚓部因维生素 B1 缺乏导致的功能损害；Wernicke 脑病经典表现之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nystagmus + inability to move eyes horizontally<br />
眼球震颤 + 水平注视麻痹</td>
<td>Lateral gaze palsy = ophthalmoplegia; completes the Wernicke triad (encephalopathy + ataxia + ophthalmoplegia)<br />
水平注视麻痹 = 眼肌麻痹；与意识混乱 + 共济失调共同构成 Wernicke 三联征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Recalls zero of three objects after 5 minutes<br />
5 分钟后三词回忆全部失败</td>
<td>Severe anterograde amnesia → Korsakoff component (irreversible if untreated)<br />
严重顺行性遗忘 → Korsakoff 成分（未治疗则不可逆）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCV 102 μm³ (macrocytosis)<br />
MCV 102 μm³（大细胞症）</td>
<td>Macrocytic anemia common in alcohol use disorder (direct marrow suppression + folate deficiency)<br />
酒精使用障碍常见大细胞性贫血（骨髓直接抑制 + 叶酸缺乏）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B12 normal/high (980 pg/mL); Folate low-normal (3.1 ng/mL)<br />
B12 正常偏高（980 pg/mL）；叶酸低正常值（3.1 ng/mL）</td>
<td>Rules out B12 and folate deficiency as the primary diagnosis; macrocytosis here is from alcohol toxicity<br />
排除 B12 和叶酸缺乏作为首要诊断；此处大细胞症来源于酒精毒性本身</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Confusion + urinary incontinence + gait instability triad<br />
意识混乱 + 尿失禁 + 步态不稳三联征</td>
<td>This triad also fits NPH — horizontal gaze palsy and nystagmus are the critical discriminators<br />
此三联征也符合正常压力脑积水——水平注视麻痹和眼球震颤是关键鉴别点</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Thiamine (Vitamin B1)** is an essential cofactor for **pyruvate dehydrogenase**, **alpha-ketoglutarate dehydrogenase**, and **transketolase** — all critical enzymes for cerebral energy metabolism via the Krebs cycle:

**硫胺素（维生素 B1）**是**丙酮酸脱氢酶**、**α-酮戊二酸脱氢酶**和**转酮酶**的必需辅因子——这些酶均通过三羧酸循环参与脑能量代谢：

- Thiamine deficiency → impaired oxidative glucose metabolism → selective neuronal injury in metabolically vulnerable brain regions\
  硫胺素缺乏 → 氧化葡萄糖代谢受损 → 对代谢高度依赖的脑区产生选择性神经元损伤

- Structures affected: mammillary bodies, medial thalami, periaqueductal gray matter, cerebellar vermis, CN VI nucleus and PPRF (horizontal gaze center)\
  受累结构：乳头体、丘脑内侧、中脑导水管周围灰质、小脑蚓部、CN VI 核及脑桥旁正中网状结构（水平注视中枢）

- Wernicke encephalopathy (acute, reversible with thiamine) → if untreated, progresses to Korsakoff syndrome (chronic, largely irreversible amnesia + confabulation)\
  Wernicke 脑病（急性，补充硫胺素可逆）→ 未治疗则进展为 Korsakoff 综合征（慢性遗忘症 + 虚构，基本不可逆）

- In alcoholism: poor nutritional intake + thiamine malabsorption + impaired cellular utilization → rapid depletion\
  酒精依赖中：营养摄入不足 + 硫胺素吸收障碍 + 细胞利用受损 → 储备迅速耗竭

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Lateral gaze palsy (CN VI nucleus + PPRF) + nystagmus localizes to brainstem/periaqueductal involvement; mammillary body atrophy on MRI is pathognomonic for WKS.

**解剖小窍门:** 水平注视麻痹（CN VI 核 + 脑桥旁正中网状结构）+ 眼球震颤定位于脑干/导水管周围病变；MRI 乳头体萎缩是 WKS 的特征性影像学表现。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Wernicke-Korsakoff Syndrome / 正确答案 (E) — Wernicke-Korsakoff 综合征

**Wernicke-Korsakoff Syndrome** is a two-stage thiamine deficiency disorder: an acute reversible phase (Wernicke encephalopathy) and a chronic irreversible phase (Korsakoff amnestic syndrome):

**Wernicke-Korsakoff 综合征**是分两个阶段的硫胺素缺乏症：急性可逆期（Wernicke 脑病）和慢性不可逆期（Korsakoff 遗忘综合征）：

- Wernicke triad: Encephalopathy (confusion) + Ataxia (cerebellar, wide-based) + Ophthalmoplegia (lateral gaze palsy, nystagmus) — all three present in this patient\
  Wernicke 三联征：脑病（意识混乱）+ 共济失调（小脑性，宽基步态）+ 眼肌麻痹（水平注视麻痹、眼球震颤）——本例三者均存在

- Korsakoff features: Anterograde \> retrograde amnesia, confabulation (unconscious fabrication of stories to fill memory gaps), preserved procedural memory\
  Korsakoff 特征：顺行性遗忘 \> 逆行性遗忘，虚构（无意识编造故事以填补记忆空白），程序性记忆保留

- Classic setting: alcohol use disorder; also hyperemesis gravidarum, bariatric surgery, prolonged TPN without supplementation\
  经典背景：酒精使用障碍；也见于妊娠剧吐、减重手术、长期无补充 TPN

**Diagnosis:** Clinical — based on classic triad + alcohol use context; MRI may show T2/FLAIR hyperintensity in mammillary bodies and periaqueductal gray matter

**诊断:** 临床诊断——基于经典三联征 + 酒精使用背景；MRI 可见乳头体及导水管周围灰质 T2/FLAIR 高信号

**Treatment:** Urgent IV/IM thiamine before any glucose (giving glucose first depletes remaining thiamine); high-dose thiamine 500 mg IV TID × 3 days, then oral maintenance; Korsakoff amnesia has poor reversibility

**治疗:** 在给予任何葡萄糖之前立即静脉/肌肉注射硫胺素（先给葡萄糖会耗尽剩余硫胺素）；硫胺素 500 mg 静脉注射 每日三次 × 3 天，随后口服维持；Korsakoff 遗忘症可逆性差

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Folic acid deficiency<br />
A — 叶酸缺乏</td>
<td>Folate is 3.1 ng/mL (within normal range 2.7–17); folate deficiency causes megaloblastic anemia and neuropsychiatric symptoms but NOT ophthalmoplegia or lateral gaze palsy<br />
叶酸 3.1 ng/mL（正常范围 2.7–17 内）；叶酸缺乏引起巨幼细胞性贫血和神经精神症状，但不引起眼肌麻痹或水平注视麻痹</td>
<td>No oculomotor findings in folate deficiency; cannot explain the full clinical picture<br />
叶酸缺乏无眼球运动异常；无法解释完整临床表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Lewy body dementia<br />
B — Lewy 体痴呆</td>
<td>Requires fluctuating cognition, parkinsonism (rigidity, bradykinesia), visual hallucinations, and REM sleep behavior disorder — none present here<br />
需要认知波动、帕金森体征（强直、运动迟缓）、视幻觉和 REM 睡眠行为障碍——本例均无</td>
<td>Lateral gaze palsy and nystagmus are not features of Lewy body dementia<br />
水平注视麻痹和眼球震颤不是 Lewy 体痴呆的特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Normal-pressure hydrocephalus<br />
C — 正常压力脑积水</td>
<td>Classic triad (dementia + incontinence + gait instability) overlaps — but NPH does NOT cause ophthalmoplegia or nystagmus; gait in NPH is "magnetic" (shuffling), not ataxic<br />
经典三联征（痴呆 + 尿失禁 + 步态不稳）重叠——但 NPH 不引起眼肌麻痹或眼球震颤；NPH 步态是"磁性"（拖曳），非共济失调</td>
<td>Horizontal gaze palsy and nystagmus are the pivot discriminators against NPH<br />
水平注视麻痹和眼球震颤是排除 NPH 的枢纽鉴别点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Progressive supranuclear palsy<br />
D — 进行性核上性麻痹</td>
<td>PSP causes VERTICAL gaze palsy (especially downgaze), NOT horizontal; plus axial rigidity, frequent backward falls, frontal lobe dysfunction — different pattern entirely<br />
PSP 引起垂直注视麻痹（尤其向下），而非水平；加上轴向强直、频繁向后跌倒、额叶功能障碍——完全不同的模式</td>
<td>Horizontal (not vertical) gaze palsy + nystagmus + alcohol context → WKS, not PSP<br />
水平（非垂直）注视麻痹 + 眼球震颤 + 酒精背景 → WKS，非 PSP</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Wernicke-Korsakoff syndrome ✓<br />
E — Wernicke-Korsakoff 综合征 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — alcoholic patient with complete Wernicke triad (encephalopathy + ataxia + horizontal gaze palsy/nystagmus) and severe anterograde amnesia (0/3 recall) indicating Korsakoff component<br />
正确——酒精患者具备完整 Wernicke 三联征（脑病 + 共济失调 + 水平注视麻痹/眼球震颤）及严重顺行性遗忘（0/3 回忆）提示 Korsakoff 成分</td>
<td>Full classic triad + alcohol use disorder + anterograde amnesia = WKS<br />
完整经典三联征 + 酒精使用障碍 + 顺行性遗忘 = WKS</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is C (NPH), which shares the dementia + urinary incontinence + gait instability triad — the lateral gaze palsy and nystagmus are the exclusive pivot clues pointing to Wernicke encephalopathy over NPH.*

最易误选的干扰项是 C（正常压力脑积水），因其同样有痴呆 + 尿失禁 + 步态不稳三联征——水平注视麻痹和眼球震颤是唯一指向 Wernicke 脑病而非 NPH 的枢纽线索。

<strong>正常压力脑积水</strong></th>
