MRI：乳头体萎缩，导水管周围 T2 信号</td>
<td>CT/MRI: enlarged ventricles; normal LP opening pressure<br />
CT/MRI：脑室扩大；腰穿开放压正常</td>
<td>MRI: midbrain atrophy ("hummingbird sign")<br />
MRI：中脑萎缩（"蜂鸟征"）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reversibility<br />
可逆性</td>
<td>Wernicke: yes with thiamine; Korsakoff: mostly irreversible<br />
Wernicke：补硫胺素可逆；Korsakoff：基本不可逆</td>
<td>Partially reversible with VP shunt<br />
VP 分流后部分可逆</td>
<td>Progressive, no disease-modifying treatment<br />
进行性，无疾病修饰治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic etiology<br />
典型病因</td>
<td>Alcohol use disorder (thiamine deficiency)<br />
酒精使用障碍（硫胺素缺乏）</td>
<td>Idiopathic; prior meningitis or subarachnoid hemorrhage<br />
特发性；既往脑膜炎或蛛网膜下腔出血</td>
<td>Neurodegenerative tauopathy<br />
神经退行性 tau 蛋白病</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An alcoholic patient presenting with the triad of encephalopathy, ataxia, and horizontal gaze palsy/nystagmus has Wernicke-Korsakoff syndrome — give IV thiamine immediately, before any glucose.**

**酒精依赖患者出现脑病、共济失调和水平注视麻痹/眼球震颤三联征，诊断为 Wernicke-Korsakoff 综合征——立即静脉给予硫胺素，且须在任何葡萄糖之前。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — Wernicke's "AOE" Triad / 记忆钩 — Wernicke "AOE" 三联征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>taxia — wide-based gait, cerebellar vermis dysfunction / 共济失调——宽基步态，小脑蚓部功能障碍<br />
• <strong>O</strong>phthalmoplegia — horizontal gaze palsy + nystagmus (CN VI nucleus + PPRF) / 眼肌麻痹——水平注视麻痹 + 眼球震颤（CN VI 核 + 脑桥旁正中网状结构）<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ncephalopathy — confusion, anterograde amnesia → Korsakoff if untreated / 脑病——意识混乱，顺行性遗忘 → 未治疗则进展为 Korsakoff</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Wernicke-Korsakoff Syndrome & Thiamine Deficiency / 高频知识表 — Wernicke-Korsakoff 综合征与硫胺素缺乏

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Thiamine-dependent enzymes<br />
硫胺素依赖酶</td>
<td>Pyruvate dehydrogenase, alpha-ketoglutarate dehydrogenase, transketolase; deficiency → impaired Krebs cycle → neuronal energy failure in vulnerable regions<br />
丙酮酸脱氢酶、α-酮戊二酸脱氢酶、转酮酶；缺乏 → 三羧酸循环受损 → 高代谢需求脑区神经元能量衰竭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wernicke triad prevalence<br />
Wernicke 三联征的出现率</td>
<td>All three features present in only ~16% of cases; treat empirically with thiamine if alcohol use + any one feature of the triad is present<br />
三者同时出现仅约 16%；酒精使用者出现三联征任一特征即经验性给予硫胺素治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Korsakoff syndrome features<br />
Korsakoff 综合征特征</td>
<td>Anterograde &gt; retrograde amnesia; confabulation (unconscious, not deliberate lying); preserved procedural memory; poor prognosis even with thiamine<br />
顺行性遗忘 &gt; 逆行性遗忘；虚构（无意识，非故意撒谎）；程序性记忆保留；即使补充硫胺素预后仍差</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Glucose before thiamine hazard<br />
葡萄糖先于硫胺素的危害</td>
<td>Administering glucose to a thiamine-depleted patient exhausts remaining thiamine reserves → can precipitate or acutely worsen Wernicke encephalopathy<br />
给硫胺素耗竭患者葡萄糖会耗尽剩余储备 → 可诱发或急性加重 Wernicke 脑病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MRI findings<br />
MRI 表现</td>
<td>T2/FLAIR hyperintensity and atrophy of mammillary bodies (most specific), medial thalami, periaqueductal gray matter; enhancement may be present acutely<br />
T2/FLAIR 高信号及乳头体萎缩（最特异）、丘脑内侧、导水管周围灰质；急性期可有强化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Macrocytic anemia in alcoholism<br />
酒精依赖中的大细胞性贫血</td>
<td>Direct toxic effect of alcohol on bone marrow (most common cause of macrocytosis in alcoholics); + folate deficiency from poor nutrition; B12 is often normal or elevated<br />
酒精对骨髓的直接毒性（酒精患者大细胞症最常见原因）；+ 营养不良导致叶酸缺乏；B12 常正常甚至升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Non-alcoholic causes of thiamine deficiency<br />
非酒精性硫胺素缺乏病因</td>
<td>Hyperemesis gravidarum, bariatric surgery (malabsorption), prolonged TPN without supplementation, anorexia nervosa, refeeding syndrome<br />
妊娠剧吐、减重手术（吸收不良）、长期无补充 TPN、神经性厌食、再喂养综合征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Thiamine dosing protocol:** High-dose IV thiamine (500 mg TID × 3 days) is recommended for suspected WKS; oral thiamine is inadequate in alcoholics due to impaired gastrointestinal absorption\
  **硫胺素给药方案:** 疑似 WKS 推荐大剂量静脉硫胺素（500 mg 每日三次 × 3 天）；口服硫胺素因胃肠吸收受损对酒精患者效果不足

- **Confabulation distinction:** Korsakoff confabulation is unconscious gap-filling, not intentional deception — patients genuinely believe their fabricated memories; preserved insight is absent\
  **虚构的区别:** Korsakoff 虚构是无意识的记忆填补，非故意欺骗——患者真诚相信自己编造的记忆；自知力缺失

- **Prophylaxis in high-risk patients:** All patients with chronic heavy alcohol use should receive routine thiamine supplementation; empiric parenteral thiamine should be given at any ED/clinic presentation of acute intoxication or poor nutrition\
  **高危患者预防:** 所有慢性重度饮酒者均应常规补充硫胺素；急诊/门诊出现急性中毒或营养不良时应经验性给予肠外硫胺素

- **Differential of horizontal gaze palsy:** Wernicke encephalopathy (CN VI nucleus + PPRF), brainstem stroke (AICA/PICA territory), multiple sclerosis (internuclear ophthalmoplegia), Miller Fisher syndrome (GBS variant with ataxia + areflexia + ophthalmoplegia)\
  **水平注视麻痹鉴别:** Wernicke 脑病（CN VI 核 + 脑桥旁正中网状结构）、脑干卒中（AICA/PICA 供血区）、多发性硬化（核间性眼肌麻痹）、Miller Fisher 综合征（GBS 变异型，伴共济失调 + 腱反射消失 + 眼肌麻痹）

# Question 76 — Pain-Induced Hypertension in Opioid-Tolerant Postoperative Patient / 阿片耐受术后患者疼痛性高血压

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Eight days</strong> after he was involved in a motor vehicle collision in which he was the restrained driver, a hospitalized <strong>28-year-old man</strong> has <strong>hypertension</strong>. He underwent extensive reconstructive orthopaedic operations for injuries to his left clavicle, shoulder, and femur and exploratory laparotomy for a ruptured spleen. Urine toxicology screening on admission was positive for <strong>Δ9-tetrahydrocannabinol, cocaine, and opiates</strong>. He was intubated and mechanically ventilated during the procedures and was extubated on hospital day 4. He receives oral acetaminophen-oxycodone as needed. His <strong>blood pressure has been 180/110 mm Hg</strong>; it <strong>decreases to 150/80 mm Hg when he receives his pain medication</strong>. An abdominal bandage covers the surgical incision. The nurse tells the physician that the patient <strong>rates his pain as a 10 on a 10-point scale</strong> and is <strong>constantly asking for pain medications</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in pharmacotherapy for this patient's hypertension?</strong></p>
<p>A) Continued administration of acetaminophen-oxycodone every 4 hours<br />
B) Continuous intravenous labetalol infusion with titration<br />
C) Intravenous nitroprusside therapy<br />
D) Patient-controlled morphine<br />
E) Switching from acetaminophen-oxycodone to tramadol</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Urine toxicology positive for opiates on admission<br />
入院时尿毒理学阿片类阳性</td>
<td>Prior opiate use → opioid tolerance established → standard doses are subtherapeutic<br />
既往阿片类使用→已建立阿片耐受→标准剂量效果不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP decreases to 150/80 when pain medication given<br />
使用镇痛药后血压降至 150/80</td>
<td>Directly proves pain is driving hypertension, not primary or renovascular HTN<br />
直接证明疼痛是高血压的驱动因素，而非原发性或肾血管性高血压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain rated 10/10, constantly asking for medications<br />
疼痛评分 10/10，不断要求用药</td>
<td>Current PRN oral opioid regimen is failing to control pain<br />
当前按需口服阿片类方案无法控制疼痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Oral acetaminophen-oxycodone as needed (PRN)<br />
按需口服对乙酰氨基酚-羟考酮</td>
<td>PRN dosing creates peak-trough fluctuations; inadequate for high-burden pain in tolerant patients<br />
按需给药产生峰谷波动；对耐受患者的高负荷疼痛不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Extensive reconstructive orthopaedic surgery + laparotomy<br />
大范围骨科重建手术 + 剖腹探查</td>
<td>Multiple surgical sites produce exceptionally high postoperative pain burden<br />
多处手术部位产生极高的术后疼痛负荷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eight days postoperative, still hospitalized<br />
术后第 8 天，仍住院</td>
<td>Significant acute postoperative pain is expected to persist at this stage<br />
此阶段预期会持续存在显著的急性术后疼痛</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Inadequate pain control** activates the **sympathetic nervous system**, causing catecholamine-mediated hypertension that resolves when analgesia is achieved:

**镇痛不足**激活**交感神经系统**，引起儿茶酚胺介导的高血压，镇痛实现后即缓解：

- Nociceptive stimuli → hypothalamic-pituitary-adrenal axis activation → **catecholamine and cortisol** release\
  伤害性刺激→下丘脑-垂体-肾上腺轴激活→**儿茶酚胺和皮质醇**释放

- Catecholamines → **α1-adrenergic vasoconstriction** → ↑SVR → ↑BP; also ↑HR via β1 stimulation\
  儿茶酚胺→**α1肾上腺素能血管收缩**→↑体循环血管阻力→↑血压；同时通过β1刺激↑心率

- In **opioid-tolerant** patients, standard oral opioid doses produce subtherapeutic analgesia → pain persists → sympathetic activation is sustained\
  在**阿片耐受**患者中，标准口服阿片剂量镇痛效果不足→疼痛持续→交感神经激活持续

- **IV PCA (patient-controlled analgesia)** delivers on-demand boluses of parenteral opioid with lockout intervals, maintaining therapeutic plasma levels that oral dosing cannot achieve in tolerant patients\
  **静脉PCA（患者自控镇痛）**按需给予肠外阿片类冲击剂量，设有锁定间隔，维持耐受患者口服给药无法达到的治疗血药浓度

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The pain-sympathetic-HTN axis means that in postoperative patients, always verify whether BP spikes temporally correlate with pain peaks before adding antihypertensives — if they do, treat the pain first.

**解剖小窍门:** 疼痛-交感-高血压轴意味着，在术后患者中，加用降压药前务必核实血压升高是否与疼痛高峰时间相关——若相关，应先治疗疼痛。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Patient-Controlled Analgesia / 正确答案 (D) — 患者自控镇痛

**Patient-controlled analgesia (PCA)** is a pain delivery system that allows patients to self-administer small IV opioid boluses within preset safety parameters:

**患者自控镇痛（PCA）**是一种疼痛给药系统，允许患者在预设安全参数范围内自行给予少量静脉阿片类冲击剂量：

- Programmable pump delivers morphine IV bolus on button press; **lockout interval** (e.g., 6–10 min) prevents dose stacking\
  可编程泵在按键时给予静脉吗啡冲击剂量；**锁定间隔**（如6–10分钟）防止剂量叠加

- Provides **steady-state analgesia** superior to PRN oral opioids, particularly for opioid-tolerant patients requiring higher effective doses\
  提供**稳态镇痛**，优于按需口服阿片类，尤其适用于需要更高有效剂量的阿片耐受患者

- Addresses the **root cause** of this patient's hypertension (inadequate pain control) rather than masking it with antihypertensives\
  针对该患者高血压的**根本原因**（镇痛不足），而非用降压药掩盖

- Total PCA opioid consumption data informs calculation of equianalgesic oral doses for eventual transition at discharge\
  PCA总阿片消耗量数据有助于计算出院时过渡的等镇痛口服剂量

**Diagnosis:** Hypertension secondary to undertreated pain in an opioid-tolerant patient; confirmed by BP improvement following opioid administration.

**诊断:** 阿片耐受患者镇痛不足所致继发性高血压；阿片类药物给药后血压改善证实此诊断。

**Treatment:** IV PCA morphine bypasses GI absorption variability, delivers parenteral opioid at doses sufficient for tolerance, and empowers the patient to maintain analgesia continuously.

**治疗:** 静脉PCA吗啡绕过胃肠道吸收变异性，以足以克服耐受的剂量肠外给予阿片类药物，并使患者能够持续维持镇痛。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Continued acetaminophen-oxycodone every 4 hours<br />
A — 每4小时继续给予对乙酰氨基酚-羟考酮</td>
<td>Current oral PRN opioids are already failing; switching to scheduled q4h still does not address opioid tolerance or provide adequate plasma levels<br />
当前口服按需阿片类已失败；改为每4小时定时给药仍无法解决阿片耐受或提供足够血药浓度</td>
<td>Oral route + fixed dose cannot match IV PCA in a tolerant patient with severe pain<br />
口服途径+固定剂量无法与严重疼痛耐受患者的静脉PCA相比</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Continuous IV labetalol infusion<br />
B — 持续静脉拉贝洛尔输注</td>
<td>Treats the symptom (BP) not the cause (pain); leaves pain untreated → prolonged recovery, patient dissatisfaction, risk of complications<br />
治疗症状（血压）而非病因（疼痛）；疼痛仍未处理→延迟康复、患者不满、并发症风险</td>
<td>Pain is confirmed as the driver (BP responds to opioids); antihypertensives are inappropriate as first-line here<br />
疼痛已被确认为驱动因素（阿片类药物改善血压）；降压药在此不适合作为一线治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Intravenous nitroprusside therapy<br />
C — 静脉硝普钠治疗</td>
<td>Nitroprusside is reserved for hypertensive emergencies with end-organ damage; 180/110 without encephalopathy or dissection is a hypertensive urgency, not emergency<br />
硝普钠用于伴靶器官损害的高血压急症；无脑病或夹层的180/110是高血压紧迫症，而非急症</td>
<td>No evidence of end-organ damage; pain-targeted therapy is safer and addresses the underlying cause<br />
无靶器官损害证据；针对疼痛的治疗更安全且针对根本病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Patient-controlled morphine ✓<br />
D — 患者自控吗啡 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — IV PCA overcomes opioid tolerance, provides superior steady-state analgesia, and treats the identified cause of hypertension<br />
正确——静脉PCA克服阿片耐受，提供更优的稳态镇痛，并治疗已确认的高血压病因</td>
<td>BP improves with opioids = pain is the driver; IV PCA is the appropriate escalation for a tolerant patient failing oral opioids<br />
阿片类药物改善血压=疼痛是驱动因素；对于口服阿片类失败的耐受患者，静脉PCA是适当的升级方案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Switch to tramadol<br />
E — 换用曲马多</td>
<td>Tramadol is weaker than oxycodone (lower analgesic ceiling); switching would worsen pain control and therefore worsen hypertension<br />
曲马多弱于羟考酮（镇痛天花板更低）；换药会加重镇痛效果不足，从而加重高血压</td>
<td>Never downgrade opioid potency in an undertreated patient; tramadol also carries seizure risk and serotonin syndrome potential<br />
在镇痛不足患者中切勿降级阿片效能；曲马多还有癫痫风险和血清素综合征潜在风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Choice A — scheduled oral oxycodone feels like an upgrade from PRN, but it still fails the opioid-tolerant patient who needs IV delivery to achieve therapeutic plasma levels.*

选项 A 是最具迷惑性的干扰项——定时口服羟考酮看起来比按需给药更好，但对于需要静脉给药才能达到治疗血药浓度的阿片耐受患者，仍然不够。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — PRN Oral Opioids vs. IV Patient-Controlled Analgesia / 按需口服阿片类 vs. 静脉患者自控镇痛

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>PRN Oral Opioids</strong><br />
<strong>按需口服阿片类</strong></th>
<th><strong>IV PCA</strong><br />
<strong>静脉患者自控镇痛</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Route<br />
给药途径</td>
<td>Oral; requires intact GI function and absorption<br />
口服；需要完整胃肠道功能和吸收</td>
<td>Intravenous; direct systemic delivery, no first-pass effect<br />
静脉；直接全身给药，无首过效应</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Onset of action<br />
起效时间</td>
<td>30–60 minutes<br />
30–60 分钟</td>
<td>5–15 minutes<br />
5–15 分钟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Plasma level pattern<br />
血药浓度模式</td>
<td>Peak-trough fluctuations; pain recurs between doses<br />
峰谷波动；剂量间疼痛复发</td>
<td>Near-steady-state with on-demand supplementation<br />
接近稳态，按需补充</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Opioid-tolerant patients<br />
阿片耐受患者</td>
<td>Often inadequate; higher oral doses carry GI/sedation risks<br />
常不足；较高口服剂量存在胃肠道/镇静风险</td>
<td>Preferred; lockout + max dose allows higher bolus levels safely<br />
首选；锁定间隔+最大剂量允许更高冲击剂量，安全性可控</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patient autonomy<br />
患者自主性</td>
<td>Dependent on nurse availability and scheduling delays<br />
依赖护士可及性和排班延迟</td>
<td>Patient controls timing; reduces anxiety, improves satisfaction<br />
患者控制时机；减少焦虑，提高满意度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Overdose protection<br />
过量保护</td>
<td>Fixed dose per administration<br />
每次给药固定剂量</td>
<td>Lockout interval + hourly maximum dose programmed into pump<br />
泵内编程锁定间隔+每小时最大剂量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Transition planning value<br />
过渡计划价值</td>
<td>Limited data on actual opioid requirement<br />
实际阿片需求量数据有限</td>
<td>Total consumption calculates equianalgesic oral regimen for discharge<br />
总消耗量计算出院等镇痛口服方案</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When postoperative hypertension responds to opioid administration, the cause is undertreated pain — escalate to IV PCA, especially in opioid-tolerant patients who fail oral regimens.**

**当术后高血压对阿片类药物给药有反应，病因是镇痛不足——升级为静脉PCA，尤其对于口服方案失败的阿片耐受患者。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PAIN drives BP / 记忆钩 — 疼痛驱动血压:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>rior opioid use → tolerance → standard doses subtherapeutic / 既往阿片类使用→耐受→标准剂量效果不足<br />
• <strong>A</strong>nalgesic response = proof that pain is the BP driver / 镇痛有效=证明疼痛是血压驱动因素<br />
• <strong>I</strong>V PCA overcomes tolerance, maintains steady-state analgesia / 静脉PCA克服耐受，维持稳态镇痛<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ever treat with antihypertensives before treating the pain cause / 在治疗疼痛病因之前切勿用降压药治疗</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — PCA, Opioid Tolerance, and Postoperative Hypertension / 高频知识表 — PCA、阿片耐受与术后高血压

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>PCA mechanism and safety<br />
PCA 机制与安全性</td>
<td>Programmable pump delivers IV opioid bolus on patient demand; lockout interval (6–10 min) prevents dose stacking; hourly maximum dose caps total exposure; naloxone must be bedside<br />
可编程泵按患者需求给予静脉阿片类冲击剂量；锁定间隔（6–10分钟）防止剂量叠加；每小时最大剂量限制总暴露量；纳洛酮必须备于床旁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Opioid tolerance<br />
阿片耐受</td>
<td>Reduced analgesic effect from same dose due to prior chronic exposure; requires higher doses for equivalent analgesia; cross-tolerance exists among opioid agonists; abrupt cessation causes withdrawal<br />
既往长期暴露导致相同剂量镇痛效果减弱；需要更高剂量达到等效镇痛；阿片激动剂之间存在交叉耐受；突然停药引起戒断症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain-induced secondary hypertension<br />
疼痛诱发继发性高血压</td>
<td>SNS activation → catecholamine surge → ↑HR + ↑SVR → ↑BP; resolves with analgesia; key clue is BP improvement after opioid administration; adding antihypertensives without treating pain is inappropriate<br />
交感神经系统激活→儿茶酚胺激增→↑心率+↑体循环血管阻力→↑血压；镇痛后缓解；关键线索是阿片给药后血压改善；不治疗疼痛而加用降压药是不恰当的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypertensive urgency vs. emergency<br />
高血压紧迫症 vs. 急症</td>
<td>Urgency: BP ≥180/110 without end-organ damage → oral agents or treat underlying cause; Emergency: BP ≥180/120 with encephalopathy, ACS, aortic dissection → IV nitroprusside or labetalol<br />
紧迫症：BP≥180/110无靶器官损害→口服药物或治疗潜在病因；急症：BP≥180/120伴脑病、ACS、主动脉夹层→静脉硝普钠或拉贝洛尔</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tramadol limitations<br />
曲马多局限性</td>
<td>Weak μ-opioid agonist + SNRI; lower analgesic ceiling than oxycodone; lowers seizure threshold; serotonin syndrome risk with SSRIs/SNRIs/MAOIs; not appropriate for acute severe or escalating pain<br />
弱μ阿片激动剂+SNRI；镇痛天花板低于羟考酮；降低癫痫阈值；与SSRIs/SNRIs/MAOIs联用有血清素综合征风险；不适用于急性重度或升级性疼痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Multimodal analgesia perioperatively<br />
围手术期多模式镇痛</td>
<td>Combines acetaminophen, NSAIDs (if not contraindicated), regional nerve blocks, and opioids; reduces total opioid requirement; preferred strategy especially for opioid-tolerant patients<br />
结合对乙酰氨基酚、NSAIDs（如无禁忌）、区域神经阻滞和阿片类药物；减少总阿片需求量；首选策略，尤其对阿片耐受患者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PCA to oral transition<br />
PCA 过渡至口服</td>
<td>Sum total IV morphine consumed per 24 hours via PCA → convert to oral morphine equivalent (IV:oral = 1:3) → prescribe 50–75% of equianalgesic dose as long-acting oral opioid with short-acting breakthrough<br />
统计PCA每24小时静脉吗啡总消耗量→换算为口服吗啡等效剂量（静脉:口服=1:3）→以50–75%等镇痛剂量处方长效口服阿片类药物+短效突破剂量</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Opioid equianalgesic dosing:** Morphine IV is the reference (1 mg IV = 3 mg oral); oxycodone oral is ~1.5× morphine oral potency; fentanyl IV is ~100× morphine IV — miscalculating equivalences causes under- or overdosing when switching agents\
  **阿片等镇痛剂量:** 静脉吗啡为参考（1 mg静脉=3 mg口服）；口服羟考酮效力约为口服吗啡的1.5倍；静脉芬太尼效力约为静脉吗啡的100倍——换药时等效剂量计算错误会导致剂量不足或过量

- **Differential of postoperative hypertension:** Pain (most common) → urinary retention → anxiety → medication effect (vasopressor wean, NSAID discontinuation) → pre-existing primary HTN → autonomic dysreflexia (cervical/thoracic SCI) — always check pain score and bladder before adding antihypertensives\
  **术后高血压鉴别:** 疼痛（最常见）→尿潴留→焦虑→药物效应（升压药撤停、NSAIDs停用）→既往原发性高血压→自主神经反射异常（颈/胸段脊髓损伤）——加用降压药前务必检查疼痛评分和膀胱状态

- **Substance use context here:** Admission urine toxicology positive for opiates, cocaine, and THC; prior opiate use is the critical tolerance factor; cocaine abstinence during hospitalization may itself contribute to catecholamine dysregulation, compounding pain-driven HTN\
  **本题物质使用背景:** 入院尿毒理学阿片类、可卡因和THC阳性；既往阿片类使用是关键耐受因素；住院期间可卡因戒断本身可能导致儿茶酚胺失调，加重疼痛驱动的高血压

- **When antihypertensives ARE appropriate postoperatively:** Once adequate analgesia is confirmed and BP remains elevated → suspect pre-existing HTN or renal/renovascular etiology → begin oral amlodipine or lisinopril; IV labetalol/hydralazine reserved for true hypertensive urgency/emergency\
  **术后确实需要降压药的情况:** 确认充分镇痛后血压仍然升高→怀疑既往高血压或肾/肾血管性病因→开始口服氨氯地平或赖诺普利；静脉拉贝洛尔/肼屈嗪仅用于真正的高血压紧迫症/急症

# Question 77 — Patient Autonomy and Decisional Capacity / 患者自主权与决策能力

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>37-year-old primigravid woman</strong> at <strong>16 weeks' gestation</strong> comes to the physician to discuss the results of amniocentesis. She has an <strong>IQ of 70</strong>. She is <strong>employed as a housekeeping assistant</strong> in a hotel and has been <strong>married</strong> to a coworker for 6 months. She has no family history of serious illness. Karyotype analysis of the fetus showed <strong>trisomy 21</strong>. Her pregnancy has been otherwise uncomplicated. She is informed of the abnormalities associated with the fetal genotype and <strong>still wants to continue the pregnancy</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Schedule the patient for ongoing prenatal care<br />
B) Discuss the situation with the patient's husband<br />
C) Try to convince the patient to change her decision<br />
D) Seek a court-appointed guardian<br />
E) Refer the patient for psychiatric evaluation to determine competence</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>IQ of 70<br />
智商 70</td>
<td>Low IQ alone does not equal intellectual disability by DSM-5; adaptive functioning must be assessed<br />
低智商本身不等于 DSM-5 定义的智力残疾，必须评估适应功能</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Employed as housekeeping assistant<br />
担任客房服务助理</td>
<td>Demonstrates functional independence in daily life, supporting preserved capacity<br />
体现日常生活中的功能独立性，支持其决策能力完整</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Married to a coworker for 6 months<br />
与同事结婚 6 个月</td>
<td>Evidence of intact social adaptive skills and autonomous life decisions<br />
体现社交适应能力及自主生活决策能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Informed of fetal trisomy 21 abnormalities<br />
已被告知胎儿 21 三体异常</td>
<td>Confirms she received and can process the relevant medical information<br />
确认她已接收并能处理相关医疗信息</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Still wants to continue the pregnancy<br />
仍希望继续妊娠</td>
<td>Expresses a clear, consistent choice — a key criterion of decisional capacity<br />
表达明确、一贯的选择——决策能力的核心标准之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No psychiatric disorder or acute illness<br />
无精神疾病或急性病史</td>
<td>Removes the primary clinical indications for questioning capacity<br />
排除质疑决策能力的主要临床依据</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Decisional capacity** is a clinical, decision-specific assessment of whether a patient can make a particular informed medical decision at a given moment:

**决策能力**是临床性、决策特异性的评估，判断患者在特定时刻是否能就某一具体医疗决策做出知情选择：

- Patient must understand the diagnosis and the proposed intervention\
  患者须能理解诊断及所提议的干预措施

- Patient must appreciate how the information applies to their own personal situation\
  患者须能认识到信息对其自身处境的意义

- Patient must reason through options and weigh their consequences\
  患者须能对各选项及其后果进行逻辑推理

- Patient must communicate a clear, consistent choice\
  患者须能表达清晰、前后一致的选择

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** DSM-5 replaced IQ cutoffs as the criterion for intellectual disability with impairment in adaptive functioning across conceptual, social, and practical domains — and even among those with confirmed intellectual disability, capacity must be assessed case-by-case.

**解剖小窍门:** DSM-5 以概念、社交和实际三个适应功能领域的损害取代了智商截断值作为智力残疾诊断标准——即使对已确诊智力残疾的患者，决策能力也必须逐案评估。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Respect Preserved Decisional Capacity / 正确答案 (A) — 尊重保留的决策能力

**Patient autonomy** requires that physicians respect the informed decisions of individuals who demonstrate decisional capacity, regardless of IQ or perceived intellectual limitations:

**患者自主权**要求医生尊重具备决策能力的个体的知情决定，无论其智商或表面的智识局限：

- She understands that her fetus has trisomy 21 and knows the associated complications\
  她理解胎儿患有 21 三体综合征及相关并发症

- She has expressed a clear, consistent preference to continue the pregnancy after being informed\
  在被告知后，她明确、一贯地表达了继续妊娠的意愿

- Her employment, marriage, and daily functioning demonstrate intact adaptive capacity\
  其就业状况、婚姻关系和日常功能均证明其具备完整的适应能力

**Diagnosis:** This patient demonstrates decisional capacity; no further evaluation or override of her decision is warranted.

**诊断:** 该患者具备决策能力，无需对其决定进行进一步评估或推翻。

**Treatment:** Schedule for routine ongoing prenatal care in accordance with her expressed, informed preference.

**治疗:** 按其表达的知情意愿，安排常规持续产前保健。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Schedule the patient for ongoing prenatal care ✓<br />
A — 安排持续产前保健 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Patient has decisional capacity and has made an informed choice; her autonomy must be respected<br />
正确——患者具备决策能力且做出知情选择，必须尊重其自主权</td>
<td>Capacity, not IQ, determines right to self-determination<br />
决策能力而非智商决定自主决定权</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Discuss the situation with the patient's husband<br />
B — 与患者丈夫讨论情况</td>
<td>Violates patient confidentiality and bypasses her autonomy; husband input is only relevant if she lacks capacity<br />
违反保密原则并绕开患者自主权；仅在患者缺乏决策能力时配偶意见才相关</td>
<td>Patient is the decision-maker, not the spouse<br />
患者是决策者，而非配偶</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Try to convince the patient to change her decision<br />
C — 说服患者改变决定</td>
<td>Paternalistic and inappropriate; undermines the patient-physician relationship and violates patient autonomy<br />
家长式行为，不当；破坏医患关系并违反患者自主权</td>
<td>Physician informs, not coerces<br />
医生提供信息，而非施压强迫</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Seek a court-appointed guardian<br />
D — 申请法院指定监护人</td>
<td>No evidence of incapacity; court guardianship is reserved for individuals legally deemed incompetent<br />
无决策能力丧失证据；法院监护权仅适用于法院认定无行为能力的个体</td>
<td>Guardianship requires judicial finding of incompetency<br />
监护权须经司法认定无行为能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Refer the patient for psychiatric evaluation to determine competence<br />
E — 转介精神科评估法律行为能力</td>
<td>Capacity is clinical and decision-specific (any physician may assess); competency is a legal determination made by a judge, not a psychiatrist<br />
决策能力是临床且决策特异性评估（任何医生可完成）；法律行为能力由法官认定，而非精神科医生</td>
<td>Capacity ≠ competency; no psychiatric indication here<br />
决策能力≠法律行为能力；此处无精神科转介指征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice E — examinees confuse "decisional capacity" (clinical, reversible, decision-specific, assessed by any physician) with "legal competency" (global, determined by a court judge, not a psychiatrist).*

最危险的干扰项是选项 E——考生常混淆"决策能力"（临床性、可逆、决策特异性，任何医生可评估）与"法律行为能力"（全局性，由法院法官认定，而非精神科医生）。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Decisional Capacity vs. Legal Competency / 决策能力 vs. 法律行为能力

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />

<th><strong>Decisional Capacity</strong><br />

<strong>法律行为能力</strong></th>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Who assesses<br />
评估者</td>
<td>Any physician<br />
任何医生</td>

法官（法院）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Scope<br />
范围</td>
<td>Decision-specific<br />
决策特异性</td>
<td>Global (all decisions)<br />
全局性（所有决策）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Timing<br />
时效性</td>
<td>Can fluctuate moment to moment<br />
可随时间波动</td>
<td>Static, legally binding determination<br />
静态、具法律约束力的认定</td>

<tr>

评估依据</td>

临床访谈：UARC 四标准</td>

</tr>

智商的作用</td>
<td>Not determinative; DSM-5 uses adaptive functioning<br />

单独亦非决定性因素</td>

<tr>
<td>Who can override<br />
谁可推翻</td>
<td>Physician, if patient loses capacity<br />
医生，若患者丧失决策能力</td>
<td>Court judgment only<br />
仅法院判决</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient with IQ 70 who is employed, married, understands her fetus has trisomy 21, and consistently chooses to continue her pregnancy has preserved decisional capacity and must be scheduled for ongoing prenatal care.**

**一名智商 70、有工作、已婚、理解胎儿患有 21 三体且始终选择继续妊娠的患者具备完整的决策能力，必须为其安排持续产前保健。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — UARC: The 4 Pillars of Decisional Capacity / 记忆钩 — UARC：决策能力四大支柱:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>U</strong>nderstanding — Can the patient state what the diagnosis and options mean? / 理解——患者能否陈述诊断和选项的含义？<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ppreciation — Does the patient recognize how this applies to their own personal situation? / 认识——患者能否认识到决策对自身处境的意义？<br />
• <strong>R</strong>easoning — Can the patient weigh the pros and cons of each option? / 推理——患者能否权衡各选项的利弊？<br />
• <strong>C</strong>hoice — Does the patient express a clear, consistent decision? / 选择——患者能否表达清晰、前后一致的决定？</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Decisional Capacity and Medical Ethics / 高频知识表 — 决策能力与医学伦理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 criteria for intellectual disability<br />
DSM-5 智力残疾诊断标准</td>
<td>Replaced IQ cutoffs with deficits in adaptive functioning across conceptual, social, and practical domains; IQ 70 alone is insufficient for diagnosis<br />
以概念、社交和实际领域的适应功能缺陷取代智商截断值；智商 70 本身不足以诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Four elements of decisional capacity (UARC)<br />
决策能力四要素（UARC）</td>
<td>Understanding, Appreciation, Reasoning, Choice — all four must be present; any physician may assess<br />
理解、认识、推理、选择——四项均需具备；任何医生均可评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Capacity is decision-specific<br />
决策能力具有决策特异性</td>
<td>A patient may have capacity for simple decisions but not complex ones; fluctuates with medical state<br />
患者对简单决策可能具备能力，对复杂决策则可能不具备；随病情波动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When to formally question capacity<br />
何时正式质疑决策能力</td>
<td>Acute delirium, active psychosis, severe depression with psychotic features, advanced dementia, or acute intoxication — NOT IQ alone<br />
急性谵妄、活动性精神病、伴精神病性特征的严重抑郁、晚期痴呆或急性中毒——而非单凭智商</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surrogate decision-making<br />
代理决策</td>
<td>Only invoked when capacity is absent; hierarchy: healthcare proxy → spouse → adult children → parents → siblings<br />
仅在患者缺乏决策能力时启用；层级：医疗代理人→配偶→成年子女→父母→兄弟姐妹</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Physician's duty and paternalism<br />
医生职责与家长主义</td>
<td>Physician must inform and support autonomous choice; attempting to coerce or override without evidence of incapacity is an ethical violation<br />
医生须提供信息并支持自主选择；在无决策能力丧失证据的情况下强迫或推翻属于伦理违规</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of capacity impairment:** Delirium (acute, fluctuating), dementia (progressive), acute psychosis, severe mood disorder with psychotic features, or substance intoxication — none present here\
  **决策能力受损的鉴别:** 谵妄（急性、波动性）、痴呆（进行性）、急性精神病、伴精神病性特征的严重情感障碍或物质中毒——本题患者均不符合

- **Key complication:** Paternalism — overriding an autonomous decision without evidence of incapacity constitutes a medical ethics violation and damages the therapeutic relationship\
  **关键并发症:** 家长主义——在无决策能力丧失证据的情况下推翻自主决定，构成医学伦理违规并损害治疗关系

- **Variant:** If this patient had acute delirium or active psychosis, formal capacity assessment and surrogate involvement would then be appropriate; competency determination would still require a court\
  **题目变式:** 若患者出现急性谵妄或活动性精神病，则适合进行正式决策能力评估并纳入代理决策者；法律行为能力认定仍须经法院

- **Mnemonic:** "Capacity → Clinician; Competency → Court" — capacity is assessed bedside by any physician; competency is a judicial determination and cannot be assigned by a psychiatrist\
  **记忆口诀:** "决策能力→临床医生；法律行为能力→法院"——决策能力由任何医生在床旁评估；法律行为能力是司法认定，精神科医生无权赋予

# Question 78 — Chronic Osteomyelitis with Draining Sinus Tract / 慢性骨髓炎伴窦道

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>29-year-old male US Navy veteran</strong> comes to the local Veterans Affairs clinic because of a <strong>2-week history of purulent drainage</strong> from a small opening at the site of <strong>amputation of his left arm</strong>. For the past <strong>10 days</strong>, he has had increasing pain, tenderness, and redness at the wound site. <strong>Thirteen months ago</strong>, the patient sustained a traumatic amputation of the left arm below the elbow when an <strong>improvised explosive device</strong> detonated while he was on a combat mission in the Middle East. Management at that time consisted of <strong>aggressive surgical debridement</strong> of the residual limb, which has healed slowly; <strong>a small part of the wound appeared to heal incompletely</strong>. The patient appears well. Vital signs are within normal limits. Examination of the left upper extremity shows a <strong>3-mm opening in the scar</strong> with surrounding erythema; the site is <strong>draining purulent material</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Which of the following studies is most likely to confirm the diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following studies is most likely to confirm the diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bone biopsy of the wound site<br />
B) Complete blood count with differential<br />
C) Erythrocyte sedimentation rate and serum C-reactive protein concentration<br />
D) X-ray of the left upper extremity residual limb</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>13 months after traumatic amputation with incomplete wound healing<br />
截肢13个月后伤口愈合不完全</td>
<td>Prolonged incomplete healing after a contaminated war wound strongly suggests occult bone infection seeded at the time of injury<br />
战创伤后伤口长期愈合不全，高度提示受伤时骨骼已被细菌种植，形成隐匿性感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Small opening in scar draining purulent material<br />
瘢痕处小开口持续流脓</td>
<td>Classic presentation of a draining sinus tract, the hallmark of chronic osteomyelitis<br />
引流窦道是慢性骨髓炎的标志性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2-week purulent drainage + 10 days of pain/redness<br />
2周流脓 + 10天疼痛/红肿</td>
<td>Subacute-to-chronic timeline; not a fulminant acute infection — suggests indolent bone infection with periodic exacerbation<br />
亚急性至慢性时间线，非暴发性急性感染，提示隐匿性骨感染周期性加重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vital signs normal, patient appears well<br />
生命体征正常，患者一般情况良好</td>
<td>Absence of systemic illness is characteristic of chronic osteomyelitis; distinguishes it from acute hematogenous osteomyelitis<br />
无全身性疾病表现是慢性骨髓炎的特征，与急性血源性骨髓炎相鉴别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>IED blast injury requiring aggressive surgical debridement<br />
IED爆炸伤需要积极手术清创</td>
<td>Blast injuries introduce soil/foreign material directly into bone; polymicrobial contamination is common in combat wounds<br />
爆炸伤将污染物直接引入骨骼，战伤中多微生物感染常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-mm sinus opening at amputation stump<br />
截肢残端3毫米窦道开口</td>
<td>A sinus tract communicating with underlying bone is virtually pathognomonic for an osteomyelitis focus beneath<br />
与深部骨骼相通的窦道几乎是下方骨髓炎病灶的特征性表现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Chronic osteomyelitis** develops when bacteria become embedded in **necrotic bone (sequestrum)** at the time of injury and persist despite initial surgical debridement:

**慢性骨髓炎**是指细菌在损伤时植入**坏死骨组织（死骨片）**，尽管经过初步手术清创后仍持续存在：

- Blast injury directly inoculates bone with skin flora and environmental organisms (S. aureus, gram-negative rods, anaerobes)\
  爆炸伤将皮肤菌群及环境微生物（金黄色葡萄球菌、革兰阴性杆菌、厌氧菌）直接种植入骨

- Devitalized bone (sequestrum) forms an avascular niche where bacteria are shielded from immune cells and systemic antibiotics\
  死骨片形成无血管微环境，细菌在此处免受免疫细胞和全身抗生素的攻击

- Surrounding reactive periosteal bone (involucrum) forms but cannot fully contain or eliminate the infection\
  周围反应性骨膜新骨（包壳骨）形成，但无法完全包裹或消灭感染

- Sinus tract develops as pus follows the path of least resistance through soft tissue to the skin surface\
  脓液沿阻力最小路径穿透软组织至皮肤表面，形成窦道

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** A sinus tract that communicates with underlying bone virtually always indicates osteomyelitis until proven otherwise — the tract itself is the single most important diagnostic clue in this case.

**解剖小窍门:** 与深部骨骼相通的窦道，在排除其他可能性之前几乎必然提示骨髓炎——本题中窦道本身就是最重要的诊断线索。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Bone Biopsy / 正确答案 (A) — 骨活检

**Bone biopsy** is the gold standard for confirming chronic osteomyelitis and identifying the causative organism for targeted therapy:

**骨活检**是确诊慢性骨髓炎并鉴定致病微生物以指导针对性治疗的金标准：

- Provides histopathologic confirmation of infection (neutrophilic infiltrate, necrotic bone with empty lacunae)\
  提供感染的组织病理学确认（中性粒细胞浸润、含空陷窝的坏死骨）

- Culture of bone tissue identifies the causative organism with far greater accuracy than surface sinus tract cultures, which grow colonizing flora\
  骨组织培养鉴定致病菌的准确性远高于表面窦道培养（后者培养出的是定植菌群）

- Antibiotic susceptibility testing from bone culture enables targeted, organism-specific therapy rather than empiric broad-spectrum coverage\
  骨培养药敏试验使针对性抗生素治疗成为可能，而非单纯经验性广谱覆盖

**Diagnosis:** Chronic osteomyelitis requires histopathologic evidence of bone infection combined with positive culture from bone tissue — biopsy simultaneously provides both the confirmatory diagnosis and the microbiological roadmap for treatment.

**诊断:** 慢性骨髓炎的诊断需要骨感染的组织病理学证据以及骨组织阳性培养——活检可同时提供确诊依据和指导治疗的微生物学信息。

**Treatment:** Surgical debridement (sequestrectomy, removal of all necrotic bone and infected tissue) combined with prolonged antibiotic therapy (typically 4–6 weeks IV followed by oral) guided by bone culture sensitivities.

**治疗:** 手术清创（死骨切除，去除所有坏死骨和感染组织），结合根据骨培养药敏结果指导的长期抗生素治疗（通常静脉给药4–6周后续以口服）。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Bone biopsy of the wound site ✓<br />
A — 伤口部位骨活检 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Histologically confirms osteomyelitis AND cultures the causative organism to guide antibiotic selection<br />
正确——组织学确诊骨髓炎，同时培养致病菌以指导抗生素选择</td>
<td>Gold standard: simultaneously confirms diagnosis and guides targeted treatment<br />
金标准：同时确诊并指导针对性治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Complete blood count with differential<br />
B — 全血细胞计数+分类</td>
<td>Leukocytosis with left shift supports infection but is nonspecific; chronic osteomyelitis often shows minimal or absent leukocytosis given its indolent course<br />
白细胞增多伴核左移支持感染，但无特异性；慢性骨髓炎因其隐匿病程常见白细胞升高不明显甚至正常</td>
<td>CBC supports infection broadly but cannot confirm bone involvement<br />
CBC仅广泛支持感染，无法确认骨骼受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Erythrocyte sedimentation rate and serum C-reactive protein concentration<br />
C — 红细胞沉降率和血清C反应蛋白</td>
<td>Both elevated in osteomyelitis but are nonspecific inflammatory markers; they are best used to monitor treatment response (should normalize with successful therapy), not to confirm diagnosis<br />
两者在骨髓炎中升高，但属非特异性炎症标志物；最适合监测治疗反应（成功治疗后应恢复正常），而非确诊</td>
<td>Useful for monitoring disease activity and treatment efficacy, but lack diagnostic specificity for osteomyelitis<br />
用于监测疾病活动度和治疗效果，但对骨髓炎缺乏诊断特异性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — X-ray of the left upper extremity residual limb<br />
D — 左上肢残端X线片</td>
<td>X-ray may show periosteal reaction, cortical destruction, or lytic lesions in chronic osteomyelitis, but these changes appear late and require 30–50% bone mineral loss to become visible; normal X-ray cannot rule out osteomyelitis<br />
X线可显示骨膜反应、皮质破坏或溶骨病变，但这些改变出现晚，需30–50%骨矿物质丢失才可见；正常X线无法排除骨髓炎</td>
<td>Suggestive but not confirmatory; too insensitive and too late to confirm or exclude<br />
可提示但无法确诊；敏感性低且改变出现太晚，不足以确诊或排除</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (ESR/CRP) — these markers are expected to be elevated and are part of the standard osteomyelitis workup, but their role is monitoring treatment response, not confirming the diagnosis; that distinction is the core teaching point of this question.*

选项C（ESR/CRP）是最具迷惑性的干扰项——这两项标志物在骨髓炎中确实升高，也是标准检查流程的一部分，但其作用是监测治疗反应而非确诊；这一区别正是本题的核心考点。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Acute vs. Chronic Osteomyelitis / 急性骨髓炎 vs. 慢性骨髓炎

<tr>
<td>Timeline<br />
时间线</td>

数月至数年；隐匿、缓慢起病</td>

<tr>

全身症状</td>

发热、寒战、白细胞增多常见</td>

</tr>
<tr>

病理特征</td>

早期通常正常；软组织肿胀</td>

最佳确诊检查</td>

MRI（早期最敏感）+ 骨活检</td>

骨活检培养——组织学 + 微生物鉴定 + 药敏试验</td>
</tr>

<td>S. aureus (most common); Salmonella in sickle cell disease<br />
金黄色葡萄球菌（最常见）；镰状细胞病中沙门菌</td>
<td>S. aureus; polymicrobial in traumatic/combat wounds<br />
金黄色葡萄球菌；创伤/战伤中多微生物感染</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A draining sinus tract at a traumatic amputation site months after injury = chronic osteomyelitis; bone biopsy is the only test that both confirms the diagnosis histologically and identifies the causative organism for targeted antibiotic therapy.**

**创伤性截肢部位伤后数月出现引流窦道 = 慢性骨髓炎；骨活检是唯一能同时提供组织学确诊依据并鉴定致病菌以指导针对性抗生素治疗的检查手段。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CHRONIC" Osteomyelitis / 记忆钩 — 慢性骨髓炎"CHRONIC"要点:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ulture via bone biopsy — the only test to confirm AND guide therapy / 活检培养——唯一既能确诊又能指导治疗的检查<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ealing incomplete → sinus tract forms to drain pus to skin / 愈合不完全→形成窦道将脓引流至皮肤<br />
• <strong>R</strong>eactive involucrum surrounds avascular sequestrum / 包壳骨包绕无血管死骨片<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ld injury or seeding event is always the inciting cause / 旧伤或种植事件始终是诱发原因<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ormal vitals and well-appearing patient — indolent by definition / 生命体征正常、患者一般情况良好——本质上是隐匿性病程<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nflammatory markers (ESR/CRP) elevated but nonspecific — for monitoring, not diagnosis / 炎症标志物升高但无特异性——用于监测而非确诊<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ortical destruction on X-ray is a late sign requiring 30–50% bone loss / X线皮质破坏是需30–50%骨质丢失才显现的晚期征象</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Osteomyelitis Workup & Management / 高频知识表 — 骨髓炎检查与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard for diagnosis<br />
诊断金标准</td>
<td>Bone biopsy with culture: histology shows PMNs + necrotic bone; culture identifies organism + susceptibilities; both needed together<br />
骨活检培养：组织学见中性粒细胞 + 坏死骨；培养鉴定微生物 + 药敏；两者缺一不可</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why sinus tract wound cultures are unreliable<br />
窦道伤口培养不可靠的原因</td>
<td>Surface cultures grow skin colonizers, not the deep bone pathogen; the correlate rate between sinus cultures and bone cultures is only ~44%<br />
表面培养出定植于皮肤的菌群，而非深部骨组织病原体；窦道培养与骨培养的一致率仅约44%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MRI vs. X-ray in osteomyelitis<br />
MRI与X线在骨髓炎中的比较</td>
<td>MRI most sensitive (detects marrow edema within 3–5 days); X-ray requires 30–50% bone mineral loss to show changes (appears 10–21 days after onset)<br />
MRI最敏感（3–5天内即可检测骨髓水肿）；X线需30–50%骨矿物质丢失才显示改变（起病后10–21天出现）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ESR/CRP role in osteomyelitis<br />
ESR/CRP在骨髓炎中的作用</td>
<td>Elevated in active disease; used primarily to monitor treatment response — normalization of CRP indicates adequate therapy; NOT specific enough to confirm diagnosis<br />
活动期升高；主要用于监测治疗反应——CRP正常化提示治疗充分；特异性不足以确诊</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sequestrum vs. involucrum<br />
死骨片 vs. 包壳骨</td>
<td>Sequestrum = avascular necrotic bone fragment (antibiotic-impenetrable bacterial sanctuary); Involucrum = reactive periosteal new bone surrounding and encasing the sequestrum<br />
死骨片 = 无血管坏死骨碎片（抗生素无法渗透的细菌庇护所）；包壳骨 = 包绕并封闭死骨片的反应性骨膜新骨</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Combat wound microbiology<br />
战伤微生物学</td>
<td>IED blast wounds: polymicrobial — S. aureus (most common single organism), Acinetobacter baumannii, Pseudomonas aeruginosa, anaerobes; culture is essential<br />
IED爆炸伤：多微生物感染——金黄色葡萄球菌（最常见单一微生物）、鲍曼不动杆菌、铜绿假单胞菌、厌氧菌；培养至关重要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment principles<br />
治疗原则</td>
<td>Surgical sequestrectomy (remove ALL necrotic bone and hardware) + 4–6 weeks IV antibiotics then oral, guided strictly by bone culture sensitivities<br />
手术死骨切除（彻底去除所有坏死骨和内固定装置）+ 静脉抗生素4–6周后续口服，严格依据骨培养药敏结果</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of draining sinus tract overlying bone:** Also consider infected retained foreign body (shrapnel, hardware), actinomycosis ("sulfur granules" on discharge), and Brodie abscess; bone biopsy and culture distinguish all of these\
  **骨骼上方引流窦道的鉴别诊断:** 也需考虑感染性残留异物（弹片、内固定器械）、放线菌病（分泌物含"硫磺颗粒"）和Brodie脓肿；骨活检培养可鉴别所有情况

- **Brodie abscess variant:** Subacute osteomyelitis presenting as a walled-off intramedullary abscess on MRI/CT without systemic signs; most common in the metaphysis of long bones in children; treated with surgical drainage + antibiotics\
  **Brodie脓肿变异型:** 亚急性骨髓炎，MRI/CT表现为包裹性髓内脓肿，无全身症状；最常见于儿童长骨干骺端；手术引流联合抗生素治疗

- **Key long-term complication — Marjolin's ulcer:** Squamous cell carcinoma arising in a chronic non-healing sinus tract after years of inflammation; suspect if sinus opening grows rapidly, bleeds, or develops an indurated margin\
  **关键长期并发症——Marjolin溃疡:** 鳞状细胞癌发生于多年慢性不愈合窦道的炎症基础上；若窦道开口迅速增大、出血或边缘硬结，高度怀疑

- **Osteomyelitis organism by host:** Sickle cell disease → Salmonella; IV drug users → Pseudomonas aeruginosa; diabetic foot → S. aureus + Streptococcus + gram-negatives (polymicrobial); neonates → Group B Strep + S. aureus\
  **各宿主类型的骨髓炎致病菌:** 镰状细胞病→沙门菌；静脉吸毒者→铜绿假单胞菌；糖尿病足→金黄色葡萄球菌+链球菌+革兰阴性菌（多微生物）；新生儿→B族链球菌+金黄色葡萄球菌

# Question 79 — Neuroblastoma with Opsoclonus-Myoclonus Syndrome / 神经母细胞瘤合并眼阵挛-肌阵挛综合征

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>2-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician because of a <strong>2-week history of difficulty walking</strong> and <strong>intermittent crossing of the eyes</strong>. She also has had <strong>three to four episodes of watery diarrhea daily</strong> during this time. She has not had fever or vomiting. She has no history of serious illness and receives no medications. She is alert but <strong>irritable and tearful</strong>; she clings to her mother during the examination. She is at the 50th percentile for length, 25th percentile for weight, and 50th percentile for head circumference. Her pulse is 100/min, respirations are 20/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 120/80 mm Hg</strong>. The abdomen is soft and nontender; a <strong>smooth, firm mass is palpated over the right upper quadrant</strong>. Neurologic examination shows <strong>rapid, chaotic, multidirectional saccades of the eyes</strong>. There are <strong>jerking motions of the extremities</strong>, which are exacerbated by intentional movement. There is <strong>truncal ataxia</strong>, and the patient is unable to sit or walk without assistance. Which of the following is the most likely underlying cause of this patient's symptoms?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely underlying cause of this patient's symptoms?</strong></p>
<p>A) Hepatoblastoma<br />
B) Medulloblastoma<br />
C) Nephroblastoma (Wilms tumor)<br />
D) Neuroblastoma<br />
E) Non-Hodgkin lymphoma<br />
F) Rhabdomyosarcoma</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>2-year-old girl, difficulty walking, eye crossing × 2 weeks<br />
2岁女孩，行走困难、眼球交叉2周</td>
<td>Classic OMS age window (1–3 years); triad of ataxia + opsoclonus + myoclonus points to paraneoplastic syndrome<br />
OMS经典发病年龄窗（1–3岁）；三联征提示副肿瘤综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rapid, chaotic, multidirectional saccades of the eyes<br />
快速、混乱、多方向眼球扫视</td>
<td>Pathognomonic opsoclonus — distinguishes from nystagmus by absence of intersaccadic interval<br />
眼阵挛的病理性特征——无扫视间期，可与眼震鉴别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Jerking motions of extremities, exacerbated by intentional movement<br />
四肢抖动，随意运动加重</td>
<td>Myoclonus — second limb of OMS triad<br />
肌阵挛——OMS三联征第二项</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Truncal ataxia, unable to sit/walk without assistance<br />
躯干共济失调，无法独坐/独走</td>
<td>Cerebellar dysfunction from paraneoplastic antibodies<br />
副肿瘤抗体导致小脑功能受损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Smooth, firm RUQ mass<br />
右上腹光滑、质硬肿块</td>
<td>Adrenal/retroperitoneal neuroblastoma — does NOT arise from kidney (Wilms would be flank mass)<br />
肾上腺/腹膜后神经母细胞瘤——注意非肾脏来源（Wilms瘤为侧腹块）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blood pressure 120/80 mmHg in a 2-year-old<br />
2岁儿童血压120/80 mmHg</td>
<td>Diastolic hypertension from catecholamine excess — hallmark of neuroblastoma<br />
儿茶酚胺过量导致舒张期高血压——神经母细胞瘤标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Watery diarrhea 3–4×/day<br />
每日水样腹泻3–4次</td>
<td>VIP (vasoactive intestinal peptide) secretion by neuroblastoma → secretory diarrhea<br />
神经母细胞瘤分泌VIP→分泌性腹泻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Irritability, weight loss (25th percentile)<br />
易激惹、体重不足（第25百分位）</td>
<td>Systemic catecholamine excess + paraneoplastic behavioral regression<br />
儿茶酚胺全身效应+副肿瘤行为倒退</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Neuroblastoma** is a neoplasm of **neuroendocrine cells** of the sympathetic nervous system, arising from **neural crest–derived** tissue; **MYCN oncogene amplification** drives aggressive disease and confers poor prognosis:

**神经母细胞瘤**是交感神经系统**神经内分泌细胞**肿瘤，起源于**神经嵴衍生**组织；**MYCN癌基因扩增**驱动侵袭性病变并预示不良预后：

- Tumor secretes **catecholamines** (dopamine, norepinephrine) → elevated urinary HVA/VMA → diastolic HTN\
  肿瘤分泌**儿茶酚胺**（多巴胺、去甲肾上腺素）→尿HVA/VMA升高→舒张期高血压

- Tumor secretes **VIP** → inhibits gut water absorption → secretory diarrhea unrelated to fever\
  肿瘤分泌**VIP**→抑制肠道水分吸收→分泌性腹泻，与发热无关

- **Paraneoplastic OMS**: anti-neuronal antibodies (anti-Hu, others) cross-react with cerebellar/brainstem neurons → opsoclonus + myoclonus + ataxia\
  **副肿瘤OMS**：抗神经元抗体（抗Hu等）与小脑/脑干神经元交叉反应→眼阵挛+肌阵挛+共济失调

- Adrenal gland is the **most common primary site** in children; tumor may cross midline (unlike Wilms)\
  肾上腺是儿童**最常见原发部位**；肿瘤可越过中线（Wilms瘤通常不越过）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Neuroblastoma = adrenal/retroperitoneal, crosses midline, calcifications on imaging; Wilms = intrarenal, distorts calices on IVP, does NOT cross midline.

**解剖小窍门:** 神经母细胞瘤=肾上腺/腹膜后，越过中线，影像可见钙化；Wilms瘤=肾内，IVP显示肾盏变形，通常不越中线。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Neuroblastoma with Paraneoplastic OMS / 正确答案 (D) — 神经母细胞瘤合并副肿瘤性OMS

**Neuroblastoma** is the most common extracranial solid tumor in children and the most common adrenal malignancy in pediatric patients:

**神经母细胞瘤**是儿童最常见的颅外实体肿瘤，也是儿童最常见的肾上腺恶性肿瘤：

- Arises from **neural crest** → sympathetic ganglia, adrenal medulla; peak age 1–2 years\
  起源于**神经嵴**→交感神经节、肾上腺髓质；发病高峰1–2岁

- OMS (opsoclonus + myoclonus + ataxia) occurs in ~2–3% of neuroblastoma; paradoxically associated with **better prognosis** tumors\
  OMS（眼阵挛+肌阵挛+共济失调）见于约2–3%的神经母细胞瘤；矛盾的是常提示**预后较好**的肿瘤

- Staging relies on **INRG** system; MYCN amplification = high-risk regardless of stage\
  分期采用**INRG**体系；MYCN扩增=无论分期均为高危

**Diagnosis:** Elevated urinary catecholamine metabolites (HVA, VMA) + abdominal mass on imaging (calcifications, crossing midline) + MIBG scan for metastases; biopsy for histology and MYCN status.

**诊断:** 尿儿茶酚胺代谢物升高（HVA、VMA）+影像学腹部肿块（钙化、越中线）+MIBG扫描评估转移；活检明确组织学及MYCN状态。

**Treatment:** Based on risk stratification — low-risk: surgery ± observation; intermediate: surgery + chemotherapy; high-risk: intensive chemo + surgery + radiation + autologous HSCT + dinutuximab (anti-GD2 antibody).

**治疗:** 根据危险分层——低危：手术±观察；中危：手术+化疗；高危：强化化疗+手术+放疗+自体HSCT+dinutuximab（抗GD2抗体）。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Hepatoblastoma<br />
A — 肝母细胞瘤</td>
<td>Wrong — presents with RUQ hepatic mass + elevated AFP; not associated with OMS; no catecholamine excess<br />
错误——表现为右上腹肝脏肿块+AFP升高；不引起OMS；无儿茶酚胺过量</td>
<td>No opsoclonus/myoclonus; AFP elevated; Beckwith-Wiedemann association<br />
无眼/肌阵挛；AFP升高；与Beckwith-Wiedemann综合征相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Medulloblastoma<br />
B — 髓母细胞瘤</td>
<td>Wrong — primary CNS tumor causing ataxia but NOT OMS; presents age 5–9 with ICP signs (headache, vomiting), NOT abdominal mass<br />
错误——原发CNS肿瘤可引起共济失调但不引起OMS；5–9岁发病，表现为颅内压升高（头痛、呕吐），无腹部肿块</td>
<td>No abdominal mass; age 5–9 not 1–3; headache/vomiting prominent<br />
无腹部肿块；发病5–9岁非1–3岁；头痛/呕吐突出</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Nephroblastoma (Wilms tumor)<br />
C — 肾母细胞瘤（Wilms瘤）</td>
<td>Wrong — intrarenal mass, does NOT cross midline, not associated with OMS; no catecholamine excess or VIP diarrhea<br />
错误——肾内肿块，不越中线，不引起OMS；无儿茶酚胺过量或VIP性腹泻</td>
<td>Wilms = flank mass, hematuria, does NOT cross midline; no HTN from catecholamines<br />
Wilms=侧腹肿块、血尿、不越中线；无儿茶酚胺性高血压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Neuroblastoma ✓<br />
D — 神经母细胞瘤 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — neural crest tumor secreting catecholamines (HTN, HVA/VMA↑) and VIP (diarrhea); paraneoplastic OMS is classic association<br />
正确——神经嵴肿瘤分泌儿茶酚胺（高血压、HVA/VMA↑）和VIP（腹泻）；副肿瘤性OMS是经典关联</td>
<td>RUQ mass + HTN + OMS triad + VIP diarrhea in toddler = neuroblastoma<br />
幼儿右上腹块+高血压+OMS三联征+VIP腹泻=神经母细胞瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Non-Hodgkin lymphoma<br />
E — 非霍奇金淋巴瘤</td>
<td>Wrong — presents with constitutional B symptoms (fever, night sweats, weight loss), lymphadenopathy, mediastinal mass; NOT OMS<br />
错误——表现为B症状（发热、盗汗、体重下降）、淋巴结肿大、纵隔肿块；不引起OMS</td>
<td>Lymphadenopathy prominent; B symptoms; no catecholamine excess; no OMS<br />
淋巴结肿大突出；B症状；无儿茶酚胺过量；无OMS</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Rhabdomyosarcoma<br />
F — 横纹肌肉瘤</td>
<td>Wrong — mesenchymal tumor of orbit (proptosis) or GU tract; does NOT produce paraneoplastic OMS; typical age 5–7 years<br />
错误——眼眶（眼球突出）或泌尿生殖道间叶源性肿瘤；不产生副肿瘤性OMS；典型年龄5–7岁</td>
<td>Proptosis or GU mass; no OMS; no catecholamines; different age<br />
眼球突出或泌尿生殖道肿块；无OMS；无儿茶酚胺；年龄不符</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is Wilms tumor (C) because both present with an abdominal mass in a toddler — but Wilms lacks OMS, catecholamine hypertension, and VIP diarrhea, and its mass stays within the flank without crossing midline.*

Wilms瘤（C）是最容易混淆的干扰项，因为两者均为幼儿腹部肿块——但Wilms瘤无OMS、无儿茶酚胺性高血压、无VIP腹泻，且肿块局限于侧腹不越中线。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a toddler (age 1–3) presenting with the OMS triad (opsoclonus + myoclonus + truncal ataxia), diastolic hypertension, VIP-mediated diarrhea, and a retroperitoneal mass crossing the midline, the underlying diagnosis is neuroblastoma — a neural crest tumor with MYCN amplification and elevated urinary catecholamine metabolites.**

**幼儿（1–3岁）出现OMS三联征（眼阵挛+肌阵挛+躯干共济失调）、舒张期高血压、VIP性腹泻及越中线腹膜后肿块，应诊断为神经母细胞瘤——一种伴MYCN扩增、尿儿茶酚胺代谢物升高的神经嵴肿瘤。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "OMS DANCE" for Neuroblastoma / 记忆钩 — 神经母细胞瘤"OMS DANCE"口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>O</strong>psoclonus-myoclonus-ataxia — paraneoplastic triad in toddlers / 眼阵挛-肌阵挛-共济失调——幼儿副肿瘤三联征<br />
• <strong>D</strong>iastolic HTN — catecholamine excess from tumor / 舒张期高血压——肿瘤儿茶酚胺过量<br />
• <strong>A</strong>drenal origin — most common pediatric adrenal malignancy / 肾上腺起源——最常见儿童肾上腺恶性肿瘤<br />
• <strong>N</strong>eural crest derivation — MYCN amplification = poor prognosis / 神经嵴起源——MYCN扩增=预后差<br />
• <strong>C</strong>rosses midline — distinguishes from Wilms tumor / 越过中线——区别于Wilms瘤<br />
• <strong>E</strong>levated urine HVA/VMA — diagnostic metabolites / 尿HVA/VMA升高——诊断性代谢物</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Neuroblastoma & Opsoclonus-Myoclonus Syndrome / 高频知识表 — 神经母细胞瘤与眼阵挛-肌阵挛综合征

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>OMS epidemiology<br />
OMS流行病学</td>
<td>Age 1–3 years; occurs in ~2–3% of neuroblastoma; paradoxically associated with lower-stage, better-prognosis tumors<br />
1–3岁；约2–3%神经母细胞瘤出现OMS；矛盾的是提示低分期、较好预后</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Opsoclonus vs. nystagmus<br />
眼阵挛vs.眼震</td>
<td>Opsoclonus: rapid, arrhythmic, multivectorial saccades with NO intersaccadic interval; nystagmus has slow + fast phases<br />
眼阵挛：快速、不规律、多方向扫视，无扫视间期；眼震有慢相+快相</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Catecholamine metabolites<br />
儿茶酚胺代谢物</td>
<td>Dopamine → HVA (homovanillic acid); Norepinephrine → VMA (vanillylmandelic acid); both elevated in neuroblastoma urine<br />
多巴胺→HVA（高香草酸）；去甲肾上腺素→VMA（香草扁桃酸）；神经母细胞瘤尿中均升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MYCN amplification<br />
MYCN扩增</td>
<td>Present in ~20% of neuroblastomas; single most important adverse prognostic factor; associated with rapid progression<br />
约20%神经母细胞瘤存在；最重要的不良预后因素；与快速进展相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Staging &amp; risk groups<br />
分期与危险分组</td>
<td>INRG system: low/intermediate/high risk; high-risk (~40% of cases) = MYCN amplified OR metastatic OR age &gt;18mo with unfavorable histology<br />
INRG体系：低/中/高危；高危（约40%）=MYCN扩增或转移或&gt;18月不良组织学</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MIBG scan<br />
MIBG扫描</td>
<td>Meta-iodobenzylguanidine taken up by catecholamine-producing cells; gold standard for staging and monitoring neuroblastoma<br />
间碘苯甲胍被儿茶酚胺分泌细胞摄取；神经母细胞瘤分期和监测的金标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment overview<br />
治疗概述</td>
<td>High-risk: induction chemo → surgery → consolidation (ASCT) → maintenance (dinutuximab anti-GD2 + isotretinoin)<br />
高危：诱导化疗→手术→巩固（自体干细胞移植）→维持（dinutuximab抗GD2+异维A酸）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of pediatric abdominal masses:** Neuroblastoma (adrenal, crosses midline, age \<2), Wilms (renal, flank, age 3–4), Hepatoblastoma (hepatic, AFP↑, age \<3), Rhabdomyosarcoma (GU/pelvic)\
  **儿童腹部肿块鉴别:** 神经母细胞瘤（肾上腺、越中线、\<2岁）、Wilms瘤（肾脏、侧腹、3–4岁）、肝母细胞瘤（肝脏、AFP升高、\<3岁）、横纹肌肉瘤（泌尿生殖/盆腔）

- **OMS treatment:** Immunotherapy (ACTH, IVIG, rituximab) for OMS itself in addition to tumor resection; OMS may persist or relapse even after tumor removal\
  **OMS治疗:** 肿瘤切除同时针对OMS本身给予免疫治疗（ACTH、IVIG、利妥昔单抗）；即使切除肿瘤后OMS仍可持续或复发

- **Beckwith-Wiedemann syndrome overlap:** Associated with Wilms tumor AND hepatoblastoma (NOT neuroblastoma); features include macroglossia, hemihypertrophy, omphalocele, neonatal hypoglycemia\
  **Beckwith-Wiedemann综合征重叠:** 与Wilms瘤和肝母细胞瘤相关（非神经母细胞瘤）；特征包括巨舌、半侧肥大、脐膨出、新生儿低血糖

- **VIP-secreting neuroblastoma (Kerner-Morrison syndrome):** Watery diarrhea, hypokalemia, achlorhydria (WDHA) — rare but classic Step 2 association with neuroblastoma\
  **VIP分泌性神经母细胞瘤（Kerner-Morrison综合征）:** 水样腹泻、低钾血症、无胃酸（WDHA）——罕见但为Step 2经典考点

- **Prognosis paradox:** OMS-associated neuroblastoma tends to be localized (stage 1–2) with favorable histology, yet 50–70% of OMS survivors have long-term neurologic sequelae from immune damage\
  **预后悖论:** OMS相关神经母细胞瘤多为局限期（1–2期）、组织学良好，但50–70%的OMS幸存者因免疫损伤遗留长期神经系统后遗症

# Question 80 — Infective Endocarditis with Acute Aortic Valvular Damage / 感染性心内膜炎并急性主动脉瓣损害

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Three days</strong> after admission to the hospital for <strong>acute bacterial endocarditis</strong>, a <strong>62-year-old man</strong> has <strong>shortness of breath</strong> that began 5 minutes ago while walking for the first time since admission. On admission, he had a <strong>10-day history of fever</strong>; examination showed <strong>splinter hemorrhages</strong> and normal heart sounds without murmurs. His current pulse is <strong>110/min</strong>, respirations are <strong>24/min</strong>, and blood pressure is <strong>100/50 mm Hg</strong>. <strong>Crackles are heard over both lung bases</strong>. S1 and S2 are soft; there is an <strong>S3</strong>. A <strong>new grade 2/6, early diastolic murmur</strong> is heard at the apex and the left sternal border, and a <strong>grade 4/6, systolic ejection murmur</strong> is heard best in the carotids and at the left sternal border. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Echocardiography<br />
B) Ventilation-perfusion lung scans<br />
C) Intravenous furosemide therapy<br />
D) Intravenous heparin therapy<br />
E) Sublingual nitroglycerin therapy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Acute bacterial endocarditis, 3 days after admission<br />
急性细菌性心内膜炎，入院第3天</td>
<td>Establishes the underlying diagnosis; acute IE is at high risk for rapid valve destruction<br />
明确基础诊断；急性IE瓣膜破坏风险高且进展迅速</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Splinter hemorrhages, no murmur on admission<br />
入院时有裂片状出血，无杂音</td>
<td>Peripheral stigmata confirm IE; absence of initial murmur makes any new murmur highly significant<br />
外周征象确认IE；初始无杂音使新出现的杂音尤为重要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>New grade 2/6 early diastolic murmur at LSB and apex<br />
左胸骨缘和心尖部新出现的2/6级早期舒张期杂音</td>
<td>Strongly suggests new aortic regurgitation from valve leaflet destruction by infection<br />
强烈提示感染性瓣叶破坏导致的新发主动脉瓣反流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Grade 4/6 systolic ejection murmur radiating to carotids<br />
放射至颈动脉的4/6级收缩期射血性杂音</td>
<td>Radiation to carotids indicates aortic outflow tract involvement; reflects turbulent flow through damaged aortic valve<br />
放射至颈动脉提示主动脉瓣口受累；反映受损主动脉瓣的湍流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 100/50, HR 110, bibasilar crackles, S3<br />
血压100/50，心率110，双肺底湿啰音，S3</td>
<td>Classic signs of acute heart failure — wide pulse pressure + S3 + pulmonary edema — consequence of acute severe AR<br />
急性心力衰竭的经典体征——宽脉压+S3+肺水肿——急性重度AR的后果</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute onset dyspnea with first ambulation<br />
首次活动时急性起病的呼吸困难</td>
<td>Acute decompensation suggests sudden new valvular regurgitation overwhelming cardiac reserve<br />
急性失代偿提示突发瓣膜反流超过心脏储备能力</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Infective endocarditis** causes valvular damage via direct bacterial invasion and inflammatory destruction of **valve leaflets and supporting structures**, leading to **acute valvular regurgitation**:

**感染性心内膜炎**通过细菌直接侵袭和炎症破坏**瓣叶及支撑结构**，导致**急性瓣膜反流**：

- Bacterial vegetations form on valve leaflets → leaflet perforation or destruction → **acute aortic regurgitation (AR)**\
  细菌赘生物在瓣叶上形成 → 瓣叶穿孔或破坏 → **急性主动脉瓣反流（AR）**

- Acute severe AR causes sudden volume overload on the left ventricle → elevated LVEDP → pulmonary edema and **acute heart failure**\
  急性重度AR导致左心室突然容量超负荷 → 左室舒张末压升高 → 肺水肿和**急性心力衰竭**

- Chronic AR allows LV compensation (dilation); **acute** AR does not → LV cannot dilate fast enough → rapid decompensation\
  慢性AR允许左室代偿性扩张；**急性**AR则不然 → 左室来不及扩张 → 迅速失代偿

- S3 gallop reflects rapid ventricular filling into a volume-overloaded, non-compliant LV\
  S3奔马律反映容量超负荷且顺应性下降的左室快速充盈

- Wide pulse pressure (100/50 → pulse pressure 50 mmHg) is a hallmark of significant AR\
  宽脉压（100/50 → 脉压50 mmHg）是显著AR的标志性表现

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Aortic regurgitation murmur is best heard at the left sternal border (3rd–4th intercostal space) with the patient leaning forward, breath held at end-expiration.

**解剖小窍门:** 主动脉瓣反流杂音在患者前倾、呼气末屏气时，于胸骨左缘第3-4肋间最为清晰。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Echocardiography / 正确答案 (A) — 超声心动图

**Echocardiography** is the gold-standard tool for evaluating suspected valvular damage in infective endocarditis, providing real-time assessment of valve morphology, vegetation size, regurgitant severity, and ventricular function:

**超声心动图**是评估感染性心内膜炎可疑瓣膜损害的金标准工具，可实时评估瓣膜形态、赘生物大小、反流严重程度及心室功能：

- Confirms presence and severity of new valvular regurgitation or stenosis\
  确认新发瓣膜反流或狭窄的存在及严重程度

- Detects vegetations, leaflet perforation, perivalvular abscess, or intracardiac fistula formation\
  检测赘生物、瓣叶穿孔、瓣周脓肿或心内瘘管形成

- Guides surgical decision-making: severe AR with acute HF is an indication for emergency valve replacement\
  指导手术决策：急性心衰合并重度AR是紧急瓣膜置换的适应证

- TTE is first-line (sensitivity ~50–60% for vegetations); TEE is used if TTE is negative but suspicion remains high, or if prosthetic valve or perivalvular complication is suspected (sensitivity ~90–95%)\
  TTE为一线检查（赘生物灵敏度约50–60%）；若TTE阴性但仍高度疑诊，或为人工瓣膜、或疑有瓣周并发症，则行TEE（灵敏度约90–95%）

**Diagnosis:** New early diastolic murmur at LSB + systolic ejection murmur radiating to carotids + acute heart failure signs in the setting of IE → acute aortic valve destruction with AR and possible perivalvular damage requiring urgent structural characterization.

**诊断:** 左胸骨缘新发早期舒张期杂音 + 放射至颈动脉的收缩期射血性杂音 + IE背景下急性心衰体征 → 主动脉瓣急性破坏伴AR及可能的瓣周损害，需紧急明确结构性病因。

**Treatment:** Continued antibiotics + urgent echocardiography (TTE, then TEE if needed) + surgical consultation for valve replacement if severe regurgitation with hemodynamic compromise is confirmed.

**治疗:** 继续抗生素 + 紧急超声心动图（TTE，必要时TEE）+ 外科会诊，若确认重度反流合并血流动力学障碍则行瓣膜置换术。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Echocardiography ✓<br />
A — 超声心动图 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — New murmur in IE requires immediate echocardiographic evaluation to characterize valvular damage and guide management<br />
正确——IE中新出现的杂音需立即行超声心动图评估瓣膜损害并指导处理</td>
<td>New murmur + IE = echocardiography first<br />
新杂音 + IE = 首选超声心动图</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Ventilation-perfusion lung scans<br />
B — 通气/灌注肺扫描</td>
<td>Wrong — VQ scan evaluates for PE; while septic pulmonary emboli occur in right-sided IE, this patient has left-sided IE with new murmur and HF, pointing to valvular damage, not PE<br />
错误——VQ扫描用于评估肺栓塞；右心IE可发生肺部感染性栓塞，但此患者为左心IE伴新发杂音和心衰，指向瓣膜损害而非PE</td>
<td>Right-sided IE → pulmonary septic emboli; left-sided IE → valvular damage + systemic emboli<br />
右心IE → 肺部感染性栓塞；左心IE → 瓣膜损害 + 体循环栓塞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Intravenous furosemide therapy<br />
C — 静脉呋塞米治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — Furosemide addresses pulmonary edema symptoms but not the underlying cause; in IE with a new murmur, structural diagnosis must precede treatment<br />
错误——呋塞米对症处理肺水肿，但不解决根本原因；IE新发杂音时，必须先明确结构诊断再治疗</td>
<td>Treating symptoms before structural diagnosis in new-murmur IE is inappropriate<br />
IE新发杂音时先对症治疗而不明确结构诊断是不恰当的</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Intravenous heparin therapy<br />
D — 静脉肝素治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — Heparin is for thromboembolic disease; exam findings (new murmur, wide pulse pressure, S3, bibasilar crackles) indicate valvular dysfunction, not thromboembolism; heparin is also generally avoided in IE due to intracranial hemorrhage and mycotic aneurysm rupture risk<br />
错误——肝素用于血栓栓塞性疾病；体征（新发杂音、宽脉压、S3、双肺底湿啰音）提示瓣膜功能障碍而非血栓栓塞；IE中肝素因颅内出血和真菌性动脉瘤破裂风险通常需避免</td>
<td>No thromboembolic features; IE structural signs dominate<br />
无血栓栓塞特征；IE结构性体征为主</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Sublingual nitroglycerin therapy<br />
E — 舌下硝酸甘油治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — NTG is for ischemic chest pain or hypertensive urgency; no evidence of ACS; using NTG in acute AR with hypotension (BP 100/50) can cause dangerous cardiovascular collapse<br />
错误——硝酸甘油用于缺血性胸痛或高血压危象；无急性冠脉综合征证据；低血压性急性AR中使用硝酸甘油（BP 100/50）可导致危险性循环衰竭</td>
<td>No ischemic features; NTG relatively contraindicated with hypotension and acute AR<br />
无缺血特征；低血压合并急性AR时硝酸甘油相对禁忌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (furosemide) because bibasilar crackles and an S3 clearly indicate pulmonary edema — but the "diagnose before treating" principle mandates echocardiography first to define the structural cause and determine whether valve surgery is urgently needed.*

最易混淆的干扰项是选项C（呋塞米），因为双肺底湿啰音和S3明确提示肺水肿——但"治疗前先诊断"原则要求先行超声心动图明确结构性病因，并判断是否需要紧急瓣膜手术。

TEE（对脓肿灵敏度优于TTE）</td>

受累器官CT；TEE评估赘生物大小</td>

抗生素 ± 紧急瓣膜手术</td>

手术清创 + 长程抗生素</td>

</tr>

手术适应证</td>
<td>Severe regurgitation + HF; uncontrolled infection; large vegetation (&gt;10 mm)<br />
重度反流 + 心衰；感染未控制；大型赘生物（&gt;10 mm）</td>
<td>AV block or extension to periaortic/intervalvular structures<br />
房室传导阻滞或向主动脉旁/瓣间结构扩展</td>
<td>Recurrent emboli despite antibiotics; anterior mitral leaflet vegetation<br />
抗生素治疗后反复栓塞；二尖瓣前叶赘生物</td>
</tr>
