## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A 16-year-old with primary amenorrhea, short stature, absent secondary sexual characteristics, and markedly elevated FSH has Turner syndrome (45,X gonadal dysgenesis) — confirmed by karyotype analysis.**

**16岁女孩原发性闭经、矮小、无继发性性征、FSH显著升高，诊断为特纳综合征（45,X性腺发育不全）——染色体核型分析确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — Turner Syndrome "CHEST" / 记忆钩 — 特纳综合征"CHEST":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>oarctation of aorta (+ bicuspid aortic valve) — most important cardiac defect; risk of dissection / 主动脉缩窄（+二叶主动脉瓣）——最重要心脏缺陷；夹层风险<br />
• <strong>H</strong>orseshoe kidney — most common renal anomaly / 马蹄肾——最常见肾脏异常<br />
• <strong>E</strong>levated FSH/LH — hypergonadotropic, streak gonads, no negative feedback / FSH/LH升高——高促性腺激素性，条索状性腺，无负反馈<br />
• <strong>S</strong>hort stature + no Secondary sex characteristics — SHOX loss + no estrogen / 矮小+无继发性性征——SHOX缺失+无雌激素<br />
• <strong>T</strong>urner neck — webbed neck (pterygium colli), classic physical finding / 特纳颈——蹼状颈（翼状颈），经典体征</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Turner Syndrome (45,X) / 高频知识表 — 特纳综合征（45,X）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Genetics<br />
遗传学</td>
<td>45,X (most common, ~55%); mosaic 45,X/46,XX (milder); isochromosome Xq, ring X chromosome also possible<br />
45,X（最常见，约55%）；嵌合型45,X/46,XX（较轻）；等臂染色体Xq、环状X染色体亦可见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common cause of primary amenorrhea<br />
原发性闭经最常见原因</td>
<td>Turner syndrome accounts for ~50% of hypergonadotropic hypogonadism in adolescent females; overall most common chromosomal cause of primary amenorrhea<br />
特纳综合征占青春期女性高促性腺激素性性腺功能减退约50%；是原发性闭经最常见的染色体病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cardiac complications<br />
心脏并发症</td>
<td>Bicuspid aortic valve (~30%, most common); coarctation of aorta (~10%); aortic dissection risk — echocardiography mandatory at diagnosis and periodically thereafter<br />
二叶主动脉瓣（约30%，最常见）；主动脉缩窄（约10%）；主动脉夹层风险——诊断时及此后定期行超声心动图检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Renal anomalies<br />
肾脏异常</td>
<td>Horseshoe kidney (most common); duplicated collecting system; renal ultrasound recommended at diagnosis<br />
马蹄肾（最常见）；重复集合系统；诊断时推荐行肾脏超声</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Autoimmune associations<br />
自身免疫相关</td>
<td>Hypothyroidism (Hashimoto's, ~15–30%); celiac disease; type 1 diabetes — screen periodically with TSH, TTG-IgA<br />
甲状腺功能减退（桥本病，约15-30%）；乳糜泻；1型糖尿病——定期筛查TSH、TTG-IgA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fertility and pregnancy<br />
生育力与妊娠</td>
<td>Generally infertile (streak gonads); pregnancy possible via donor oocyte IVF; pregnancy carries high risk of aortic dissection — pre-pregnancy cardiac evaluation essential<br />
通常不育（条索状性腺）；可通过捐卵试管婴儿妊娠；妊娠期主动脉夹层风险高——妊娠前心脏评估至关重要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment priorities<br />
治疗重点</td>
<td>Growth hormone (childhood, for height); estrogen monotherapy (~age 12–13); add progestogen for uterine protection once breakthrough bleeding occurs; lifelong hormone replacement until age ~51<br />
生长激素（儿童期增高）；雌激素单药（约12-13岁）；出现突破性出血后联合孕激素保护子宫；终身激素替代至约51岁</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of hypergonadotropic hypogonadism in adolescent females:** Turner syndrome (45,X), Swyer syndrome (46,XY gonadal dysgenesis — streak gonads but XY karyotype, presents identically but Y chromosome requires gonadectomy due to gonadoblastoma risk), premature ovarian insufficiency (autoimmune, post-chemotherapy, post-radiation)\
  **青春期女性高促性腺激素性性腺功能减退鉴别:** 特纳综合征（45,X）、Swyer综合征（46,XY性腺发育不全——条索状性腺但核型为XY，表现相同但因性腺母细胞瘤风险需切除性腺）、卵巢早衰（自身免疫、化疗后、放疗后）

- **Key complication — Pregnancy risk:** Turner patients who achieve pregnancy via donor oocyte IVF have markedly elevated risk of aortic dissection due to hemodynamic stress on an already-compromised aorta — thorough pre-pregnancy cardiac imaging is mandatory\
  **关键并发症——妊娠风险:** 通过捐卵试管婴儿妊娠的特纳综合征患者，因血流动力学应激作用于已受损的主动脉，主动脉夹层风险显著升高——妊娠前必须完整进行心脏影像学评估

- **Variant — Mosaic Turner (45,X/46,XX):** May have partial or even complete spontaneous puberty and rare spontaneous pregnancies; phenotype ranges from classic Turner to near-normal; karyotype on ≥30 cells (or FISH) still confirms\
  **题目变式——嵌合型特纳（45,X/46,XX）:** 可有部分甚至完全自发青春期发育及罕见自发妊娠；表型从经典特纳到接近正常不等；仍可通过≥30个细胞核型分析（或FISH）确诊

- **Mnemonic contrast — AIS vs. Turner:** Both present with primary amenorrhea and absent menarche, but AIS (46,XY) has normal breast development (peripheral estrogen from testosterone aromatization), no pubic/axillary hair, and no uterus — the opposite pattern from Turner\
  **记忆对比——AIS与特纳综合征:** 两者均表现为原发性闭经，但AIS（46,XY）有正常乳房发育（睾酮芳香化产生雌激素）、无阴毛/腋毛、无子宫——与特纳综合征的表现模式恰好相反

# Question 87 — Pityriasis Rosea / 玫瑰糠疹

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>7-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the physician because of a <strong>4-day history of a dry, mildly itchy rash</strong>. The rash began as a <strong>small, pink, oval area on his chest</strong> and progressed to <strong>scaly, red patches over his arms, legs, and body</strong>. His mother applied calamine lotion and a topical corticosteroid cream without relief. He is currently taking <strong>amoxicillin for streptococcal pharyngitis</strong> diagnosed 4 days ago. He has no other history of rash or serious illness. He is alert and cooperative and in no acute distress. The pharynx is pink, and the <strong>tonsils are slightly enlarged with no exudate</strong>. The neck is supple with <strong>no adenopathy</strong>. A photograph of the rash over the trunk is shown. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Drug allergy<br />
B) Pityriasis rosea<br />
C) Scarlet fever<br />
D) Seborrheic dermatitis<br />
E) Tinea corporis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Small, pink, oval area on chest first<br />
胸部首发小椭圆形粉色斑</td>
<td>Classic "herald patch" — the hallmark first lesion of pityriasis rosea preceding the generalized eruption<br />
经典"前驱母斑"——玫瑰糠疹在泛发皮疹前出现的标志性初始病灶</td>

</tr>

<td>Pruritus is characteristic but mild — distinguishes from severe allergic urticaria or contact dermatitis<br />
瘙痒是其特点但程度轻，可与严重过敏性荨麻疹或接触性皮炎区分</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Pityriasis rosea** is thought to be triggered by a **viral reactivation**, most commonly **human herpesvirus 6 (HHV-6) and 7 (HHV-7)**, leading to a T-cell–mediated inflammatory response in the skin:

**玫瑰糠疹**被认为由**病毒再激活**触发，最常见为**人类疱疹病毒6型（HHV-6）和7型（HHV-7）**，引发皮肤T细胞介导的炎症反应：

- The initial **herald patch** (母斑) appears as a single oval pink plaque on the trunk, 2–5 cm in size, with a collarette of fine scale at the inner border\
  初始**母斑**表现为躯干单个椭圆形粉红色斑块，直径2–5 cm，内缘有细小鳞屑领圈

- Within 1–2 weeks, **secondary lesions** (子斑) erupt in a "Christmas tree" pattern along the Langer's lines of the trunk, oriented parallel to rib lines\
  1–2周内，**继发皮损**沿Langer皮肤张力线呈"圣诞树"形分布于躯干，方向平行于肋骨走向

- Individual lesions are **oval, salmon-colored plaques** with peripheral trailing scale ("collarette scale") — scale points inward toward center\
  各皮损为**椭圆形鲑鱼色斑块**，外周有向内指向中心的"领圈状鳞屑"

- Condition is **self-limiting** (6–8 weeks), reflecting immune clearance of the reactivated virus\
  疾病具有**自限性**（6–8周），反映免疫系统对再激活病毒的清除

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The "Christmas tree" distribution on the back — long axis of each oval patch parallels the ribs — is pathognomonic when seen on exam photos.

**解剖小窍门:** 背部的"圣诞树"分布——每个椭圆斑长轴平行于肋骨走向——在体检照片中见到即可确诊。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Pityriasis Rosea / 正确答案 (B) — 玫瑰糠疹

**Pityriasis rosea** is a self-limited papulosquamous eruption triggered by viral infection (HHV-6/7), classically beginning with a herald patch followed by a generalized secondary eruption in a Christmas tree distribution:

**玫瑰糠疹**是一种自限性丘疹鳞屑性皮疹，由病毒感染（HHV-6/7）触发，经典表现为母斑后出现圣诞树形分布的泛发继发皮疹：

- Herald patch appears first — single, oval, salmon-colored, 2–5 cm, with collarette scale\
  母斑首先出现——单个、椭圆形、鲑鱼色、直径2–5 cm、有领圈状鳞屑

- Secondary eruption follows 1–2 weeks later with smaller "daughter" plaques oriented along skin tension lines\
  继发皮疹在1–2周后出现，较小的"子斑"沿皮肤张力线排列

- Distribution: trunk and proximal extremities; spares face, palms, and soles\
  分布：躯干和四肢近端；面部、手掌和足底不受累

- Mild pruritus; no systemic symptoms; no lymphadenopathy\
  轻度瘙痒；无全身症状；无淋巴结肿大

- More visible/papular in darker skin tones; may show hyperpigmentation\
  深色皮肤中表现更明显或呈丘疹状，可出现色素沉着

**Diagnosis:** Clinical — herald patch + Christmas tree distribution + recent viral prodrome; no lab workup typically needed.

**诊断:** 临床诊断——母斑+圣诞树分布+近期病毒前驱症状；通常无需实验室检查。

**Treatment:** Self-resolves in 6–8 weeks; topical corticosteroids or oral antihistamines for symptomatic pruritus; oral acyclovir may shorten course if started early.

**治疗:** 6–8周自行消退；局部激素或口服抗组胺药缓解瘙痒；早期口服阿昔洛韦可能缩短病程。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Drug allergy<br />
A — 药物过敏</td>
<td>Drug rash typically presents as urticaria (wheals) or erythema multiforme (targetoid lesions on palms/soles) — not scaly oval plaques in Christmas tree pattern<br />
药疹通常表现为荨麻疹或多形性红斑（靶形损害，见于手掌足底），而非圣诞树形鳞屑斑</td>
<td>Morphology: drug allergy → wheals or targets; pityriasis → oval scaly plaques<br />
形态：药疹→风团或靶形；玫瑰糠疹→椭圆形鳞屑斑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Pityriasis rosea ✓<br />
B — 玫瑰糠疹 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Herald patch on chest followed by generalized scaly oval patches in Christmas tree distribution, concurrent with recent viral/bacterial illness<br />
正确——胸部母斑后出现泛发椭圆形鳞屑斑，呈圣诞树分布，伴近期病毒/细菌感染</td>
<td>Herald patch + Christmas tree pattern is pathognomonic<br />
母斑+圣诞树形态为特征性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Scarlet fever<br />
C — 猩红热</td>
<td>Scarlet fever rash is a rough, diffuse, sandpaper-like erythema (not scaly plaques), associated with strawberry tongue and perioral pallor; desquamation of palms/soles occurs later<br />
猩红热皮疹为粗糙、弥漫性砂纸样红斑（非鳞屑斑），伴草莓舌和口周苍白圈；后期手掌足底脱皮</td>
<td>No strawberry tongue, no sandpaper texture, no perioral pallor in this case<br />
本例无草莓舌、无砂纸感、无口周苍白圈</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Seborrheic dermatitis<br />
D — 脂溢性皮炎</td>
<td>Seborrheic dermatitis causes chronic greasy scaling and erythema on scalp, nasolabial folds, and intertriginous areas — not acute widespread scaly plaques on trunk<br />
脂溢性皮炎表现为慢性油腻性脱屑和红斑，好发于头皮、鼻唇沟和间擦部位，而非急性躯干广泛鳞屑斑</td>
<td>Distribution and chronicity differ: seborrhea→scalp/folds/chronic; pityriasis→trunk/acute<br />
分布和病程不同：脂溢性→头皮/间擦/慢性；玫瑰糠疹→躯干/急性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Tinea corporis<br />
E — 体癣</td>
<td>Tinea corporis presents as one or few annular plaques with central clearing and scaly advancing border — not multiple oval patches in a generalized distribution<br />
体癣表现为一个或少数环形斑块，中央清晰，边缘鳞屑性扩张，而非多发椭圆斑泛发分布</td>
<td>Shape: tinea→annular with central clearing; pityriasis→oval without central clearing<br />
形状：体癣→环形伴中央消退；玫瑰糠疹→椭圆形无中央消退</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Drug allergy (A) because the rash onset coincides with amoxicillin use — but the oval scaly morphology and Christmas tree distribution are incompatible with drug allergy and instead point firmly to pityriasis rosea.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是药物过敏（A），因为皮疹出现时间与使用阿莫西林重合——但椭圆形鳞屑性形态和圣诞树分布与药疹不符，反而强烈提示玫瑰糠疹。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Pityriasis rosea classically begins with a single herald patch on the trunk, followed 1–2 weeks later by multiple smaller oval scaly plaques in a Christmas tree distribution, triggered by HHV-6/7 and self-resolving in 6–8 weeks.**

**玫瑰糠疹经典表现为躯干单个母斑起病，1–2周后出现多个较小椭圆形鳞屑斑呈圣诞树分布，由HHV-6/7触发，6–8周自行消退。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "Herald the Christmas Tree" / 记忆钩 — "母斑报告圣诞树":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>erald patch first — single large oval plaque on chest/trunk / 母斑先出现——胸部或躯干单个大椭圆形斑块<br />
• <strong>C</strong>hristmas tree pattern next — secondary oval plaques along Langer's lines / 接着出现圣诞树形——继发椭圆形斑沿Langer线排列<br />
• <strong>H</strong>HV-6 and 7 — the viral trigger (not the strep, not the drug) / HHV-6和7——病毒诱因（不是链球菌，不是药物）<br />
• <strong>S</strong>elf-limited — resolves in 6–8 weeks without specific treatment / 自限性——6–8周无需特殊治疗自行消退</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pityriasis Rosea / 高频知识表 — 玫瑰糠疹

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Herald patch (母斑)<br />
母斑特征</td>
<td>First lesion; single, oval, salmon-pink, 2–5 cm, collarette scale at inner border; appears 1–2 weeks before secondary eruption<br />
首发皮损；单个、椭圆形、鲑鱼粉色、2–5 cm、内缘领圈状鳞屑；继发皮疹前1–2周出现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secondary eruption distribution<br />
继发皮疹分布</td>
<td>Trunk and proximal extremities; "Christmas tree" pattern on back; long axis of ovals parallels ribs; spares face, palms, soles<br />
躯干和四肢近端；背部"圣诞树"形；椭圆长轴平行肋骨；面部、手掌、足底不受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Etiology<br />
病因</td>
<td>HHV-6 and HHV-7 reactivation; often preceded by URI or other viral prodrome; not directly contagious<br />
HHV-6和HHV-7再激活；常有上呼吸道感染或其他病毒前驱症状；无直接传染性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clinical course<br />
临床病程</td>
<td>Self-resolves in 6–8 weeks; pruritus mild to moderate; recurrence uncommon (immunity after first episode)<br />
6–8周自行消退；瘙痒轻至中度；复发少见（首次发病后获得免疫）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin of color presentation<br />
深色皮肤表现</td>
<td>Lesions may appear more papular; post-inflammatory hyperpigmentation common; Christmas tree pattern less obvious<br />
皮损可呈更明显丘疹状；炎症后色素沉着常见；圣诞树形不明显</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Supportive: topical corticosteroids ± oral antihistamines for itch; phototherapy (UVB) can accelerate resolution; oral acyclovir if started early may shorten course<br />
对症治疗：局部激素±口服抗组胺药止痒；UVB光疗可加速消退；早期口服阿昔洛韦可能缩短病程</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of herald patch alone:** A solitary herald patch can be mistaken for tinea corporis (annular) or nummular eczema — KOH prep negative in pityriasis rosea; biopsy shows characteristic spongiosis with mounds of parakeratosis\
  **单独母斑的鉴别:** 单个母斑易被误诊为体癣（环形）或钱币状湿疹——玫瑰糠疹KOH涂片阴性；活检显示特征性海绵样变伴角化不全堆积

- **Key complication:** Secondary bacterial superinfection from scratching is rare but possible; widespread disease in immunocompromised patients (HIV) may persist or disseminate more severely\
  **关键并发症:** 搔抓引起的继发细菌感染少见但可能；免疫功能低下患者（HIV）中疾病可能持续或更严重播散

- **Variant — inverse pityriasis rosea:** Atypical distribution involving face, axillae, or groin rather than classic trunk; seen more often in children and pregnant women\
  **题目变式——反向玫瑰糠疹:** 非典型分布，累及面部、腋窝或腹股沟而非经典躯干；儿童和孕妇中更常见

- **USMLE trigger recognition:** Any question showing an "initial single oval lesion on trunk" followed by a "Christmas tree rash" — always think pityriasis rosea first, even if antibiotics or strep are mentioned concurrently\
  **USMLE触发词识别:** 任何题目出现"躯干初发单个椭圆形皮损"后继以"圣诞树皮疹"——即使同时提及抗生素或链球菌，始终首先考虑玫瑰糠疹

# Question 88 — Congenital Hypothyroidism / 先天性甲状腺功能减退症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>3-month-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician because of <strong>constipation</strong>. She was born at home at term following an uncomplicated pregnancy and weighed 3118 g (6 lb 14 oz). She has not had routine well-child examinations. She is <strong>unable to hold her head up</strong>, does not roll over, and <strong>does not smile</strong>. She is at the 10th percentile for length, 5th percentile for weight, and <strong>75th percentile for head circumference</strong>. The <strong>posterior fontanel is 2 cm in diameter</strong>. The <strong>tongue is large and protuberant</strong>. Which of the following is most likely to confirm the diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is most likely to confirm the diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Diet history<br />
B) Thyroid function tests<br />
C) Upper gastrointestinal series<br />
D) Cranial ultrasonography<br />
E) Rectal biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>3-month-old, born at home, no well-child exams<br />
3 月龄，家中出生，未接受常规体检</td>
<td>Missed newborn screening — congenital hypothyroidism would have been caught on TSH/T4 screen; this baby slipped through<br />
错过新生儿筛查——先天性甲减本可在 TSH/T4 筛查中发现，该婴儿未被发现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Unable to hold head up, no rolling, no smiling<br />
无法抬头、不翻身、不微笑</td>
<td>Global developmental delay at 3 months; hypotonia and intellectual delay are hallmarks of untreated congenital hypothyroidism<br />
3 月龄全面发育落后；肌张力低下和智力发育迟缓是未经治疗先天性甲减的标志</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Weight 5th %ile, length 10th %ile, head 75th %ile<br />
体重第 5 百分位，身长第 10 百分位，头围第 75 百分位</td>
<td>Disproportionate macrocephaly relative to body; myxedematous tissue accumulation increases apparent head size<br />
头围相对体格不成比例地偏大；黏液水肿性组织堆积使头围外观增大</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Posterior fontanel 2 cm in diameter<br />
后囟直径 2 cm</td>
<td>Posterior fontanel normally closes by 6–8 weeks; persistent open fontanel = delayed bone maturation from hypothyroidism<br />
后囟通常在 6-8 周关闭；持续未闭 = 甲减导致骨成熟延迟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Large, protuberant tongue (macroglossia)<br />
舌体大且突出（巨舌）</td>
<td>Classic myxedematous change; glycosaminoglycan deposition enlarges tongue — key discriminating feature<br />
典型黏液水肿改变；糖胺聚糖沉积致舌体增大——关键鉴别特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Constipation<br />
便秘</td>
<td>Hypothyroidism slows GI motility; in neonates, constipation + hypotonia should always prompt thyroid evaluation<br />
甲减减慢胃肠蠕动；新生儿便秘 + 肌张力低下应始终提示甲状腺评估</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Thyroid hormone** is essential for normal **neuronal myelination**, **bone maturation**, and **metabolic rate** in early infancy:

**甲状腺激素**在婴儿早期对正常**神经元髓鞘化**、**骨骼成熟**和**代谢率**至关重要：

- Thyroid dysgenesis (aplasia/ectopia) is the most common cause (~85%); results in absent or insufficient T3/T4 production\
  甲状腺发育不良（发育不全/异位）是最常见原因（约 85%）；导致 T3/T4 生成缺失或不足

- Low T4 → loss of negative feedback → elevated TSH → newborn screen detects elevated TSH before symptoms appear (this baby missed screening)\
  T4 低下 → 失去负反馈 → TSH 升高 → 新生儿筛查在症状出现前检测到 TSH 升高（该婴儿未接受筛查）

- Without thyroid hormone, glycosaminoglycans accumulate in skin and tissues → **myxedema**: macroglossia, coarse facies, large fontanels\
  缺乏甲状腺激素，糖胺聚糖在皮肤和组织中堆积 → **黏液水肿**：巨舌、粗糙面容、大囟门

- Slowed neuronal development → hypotonia, developmental delay; **critical window is first 3 years of life**\
  神经元发育减慢 → 肌张力低下、发育迟缓；**关键窗口期为生命最初 3 年**

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Posterior fontanel closes by 6–8 weeks; anterior by 18–24 months — an open posterior fontanel at 3 months is always abnormal.

**解剖小窍门:** 后囟在 6-8 周关闭；前囟在 18-24 月关闭——3 月龄时后囟未闭始终属于异常。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Thyroid Function Tests / 正确答案 (B) — 甲状腺功能检查

**Thyroid function tests (TSH + free T4)** are the confirmatory tests for congenital hypothyroidism, demonstrating elevated TSH and low free T4:

**甲状腺功能检查（TSH + 游离 T4）**是先天性甲减的确诊检查，表现为 TSH 升高、游离 T4 降低：

- Elevated TSH reflects loss of negative feedback from insufficient T4\
  TSH 升高反映 T4 不足导致的负反馈丧失

- Low free T4 confirms primary thyroid failure (vs. central hypothyroidism where TSH is also low)\
  游离 T4 降低证实原发性甲状腺衰竭（与中枢性甲减不同，后者 TSH 也低）

- Newborn screening measures TSH (heel-stick filter paper) — this infant missed it due to home birth\
  新生儿筛查测量 TSH（足跟血滤纸片）——该婴儿因在家出生而错过

**Diagnosis:** Congenital hypothyroidism is confirmed when TSH is elevated (\>10 mIU/L on confirmatory serum testing) with low or low-normal free T4 in the clinical context of signs and symptoms.

**诊断:** 在具有典型症状体征的临床背景下，血清确认性检测显示 TSH 升高（\>10 mIU/L）伴游离 T4 低或低正常，即可确诊先天性甲减。

**Treatment:** Levothyroxine (L-T4) oral replacement, started as early as possible; if untreated, results in irreversible intellectual disability (cretinism) and sensorineural hearing loss.

**治疗:** 口服左甲状腺素（L-T4）替代治疗，尽早开始；若未治疗，将导致不可逆智力残障（克汀病）和感音神经性听力损失。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Diet history<br />
A — 饮食史</td>
<td>Could detect iodine deficiency hypothyroidism, but iodine deficiency is rare in developed countries where breast milk and formula contain adequate iodine<br />
可检测碘缺乏性甲减，但在发达国家碘缺乏罕见，母乳和配方奶中碘含量充足</td>
<td>Iodine deficiency is a concern in developing nations, not the US; this presentation fits structural thyroid dysgenesis, not nutritional<br />
碘缺乏是发展中国家的问题，非美国；该表现符合结构性甲状腺发育不良，而非营养性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Thyroid function tests ✓<br />
B — 甲状腺功能检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Confirms elevated TSH and low free T4 consistent with primary congenital hypothyroidism<br />
正确——确认 TSH 升高和游离 T4 降低，与原发性先天性甲减一致</td>
<td>Macroglossia + open posterior fontanel + constipation + developmental delay in unscreened newborn = classic congenital hypothyroidism<br />
巨舌 + 后囟未闭 + 便秘 + 未筛查新生儿的发育迟缓 = 典型先天性甲减</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Upper gastrointestinal series<br />
C — 上消化道造影</td>
<td>Evaluates GI motility and structural causes of vomiting/obstruction, not appropriate for this presentation<br />
评估胃肠动力和结构性呕吐/梗阻原因，不适用于该表现</td>
<td>Constipation here is systemic (hormonal), not anatomic; UGI series would not explain macroglossia, fontanel, or developmental delay<br />
此处便秘为全身性（激素性），而非解剖性；上消化道造影无法解释巨舌、囟门或发育迟缓</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Cranial ultrasonography<br />
D — 颅脑超声</td>
<td>Useful for intracranial hemorrhage or structural brain anomalies (e.g., corpus callosum agenesis), not for hypothyroidism<br />
适用于颅内出血或脑结构异常（如胼胝体发育不全），不适用于甲减</td>
<td>Macrocrania here is from myxedema, not intracranial pathology; no symptoms of hemorrhage (no bulging fontanel, no seizure)<br />
此处头围增大源于黏液水肿，非颅内病变；无出血症状（无囟门膨隆、无抽搐）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Rectal biopsy<br />
E — 直肠活检</td>
<td>Confirms Hirschsprung disease (absence of myenteric ganglion cells in distal colon), a different cause of neonatal constipation<br />
确诊 Hirschsprung 病（远端结肠肌间神经节细胞缺失），是新生儿便秘的另一病因</td>
<td>Hirschsprung presents with failure to pass meconium in first 24–48 hours and abdominal distension; it does not cause macroglossia, open fontanel, or developmental delay<br />
Hirschsprung 病表现为出生后 24-48 小时内未排胎粪及腹胀；不引起巨舌、囟门未闭或发育迟缓</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice E (rectal biopsy for Hirschsprung disease) because both cause constipation in infants — the key discriminators are macroglossia, open posterior fontanel, and global developmental delay, which point exclusively to hypothyroidism.*

最易混淆的干扰项是选项 E（Hirschsprung 病直肠活检），因为两者均可导致婴儿便秘——关键鉴别点是巨舌、后囟未闭和全面发育迟缓，这些特征仅指向甲减。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A 3-month-old unscreened infant with constipation, macroglossia, open posterior fontanel, and global developmental delay has congenital hypothyroidism confirmed by elevated TSH and low free T4.**

**一名 3 月龄未筛查婴儿表现为便秘、巨舌、后囟未闭及全面发育迟缓，诊断为先天性甲减，由 TSH 升高和游离 T4 降低确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CHIMP" Signs of Congenital Hypothyroidism / 记忆钩 — 先天性甲减的 "CHIMP" 五联征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>onstipation — slow GI motility from low thyroid hormone / 便秘——甲状腺激素不足导致肠蠕动减慢<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ypotonia &amp; developmental delay — absent T3/T4 impairs myelination / 肌张力低下和发育迟缓——缺乏 T3/T4 损害髓鞘化<br />
• <strong>I</strong>ncreased head circumference (open fontanel) — delayed bone maturation / 头围增大（囟门未闭）——骨骼成熟延迟<br />
• <strong>M</strong>acroglossia — glycosaminoglycan deposition in tissues (myxedema) / 巨舌——糖胺聚糖在组织中沉积（黏液水肿）<br />
• <strong>P</strong>oor growth (weight &lt; length &lt; head %) — systemic metabolic slowing / 生长迟缓（体重 &lt; 身长 &lt; 头围百分位）——全身代谢减慢</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Congenital Hypothyroidism / 高频知识表 — 先天性甲减

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Incidence &amp; etiology<br />
发病率与病因</td>
<td>1 in 2,000–4,000 newborns; most common preventable cause of intellectual disability; thyroid dysgenesis (~85%) is most common cause, followed by dyshormonogenesis (~15%)<br />
每 2,000-4,000 名新生儿中 1 例；最常见的可预防性智力残障病因；甲状腺发育不良（约 85%）最常见，其次为甲状腺激素合成障碍（约 15%）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Newborn screening<br />
新生儿筛查</td>
<td>Heel-stick TSH (or T4 + TSH) on day 2–5 of life; elevated TSH prompts confirmatory serum TSH + free T4; early treatment (within 2 weeks) prevents irreversible neurologic damage<br />
出生后 2-5 天足跟血 TSH（或 T4 + TSH）；TSH 升高需行血清 TSH + 游离 T4 确认；早期治疗（2 周内）可防止不可逆神经损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic presentation<br />
典型表现</td>
<td>Prolonged neonatal jaundice, large posterior fontanel, macroglossia, umbilical hernia, constipation, hypotonia, hoarse cry, hypothermia, poor feeding, myxedematous facies<br />
新生儿黄疸延迟、后囟偏大、巨舌、脐疝、便秘、肌张力低下、哭声嘶哑、体温低、喂养困难、黏液水肿面容</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>If untreated<br />
未经治疗后果</td>
<td>Cretinism: severe intellectual disability, short stature, sensorineural hearing loss, ataxia; damage is largely irreversible after 3 years of age<br />
克汀病：重度智力残障、矮身材、感音神经性听力损失、共济失调；3 岁后损伤基本不可逆</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗方案</td>
<td>Levothyroxine (L-T4) 10–15 mcg/kg/day orally; monitor TSH every 1–2 months in first year; goal: maintain TSH in low-normal range (0.5–2 mIU/L)<br />
左甲状腺素（L-T4）口服 10-15 mcg/kg/天；第一年每 1-2 月监测 TSH；目标：维持 TSH 在低正常范围（0.5-2 mIU/L）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Transient vs. permanent<br />
一过性 vs. 永久性</td>
<td>Transient causes: maternal antithyroid antibodies, maternal antithyroid drugs (PTU, methimazole), iodine excess or deficiency; permanent: dysgenesis, inborn errors of thyroid synthesis<br />
一过性病因：母体抗甲状腺抗体、母体抗甲状腺药（PTU、甲巯咪唑）、碘过量或缺乏；永久性：发育不良、甲状腺合成先天缺陷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Associations<br />
相关联病症</td>
<td>2× higher risk of congenital heart disease; also associated with congenital deafness; Down syndrome patients have increased rate of congenital hypothyroidism<br />
先天性心脏病风险增加 2 倍；也与先天性耳聋相关；唐氏综合征患者先天性甲减发生率更高</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of neonatal hypotonia + macroglossia:** Down syndrome (karyotype), Beckwith-Wiedemann syndrome (IGF2 overgrowth, omphalocele, hypoglycemia), Pompe disease (lysosomal storage, cardiac involvement), congenital hypothyroidism (TSH/T4)\
  **新生儿肌张力低下 + 巨舌的鉴别:** 唐氏综合征（核型分析）、Beckwith-Wiedemann 综合征（IGF2 过度增殖、脐膨出、低血糖）、Pompe 病（溶酶体储积、心脏受累）、先天性甲减（TSH/T4）

- **Variant — central hypothyroidism:** TSH is low or normal (not elevated) with low T4; caused by pituitary or hypothalamic failure; newborn screening (TSH-based) may miss it — screen with free T4 if suspected\
  **变式——中枢性甲减:** TSH 低或正常（而非升高）伴 T4 降低；由垂体或下丘脑衰竭引起；基于 TSH 的新生儿筛查可能漏诊——若怀疑应检测游离 T4

- **Key complication of delayed treatment:** Irreversible intellectual disability (cretinism); the brain is most vulnerable in the first 6 months — treatment before 2 weeks of age results in near-normal IQ\
  **延误治疗的关键并发症:** 不可逆智力残障（克汀病）；大脑在前 6 个月最脆弱——2 周龄前开始治疗可获近正常智商

- **Risk factor — home birth:** Missed mandatory newborn metabolic screening; USMLE frequently tests unscreened neonates presenting late with preventable conditions (PKU, congenital hypothyroidism, galactosemia)\
  **危险因素——家中出生:** 错过强制性新生儿代谢筛查；USMLE 常以未筛查新生儿晚期出现可预防疾病为考题（苯丙酮尿症、先天性甲减、半乳糖血症）

# Question 89 — Pneumococcal Revaccination in HIV / HIV 患者肺炎球菌疫苗复种

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>32-year-old man</strong> comes to the office for a routine examination. He was diagnosed with <strong>HIV infection 7 years ago</strong> and began antiretroviral therapy 6 years ago. He <strong>received the appropriate immunizations at the time of diagnosis</strong>. He has tolerated his medication regimen well. He used illicit intravenous drugs for 5 years but stopped 7 years ago. He is in a monogamous relationship with one female partner; they use condoms consistently. Examination shows no abnormalities. His <strong>CD4+ T-lymphocyte count is 645/mm³</strong> (Normal≥500), and <strong>plasma HIV viral load is 1000 copies/mL</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following immunizations is most appropriate to administer at this time?</strong></p>
<p>A) Hepatitis A<br />
B) Hepatitis B<br />
C) Human papillomavirus<br />
D) Meningococcal<br />
E) Pneumococcal</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>HIV diagnosed 7 years ago<br />
HIV 感染确诊于 7 年前</td>
<td>Sets the timeline: vaccines given at diagnosis are ~7 years old, potentially past their revaccination windows<br />
确立时间线：确诊时接种的疫苗已约 7 年，可能已超过复种时间窗口</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Received appropriate immunizations at time of diagnosis<br />
确诊时已完成相应免疫接种</td>
<td>Signals that Hep A, Hep B, HPV, meningococcal, AND initial pneumococcal series were all given then — question asks what is due NOW<br />
提示甲肝、乙肝、HPV、脑膜炎球菌及肺炎球菌初始系列均已在确诊时接种——题目考查现在应补种什么</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CD4+ count 645/mm³ (normal)<br />
CD4+ 计数 645/mm³（正常）</td>
<td>CD4+ above 500 = preserved immune function; however, HIV itself is a permanent immunocompromising indication independent of CD4+ count<br />
CD4+ 高于 500 = 免疫功能保留；但 HIV 本身是独立于 CD4+ 计数的永久性免疫功能低下指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Plasma HIV viral load 1000 copies/mL (detectable)<br />
血浆 HIV 病毒载量 1000 拷贝/mL（可检测）</td>
<td>Not fully suppressed (goal &lt;50 copies/mL) → ongoing immunocompromised state → heightened infection risk<br />
未完全抑制（目标 &lt;50 拷贝/mL）→ 持续免疫缺陷状态 → 感染风险持续升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Former IV drug user, stopped 7 years ago<br />
前静脉吸毒者，已戒断 7 年</td>
<td>Historical risk factor for Hep B/C and HIV; hepatitis vaccines were presumably completed at diagnosis — no active risk remaining<br />
乙型/丙型肝炎和 HIV 的历史风险因素；肝炎疫苗已于确诊时完成——目前无活动性风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Routine examination, no current abnormalities<br />
常规复诊，目前无异常体征</td>
<td>Preventive care context — the question is about scheduled vaccine maintenance, not acute illness management<br />
预防保健情境——考查的是计划疫苗维护，而非急性疾病处理</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

HIV-infected patients are classified as **functionally immunocompromised** regardless of current CD4+ count, placing them at dramatically higher risk for **invasive pneumococcal disease** (bacteremia, meningitis, pneumonia). The **Advisory Committee on Immunization Practices (ACIP)** therefore mandates a lifelong pneumococcal vaccination strategy with fixed revaccination intervals for all HIV-positive adults:

HIV 感染者无论当前 CD4+ 计数如何，均被归类为**功能性免疫低下状态**，其发生侵袭性**肺炎球菌病**（菌血症、脑膜炎、肺炎）的风险显著升高。因此，**美国免疫实践咨询委员会（ACIP）**为所有 HIV 阳性成人规定了终身肺炎球菌接种策略及固定复种间隔：

- Initial series: PCV13 first → PPSV23 ≥8 weeks later — given at time of HIV diagnosis\
  初始系列：先接种 PCV13 → ≥8 周后 PPSV23——在 HIV 确诊时给予

- PPSV23 revaccination: required ≥5 years after the initial PPSV23 dose (this patient is 7 years out → overdue)\
  PPSV23 复种：初次接种后 ≥5 年进行（本患者已过 7 年 → 已逾期）

- Final PPSV23 booster: administered again at age 65 if all prior doses were given before age 65\
  最终 PPSV23 加强针：若所有既往接种均在 65 岁前完成，则 65 岁时再次接种

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Encapsulated bacteria (Streptococcus pneumoniae, Haemophilus influenzae, Neisseria meningitidis) evade opsonization and splenic clearance in immunocompromised hosts, explaining why HIV patients — like asplenic patients — are at extreme risk for overwhelming infection.

**解剖小窍门:** 有荚膜细菌（肺炎链球菌、流感嗜血杆菌、脑膜炎奈瑟菌）在免疫功能低下宿主中可逃避调理作用和脾脏清除，这解释了 HIV 患者——如同无脾患者——为何面临压倒性感染的极高风险。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Pneumococcal Revaccination / 正确答案 (E) — 肺炎球菌复种疫苗

**Pneumococcal vaccine (PPSV23)** revaccination is unconditionally recommended for all HIV-positive adults ≥5 years after their prior dose, regardless of age, CD4+ count, or viral load:

**肺炎球菌疫苗（PPSV23）**复种无条件推荐用于所有 HIV 阳性成人，距上次接种 ≥5 年后，与年龄、CD4+ 计数或病毒载量无关：

- HIV is a permanent, absolute indication for PPSV23 revaccination — not conditional on immune status\
  HIV 是 PPSV23 复种的永久性、绝对性指征——不以免疫状态为条件

- This patient received initial series approximately 7 years ago → PPSV23 revaccination is already overdue by 2 years\
  本患者约 7 年前接种初始系列 → PPSV23 复种已逾期 2 年

- A final PPSV23 dose will also be required at age 65 if all prior doses were administered before age 65\
  若所有既往接种均在 65 岁前完成，65 岁时还需最终一剂 PPSV23

**Diagnosis:** HIV-infected adult at preventive care visit, 7 years post-initial pneumococcal series with preserved CD4+ but detectable viral load → PPSV23 revaccination due per ACIP guidelines

**诊断:** HIV 感染成人于预防保健就诊，距初始肺炎球菌系列已 7 年，CD4+ 保留但病毒载量可检测 → 依据 ACIP 指南应行 PPSV23 复种

**Treatment:** Administer PPSV23 now; schedule final PPSV23 dose at age 65

**治疗:** 现在接种 PPSV23；安排 65 岁时最终一剂 PPSV23

<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />

<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Hepatitis A<br />
A — 甲型肝炎</td>
<td>Already received at HIV diagnosis 7 years ago; 2-dose series is complete with no routine revaccination indicated<br />
已于 7 年前 HIV 确诊时接种；2 剂系列完成，无常规复种指征</td>
<td>Hep A provides lifelong immunity after completed series; no booster schedule exists<br />
甲肝完成系列后提供终身免疫；无加强接种计划</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Hepatitis B<br />
B — 乙型肝炎</td>
<td>Already received at diagnosis; 2- or 3-dose series complete; no routine revaccination in adults after completed series<br />
已于确诊时接种；2 或 3 剂系列完成；成人完成系列后无常规复种</td>
<td>Hep B serologic testing (anti-HBs titer) may be checked in immunocompromised, but routine booster is not standard practice<br />
免疫功能低下者可查乙肝血清效价（抗 HBs），但常规加强接种非标准做法</td>

<tr>
<td>C — Human papillomavirus<br />

<td>Series was received at diagnosis; HPV vaccination is routinely recommended through age 26 only; at age 32 it requires shared decision-making (ages 27–45), not routine administration<br />
系列已于确诊时完成；HPV 疫苗常规推荐至 26 岁；32 岁时需共同决策（27–45 岁），非常规接种</td>
<td>This patient is past the routine age window; series was already completed at diagnosis<br />
本患者已超过常规年龄窗口；系列已于确诊时完成</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Meningococcal<br />
D — 脑膜炎球菌</td>
<td>Already received at diagnosis; revaccination is every 5 years for patients who "remain at continued increased risk of exposure" — HIV qualifies, but this is a conditional rather than unconditional requirement<br />
已于确诊时接种；复种针对"持续处于高暴露风险"者每 5 年一次——HIV 符合资格，但这是条件性而非无条件要求</td>
<td>Pneumococcal PPSV23 revaccination applies to ALL HIV patients unconditionally at ≥5 years; meningococcal revaccination requires ongoing risk assessment — making pneumococcal the cleaner, higher-yield answer<br />
肺炎球菌 PPSV23 复种对所有 HIV 患者在 ≥5 年时无条件适用；脑膜炎球菌复种需要持续风险评估——使肺炎球菌成为更明确的高频考查答案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pneumococcal ✓<br />
E — 肺炎球菌 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — PPSV23 revaccination is mandated ≥5 years after initial series for ALL HIV patients; this patient's initial series was 7 years ago, making revaccination overdue<br />
正确——所有 HIV 患者初始系列后 ≥5 年须行 PPSV23 复种；本患者初始系列已过 7 年，复种已逾期</td>
<td>Only vaccine with an absolute, time-based revaccination mandate for ALL HIV patients, independent of current immune status<br />
唯一对所有 HIV 患者均有绝对时间性复种要求的疫苗，独立于当前免疫状态</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Meningococcal (D): 7 years have elapsed since diagnosis, which exceeds the 5-year revaccination interval, and HIV is itself a qualifying condition. However, ACIP frames meningococcal revaccination as conditional on "continued increased risk of exposure," whereas PPSV23 revaccination for HIV patients carries no such qualifier — it is mandatory for every HIV patient at the 5-year mark, full stop.*

脑膜炎球菌（D）是最具迷惑性的干扰项：距确诊已过 7 年，超过了 5 年复种间隔，且 HIV 本身是符合条件的风险因素。然而，ACIP 将脑膜炎球菌复种定义为以"持续高暴露风险"为条件，而 HIV 患者的 PPSV23 复种没有此类限定条件——在 5 年时间节点对每位 HIV 患者均为强制性，毫无例外。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For all HIV patients, PPSV23 pneumococcal revaccination is mandatory ≥5 years after the initial series regardless of CD4+ count — making it the only scheduled vaccine with an unconditional time-based booster requirement in HIV care.**

**对所有 HIV 患者，PPSV23 肺炎球菌复种在初始系列后 ≥5 年时为强制性，与 CD4+ 计数无关——这使其成为 HIV 诊疗中唯一具有无条件时间性加强要求的计划疫苗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PNEUMO Rule for HIV / 记忆钩 — HIV 患者"PNEUMO"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>ermanent — HIV = lifetime pneumococcal indication, no exceptions / HIV = 终身肺炎球菌接种指征，无例外<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ot age-gated — PPSV23 revaccination at ≥5 years even if patient is 30 or 40 / 不受年龄限制——即使患者 30 或 40 岁也须在 ≥5 年时复种<br />
• <strong>E</strong>very 5 years — fixed, unconditional interval for all HIV patients / 每 5 年——对所有 HIV 患者固定、无条件的间隔<br />
• <strong>U</strong>nconditional — unlike meningococcal, no "ongoing risk" qualifier needed / 无条件——与脑膜炎球菌不同，无需"持续风险"限定条件<br />
• <strong>M</strong>andatory at 65 — one final PPSV23 dose at age 65 closes the schedule / 65 岁时强制——65 岁时最终一剂 PPSV23 完结计划<br />
• <strong>O</strong>verdue check — count years since diagnosis; if &gt;5 years and no revaccination, give PPSV23 now / 逾期检查——计算确诊年数；若 &gt;5 年未复种，立即接种 PPSV23</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pneumococcal Vaccination in Immunocompromised Adults / 高频知识表 — 免疫功能低下成人肺炎球菌疫苗

<tr>
<td>Indications for PPSV23 before age 65<br />
65 岁前 PPSV23 接种指征</td>
<td>Immunocompromising conditions (HIV, asplenia, transplant, chronic steroid use, malignancy), chronic illness (DM, CHF, CKD, COPD), cigarette smoking<br />
免疫功能低下（HIV、无脾、移植、长期激素使用、恶性肿瘤）、慢性病（DM、CHF、CKD、COPD）、吸烟</td>

HIV 中活疫苗——CD4+ 阈值</td>

CD4+ ≥200：MMR 和水痘可谨慎接种；CD4+ &lt;200：所有活疫苗禁忌；LAIV（活流感疫苗）在任何 CD4+ 水平均禁忌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pneumococcal disease risk in HIV<br />
HIV 患者肺炎球菌病风险</td>
<td>Invasive pneumococcal disease occurs at ~100× higher rates in HIV vs. HIV-negative adults; bacteremic pneumococcal pneumonia carries 20–30% case fatality rate<br />
侵袭性肺炎球菌病在 HIV 患者中发生率约为 HIV 阴性成人的 100 倍；菌血症性肺炎球菌肺炎病死率达 20–30%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Meningococcal revaccination in HIV<br />
HIV 患者脑膜炎球菌复种</td>
<td>Every 5 years for patients at "continued increased risk of exposure"; HIV is a qualifying condition, but revaccination is conditional (risk-based), not unconditional like PPSV23<br />
对"持续高暴露风险"患者每 5 年；HIV 是符合条件的指征，但复种是条件性的（基于风险），不像 PPSV23 那样无条件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Viral load and immunization decisions<br />
病毒载量与接种决策</td>
<td>Viral suppression status does NOT affect scheduling of inactivated vaccines (including pneumococcal); it matters only for live vaccines (CD4+ is the threshold, not viral load)<br />
病毒抑制状态不影响灭活疫苗的接种计划（包括肺炎球菌）；它仅对活疫苗有意义（阈值是 CD4+，而非病毒载量）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Annual influenza in HIV<br />
HIV 患者年度流感接种</td>
<td>Inactivated influenza vaccine recommended annually for all HIV patients; FluMist (LAIV) is absolutely contraindicated regardless of CD4+ count<br />
灭活流感疫苗推荐所有 HIV 患者每年接种；FluMist（LAIV）无论 CD4+ 计数如何均绝对禁忌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Viral load significance:** A viral load of 1000 copies/mL indicates incomplete HIV suppression (goal is undetectable, \<50 copies/mL) — this should prompt ART adherence counseling or resistance testing, but does NOT delay or change pneumococcal vaccination timing\
  **病毒载量意义:** 病毒载量 1000 拷贝/mL 提示 HIV 抑制不完全（目标为检测不到，\<50 拷贝/mL）——应促使 ART 依从性咨询或耐药检测，但不推迟或改变肺炎球菌疫苗接种时机

- **"Appropriate immunizations at diagnosis" — NBME clue:** This phrase is a classic NBME signal meaning ALL standard HIV-entry vaccines (Hep A, Hep B, HPV, meningococcal, pneumococcal) were given — immediately eliminating A–D as new vaccines and focusing the question on which one has an elapsed revaccination requirement\
  **"确诊时已接种相应疫苗"——NBME 线索:** 此短语是经典 NBME 信号，意味着所有标准 HIV 入组疫苗（甲肝、乙肝、HPV、脑膜炎球菌、肺炎球菌）均已给予——立即排除 A–D 作为新疫苗，将焦点集中在哪种疫苗已超过复种时间

- **HPV at age 32 — shared decision-making:** ACIP recommends routine HPV vaccination through age 26; ages 27–45 involve shared clinical decision-making based on individual risk assessment. This 32-year-old with a monogamous relationship would have low benefit, and the series was already completed at diagnosis\
  **32 岁时的 HPV——共同决策:** ACIP 推荐常规 HPV 接种至 26 岁；27–45 岁基于个人风险评估进行共同临床决策。本患者处于单配偶关系，获益低，且系列已于确诊时完成

- **Asplenia parallel:** The pneumococcal revaccination logic for HIV mirrors that for asplenic patients — both are permanent high-risk states requiring PPSV23 revaccination at 5-year intervals and again at age 65, regardless of current clinical stability\
  **无脾类比:** HIV 患者的肺炎球菌复种逻辑与无脾患者相似——两者均为永久性高风险状态，需每 5 年进行 PPSV23 复种，并在 65 岁时再次接种，与当前临床稳定性无关

# Question 90 — TPN-Induced Cholestatic Hepatic Disease / TPN诱导的胆汁淤积性肝病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>24-year-old man</strong> with <strong>protein C deficiency</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>1-week history of yellowing of his skin</strong>. Three months ago, he had a mesenteric infarction and required resection of all but <strong>45 cm of the proximal small bowel</strong>. The remainder of the jejunum was anastomosed to the colon. He receives <strong>total parenteral nutrition</strong> at home. He takes no medications. Examination today shows generalized jaundice. Laboratory studies show: Leukocyte count 7000/mm³; Serum Bilirubin, total 3.6 mg/dL; <strong>Direct bilirubin 2.6 mg/dL</strong>; <strong>Alkaline phosphatase 150 U/L</strong>; <strong>AST 20 U/L</strong>; <strong>ALT 17 U/L</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's hyperbilirubinemia?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely cause of hyperbilirubinemia?</strong></p>
<p>A) Biliary stricture<br />
B) Cholestatic hepatic disease<br />
C) Hemolysis<br />
D) Hepatitis A<br />
E) Hepatitis C</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Only 45 cm of proximal small bowel remaining<br />
仅剩45cm近端小肠</td>
<td>Short bowel syndrome → severely limited oral nutrient absorption → TPN dependence<br />
短肠综合征→严重限制经口营养吸收→依赖TPN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Total parenteral nutrition (TPN) at home<br />
在家接受全肠外营养</td>
<td>TPN is the direct cause: lack of enteral stimulation → reduced bile flow → cholestasis<br />
TPN是直接病因：缺乏肠内刺激→胆汁流减少→胆汁淤积</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Direct bilirubin 2.6 mg/dL (conjugated ↑)<br />
直接胆红素2.6 mg/dL（结合型升高）</td>
<td>Conjugated hyperbilirubinemia points to intrahepatic/biliary excretion defect, not hemolysis<br />
结合型高胆红素血症指向肝内/胆道排泄障碍，而非溶血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>AST 20, ALT 17 (both normal)<br />
AST 20，ALT 17（均正常）</td>
<td>Absence of transaminase elevation rules out hepatocellular injury (viral hepatitis)<br />
转氨酶不升高排除肝细胞损伤（病毒性肝炎）模式</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Alkaline phosphatase 150 U/L (elevated)<br />
碱性磷酸酶150 U/L（升高）</td>
<td>ALP elevated disproportionately vs. AST/ALT = classic cholestatic pattern<br />
ALP升高与AST/ALT不成比例=经典胆汁淤积模式</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Protein C deficiency → prior mesenteric infarction<br />
蛋白C缺乏→既往肠系膜梗死</td>
<td>Explains the hypercoagulable event requiring massive bowel resection, leading to TPN dependence<br />
解释了高凝事件导致大量肠切除术，最终依赖TPN</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**TPN-induced cholestasis** occurs through multiple mechanisms that converge to impair **bile formation and excretion**:

**TPN诱导的胆汁淤积**通过多种机制共同损害**胆汁的形成与排泄**：

- Lack of oral/enteral intake → no cholecystokinin (CCK) release → gallbladder stasis + reduced bile flow\
  缺乏口服/肠内摄入→无胆囊收缩素（CCK）分泌→胆囊淤滞+胆汁流减少

- TPN components (lipid emulsions, amino acids) are directly hepatotoxic → bile duct inflammation and fibrosis\
  TPN成分（脂质乳剂、氨基酸）对肝脏直接毒性→胆管炎症和纤维化

- Short bowel → reduced enterohepatic circulation of bile acids → bile acid pool depletion → further impaired bile flow\
  短肠→胆汁酸肠肝循环减少→胆汁酸池耗竭→胆汁流进一步受损

- Result: **conjugated** (direct) bilirubin accumulates as hepatocytes cannot excrete bile into bile canaliculi\
  结果：肝细胞无法将胆汁排入胆小管→**结合型**（直接）胆红素蓄积

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The small bowel must be ≥100 cm for adequate enteral absorption; less than this constitutes short bowel syndrome requiring TPN.

**解剖小窍门:** 小肠需至少100cm才能进行充分肠内吸收；少于此长度构成短肠综合征，需要TPN。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — TPN-Induced Cholestasis / 正确答案 (B) — TPN诱导的胆汁淤积

**Cholestatic hepatic disease** is characterized by impaired bile secretion or flow, resulting in buildup of bile components (bilirubin, bile salts) in the blood:

**胆汁淤积性肝病**以胆汁分泌或流动受损为特征，导致血液中胆汁成分（胆红素、胆汁盐）蓄积：

- Elevated direct (conjugated) bilirubin predominates over indirect bilirubin\
  直接（结合型）胆红素升高为主，高于间接胆红素

- ALP elevated disproportionately relative to AST/ALT (the hallmark discriminator)\
  ALP升高与AST/ALT不成比例（标志性鉴别点）

- Clinical jaundice appears when total bilirubin ≥2 mg/dL, often accompanied by pruritus and dark urine\
  总胆红素≥2 mg/dL时出现临床黄疸，常伴瘙痒和尿色深

- TPN-induced cholestasis is especially prevalent in short bowel syndrome due to combined absence of enteral stimulation and direct hepatotoxicity\
  TPN诱导的胆汁淤积在短肠综合征中尤为普遍，原因是肠内刺激缺失与直接肝毒性并存

**Diagnosis:** Cholestatic LFT pattern (↑direct bilirubin, ↑ALP, normal AST/ALT) in the clinical context of TPN-dependent short bowel syndrome

**诊断:** TPN依赖性短肠综合征背景下的胆汁淤积性LFT模式（↑直接胆红素，↑ALP，正常AST/ALT）

**Treatment:** Transition to enteral feeding whenever possible; ursodeoxycholic acid (UDCA) may reduce cholestasis; intestinal rehabilitation programs for short bowel adaptation

**治疗:** 尽可能过渡至肠内喂养；熊去氧胆酸（UDCA）可减轻胆汁淤积；针对短肠适应的肠道康复计划

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Biliary stricture<br />
A — 胆管狭窄</td>
<td>Wrong — physical biliary obstruction typically linked to PBC, PSC, or stones; no underlying biliary structural disease history here<br />
错误——物理性胆道梗阻通常与PBC、PSC或结石相关；本患者无胆道结构性疾病史</td>
<td>Strictures require biliary pathology context (PSC, PBC, post-surgical); TPN use is the dominant contextual clue<br />
狭窄需要胆道病理背景（PSC、PBC、术后）；TPN使用是主导背景线索</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Cholestatic hepatic disease ✓<br />
B — 胆汁淤积性肝病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — TPN in short bowel syndrome causes cholestasis via absent enteral CCK stimulation and direct hepatotoxicity<br />
正确——短肠综合征中TPN通过缺乏肠道CCK刺激和直接肝毒性引起胆汁淤积</td>
<td>↑Direct bili + ↑ALP + normal AST/ALT + TPN-dependent short bowel = classic TPN cholestasis<br />
↑直接胆红素+↑ALP+正常AST/ALT+TPN依赖性短肠=经典TPN胆汁淤积</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Hemolysis<br />
C — 溶血</td>
<td>Wrong — hemolysis raises indirect (unconjugated) bilirubin, not direct; protein C deficiency causes thrombosis, not hemolysis<br />
错误——溶血升高间接（非结合型）胆红素，而非直接胆红素；蛋白C缺乏引起血栓而非溶血</td>
<td>Direct bili 2.6 &gt; indirect bili 1.0 (calculated) rules out hemolysis; hemolysis → indirect &gt; direct<br />
直接胆红素2.6&gt;间接胆红素1.0排除溶血；溶血→间接&gt;直接</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Hepatitis A<br />
D — 甲型肝炎</td>
<td>Wrong — HAV causes hepatocellular injury (↑↑AST/ALT); food-borne; no relevant dietary exposure history in a TPN-dependent patient<br />
错误——HAV引起肝细胞损伤（↑↑AST/ALT）；食源性；TPN依赖患者无相关饮食暴露史</td>
<td>Normal AST 20, ALT 17 exclude hepatocellular hepatitis; cholestatic pattern is inconsistent with HAV<br />
正常AST 20、ALT 17排除肝细胞性肝炎；胆汁淤积模式与HAV不符</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Hepatitis C<br />
E — 丙型肝炎</td>
<td>Wrong — HCV causes transaminitis (hepatocellular pattern) with markedly ↑AST/ALT; no risk factors (IV drug use, transfusion) mentioned<br />
错误——HCV引起转氨酶升高（肝细胞模式），AST/ALT显著升高；未提及危险因素（静脉吸毒、输血）</td>
<td>Both HAV and HCV would produce transaminitis dwarfing the bilirubin/ALP rise; the opposite is true here<br />
HAV和HCV均会产生转氨酶升高远超胆红素/ALP升高的模式；本题恰好相反</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is biliary stricture (A) — it also produces a cholestatic lab pattern, but the clinical story specifically contextualizes TPN and short bowel without any mention of biliary structural disease, making TPN-induced cholestasis the precise diagnosis.*

胆管狭窄（A）是最诱人的干扰项——其同样产生胆汁淤积性实验室模式，但临床故事明确以TPN和短肠为背景且无任何胆道结构性疾病，使TPN诱导的胆汁淤积成为精准诊断。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a TPN-dependent short bowel patient with elevated direct bilirubin and ALP but normal transaminases, TPN-induced cholestatic hepatic disease is the diagnosis.**

**在依赖TPN的短肠患者中，出现直接胆红素和ALP升高但转氨酶正常，诊断为TPN诱导的胆汁淤积性肝病。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — No Gut, No Bile / 记忆钩 — 无肠道，无胆汁:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>N</strong>o enteral intake → No CCK released / 无肠内摄入→无CCK释放<br />
• <strong>O</strong>bstructed bile flow from TPN hepatotoxicity / TPN肝毒性阻碍胆汁流<br />
• <strong>G</strong>allbladder stasis → bile sludge accumulation / 胆囊淤滞→胆泥蓄积<br />
• <strong>B</strong>ilirubin (direct) rises; transaminases stay normal / 直接胆红素升高；转氨酶保持正常</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — TPN-Induced Cholestasis & Short Bowel Syndrome / 高频知识表 — TPN诱导胆汁淤积与短肠综合征

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Short bowel syndrome definition<br />
短肠综合征定义</td>
<td>Remaining small bowel &lt;100 cm (or &lt;200 cm after colectomy); oral absorption insufficient → TPN required<br />
剩余小肠&lt;100cm（或结肠切除后&lt;200cm）；口服吸收不足→需要TPN</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TPN cholestasis mechanism<br />
TPN胆汁淤积机制</td>
<td>No enteral intake → ↓CCK → gallbladder stasis; TPN lipids/amino acids → hepatotoxicity → bile duct inflammation<br />
无肠内摄入→↓CCK→胆囊淤滞；TPN脂质/氨基酸→肝毒性→胆管炎症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lab hallmark of cholestasis<br />
胆汁淤积实验室标志</td>
<td>↑Direct bilirubin, ↑ALP, ↑GGT; AST/ALT normal or only mildly elevated (key differentiator from hepatitis)<br />
↑直接胆红素，↑ALP，↑GGT；AST/ALT正常或仅轻度升高（与肝炎的关键鉴别）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors for TPN cholestasis<br />
TPN胆汁淤积危险因素</td>
<td>Short bowel syndrome, prolonged TPN duration, sepsis, prematurity (neonates especially vulnerable)<br />
短肠综合征、TPN持续时间长、脓毒症、早产（新生儿尤其易感）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment of TPN cholestasis<br />
TPN胆汁淤积的治疗</td>
<td>Transition to enteral feeding (even minimal enteral nutrition helps); ursodeoxycholic acid (UDCA); treat underlying sepsis<br />
过渡至肠内喂养（即使极少量肠内营养也有帮助）；熊去氧胆酸（UDCA）；治疗潜在脓毒症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Protein C deficiency clinical significance<br />
蛋白C缺乏临床意义</td>
<td>Hypercoagulable state; predisposes to venous thromboembolism including mesenteric vein thrombosis → bowel ischemia/infarction<br />
高凝状态；易发生静脉血栓栓塞，包括肠系膜静脉血栓→肠道缺血/梗死</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Warfarin + protein C deficiency warning<br />
华法林+蛋白C缺乏警告</td>
<td>Starting warfarin without heparin bridging → transient ↓protein C before ↓other clotting factors → paradoxical thrombosis and skin necrosis<br />
不用肝素桥接直接启用华法林→蛋白C在其他凝血因子降低前暂时下降→矛盾性血栓和皮肤坏死</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of conjugated hyperbilirubinemia:** Intrahepatic causes (TPN cholestasis, viral hepatitis, cirrhosis, drug-induced) vs. extrahepatic obstruction (choledocholithiasis, cholangiocarcinoma, pancreatic head mass, biliary stricture)\
  **结合型高胆红素血症鉴别:** 肝内原因（TPN胆汁淤积、病毒性肝炎、肝硬化、药物性）vs. 肝外梗阻（胆总管结石、胆管癌、胰头肿块、胆管狭窄）

- **Variant — neonatal TPN cholestasis:** Premature neonates on prolonged TPN develop cholestasis faster due to immature bile acid transport; early minimal enteral feeding is the preventive strategy\
  **题目变式——新生儿TPN胆汁淤积:** 长期TPN的早产儿因胆汁酸转运不成熟，胆汁淤积发展更快；早期极少量肠内喂养是预防策略

- **Key complication — biliary cirrhosis:** Prolonged TPN cholestasis → progressive hepatic fibrosis → biliary cirrhosis → portal hypertension; intestinal transplant may ultimately be required in end-stage short bowel\
  **关键并发症——胆汁性肝硬化:** 长期TPN胆汁淤积→进行性肝纤维化→胆汁性肝硬化→门脉高压；终末期短肠最终可能需要小肠移植

- **Cause of initial mesenteric infarction:** Protein C deficiency → hypercoagulability → mesenteric vein thrombosis → venous outflow obstruction → bowel infarction (venous, not arterial etiology)\
  **肠系膜梗死最初病因:** 蛋白C缺乏→高凝状态→肠系膜静脉血栓→静脉回流受阻→肠道梗死（静脉性，非动脉性病因）

# Question 91 — Postpartum Depression (Major Depressive Disorder with Peripartum Onset) / 产后抑郁症（围产期发作的重度抑郁障碍）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Eight weeks</strong> after an uncomplicated vaginal delivery of a healthy full-term newborn, a <strong>27-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 1, para 1, is brought to the physician by her husband because of a <strong>change in personality and depressed mood</strong> over the <strong>past 10 days</strong>. She has not had headaches. Her <strong>menses have not resumed</strong> despite the <strong>discontinuation of breast-feeding 5 weeks ago</strong>. Her husband says that she has <strong>no interest in sexual intercourse</strong>. She does not use illicit drugs. She has had a <strong>2.7-kg (6-lb) weight gain</strong> since delivery. She is now 175 cm (5 ft 9 in) tall and weighs 74 kg (164 lb); BMI is 24 kg/m². Physical and neurologic examinations show no abnormalities. On mental status examination, she has a <strong>flat affect</strong> and is <strong>slow to respond</strong> to questioning. She <strong>spontaneously cries</strong> during the interview and examination. She has no suicidal ideation. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) MRI of the brain<br />
B) Antipsychotic therapy<br />
C) Cyclic progestin therapy<br />
D) Estrogen therapy<br />
E) Selective serotonin reuptake inhibitor therapy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>8 weeks postpartum, uncomplicated delivery<br />
产后8周，分娩顺利</td>
<td>PPD onset can occur within 12 months of delivery; uncomplicated delivery excludes Sheehan's syndrome, which requires hemorrhage or hypovolemic shock<br />
PPD可在产后12个月内发病；分娩顺利排除席汉综合征（需大出血或低血容量性休克史）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Personality change + depressed mood × 10 days<br />
性格改变+情绪低落持续10天</td>
<td>Approaching the ≥2-week threshold for major depressive episode; warrants active treatment rather than watchful waiting<br />
接近重度抑郁发作≥2周诊断时限；需积极治疗而非观察等待</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Menses not resumed despite stopping breastfeeding 5 weeks ago<br />
停止哺乳5周后月经仍未恢复</td>
<td>Persistent HPO axis suppression from hormonal dysregulation; distinguishes from simple lactational amenorrhea, which resolves promptly after weaning<br />
激素失调导致HPO轴持续抑制；与单纯哺乳性闭经鉴别——后者断奶后很快恢复</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Flat affect, slow to respond, spontaneous crying<br />
情感平淡、反应迟钝、自发哭泣</td>
<td>Neurovegetative signs of major depression: psychomotor retardation and dysphoric affect are hallmarks<br />
重度抑郁的神经植物性体征：精神运动迟滞和焦虑性情感是标志性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No interest in sexual intercourse<br />
对性生活无兴趣</td>
<td>Anhedonia — a core diagnostic criterion for major depressive disorder<br />
快感缺失——重度抑郁障碍的核心诊断标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2.7-kg weight gain since delivery<br />
产后体重增加2.7千克</td>
<td>Atypical weight gain (not loss) suggests depressive hyperphagia or reduced activity; also argues against thyrotoxicosis<br />
非典型体重增加（而非减轻）提示抑郁性食欲亢进或活动减少；也有助于排除甲亢</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No hallucinations, delusions, or psychotic features<br />
无幻觉、妄想或精神病性症状</td>
<td>Rules out postpartum psychosis, which requires antipsychotic therapy and hospitalization<br />
排除产后精神病——后者需要抗精神病药和住院治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Postpartum depression** arises from the abrupt withdrawal of **estrogen and progesterone** following placental delivery, dysregulating **serotonergic and noradrenergic** pathways in vulnerable individuals:

**产后抑郁症**由胎盘娩出后**雌激素和孕激素**急剧撤退引发，在易感个体中导致**5-羟色胺能和去甲肾上腺素能**通路失调：

- Estrogen normally upregulates serotonin synthesis and receptor sensitivity; its withdrawal → decreased serotonergic tone → depressed mood, anhedonia\
  雌激素通常上调5-羟色胺合成和受体敏感性；其撤退 → 5-羟色胺能张力下降 → 抑郁情绪、快感缺失

- HPA axis dysregulation: postpartum cortisol and CRH fluctuations contribute to fatigue, mood instability, and disrupted sleep architecture\
  HPA轴失调：产后皮质醇和CRH波动导致疲劳、情绪不稳和睡眠结构紊乱

- Chronic sleep deprivation amplifies mood dysregulation and impairs prefrontal executive function\
  慢性睡眠剥夺放大情绪失调并损害前额叶执行功能

- Persistent amenorrhea in this patient reflects ongoing HPO axis suppression from residual hormonal imbalance, not a pituitary structural lesion\
  该患者持续闭经反映残余激素失衡导致的HPO轴持续抑制，而非垂体结构性病变

**Hormonal timeline rule of thumb:** Estrogen/progesterone fall within 24–48 hours of delivery; baby blues peak at days 3–5 and resolve by week 2; PPD develops days to weeks later and persists without treatment

**激素时间线小窍门:** 雌激素/孕激素在产后24-48小时内急剧下降；产后忧郁在第3-5天达峰并于第2周缓解；PPD在数天至数周后逐渐发展，未治疗时持续存在

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Selective Serotonin Reuptake Inhibitor Therapy / 正确答案 (E) — 选择性5-羟色胺再摄取抑制剂治疗

**SSRIs** are evidence-based first-line pharmacotherapy for moderate-to-severe postpartum depression with an established safety profile in postpartum women:

**SSRIs（选择性5-羟色胺再摄取抑制剂）**是循证医学支持的中重度产后抑郁一线药物，在产后女性中安全性已确立：

- SSRIs block presynaptic serotonin reuptake transporters (SERT) → increased synaptic serotonin → progressive mood elevation over 2–4 weeks\
  SSRIs阻断突触前5-羟色胺再摄取转运体（SERT）→ 突触间隙5-羟色胺增加 → 2-4周内情绪逐渐改善

- Sertraline and paroxetine are preferred in breastfeeding women due to minimal transfer into breast milk\
  舍曲林和帕罗西汀因转移至母乳量极少，在哺乳期女性中为首选

- This patient has already discontinued breastfeeding, eliminating infant exposure concerns entirely\
  该患者已停止哺乳，完全消除婴儿暴露顾虑

**Diagnosis:** Postpartum depression (major depressive disorder with peripartum onset) — depressed mood, anhedonia, flat affect, psychomotor retardation, weight change, and amenorrhea occurring 8 weeks after an uncomplicated delivery

**诊断:** 产后抑郁症（围产期发作的重度抑郁障碍）——产后8周出现抑郁情绪、快感缺失、情感平淡、精神运动迟滞、体重改变和闭经，分娩经过顺利

**Treatment:** SSRIs (sertraline first-line) ± CBT; brexanolone or zuranolone for severe/refractory cases; hospitalize immediately if suicidal ideation or thoughts of harming the infant are present

**治疗:** SSRI（舍曲林为首选）± 认知行为治疗；严重/难治性病例用布雷沙诺龙或祖拉诺酮；若有自杀意念或伤害婴儿想法则立即住院

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — MRI of the brain<br />
A — 脑部MRI</td>
<td>Wrong — MRI would evaluate for Sheehan's syndrome (postpartum pituitary necrosis), but that requires significant hemorrhage or hypovolemic shock at delivery plus signs of panhypopituitarism (agalactia, hypothyroidism, adrenal insufficiency); this patient had an uncomplicated delivery with none of these features<br />
错误——MRI用于评估席汉综合征（产后垂体坏死），但需要分娩时大出血或低血容量性休克加全垂体功能减退证据（无泌乳、甲减、肾上腺皮质功能不全）；该患者分娩顺利且无上述表现</td>
<td>Uncomplicated delivery + no panhypopituitarism signs → Sheehan's excluded<br />
分娩顺利+无全垂体功能减退迹象 → 排除席汉综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Antipsychotic therapy<br />
B — 抗精神病药治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — antipsychotics treat postpartum psychosis, which features hallucinations, delusions, and disorganized thinking or behavior; this patient has a classic depressive presentation without any psychotic features<br />
错误——抗精神病药治疗产后精神病，表现为幻觉、妄想和思维或行为紊乱；该患者为典型抑郁表现，无任何精神病性症状</td>
<td>No hallucinations or delusions → postpartum psychosis excluded<br />
无幻觉或妄想 → 排除产后精神病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cyclic progestin therapy<br />
C — 周期性孕激素治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — progestins may actually worsen PPD and increase its risk; this is a classic mechanism-trap because falling progesterone contributes to PPD onset, making progestin supplementation seem logical but counterproductive<br />
错误——孕激素实际上可能加重PPD并增加其风险；这是经典的机制陷阱，因为孕激素下降参与PPD发生，使孕激素补充看似合理但实为适得其反</td>
<td>Progestins ≠ PPD treatment; may worsen it<br />
孕激素不是PPD的治疗药物；可能加重病情</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Estrogen therapy<br />
D — 雌激素治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — estrogen has mechanistic plausibility and limited preclinical/clinical data supporting PPD treatment, but lacks RCT evidence and remains experimental; SSRIs have robust, replicated efficacy data<br />
错误——雌激素在机制上合理，且有有限的临床前/临床数据支持PPD治疗，但缺乏RCT证据，仍属实验性；而SSRI有充分、可重复的疗效数据</td>
<td>Experimental only; SSRIs are evidence-based standard of care<br />
仅属实验性；SSRI是循证医学支持的标准疗法</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Selective serotonin reuptake inhibitor therapy ✓<br />
E — 选择性5-羟色胺再摄取抑制剂治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — first-line pharmacotherapy for moderate-to-severe PPD backed by robust RCT evidence and guideline consensus<br />
正确——中重度PPD的一线药物治疗，有充分RCT证据和指南共识支持</td>
<td>Evidence-based first-line treatment for PPD<br />
PPD的循证一线治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice D (estrogen), as postpartum estrogen withdrawal is mechanistically central to PPD — but experimental plausibility does not equal clinical evidence, and SSRIs remain the validated standard.*

雌激素（选项D）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，因为产后雌激素撤退在机制上是PPD的核心——但机制上的合理性不等于临床证据，SSRI仍是经过验证的标准疗法。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A postpartum woman with depressed mood, flat affect, anhedonia, and psychomotor retardation — occurring after an uncomplicated delivery without psychotic features — has postpartum depression and should receive SSRIs as first-line treatment.**

**产后女性出现抑郁情绪、情感平淡、快感缺失和精神运动迟滞——发生于顺利分娩后且无精神病性症状——诊断为产后抑郁症，应首选SSRI治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PPD "SAD PAWS" / 记忆钩 — PPD"悲伤爪印 SAD PAWS":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>leep disturbance — insomnia or hypersomnia / 睡眠障碍——失眠或嗜睡<br />
• <strong>A</strong>nhedonia — loss of interest or pleasure / 快感缺失——兴趣或乐趣丧失<br />
• <strong>D</strong>epressed mood — the core criterion / 抑郁情绪——核心诊断标准<br />
• <strong>P</strong>sychomotor retardation or agitation / 精神运动迟滞或激越<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ppetite or weight change / 食欲或体重改变<br />
• <strong>W</strong>orthlessness or excessive guilt / 无价值感或过度罪恶感<br />
• <strong>S</strong>uicidal ideation — screen every patient / 自杀意念——每位患者均须筛查</p></th>
</tr>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Postpartum Depression: Diagnosis, Risk Factors, and Management / 高频知识表 — 产后抑郁症：诊断、危险因素与治疗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 peripartum onset specifier<br />
DSM-5围产期发病标注</td>
<td>Formally defined as onset during pregnancy or within 4 weeks of delivery; clinically and in USMLE contexts, "within 12 months" is widely accepted; requires ≥5 of 9 major depressive criteria for ≥2 weeks<br />
正式定义为妊娠期间或产后4周内发病；临床及USMLE中广泛接受"12个月内"；需满足9项重度抑郁标准中≥5项持续≥2周</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Edinburgh Postnatal Depression Scale<br />
爱丁堡产后抑郁量表（EPDS）</td>
<td>Validated 10-item self-report screening tool; score ≥13 suggests PPD; item 10 specifically screens for self-harm; recommended at 1- and 2-month well-child visits<br />
经验证的10项自评筛查工具；≥13分提示PPD；第10题专门筛查自我伤害；推荐在婴儿1个月和2个月健康检查时使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key risk factors<br />
主要危险因素</td>
<td>Prior depressive episode or PPD history (strongest predictor), lack of social support, sleep deprivation, relationship conflict, unplanned pregnancy, financial stress, breastfeeding difficulty<br />
既往抑郁发作或PPD史（最强预测因素）、缺乏社会支持、睡眠剥夺、关系冲突、意外妊娠、经济压力、哺乳困难</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SSRI selection in breastfeeding<br />
哺乳期SSRI选择</td>
<td>Sertraline and paroxetine: lowest breast milk transfer, undetectable in infant serum — preferred; fluoxetine: higher transfer, longer half-life, measurable infant levels — avoid if breastfeeding<br />
舍曲林和帕罗西汀：母乳转移量最低，婴儿血清中不可检测——首选；氟西汀：转移量较高、半衰期长、婴儿血药浓度可测——哺乳期避免使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Brexanolone and zuranolone<br />
布雷沙诺龙和祖拉诺酮</td>
<td>Both are synthetic neurosteroids (allopregnanolone analogues) that modulate GABA-A receptors; brexanolone (IV, 60-hour infusion, 2019 FDA approval); zuranolone (oral, 14-day course, 2023 FDA approval) — both PPD-specific<br />
均为合成神经甾体（变孕烷醇酮类似物），调节GABA-A受体；布雷沙诺龙（静脉注射，60小时输注，2019年FDA批准）；祖拉诺酮（口服，14天疗程，2023年FDA批准）——均专门针对PPD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Postpartum thyroiditis overlap<br />
产后甲状腺炎重叠</td>
<td>Hypothyroid phase of postpartum thyroiditis mimics PPD (fatigue, depression, weight gain); check TSH to distinguish; treat hypothyroidism if present, but coexisting depression still requires SSRIs<br />
产后甲状腺炎甲减期可模拟PPD（疲劳、抑郁、体重增加）；检查TSH以鉴别；若存在甲减则治疗，但共存抑郁仍需SSRI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Consequences of untreated PPD<br />
未治疗PPD的后果</td>
<td>Impaired maternal-infant bonding, developmental delays in the child, child neglect, suicide, infanticide; any suicidal or homicidal ideation warrants emergency psychiatric referral regardless of severity<br />
母婴联结受损、儿童发育迟缓、儿童忽视、自杀、杀婴；无论严重程度，任何自杀或杀婴意念均需紧急精神科转诊</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Sheehan's syndrome distinction:** Postpartum pituitary necrosis requires documented hemorrhage or hypovolemic shock at delivery plus evidence of panhypopituitarism (failure to lactate, hypothyroidism, adrenal insufficiency, low FSH/LH); MRI shows empty sella; the uncomplicated delivery in this case makes Sheehan's essentially impossible\
  **席汉综合征鉴别:** 产后垂体坏死需要有记录的分娩时大出血或低血容量性休克加全垂体功能减退证据（无法泌乳、甲减、肾上腺皮质功能不全、FSH/LH低）；MRI显示空泡蝶鞍；本题分娩顺利，实际上不可能为席汉综合征

- **Progestin trap mechanism:** Because progesterone withdrawal triggers PPD onset, examiners expect students to reason that "replace progesterone = treat PPD" — but clinical data show progestins worsen outcome; this makes Choice C a reliable exam distractor\
  **孕激素陷阱机制:** 由于孕激素撤退触发PPD发生，命题者预期学生会推断"补充孕激素=治疗PPD"——但临床数据显示孕激素使预后更差；这使选项C成为可靠的考试干扰项

- **Postpartum psychosis and bipolar link:** 70–80% of postpartum psychosis cases occur in women with underlying bipolar disorder; lithium prophylaxis started immediately after delivery reduces relapse risk in subsequent pregnancies; family history of bipolar is a key flag\
  **产后精神病与双相情感障碍的关联:** 70-80%的产后精神病发生在有潜在双相情感障碍的女性中；产后立即开始锂剂预防性治疗可降低后续妊娠的复发风险；双相情感障碍家族史是重要警示信号

- **Amenorrhea workup consideration:** Persistent amenorrhea 5 weeks after stopping breastfeeding prompts consideration of prolactinoma or hypothyroidism — but with a clear psychiatric presentation, these are secondary; if SSRIs do not resolve amenorrhea, check prolactin and TSH\
  **闭经的检查考量:** 停止哺乳5周后持续闭经提示考虑泌乳素瘤或甲状腺功能减退——但在明确精神科表现的背景下，这些属次要考虑；若SSRI治疗后闭经未缓解，应检查泌乳素和TSH

# Question 92 — Abruptio Placentae Complicating Preeclampsia / 子痫前期并发胎盘早剥

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A 32-year-old woman, gravida 3, para 2, at <strong>37 weeks' gestation</strong> is admitted to the hospital in labor. Contractions occur every 3 minutes. She has <strong>gained 2.3 kg (5 lb) during the past week</strong> and has had occasional <strong>blurred vision</strong>. She has been otherwise healthy. Her temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 80/min, respirations are 20/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 150/110 mm Hg</strong>. Physical examination shows <strong>retinal arteriolar spasm</strong> and pedal edema. The fundus is midway between the umbilicus and xiphoid. The cervix is 3 cm dilated and 100% effaced; the vertex is at 0 station. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 12.5 g/dL, Leukocyte count 8000/mm³, Platelet count 200,000/mm³, Serum creatinine 1.2 mg/dL, <strong>Urine protein 2+</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely complication during labor?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely complication during labor?</strong></p>
<p>A) Abruptio placentae<br />
B) Amniotic fluid embolism<br />
C) Arrest of labor<br />
D) Maternal death<br />
E) Uterine rupture</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>BP 150/110 mm Hg<br />
血压 150/110 mmHg</td>
<td>Meets hypertension criterion (≥140/90) for preeclampsia; both systolic and diastolic are elevated<br />
达到子痫前期高血压诊断标准（≥140/90 mmHg），收缩压与舒张压均升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Urine protein 2+<br />
尿蛋白 2+</td>
<td>Proteinuria confirms preeclampsia diagnosis; indicates glomerular endothelial injury<br />
蛋白尿确认子痫前期诊断，提示肾小球内皮损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blurred vision<br />
视力模糊</td>
<td>Severe feature of preeclampsia; reflects CNS and retinal vasospasm<br />
子痫前期重度特征，反映中枢神经系统和视网膜血管痉挛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gained 2.3 kg in past week<br />
过去一周体重增加 2.3 kg</td>
<td>Rapid fluid retention due to decreased colloid osmotic pressure from proteinuria and capillary leak<br />
因蛋白尿致胶体渗透压下降及毛细血管渗漏，导致快速液体潴留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Retinal arteriolar spasm<br />
视网膜小动脉痉挛</td>
<td>Direct ophthalmoscopic evidence of systemic vasospasm from endothelial dysfunction<br />
眼底镜下直接可见的全身血管痉挛证据，源于内皮功能障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>37 weeks, gravida 3, para 2<br />
孕 37 周，孕 3 产 2</td>
<td>Near-term multiparous woman — preeclampsia still occurs; multiparity reduces arrest of labor risk<br />
近足月经产妇——子痫前期仍可发生；多产史降低产程停滞的风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum creatinine 1.2 mg/dL<br />
血清肌酐 1.2 mg/dL</td>
<td>Mildly elevated for a pregnant woman (normal &lt;0.8 in pregnancy); indicates early renal involvement<br />
对孕妇而言轻度升高（孕期正常值 &lt;0.8）；提示早期肾脏受累</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Preeclampsia** arises from defective **trophoblastic invasion** of the spiral arteries, causing persistent high-resistance uteroplacental flow, **placental ischemia**, and release of anti-angiogenic factors (sFlt-1, sEng) that drive **generalized endothelial dysfunction** and **vasospasm**:

**子痫前期**源于螺旋动脉**滋养细胞浸润**缺陷，导致持续高阻力的子宫胎盘血流、**胎盘缺血**，并释放抗血管生成因子（sFlt-1、可溶性内皮糖蛋白），引发**全身内皮功能障碍**和**血管痉挛**：

- Defective spiral artery remodeling → high-resistance uteroplacental circulation → placental hypoperfusion and ischemia\
  螺旋动脉重塑缺陷 → 高阻力子宫胎盘循环 → 胎盘低灌注与缺血

- Ischemic placenta releases sFlt-1 → binds free VEGF and PlGF → systemic endothelial dysfunction → HTN + proteinuria + edema\
  缺血胎盘释放 sFlt-1 → 结合游离 VEGF 和 PlGF → 全身内皮功能障碍 → 高血压 + 蛋白尿 + 水肿

- Uteroplacental vasospasm → shearing stress on decidual vessels → decidual hemorrhage → retroplacental hematoma → abruptio placentae\
  子宫胎盘血管痉挛 → 蜕膜血管剪切应力 → 蜕膜出血 → 胎盘后血肿 → 胎盘早剥

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Abruptio placentae = premature separation of a normally implanted placenta from the uterine wall prior to delivery of the fetus; the placenta implants in the upper uterine segment, distinguishing it from placenta previa.

**解剖小窍门:** 胎盘早剥 = 胎儿娩出前正常位置胎盘的过早剥离；胎盘种植于子宫上段，这一点将其与前置胎盘区分开来。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Abruptio Placentae / 正确答案 (A) — 胎盘早剥

**Abruptio placentae** is the premature separation of a normally implanted placenta, and preeclampsia is one of its strongest risk factors via the mechanism of vasospasm-driven decidual hemorrhage:

**胎盘早剥**是正常位置胎盘的过早剥离，子痫前期通过血管痉挛诱发蜕膜出血的机制，是其最强危险因素之一：

- Preeclampsia-induced uteroplacental vasospasm → ischemic necrosis of decidua basalis → retroplacental hematoma formation\
  子痫前期诱发的子宫胎盘血管痉挛 → 底蜕膜缺血坏死 → 胎盘后血肿形成

- Classic triad: sudden severe uterine/abdominal pain + dark vaginal bleeding + tetanic uterine contractions ("board-like" or "woody" uterus)\
  经典三联征：突发剧烈宫体/腹部疼痛 + 暗红色阴道出血 + 强直性宫缩（"木板样"硬子宫）

- Fetal compromise (late decelerations, bradycardia) + maternal hemorrhagic shock may follow rapidly\
  胎儿受损（晚期减速、心动过缓）+ 产妇失血性休克可迅速随之发生

**Diagnosis:** Clinical presentation is primary; ultrasound may reveal retroplacental hematoma but has only ~50% sensitivity — a negative scan does NOT rule out abruption

**诊断:** 以临床表现为主；超声可发现胎盘后血肿，但敏感性仅约 50%——阴性结果不能排除早剥

**Treatment:** Immediate delivery (vaginal if maternal/fetal status allows; emergent cesarean for non-reassuring fetal status or maternal hemodynamic instability); IV access with blood products on standby; monitor for DIC (fibrinogen \<200 is earliest sign)

**治疗:** 立即分娩（母婴状况允许时经阴道分娩；胎儿状态不reassuring或产妇血流动力学不稳定时紧急剖宫产）；建立静脉通路并备血；监测 DIC（纤维蛋白原 \<200 是最早出现的指标）

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Abruptio placentae ✓<br />
A — 胎盘早剥 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Preeclampsia-induced vasospasm directly causes decidual hemorrhage and premature placental separation<br />
正确——子痫前期诱发血管痉挛，直接导致蜕膜出血和胎盘过早剥离</td>
<td>Mechanistic link: preeclampsia → endothelial injury → vasospasm → uteroplacental hemorrhage<br />
机制关联：子痫前期 → 内皮损伤 → 血管痉挛 → 子宫胎盘出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Amniotic fluid embolism<br />
B — 羊水栓塞</td>
<td>Rare, unpredictable catastrophic event; preeclampsia is NOT a recognized risk factor for AFE<br />
罕见且不可预测的灾难性事件；子痫前期不是羊水栓塞的公认危险因素</td>
<td>AFE risk factors: precipitous labor, multiparity, polyhydramnios, uterine overdistension — not hypertension or proteinuria<br />
羊水栓塞危险因素：急产、多产、羊水过多、子宫过度膨胀——与高血压或蛋白尿无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Arrest of labor<br />
C — 产程停滞</td>
<td>Patient is G3P2 (multiparous), which significantly decreases risk; no macrosomia or cephalopelvic disproportion suggested<br />
患者为孕 3 产 2（经产妇），风险显著降低；无巨大儿或头盆不称的提示</td>
<td>Arrest of labor is most common in nulliparous women or when CPD/macrosomia is present; multiparity is protective<br />
产程停滞最常见于初产妇或存在头盆不称/巨大儿时；多产史具有保护作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Maternal death<br />
D — 产妇死亡</td>
<td>Possible in uncontrolled eclampsia, but standard magnesium sulfate prophylaxis prevents seizure progression in most cases<br />
未控制的子痫时可能发生，但标准硫酸镁预防在大多数情况下能阻止癫痫发展</td>
<td>With appropriate management (Mg²⁺ + antihypertensives), abruption is a more proximate and likely acute labor complication than death<br />
经过适当处理（镁剂 + 降压药），胎盘早剥比死亡更为直接和可能的急性产程并发症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Uterine rupture<br />
E — 子宫破裂</td>
<td>Requires prior uterine scar (e.g., prior cesarean) or trauma history; this patient has no documented uterine surgery<br />
需要既往子宫瘢痕（如剖宫产史）或外伤史；该患者无子宫手术记录</td>
<td>Key sign of uterine rupture: sudden loss of fetal station + cessation of contractions + acute peritoneal pain; mechanism unrelated to preeclampsia<br />
子宫破裂关键体征：胎先露突然上升 + 宫缩停止 + 急性腹膜刺激痛；机制与子痫前期无关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (D) Maternal death — while preeclampsia can be fatal, the question asks about labor complications, and standard magnesium prophylaxis makes eclamptic seizure and death far less likely than the mechanistically direct complication of abruptio placentae.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是 (D) 产妇死亡——子痫前期确实可以致命，但题目询问的是产程中的并发症，标准硫酸镁预防使子痫癫痫发作和死亡的概率远低于机制上直接相关的胎盘早剥。
