## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a woman with preeclampsia (new-onset hypertension + proteinuria + CNS symptoms after 20 weeks), the most likely acute labor complication is abruptio placentae, driven by vasospasm-induced decidual hemorrhage at the uteroplacental interface.**

**在一位子痫前期女性（20 周后新发高血压 + 蛋白尿 + CNS 症状）中，最可能的急性产程并发症是胎盘早剥，由血管痉挛诱发的子宫胎盘界面蜕膜出血所驱动。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ABRUPT for Abruptio Placentae Risk Factors / 记忆钩 — "ABRUPT"记胎盘早剥危险因素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>dvanced HTN / preeclampsia — vasospasm tears the decidua / 高血压/子痫前期——血管痉挛撕裂蜕膜<br />
• <strong>B</strong>lunt abdominal trauma — physical force shears placenta off uterine wall / 腹部钝挫伤——外力将胎盘从子宫壁剪切分离<br />
• <strong>R</strong>apid uterine decompression — e.g., sudden amniotomy in polyhydramnios / 子宫快速减压——如羊水过多时骤然破膜<br />
• <strong>U</strong>se of cocaine or tobacco — vasoconstriction mimics preeclampsia mechanism / 可卡因或吸烟——血管收缩模拟子痫前期机制<br />
• <strong>P</strong>rior abruption — recurrence risk 6–17% after first, ~25% after second / 既往早剥史——首次后复发风险 6–17%，第二次后约 25%<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hrombophilia (antiphospholipid syndrome) — hypercoagulability damages placental vessels / 血栓形成倾向（抗磷脂综合征）——高凝状态损伤胎盘血管</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Preeclampsia & Abruptio Placentae / 高频知识表 — 子痫前期与胎盘早剥

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Preeclampsia diagnostic criteria<br />
子痫前期诊断标准</td>
<td>BP ≥140/90 on two readings ≥4 hours apart after 20 wk + proteinuria ≥300 mg/24h OR protein:creatinine ratio ≥0.3; or severe-range BP ≥160/110 alone<br />
20 周后两次间隔≥4 小时 BP≥140/90，加蛋白尿≥300 mg/24h 或蛋白/肌酐比≥0.3；或单独出现重度 BP≥160/110</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Severe features of preeclampsia<br />
子痫前期重度表现</td>
<td>BP ≥160/110; platelets &lt;100,000; Cr &gt;1.1; doubled transaminases or RUQ pain; pulmonary edema; new headache; visual disturbance<br />
BP≥160/110；血小板 &lt;10 万；肌酐 &gt;1.1；转氨酶倍增或右上腹痛；肺水肿；新发头痛；视觉障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Abruptio placentae vs. placenta previa<br />
胎盘早剥 vs. 前置胎盘</td>
<td>Abruption: painful dark bleeding + "woody" uterus + normal placental location; Previa: painless bright-red bleeding + soft uterus + placenta covers internal os<br />
早剥：有痛暗红出血 + "木板样"宫体 + 胎盘位置正常；前置：无痛鲜红出血 + 子宫软 + 胎盘覆盖宫颈内口</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Magnesium sulfate pharmacology<br />
硫酸镁药理学</td>
<td>Seizure prophylaxis (NOT antihypertensive); toxicity: loss of DTRs (first sign) → respiratory depression → cardiac arrest; therapeutic level 4–7 mEq/L; antidote: calcium gluconate 1 g IV<br />
预防癫痫（非降压）；毒性：腱反射消失（首要体征）→ 呼吸抑制 → 心搏骤停；治疗浓度 4–7 mEq/L；解毒药：葡萄糖酸钙 1 g 静推</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DIC in abruptio placentae<br />
胎盘早剥并发 DIC</td>
<td>Retroplacental hematoma releases thromboplastin → consumptive coagulopathy; fibrinogen drops first (most sensitive early marker; &lt;200 mg/dL is critical); treat with FFP, cryoprecipitate, delivery<br />
胎盘后血肿释放凝血活酶 → 消耗性凝血病；纤维蛋白原最先下降（最敏感早期指标；&lt;200 mg/dL 为危急值）；输注 FFP、冷沉淀并立即分娩</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Antihypertensives in preeclampsia<br />
子痫前期降压药</td>
<td>Acute: IV labetalol, IV hydralazine, or oral nifedipine for BP ≥160/110; goal SBP 140–155, DBP 90–105; avoid ACE inhibitors (teratogenic)<br />
急性期：BP≥160/110 时静推拉贝洛尔、肼屈嗪或口服硝苯地平；目标收缩压 140–155，舒张压 90–105；避免 ACEI（致畸）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Definitive treatment and timing<br />
根本治疗与时机</td>
<td>Delivery is the only cure; ≥37 wk: deliver regardless of severity; 34–37 wk: deliver if severe features; &lt;34 wk: may attempt expectant management with close monitoring if no severe features<br />
分娩是唯一根治方法；≥37 周：无论严重程度均分娩；34–37 周：有重度表现则分娩；&lt;34 周：无重度表现可在密切监测下尝试期待治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of painful antepartum bleeding:** Abruptio placentae (painful + dark blood + hypertonic uterus), uterine rupture (acute pain + loss of fetal station + cessation of contractions), vasa previa (painless fetal hemorrhage + sinusoidal FHR pattern at membrane rupture)\
  **产前有痛性出血鉴别:** 胎盘早剥（有痛 + 暗红血 + 宫体强直）、子宫破裂（急性疼痛 + 胎先露消失 + 宫缩停止）、前置血管（无痛性胎儿出血 + 破膜时正弦型胎心率）

- **Variant — Concealed abruption (~20%):** Blood collects entirely behind the placenta without external vaginal bleeding; presents with pain + uterine rigidity + fetal distress alone; can be more dangerous because hemorrhage volume is underestimated\
  **变式——隐性早剥（约 20%）:** 血液完全积聚于胎盘后方，无外部阴道出血；仅表现为疼痛 + 宫体强直 + 胎儿窘迫；因出血量被低估，可能更为危险

- **Key complication — Fetal exsanguination:** In severe abruption, fetal blood can enter the retroplacental hematoma; Kleihauer-Betke test detects fetal cells in maternal blood and guides Rh immune globulin dosing in Rh-negative mothers\
  **重要并发症——胎儿失血:** 严重早剥时胎儿血液可进入胎盘后血肿；Kleihauer-Betke 试验检测母血中胎儿细胞，指导 Rh 阴性产妇抗 D 免疫球蛋白剂量

- **Risk factor — Smoking:** Tobacco causes uteroplacental vasoconstriction via nicotine, doubling the risk of abruption; counseling on smoking cessation is a key prenatal preventive measure\
  **危险因素——吸烟:** 烟草通过尼古丁引起子宫胎盘血管收缩，使早剥风险翻倍；戒烟咨询是关键的产前预防措施

# Question 93 — Huntington Disease / 亨廷顿病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>32-year-old man</strong> is brought to the physician by his wife because of a <strong>gradual change in personality during the past 2 years</strong>. She describes him as <strong>less motivated and more self-centered</strong>. During the past year, he has had several <strong>angry outbursts that were triggered by minor events</strong>. The patient says that he does not believe his personality has changed and that <strong>he does not recall these events</strong>. He is alert and attentive. On examination, eye movements are full, but <strong>saccadic eye movements are noticeably slow</strong>. Smooth pursuit and vestibular ocular movements are normal. He has occasional <strong>involuntary rapid, jerk-like movements of the trunk and extremities</strong>, but he is <strong>unaware of these movements</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) EEG<br />
B) Follow-up examination in 1 month<br />
C) Genetic testing<br />
D) Lumbar puncture<br />
E) Measurement of serum ceruloplasmin concentration<br />
F) Psychiatric assessment</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>32-year-old man with 2 years of personality change<br />
32岁男性，2年性格改变</td>
<td>HD typically presents in the 3rd–6th decade; insidious psychiatric onset is the classic early presentation<br />
HD通常在30–60岁发病；隐匿起病的精神症状是经典早期表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Less motivated, self-centered, angry outbursts<br />
动力下降、自我中心、愤怒爆发</td>
<td>Frontal-striatal circuit disruption from caudate degeneration causes personality and behavioral disinhibition<br />
尾状核变性导致额叶-纹状体环路中断，引起人格及行为脱抑制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Does not recall events / lacks insight<br />
不记得发作 / 缺乏自知力</td>
<td>Anosognosia is a feature of HD cognitive impairment; patient is unaware of own symptoms<br />
病觉缺失是HD认知损害的特征；患者对自身症状缺乏认识</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Saccadic eye movements noticeably slow<br />
扫视眼动明显减慢</td>
<td>Slow saccades are an early and characteristic neurological sign of HD, reflecting caudate nucleus dysfunction before overt chorea<br />
扫视减慢是HD早期特征性神经体征，反映明显舞蹈病出现前的尾状核功能障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Involuntary rapid, jerk-like movements of trunk and extremities<br />
躯干及四肢不自主快速抽动</td>
<td>Classic chorea — the hallmark motor symptom of HD, caused by loss of striatal GABAergic inhibitory neurons<br />
经典舞蹈病——HD标志性运动症状，由纹状体GABAergic抑制性神经元丢失所致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Patient unaware of involuntary movements<br />
患者未察觉不自主运动</td>
<td>Consistent with HD anosognosia; also helps distinguish from psychogenic movement disorder<br />
符合HD的病觉缺失；也有助于与心因性运动障碍鉴别</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Huntington disease (HD)** is caused by expansion of a **CAG trinucleotide repeat** on chromosome 4p16.3 encoding the **huntingtin protein**. When repeats exceed ~36, mutant huntingtin becomes toxic to neurons:

**亨廷顿病（HD）**由4号染色体p16.3上编码**亨廷顿蛋白**的**CAG三核苷酸重复序列**异常扩增所致。当重复次数超过约36次时，突变亨廷顿蛋白对神经元产生毒性：

- Mutant huntingtin accumulates → mitochondrial dysfunction + oxidative stress → preferential degeneration of **GABAergic medium spiny neurons** in the striatum (caudate + putamen)\
  突变亨廷顿蛋白聚积→线粒体功能障碍+氧化应激→选择性导致纹状体（尾状核+壳核）**GABAergic中型多棘神经元**变性

- Loss of striatal GABAergic inhibition on GPe → **indirect pathway fails** → subthalamic nucleus suppressed → GPi less active → thalamus disinhibited → hyperkinetic movements (chorea)\
  纹状体GABAergic对苍白球外侧部抑制丧失→**间接通路失效**→底丘脑核受抑→内侧苍白球活性降低→丘脑去抑制→运动亢进（舞蹈病）

- Caudate degeneration disrupts frontal-striatal circuits → **psychiatric and cognitive symptoms** (personality change, impulsivity, irritability, anosognosia)\
  尾状核变性破坏额叶-纹状体环路→**精神及认知症状**（人格改变、冲动、易激惹、病觉缺失）

- Slow saccades reflect early caudate/striatal dysfunction — a pre-chorea neurological sign\
  扫视减慢反映早期尾状核/纹状体功能障碍——舞蹈病前期神经体征

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Caudate atrophy → "box-car" lateral ventricles on MRI — the classic neuroimaging finding in HD.

**解剖小窍门:** 尾状核萎缩→MRI侧脑室呈"车厢样"外观——HD经典神经影像表现。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Genetic Testing for Huntington Disease / 正确答案 (C) — 亨廷顿病基因检测

**Genetic testing** (CAG repeat analysis) is the definitive confirmatory test for HD and the most appropriate next step when clinical features strongly point to this diagnosis:

**基因检测**（CAG重复次数分析）是HD的最终确诊手段，当临床特征高度指向本病时，这是最合适的下一步：

- CAG repeat ≥36 on chromosome 4p16.3 confirms HD; ≥40 repeats = full penetrance; 36–39 = reduced penetrance\
  4号染色体p16.3 CAG重复≥36次即可确诊HD；≥40次=完全外显；36–39次=外显率降低

- Autosomal dominant inheritance — one mutant allele is sufficient to cause disease\
  常染色体显性遗传——单个突变等位基因即可致病

- Anticipation: repeat length increases with successive generations → earlier onset and/or more severe disease in offspring\
  遗传早现：重复次数逐代增加→后代发病更早和/或病情更重

- This patient shows the classic sequence: psychiatric symptoms → slow saccades → chorea, before significant cognitive decline\
  该患者呈现经典顺序：精神症状→扫视减慢→舞蹈病，出现在明显认知衰退之前

**Diagnosis:** Clinical suspicion based on progressive psychiatric + motor signs in a young adult; confirmed by CAG repeat analysis (\>36 repeats) on genetic testing.

**诊断:** 根据年轻成人进行性精神及运动体征临床怀疑；通过基因检测CAG重复次数分析（\>36次）确诊。

**Treatment:** Symptomatic — tetrabenazine or deutetrabenazine (VMAT2 inhibitors, deplete presynaptic dopamine → reduce chorea); antidepressants/antipsychotics for psychiatric symptoms; no disease-modifying therapy currently available.

**治疗:** 对症治疗——丁苯那嗪或氘代丁苯那嗪（VMAT2抑制剂，耗竭突触前多巴胺→减轻舞蹈病）；抗抑郁/抗精神病药治疗精神症状；目前无疾病修饰疗法。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — EEG<br />
A — 脑电图</td>
<td>EEG evaluates seizure activity; involuntary jerk-like movements here are chorea, not epileptic myoclonus — no clinical features suggest epilepsy<br />
脑电图评估癫痫发作；此处不自主抽动为舞蹈病，非癫痫性肌阵挛——无临床特征提示癫痫</td>
<td>Chorea flows unpredictably between muscle groups; myoclonus is synchronous, stereotyped, and associated with altered consciousness<br />
舞蹈病在肌群间不规则游走；肌阵挛则同步刻板，常伴意识改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Follow-up examination in 1 month<br />
B — 1个月后随访</td>
<td>Delaying diagnosis is inappropriate given clear neurological abnormalities (chorea, slow saccades) and 2 years of functional impairment already documented<br />
鉴于明确的神经系统异常（舞蹈病、扫视减慢）及已记录的2年功能损害，延误诊断不合适</td>
<td>Objective motor findings on exam require prompt workup, not watchful waiting<br />
体格检查发现的客观运动体征需要及时评估，而非观察等待</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Genetic testing ✓<br />
C — 基因检测 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — CAG trinucleotide repeat analysis on chromosome 4 is the definitive test for this classic HD presentation with psychiatric onset, slow saccades, and chorea<br />
正确——4号染色体CAG三核苷酸重复分析是本例经典HD表现（精神症状起病、扫视减慢、舞蹈病）的确诊检测手段</td>
<td>Classic HD triad in a 30s patient makes genetic testing the unambiguous next step<br />
30多岁患者的经典HD三联征使基因检测成为明确的下一步</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Lumbar puncture<br />
D — 腰椎穿刺</td>
<td>LP is useful for CNS infections (neurosyphilis), MS, GBS, or SAH — none suggested here; progressive familial-pattern presentation points to genetics, not inflammation<br />
腰穿适用于CNS感染（神经梅毒）、MS、GBS或SAH——此处均无提示；进行性家族性表现指向遗传学而非炎症</td>
<td>No fever, meningismus, acute presentation, or signs pointing to infectious/inflammatory CNS disease<br />
无发热、脑膜刺激征、急性起病或提示感染/炎症性CNS疾病的体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Measurement of serum ceruloplasmin concentration<br />
E — 血清铜蓝蛋白浓度测定</td>
<td>Tests for Wilson disease — can mimic HD with psychiatric + movement symptoms, but typically presents with Kayser-Fleischer rings, liver disease, and earlier onset<br />
检测Wilson病——可因精神+运动症状模拟HD，但通常伴K-F环、肝脏疾病，且发病更早</td>
<td>Absence of Kayser-Fleischer rings and liver involvement; slow saccades + chorea without other Wilson features favors HD and genetic testing<br />
无K-F环及肝脏受累；扫视减慢+舞蹈病而无其他Wilson特征，支持HD并行基因检测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Psychiatric assessment<br />
F — 精神科评估</td>
<td>Objective motor abnormalities (chorea, slow saccades) clearly indicate organic neurological pathology — psychiatric-first workup risks misdiagnosis and delays appropriate testing<br />
客观运动异常（舞蹈病、扫视减慢）明确提示器质性神经系统病变——优先精神评估有误诊风险并延误适当检查</td>
<td>Organic neurological disease must be ruled out before attributing symptoms to primary psychiatric illness<br />
在将症状归因于原发性精神疾病之前，必须排除器质性神经系统疾病</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Wilson disease (Choice E) is the highest-yield distractor — it shares psychiatric symptoms, movement disorder, and young onset with HD, but the absence of Kayser-Fleischer rings and liver disease, combined with the characteristic slow saccades of HD, tips the balance decisively toward genetic testing.*

Wilson病（选项E）是本题最高价值干扰项——它与HD共享精神症状、运动障碍及年轻发病年龄，但缺乏K-F环和肝脏病变，加上HD特征性扫视减慢，使天平决定性地倾向基因检测。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A young adult with insidious personality change, angry outbursts, slow saccades, and chorea has Huntington disease — diagnosed by CAG trinucleotide repeat expansion on chromosome 4.**

**年轻成人出现隐匿性人格改变、愤怒爆发、扫视减慢及舞蹈病，诊断为亨廷顿病——通过4号染色体CAG三核苷酸重复扩增确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PACE of Huntington Disease / 记忆钩 — HD的"PACE"四步进展:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>sychiatric first — personality change, irritability, apathy precede motor symptoms by years / 精神先行——人格改变、易激惹、淡漠早于运动症状数年<br />
• <strong>A</strong>utosomal dominant + <strong>A</strong>nticipation — CAG repeats on chromosome 4 expand with each generation / 常染色体显性+遗传早现——4号染色体CAG重复逐代扩增<br />
• <strong>C</strong>horea + slow saccades — involuntary dance-like jerks; saccade slowing is the earliest objective motor sign / 舞蹈病+扫视减慢——不自主舞动；扫视减慢是最早客观运动体征<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xpansion kills striatum — mutant huntingtin → striatal GABAergic neuron death → thalamic disinhibition / 扩增毁纹状体——突变亨廷顿蛋白→纹状体GABAergic神经元死亡→丘脑去抑制</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Huntington Disease / 高频知识表 — 亨廷顿病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Genetics<br />
遗传学</td>
<td>Autosomal dominant; CAG repeat on chr 4p16.3; &gt;36 = disease (36–39 reduced penetrance; ≥40 full penetrance); anticipation — paternal transmission more commonly causes large expansions (juvenile HD)<br />
常染色体显性；4号染色体p16.3 CAG重复；&gt;36次=致病（36–39次外显率降低；≥40次完全外显）；遗传早现——父系传递更易导致大幅扩增（青少年型HD）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic presentation order<br />
经典表现顺序</td>
<td>Psychiatric (irritability, apathy, depression) → Motor (chorea, slow saccades, dystonia) → Cognitive decline (dementia) → Death 10–40 years after onset<br />
精神症状（易激惹、淡漠、抑郁）→运动症状（舞蹈病、扫视减慢、肌张力障碍）→认知衰退（痴呆）→发病后10–40年死亡</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chorea pathophysiology<br />
舞蹈病病理生理</td>
<td>Loss of striatal indirect pathway GABAergic neurons → GPe disinhibited → subthalamic nucleus suppressed → GPi less active → thalamus disinhibited → hyperkinesia<br />
纹状体间接通路GABAergic神经元丢失→GPe去抑制→底丘脑核受抑→GPi活性降低→丘脑去抑制→运动亢进</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Slow saccades as early sign<br />
扫视减慢作为早期体征</td>
<td>Voluntary rapid eye movements; slowing reflects early caudate dysfunction; smooth pursuit and VOR are preserved in early HD — a key distinguishing feature on exam<br />
自主性快速眼动；减慢反映早期尾状核功能障碍；早期HD平稳追踪和前庭眼反射保留——体格检查中的关键鉴别特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment of chorea<br />
舞蹈病治疗</td>
<td>Tetrabenazine or deutetrabenazine — VMAT2 inhibitors depleting presynaptic dopamine stores; FDA-approved for HD chorea; caution: can worsen depression and suicidality<br />
丁苯那嗪或氘代丁苯那嗪——VMAT2抑制剂耗竭突触前多巴胺储存；FDA批准用于HD舞蹈病；注意：可加重抑郁及自杀倾向</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neuroimaging findings<br />
神经影像表现</td>
<td>Caudate nucleus atrophy → "box-car" appearance of lateral ventricles on MRI (frontal horns appear expanded due to adjacent caudate volume loss)<br />
尾状核萎缩→MRI侧脑室呈"车厢样"外观（额角因邻近尾状核体积减少而显扩大）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Trinucleotide repeat anticipation<br />
三核苷酸重复遗传早现</td>
<td>During DNA replication, polymerase slips → more CAG copies incorporated; longer repeats → earlier onset and more severe disease in successive generations<br />
DNA复制时聚合酶滑脱→纳入更多CAG拷贝；重复次数越长→后续世代发病越早、病情越重</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Juvenile HD (Westphal variant):** occurs with CAG repeats \>60 (often via paternal transmission), presents before age 20 with rigidity and bradykinesia (parkinsonism phenotype) rather than chorea — the motor presentation is essentially reversed\
  **青少年型HD（Westphal变异型）:** CAG重复\>60次（常经父系传递），20岁前发病，表现为强直和运动迟缓（帕金森综合征表型）而非舞蹈病——运动表现基本相反

- **Other trinucleotide repeat disorders:** Myotonic dystrophy (CTG, chr 19, AD), Friedreich ataxia (GAA, chr 9, AR), Fragile X syndrome (CGG, chr X, XLD), Kennedy disease/SBMA (CAG, chr X, XLR) — each disorder has a unique repeat, locus, and inheritance pattern\
  **其他三核苷酸重复病：** 强直性肌营养不良（CTG，19号染色体，AD），Friedreich共济失调（GAA，9号染色体，AR），脆性X综合征（CGG，X染色体，XLD），Kennedy病/SBMA（CAG，X染色体，XLR）——每种疾病有独特的重复序列、位点和遗传方式

- **Ethical considerations in presymptomatic genetic testing:** HD testing requires genetic counseling; a positive result in an asymptomatic person has profound implications for insurance, reproductive planning, and mental health; testing of at-risk minors is generally deferred\
  **症状前基因检测的伦理考量：** HD检测需要遗传咨询；无症状者阳性结果对保险、生育计划和心理健康影响深远；通常推迟对高风险未成年人进行检测

- **Wilson disease rule-out:** When HD presentation is atypical (age \<30, liver abnormalities, Kayser-Fleischer rings, or tremor \> chorea), always measure ceruloplasmin and perform slit-lamp examination before concluding genetic HD — Wilson disease is treatable with copper chelation\
  **Wilson病排除原则：** 当HD表现不典型时（年龄\<30岁、肝脏异常、K-F环或震颤\>舞蹈病），应在确诊遗传性HD前始终测量铜蓝蛋白并行裂隙灯检查——Wilson病可通过铜螯合剂治疗

# Question 94 — Imperforate Hymen / 处女膜闭锁

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>12-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician by her mother because of a <strong>2-month history</strong> of increasing, <strong>constant, throbbing pain and pressure in the pelvic area</strong>. She has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. She has <strong>never had a menstrual period</strong>. She follows a normal diet and takes gymnastics lessons weekly. She is at the 50th percentile for height, weight, and BMI. Vital signs are within normal limits. Breast and pubic hair development are <strong>sexual maturity rating (SMR) stage 3</strong>. Examination of the external genitalia shows a <strong>bluish bulge of tissue</strong> between a normal-appearing urethra and anus. Serum studies show: Follicle-stimulating hormone 12 mIU/mL, Luteinizing hormone 15 mIU/mL, <strong>Estradiol 50 pg/mL (N=30–400)</strong>, Prolactin 10 ng/mL. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bartholin duct cyst<br />
B) Cervical stenosis<br />
C) Imperforate hymen<br />
D) Ovarian cancer<br />
E) Sarcoma botryoides</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>12-year-old girl, never had a menstrual period<br />
12岁女孩，从未来过月经</td>
<td>Primary amenorrhea in a pubertal girl suggests outflow tract obstruction or hormonal failure; normal hormones here point to anatomic obstruction<br />
青春期女孩原发性闭经提示流出道梗阻或激素异常；此处激素正常，指向解剖性梗阻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SMR stage 3 breast and pubic hair development<br />
乳房和阴毛发育 SMR 3期</td>
<td>Confirms puberty is progressing normally — HPO axis is intact and estrogen is being produced; blood IS made but cannot exit<br />
证实青春期正常进行，HPO轴完整且雌激素正在产生；月经血已产生但无法排出</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bluish bulge of tissue between urethra and anus<br />
尿道与肛门之间的蓝色隆起</td>
<td>Pathognomonic of hematocolpos behind an imperforate hymen — deoxygenated blood distends and shines through the thin hymeneal membrane<br />
处女膜闭锁后血液积聚于阴道（血阴道积血）的特征性表现——脱氧血液撑大并透过薄薄的处女膜</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Constant, throbbing pelvic pain for 2 months<br />
持续性搏动性盆腔疼痛2个月</td>
<td>Cyclical menstrual blood accumulation causes progressive distension pain; "2 months" = approximately 2 obstructed cycles<br />
月经血周期性积聚引起进行性膨胀性疼痛；"2个月"≈约2个被梗阻的月经周期</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal FSH, LH, Estradiol, Prolactin<br />
FSH、LH、雌二醇、催乳素均正常</td>
<td>Rules out gonadal dysgenesis (↑FSH/LH), hypothalamic amenorrhea (↓FSH/LH), and prolactinoma; confirms intact HPO axis with pure outflow obstruction<br />
排除性腺发育不全（FSH/LH升高）、下丘脑性闭经（FSH/LH偏低）和催乳素瘤；确认HPO轴完整，为单纯流出道梗阻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>50th percentile BMI, gymnastics weekly<br />
BMI 50百分位，每周体操课</td>
<td>Rules out exercise-induced hypothalamic amenorrhea (would need underweight/very intense training); these are deliberate distractors<br />
排除运动性下丘脑闭经（需低体重/极高强度训练）；这些是刻意设置的干扰信息</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **imperforate hymen** is a congenital anomaly where the **hymeneal membrane** fails to undergo canalization during fetal development, leaving the vaginal introitus completely occluded by an intact membrane:

**处女膜闭锁**是先天性异常，**处女膜**在胎儿发育过程中未能完成管道化，导致阴道口被完整膜性结构完全封闭：

- The hymen normally forms at the junction of the urogenital sinus and Müllerian duct system, then perforates under estrogen stimulation; in imperforate hymen, this perforation never occurs\
  处女膜正常形成于泌尿生殖窦与米勒管系统交界处，在雌激素刺激下穿孔；处女膜闭锁时此穿孔过程从未发生

- Once menstruation begins, blood accumulates sequentially: **hematocolpos** (vagina distended by blood) → **hematometra** (uterus) → **hematosalpinx** (fallopian tubes)\
  月经一旦开始，血液依次积聚：**血阴道积血**（血液撑大阴道）→**宫腔积血**（子宫）→**输卵管积血**（输卵管）

- The trapped **deoxygenated blood** distends the thin hymeneal tissue and creates the characteristic blue, bulging, translucent appearance at the introitus\
  积聚的**脱氧血液**撑大薄薄的处女膜并在阴道口形成特征性蓝色、膨出、半透明外观

- The pelvic pain is **cyclical** in nature — corresponding to each menstrual cycle — but may feel "constant" as hematocolpos expands continuously between cycles\
  盆腔疼痛本质上是**周期性**的——与每个月经周期对应——但随着血阴道积血在周期间持续扩大可感觉"持续性"

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The retrograde sequence hematocolpos → hematometra → hematosalpinx means delayed treatment risks tubal scarring, endometriosis from retrograde flow, and long-term infertility.

**解剖小窍门:** 血阴道积血→宫腔积血→输卵管积血的逆行顺序意味着延误治疗会导致输卵管瘢痕、逆流引起的子宫内膜异位症和长期不孕。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Imperforate Hymen / 正确答案 (C) — 处女膜闭锁

**Imperforate hymen** is the most common obstructive anomaly of the female genital tract, presenting classically at puberty with the triad of primary amenorrhea, cyclical pelvic pain, and a bluish introital bulge:

**处女膜闭锁**是女性生殖道最常见的梗阻性异常，典型表现为青春期原发性闭经、周期性盆腔疼痛和蓝色阴道口隆起三联征：

- Normal secondary sexual development (SMR 3) with normal FSH, LH, and estradiol confirms the HPO axis is functioning — this is not a hormonal problem\
  继发性性征正常（SMR 3期）且FSH、LH、雌二醇正常，确认HPO轴功能正常——这不是激素问题

- The **bluish midline bulge** at the introitus is caused by hematocolpos visible through the distended, vascularized hymeneal membrane — this finding alone is virtually diagnostic\
  阴道口**蓝色中线隆起**由透过充血扩张的处女膜可见的血阴道积血所致——此体征单独即近乎诊断性

- Pelvic ultrasound will show an echogenic fluid collection in the vagina (hematocolpos) and possibly extending into the uterus (hematometra)\
  盆腔超声将显示阴道内回声性液体积聚（血阴道积血），可能延伸至子宫（宫腔积血）

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis confirmed by pelvic ultrasound; the blue bulging membrane at the introitus is essentially pathognomonic and does not require invasive workup before surgical planning.

**诊断:** 临床诊断经盆腔超声确认；阴道口蓝色膨出膜基本上具有病理诊断意义，手术规划前无需侵入性检查。

**Treatment:** Hymenotomy under anesthesia — cruciate (cross-shaped) incision to drain accumulated hematocolpos and create a permanent patent opening; prognosis for fertility is excellent with timely treatment.

**治疗:** 麻醉下处女膜切开术——十字形切口引流积聚的血阴道积血并建立永久性通畅开口；及时治疗后生育预后良好。

<tr>
<td>A — Bartholin duct cyst<br />
A — 巴氏腺导管囊肿</td>
<td>Bartholin glands sit laterally at the 4 and 8 o'clock positions of the introitus — not midline. Do not cause amenorrhea, cyclical pain, or hematocolpos<br />
巴氏腺位于阴道口4点和8点外侧位置——非中线。不引起闭经、周期性疼痛或血阴道积血</td>

<td>Could cause hematometra and cyclical pain, but produces NO visible introital bulge — the obstruction is internal at the cervix; typically acquired (post-procedure/radiation), not congenital in a 12-year-old<br />
可引起宫腔积血和周期性疼痛，但不产生可见的阴道口隆起——梗阻位于宫颈内部；通常为继发性（手术/放疗后），12岁女孩不应出现</td>

正确——经典三联征：激素正常的青春期女孩原发性闭经+周期性盆腔疼痛+蓝色中线阴道口隆起=处女膜闭锁致血阴道积血</td>
<td>All findings converge on outflow obstruction with intact HPO axis<br />
所有表现均指向HPO轴完整的流出道梗阻</td>

<td>Uncommon before menarche; presents as ovarian mass on imaging, not introital bulge; does not cause hematocolpos; functional tumors may cause hormonal abnormalities, not normal levels<br />
初潮前少见；表现为影像学卵巢肿块而非阴道口隆起；不引起血阴道积血；功能性肿瘤可致激素异常而非正常水平</td>
<td>Ovarian mass on imaging; no introital bulge; abnormal hormones expected<br />
影像学卵巢肿块；无阴道口隆起；预期激素异常</td>
</tr>

<td>E — Sarcoma botryoides<br />
E — 葡萄状肉瘤</td>
<td>Embryonal rhabdomyosarcoma presenting in children &lt;3 years old with grape-like polypoid vaginal mass and vaginal bleeding — not amenorrhea; this 12-year-old is completely outside the expected age range<br />
胚胎型横纹肌肉瘤发生于3岁以下幼儿，表现为葡萄样息肉状阴道肿块及阴道出血——非闭经；12岁完全超出预期年龄范围</td>
<td>Age &lt;3 years; vaginal bleeding not amenorrhea; polypoid grape-like mass<br />
年龄&lt;3岁；阴道出血而非闭经；葡萄样息肉状肿块</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is cervical stenosis (B) — it can explain the pain and even hematometra, but cannot explain the visible bluish introital bulge, which is the decisive physical finding here.*

最危险的干扰项是宫颈狭窄（B选项）——它能解释疼痛甚至宫腔积血，但无法解释可见的蓝色阴道口隆起，后者是此处决定性的体征。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A pubertal girl with normal hormones, primary amenorrhea, cyclical pelvic pain, and a bluish introital bulge has imperforate hymen with hematocolpos until proven otherwise.**

**青春期女孩激素正常、原发性闭经、周期性盆腔疼痛伴蓝色阴道口隆起，在排除其他诊断之前应视为处女膜闭锁伴血阴道积血。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "BLUE" Clues for Imperforate Hymen / 记忆钩 — 处女膜闭锁的"BLUE"四要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>lue bulge at the introitus — the pathognomonic physical finding / 阴道口蓝色隆起——特征性体征<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ack of periods (primary amenorrhea) despite normal puberty (SMR 3) / 尽管青春期正常（SMR 3期）仍缺乏月经（原发性闭经）<br />
• <strong>U</strong>ltrasound shows hematocolpos — echogenic fluid filling the vagina / 超声显示血阴道积血——回声性液体充满阴道<br />
• <strong>E</strong>strogen and all hormones normal — HPO axis intact, the blood is made but cannot exit / 雌激素及所有激素正常——HPO轴完整，月经血产生但无法排出</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Imperforate Hymen & Primary Amenorrhea Workup / 高频知识表 — 处女膜闭锁与原发性闭经检查

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Embryologic origin<br />
胚胎学来源</td>
<td>Hymen forms at junction of urogenital sinus and Müllerian system; imperforate hymen results from failure of sinovaginal bulb canalization — no perforation forms<br />
处女膜形成于泌尿生殖窦与米勒管系统交界处；处女膜闭锁源于阴道球管道化失败——穿孔未能形成</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epidemiology<br />
流行病学</td>
<td>Most common obstructive anomaly of female genital tract; incidence ~1:1,000–2,000 female births; usually sporadic<br />
女性生殖道最常见梗阻性异常；发生率约1:1,000-2,000女婴；通常散发性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hematocolpos progression sequence<br />
血阴道积血进展顺序</td>
<td>Hematocolpos (vagina) → hematometra (uterus) → hematosalpinx (tubes) → retrograde flow → endometriosis + infertility if untreated<br />
血阴道积血（阴道）→宫腔积血（子宫）→输卵管积血（输卵管）→逆行流→未治疗致子宫内膜异位症+不孕</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary amenorrhea: hormone-based workup approach<br />
原发性闭经：基于激素的检查方法</td>
<td>↑FSH/LH → gonadal failure (Turner syndrome); ↓FSH/LH → hypothalamic/pituitary cause; Normal FSH/LH + normal E2 → anatomic obstruction or androgen insensitivity<br />
FSH/LH升高→性腺衰竭（特纳综合征）；FSH/LH偏低→下丘脑/垂体原因；FSH/LH正常+雌二醇正常→解剖性梗阻或雄激素不敏感</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard workup<br />
标准检查流程</td>
<td>Pelvic ultrasound first — shows echogenic fluid in vagina; MRI if anatomy is unclear or septum suspected; no invasive testing needed before ultrasound<br />
首选盆腔超声——显示阴道内回声性液体；解剖不清或怀疑横隔时行MRI；超声前无需侵入性检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surgical treatment details<br />
手术治疗细节</td>
<td>Hymenotomy under general anesthesia; cruciate (cross-shaped) incision drains hematocolpos; edges sutured to prevent re-closure; fertility prognosis excellent with timely treatment<br />
全麻下处女膜切开术；十字形切口引流血阴道积血；边缘缝合防止再次闭合；及时治疗后生育预后极佳</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why NOT do biopsy or needle aspiration<br />
为何不做活检或针刺引流</td>
<td>Risk of introducing infection into sterile hematocolpos (iatrogenic pyocolpos); always proceed to formal surgical hymenotomy in operating room<br />
有将感染引入无菌血阴道积血的风险（医源性脓阴道积血）；应始终在手术室进行正式手术处女膜切开术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of primary amenorrhea with normal hormones:** Imperforate hymen, transverse vaginal septum, Müllerian agenesis (MRKH syndrome — absent uterus/upper vagina), and complete androgen insensitivity syndrome (46,XY, no uterus, testes present)\
  **激素正常的原发性闭经鉴别:** 处女膜闭锁、阴道横隔、米勒管发育不全（MRKH综合征——无子宫/阴道上段）和完全型雄激素不敏感综合征（46,XY，无子宫，存在睾丸）

- **Variant — Microperforated hymen:** Small opening present; may allow passage of some discharge but not menstrual blood; presents similarly but with slower blood accumulation and more subtle bulge; treated similarly with hymenotomy\
  **题目变式——微穿孔处女膜:** 存在小开口；可允许部分分泌物通过但月经血不能；表现类似但血液积聚较慢、隆起较不明显；同样行处女膜切开术治疗

- **Key complication if untreated beyond months:** Retrograde menstruation via fallopian tubes creates peritoneal implants → endometriosis, pelvic adhesions, secondary infertility; early diagnosis at puberty is therefore critical\
  **数月内未治疗的关键并发症:** 经输卵管逆行的月经血在腹膜形成种植灶→子宫内膜异位症、盆腔粘连、继发性不孕；因此青春期早期诊断至关重要

- **Risk factor distinction — MRKH vs imperforate hymen:** Both have primary amenorrhea + normal hormones, but MRKH has NO uterus on ultrasound and NO introital bulge; imperforate hymen has uterus present (distended with blood) and the classic blue bulge\
  **鉴别要点——MRKH综合征vs处女膜闭锁:** 两者均有原发性闭经+激素正常，但MRKH超声无子宫且无阴道口隆起；处女膜闭锁有子宫（充满血液而扩张）且有经典蓝色隆起

# Question 95 — Normal Female Pubertal Development / 正常女性青春期发育

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>9-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician by her father for a well-child examination. He is concerned that she is <strong>beginning to develop breasts at an early age</strong>. <strong>Menarche has not occurred</strong>. Her mother's menarche began at the age of <strong>12 years</strong>. The patient is at the <strong>75th percentile for height</strong> and <strong>50th percentile for weight</strong>. <strong>Breast development is sexual maturity rating (SMR) stage 2</strong>, and <strong>pubic hair development is SMR stage 1</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Reassurance<br />
B) Measurement of serum estrogen concentration<br />
C) Measurement of serum follicle-stimulating hormone concentration<br />
D) X-ray of the wrist to assess bone age<br />
E) Transvaginal ultrasonography<br />
F) Pelvic examination</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>9-year-old girl<br />
9岁女孩</td>
<td>Precocious puberty in females = onset before age 8; age 9 is within the normal puberty range (9–12 years)<br />
女性性早熟定义为8岁前出现第二性征；9岁属正常青春期范围（9~12岁）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SMR stage 2 breast development<br />
乳房发育 SMR 2期</td>
<td>Thelarche (breast budding) is the first sign of normal female puberty; SMR stage 2 onset at age 8–13 is normal<br />
乳芽期是女性正常青春期的第一征象；8~13岁出现SMR 2期属正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SMR stage 1 pubic hair<br />
阴毛发育 SMR 1期</td>
<td>Stage 1 = no pubic hair present; pubarche follows thelarche in normal sequence<br />
1期 = 无阴毛；阴毛初现在正常青春期中晚于乳芽期出现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Menarche has not occurred<br />
尚未月经初潮</td>
<td>Menarche typically occurs 2–3 years after thelarche (at SMR stage 4); absence is expected at SMR stage 2<br />
月经初潮通常在乳芽期后2~3年（SMR 4期）出现；SMR 2期时尚未来潮属正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal height/weight percentiles<br />
身高体重百分位数正常</td>
<td>Argues against pathologic causes such as adrenal tumor or growth-accelerating endocrinopathy<br />
排除病理性原因，如肾上腺肿瘤或导致生长加速的内分泌疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mother's menarche at age 12<br />
母亲12岁月经初潮</td>
<td>Family history of normal puberty timing supports constitutional (physiologic) development in this patient<br />
家族性正常青春期时间支持该患者为体质性（生理性）发育</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

Normal puberty is triggered by **reactivation of the hypothalamic-pituitary-gonadal (HPG) axis**, leading to pulsatile **GnRH** secretion that drives **FSH/LH** release, ultimately stimulating **estradiol** production from the ovaries:

正常青春期由**下丘脑-垂体-性腺（HPG）轴的重新激活**触发，脉冲式**GnRH**分泌驱动**FSH/LH**释放，最终刺激卵巢产生**雌二醇**：

- Thelarche (SMR 2) → estrogen-driven breast budding; first pubertal sign in females, age 8–13\
  乳芽期（SMR 2）→ 雌激素驱动的乳房萌芽；女性青春期第一征象，8~13岁

- Pubarche (SMR 2–3) → driven by adrenal DHEA-S (adrenarche), occurs shortly after thelarche\
  阴毛初现（SMR 2~3）→ 由肾上腺DHEA-S（肾上腺功能初现）驱动，出现于乳芽期后不久

- Peak height velocity → occurs at SMR 2–3 in females (earlier than males)\
  生长高峰速率 → 女性出现于SMR 2~3期（早于男性）

- Menarche (SMR 4) → ~2–3 years after thelarche; mean age 12.5 years in the United States\
  月经初潮（SMR 4）→ 乳芽期后约2~3年；美国平均年龄12.5岁

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Precocious puberty = secondary sexual characteristics before age **8** in females, before age **9** in males.

**解剖小窍门:** 性早熟 = 女性**8**岁前、男性**9**岁前出现第二性征。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Normal Pubertal Development / 正确答案 (A) — 正常青春期发育

**Normal pubertal development** in females begins between ages 8–13 and follows a predictable hormonal sequence; a 9-year-old with SMR stage 2 breast development falls squarely within normal limits:

**正常青春期发育**在女性中始于8~13岁，遵循可预测的激素序列；9岁出现SMR 2期乳房发育完全属于正常范围：

- Precocious puberty threshold for females is age 8, not age 9 — this patient does not meet diagnostic criteria\
  女性性早熟阈值为8岁而非9岁——该患者不符合性早熟诊断标准

- Normal height/weight percentiles and positive family history (mother's menarche at 12) further support physiologic timing\
  正常身高体重百分位数及阳性家族史（母亲12岁初潮）进一步支持生理性发育时间

- No red flags (café-au-lait spots, neurologic signs, virilization, rapid bone age advancement) are present\
  无危险信号（牛奶咖啡斑、神经系统征象、男性化、骨龄快速提前）

**Diagnosis:** Normal puberty in a 9-year-old female beginning thelarche — no laboratory or imaging workup required

**诊断:** 9岁女孩开始乳芽期，属正常青春期——无需实验室或影像学检查

**Treatment:** Reassurance of the father and routine well-child follow-up to monitor pubertal progression

**治疗:** 安慰父亲，定期常规儿童保健随访以监测青春期进展

<tr>
<td>A — Reassurance ✓<br />
A — 安慰告知 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Patient is 9 years old; female precocious puberty threshold is &lt;8 years; SMR 2 thelarche at age 9 is entirely normal<br />
正确——患者9岁；女性性早熟阈值&lt;8岁；9岁出现SMR 2期乳芽完全正常</td>

<tr>
<td>B — Measurement of serum estrogen concentration<br />

<td>Appropriate in the workup for precocious puberty (&lt;8 years), not for age-appropriate puberty at age 9<br />
适用于性早熟（&lt;8岁）的评估，不适用于9岁的年龄相符青春期</td>
<td>Serum estradiol indicated only if age &lt;8 or additional findings such as café-au-lait spots or rapid growth<br />

<td>C — Measurement of serum FSH concentration<br />
C — 血清FSH浓度测定</td>
<td>Used to distinguish central (gonadotropin-dependent, elevated LH/FSH) from peripheral precocious puberty (suppressed); not needed in normal puberty<br />
用于区分中枢性（促性腺激素依赖性，LH/FSH升高）与外周性性早熟（受抑制）；正常青春期不需要</td>
<td>FSH/LH ratio classifies precocious puberty type; irrelevant when puberty onset is age-appropriate<br />
FSH/LH比值用于分类性早熟类型；青春期发育时间合适时无意义</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — X-ray of the wrist to assess bone age<br />
D — 腕部X线评估骨龄</td>
<td>Bone age &gt;2 SD above chronologic age supports precocious puberty; not indicated when development is age-appropriate<br />
骨龄超过实际年龄2个标准差支持性早熟；发育年龄相符时无指征</td>
<td>Bone age assessment reserved for suspected precocious puberty to quantify skeletal advancement<br />
骨龄评估仅保留用于疑似性早熟时量化骨骼提前成熟程度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Transvaginal ultrasonography<br />
E — 经阴道超声</td>
<td>Invasive and not recommended in a 9-year-old; transabdominal ultrasonography is preferred if pelvic imaging is ever needed<br />
有创性检查，9岁儿童不推荐；如需盆腔影像，优选经腹超声</td>
<td>Pelvic imaging (transabdominal) used only if ovarian/uterine pathology suspected in true precocious puberty<br />
盆腔影像（经腹超声）仅在真性性早熟疑似卵巢/子宫病变时使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Pelvic examination<br />
F — 盆腔检查</td>
<td>Internal pelvic exam is invasive and unnecessary; external genitalia SMR assessment already performed and is sufficient<br />
内部盆腔检查有创且不必要；外生殖器SMR评估已完成且已充分</td>
<td>Internal pelvic exam not recommended in early pubertal children without specific clinical indication<br />
无特定临床指征时，不推荐对青春期早期儿童行内部盆腔检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The strongest distractors are B and C (hormone studies) — they are appropriate only when precocious puberty is suspected (\<8 years); because this 9-year-old is in the normal range, no laboratory evaluation is warranted.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是B和C（激素检测）——仅在疑似性早熟（\<8岁）时适用；该患者9岁处于正常范围，无需任何实验室评估。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A 9-year-old girl with SMR stage 2 breast development is experiencing normal puberty — not precocious puberty — because the precocious puberty threshold in females is age 8, so reassurance alone is appropriate.**

**9岁女孩出现SMR 2期乳房发育属正常青春期而非性早熟，因为女性性早熟阈值为8岁，仅需安慰告知即可。**

<colgroup>

<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "The 8-9 Cutoff" for Precocious Puberty / 记忆钩 — 性早熟"8与9分界线":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>E</strong>ight (8) — females: precocious puberty if secondary sex characteristics appear before age 8 / 女性：8岁前出现第二性征 = 性早熟<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ine (9) — males: precocious puberty if before age 9 / 男性：9岁前出现第二性征 = 性早熟<br />
• <strong>T</strong>helarche first — breast budding is always the first sign of normal female puberty / 乳芽期在先——乳房萌芽始终是女性正常青春期的第一征象<br />
• <strong>M</strong>enarche last — arrives 2–3 years after thelarche at SMR stage 4 / 月经初潮在后——乳芽期后2~3年，SMR 4期出现</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Female Puberty & Precocious Puberty / 高频知识表 — 女性青春期与性早熟

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Normal female puberty sequence (SMR stages)<br />
女性正常青春期顺序（SMR分期）</td>
<td>Thelarche (SMR 2, age 8–13) → Pubarche (SMR 2–3) → Peak height velocity → Menarche (SMR 4, ~2–3 years after thelarche) → Adult (SMR 5)<br />
乳芽期（SMR 2，8~13岁）→ 阴毛初现（SMR 2~3）→ 生长高峰 → 月经初潮（SMR 4，乳芽期后~2~3年）→ 成熟（SMR 5）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Precocious puberty definition<br />
性早熟定义</td>
<td>Females: secondary sex characteristics before age 8; Males: before age 9; note males have a one-year later threshold<br />
女性：8岁前出现第二性征；男性：9岁前；注意男性阈值晚一年</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Central precocious puberty<br />
中枢性性早熟</td>
<td>GnRH-dependent; elevated LH/FSH; causes: idiopathic (most common in girls), CNS tumors, hypothalamic hamartoma, hydrocephalus, prior CNS irradiation<br />
GnRH依赖性；LH/FSH升高；病因：特发性（女孩最常见）、CNS肿瘤、下丘脑错构瘤、脑积水、既往CNS放疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peripheral precocious puberty<br />
外周性性早熟</td>
<td>GnRH-independent; LH/FSH suppressed; causes: McCune-Albright (GNAS mutation), granulosa cell tumor, adrenal tumor, congenital adrenal hyperplasia, exogenous estrogen<br />
非GnRH依赖性；LH/FSH被抑制；病因：McCune-Albright（GNAS突变）、颗粒细胞瘤、肾上腺肿瘤、先天性肾上腺皮质增生症、外源性雌激素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>McCune-Albright syndrome<br />
McCune-Albright综合征</td>
<td>Classic triad: café-au-lait spots (irregular "coast of Maine" borders) + polyostotic fibrous dysplasia + GnRH-independent precocious puberty; caused by activating GNAS mutation<br />
经典三联征：牛奶咖啡斑（不规则"缅因州海岸线"边缘）+ 多骨性纤维性发育不良 + 非GnRH依赖性性早熟；由GNAS激活性突变引起</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Precocious puberty workup<br />
性早熟检查流程</td>
<td>Bone age X-ray (advanced if &gt;2 SD), serum LH/FSH/estradiol/testosterone, GnRH stimulation test (LH &gt;5 IU/L = central); brain MRI if central cause suspected<br />
骨龄X线（&gt;2 SD提示提前），血清LH/FSH/雌二醇/睾酮，GnRH刺激试验（LH &gt;5 IU/L = 中枢性）；疑中枢性病因行脑MRI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment of central precocious puberty<br />
中枢性性早熟治疗</td>
<td>GnRH agonist (e.g., leuprolide depot) — paradoxically suppresses HPG axis by eliminating pulsatility; goal is to preserve adult height potential<br />
GnRH激动剂（如醋酸亮丙瑞林缓释剂）——通过消除脉冲性矛盾性抑制HPG轴；目标是保留成人身高潜力</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Premature thelarche vs. precocious puberty:** Isolated breast development without pubic hair, bone age advancement, or growth acceleration; most common in girls \<2 years old; benign, self-limited, requires observation only\
  **单纯乳房早发育 vs. 性早熟:** 孤立性乳房发育，无阴毛、骨龄提前或生长加速；最常见于\<2岁女孩；良性自限性，仅需观察

- **Premature adrenarche:** Isolated pubic/axillary hair before age 8 (girls) or 9 (boys) from early adrenal androgen secretion; DHEA-S elevated; associated with later risk of PCOS and insulin resistance\
  **单纯肾上腺早现:** 女孩8岁前（男孩9岁前）孤立性阴毛/腋毛，由肾上腺雄激素过早分泌引起；DHEA-S升高；与后期PCOS及胰岛素抵抗风险相关

- **Delayed puberty in females:** No thelarche by age 13 (primary amenorrhea workup if no menarche by 15); causes include Turner syndrome (45,X — short stature, webbed neck, shield chest), hypothyroidism, hyperprolactinemia, functional hypothalamic amenorrhea\
  **女性青春期延迟:** 13岁前无乳芽期（15岁前无月经行原发性闭经检查）；病因包括Turner综合征（45,X——矮小、颈蹼、盾形胸）、甲状腺功能减退、高泌乳素血症、功能性下丘脑性闭经

- **Obesity and puberty timing:** Higher BMI is associated with earlier puberty onset in females, possibly due to adipose-derived leptin stimulating GnRH; this patient's normal weight percentile makes this less relevant\
  **肥胖与青春期时间:** 较高BMI与女性青春期提前相关，可能因脂肪源性瘦素刺激GnRH；该患者体重百分位数正常，此因素相关性较低

# Question 96 — Spontaneous Bacterial Peritonitis / 自发性细菌性腹膜炎

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>1-week history of shortness of breath</strong> and <strong>swelling of his legs</strong>. He says his shortness of breath occurs most frequently <strong>when he lies down</strong>. During the past month, he has had the sensation of <strong>abdominal fullness</strong> and pulling and has noticed a <strong>progressive increase in his belt size</strong>. Five years ago, he received the diagnosis of <strong>bleeding esophageal varices and alcoholic cirrhosis</strong>. He underwent sclerosis of the varices and has abstained from alcohol since then. His temperature is 36.9°C (98.4°F). The abdomen is moderately tense and nontender with <strong>shifting dullness</strong>. There is <strong>3+ pitting edema</strong> of the lower extremities. Paracentesis is performed. Laboratory studies show: Serum protein total 2.8 g/dL, albumin <strong>1.8 g/dL</strong>; Peritoneal fluid leukocyte count <strong>900/mm³</strong>, segmented neutrophils <strong>67%</strong>, lymphocytes 28%, protein total 1.8 g/dL, albumin 1 g/dL. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Echocardiography<br />
B) Ultrasonography of the hepatic veins<br />
C) Antibiotic therapy<br />
D) Laparoscopy<br />
E) Liver biopsy<br />
F) CT angiography of the liver</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>History of alcoholic cirrhosis<br />
酒精性肝硬化病史</td>
<td>Cirrhosis is the #1 risk factor for SBP due to impaired immune clearance and bacterial translocation<br />
肝硬化是SBP最主要危险因素，原因在于免疫清除受损及细菌移位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Shifting dullness + progressive belt size increase<br />
移浊音 + 腰围进行性增大</td>
<td>Confirms significant ascites — the fluid medium in which SBP develops; paracentesis is mandatory<br />
确认大量腹水——SBP发生的液体介质；必须行腹腔穿刺术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peritoneal fluid PMN = 900 × 67% = 603/mm³<br />
腹水PMN绝对值 = 900 × 67% = 603/mm³</td>
<td>Exceeds the diagnostic threshold of &gt;250 PMN/mm³ — this single value diagnoses SBP<br />
超过诊断阈值&gt;250 PMN/mm³——这一单一数值即可确诊SBP</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum albumin 1.8 g/dL<br />
血清白蛋白1.8 g/dL</td>
<td>Severe hypoalbuminemia from hepatic synthetic failure; also risk factor for hepatorenal syndrome<br />
肝脏合成功能衰竭引起的严重低白蛋白血症；也是肝肾综合征的危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Abdomen nontender, afebrile<br />
腹部无压痛、无发热</td>
<td>SBP frequently presents with minimal or atypical symptoms — classic fever + pain are not required to diagnose<br />
SBP常以轻微或不典型症状表现——无需典型发热和腹痛才能诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Orthopnea and 3+ pitting edema<br />
端坐呼吸和3+凹陷性水肿</td>
<td>Reflects systemic fluid overload from hypoalbuminemia and portal hypertension, not primary cardiac failure<br />
反映低白蛋白血症和门静脉高压引起的全身液体过负荷，而非原发性心力衰竭</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Cirrhosis** sets the stage for **spontaneous bacterial peritonitis (SBP)** through a cascade of immune failure and microbial translocation:

**肝硬化**通过免疫衰竭和微生物移位的级联反应，为**自发性细菌性腹膜炎（SBP）**的发生创造条件：

- Cirrhosis → portal hypertension → gut mucosal congestion → increased bacterial translocation across the intestinal wall\
  肝硬化 → 门静脉高压 → 肠黏膜充血 → 肠壁细菌移位增加

- Impaired reticuloendothelial system (Kupffer cells) → bacteria bypass hepatic clearance → bacteremia\
  网状内皮系统（Kupffer细胞）功能受损 → 细菌绕过肝脏清除 → 菌血症

- Low ascitic fluid protein → poor opsonic activity → bacteria proliferate unopposed in ascites\
  腹水蛋白质低下 → 调理素活性差 → 细菌在腹水中无阻碍地大量繁殖

- PMN recruitment into ascitic fluid → PMN count crosses \>250/mm³ threshold → SBP diagnosed\
  中性粒细胞募集入腹水 → PMN计数超过\>250/mm³阈值 → 确诊SBP

**Diagnostic shortcut:** Total WBC × % PMN = 900 × 0.67 = 603/mm³ — this exceeds 250, so culture results are irrelevant for the decision to treat

**诊断捷径:** 总白细胞 × PMN百分比 = 900 × 0.67 = 603/mm³ — 已超过250，治疗决策无需等待培养结果

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Antibiotic Therapy / 正确答案 (C) — 抗生素治疗

**Antibiotic therapy** is mandated immediately once peritoneal fluid PMN exceeds 250/mm³, without waiting for culture confirmation:

**抗生素治疗**在腹水PMN超过250/mm³时须立即启动，无需等待培养确认：

- PMN \>250/mm³ is both diagnostic and sufficient grounds for empiric treatment — cultures are positive in only ~40% of cases\
  PMN \>250/mm³ 既是诊断标准，也是经验性治疗的充分依据——培养阳性率仅约40%

- Third-generation cephalosporins (cefotaxime 2 g IV q8h × 5 days) provide the gram-negative coverage needed\
  第三代头孢菌素（头孢噻肟2 g IV q8h × 5天）提供所需的革兰阴性菌覆盖

- IV albumin (1.5 g/kg on day 1, then 1 g/kg on day 3) co-administration reduces hepatorenal syndrome from 33% to 10%\
  同时静注白蛋白（第1天1.5 g/kg，第3天1 g/kg）可将肝肾综合征发生率从33%降至10%

**Diagnosis:** SBP is confirmed by peritoneal fluid PMN \>250/mm³ in the setting of ascites. Most common pathogens are E. coli, Klebsiella pneumoniae, and Streptococcus pneumoniae — almost always monomicrobial.

**诊断:** 腹水背景下腹水PMN \>250/mm³即可确诊SBP。最常见病原体为大肠杆菌、肺炎克雷伯菌和肺炎链球菌——几乎均为单一病原体。

**Treatment:** Empiric IV cefotaxime or ceftriaxone for 5 days; follow with indefinite oral norfloxacin for secondary prophylaxis given ~70% one-year recurrence rate.

**治疗:** 经验性静注头孢噻肟或头孢曲松5天；因1年内复发率约70%，随后长期口服诺氟沙星进行二级预防。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Echocardiography<br />
A — 超声心动图</td>
<td>Wrong — no role in SBP evaluation; only appropriate if primary cardiac failure were suspected, which this presentation does not support<br />
错误——不用于SBP评估；仅当怀疑原发性心力衰竭时适用，本题临床表现不支持</td>
<td>Leg edema and orthopnea here are due to hypoalbuminemia and portal HTN, not pump failure<br />
此处下肢水肿和端坐呼吸源于低白蛋白血症和门静脉高压，不是心泵衰竭</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Ultrasonography of the hepatic veins<br />
B — 肝静脉超声</td>
<td>Wrong — appropriate for Budd-Chiari syndrome (acute RUQ pain, congestive hepatopathy, hepatic vein thrombosis), but antibiotics cannot be delayed once SBP is diagnosed<br />
错误——适用于Budd-Chiari综合征（急性右上腹痛、充血性肝病、肝静脉血栓），但SBP确诊后不能延误抗生素治疗</td>
<td>Budd-Chiari presents acutely with RUQ pain and liver failure — not this chronic cirrhotic picture<br />
Budd-Chiari急性起病伴右上腹痛和肝衰竭——不符合本题慢性肝硬化表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Antibiotic therapy ✓<br />
C — 抗生素治疗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — peritoneal PMN 603/mm³ exceeds the 250/mm³ diagnostic threshold for SBP; empiric antibiotics are the immediate next step<br />
正确——腹水PMN 603/mm³超过SBP诊断阈值250/mm³；经验性抗生素是立即的下一步</td>
<td>PMN &gt;250 = treat now, confirm later; do not wait for culture<br />
PMN &gt;250 = 立即治疗，稍后确认；不要等待培养</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Laparoscopy<br />
D — 腹腔镜</td>
<td>Wrong — invasive surgical procedure not indicated for SBP; reserved for suspected bowel perforation or other surgical abdomen<br />
错误——侵入性外科操作不适用于SBP；用于怀疑肠穿孔或其他外科急腹症</td>
<td>Abdomen is nontender with no signs of surgical emergency; SBP is a medical diagnosis<br />
腹部无压痛，无外科急诊征象；SBP是内科诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Liver biopsy<br />
E — 肝活检</td>
<td>Wrong — useful for diagnosing etiology of liver disease, but cirrhosis is already established and biopsy must never delay antibiotics when SBP is diagnosed<br />
错误——有助于诊断肝病病因，但肝硬化诊断已明确，SBP确诊后活检绝不能延误抗生素治疗</td>
<td>Diagnose the acute emergency first; chronic liver workup can wait<br />
急性紧急情况优先处理；慢性肝病检查可以等待</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — CT angiography of the liver<br />
F — 肝脏CT血管造影</td>
<td>Wrong — evaluates vascular patency and is used in thromboembolic or atherosclerotic disease; has no role in diagnosing or treating SBP<br />
错误——评估血管通畅性，用于血栓栓塞或动脉硬化性疾病；对SBP的诊断或治疗毫无帮助</td>
<td>CT angiography evaluates vessels, not ascitic fluid infection<br />
CT血管造影评估血管，而非腹水感染</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice B (hepatic vein ultrasonography for Budd-Chiari) — but even if Budd-Chiari were on the differential, the PMN count here already crosses the SBP threshold and antibiotic therapy cannot be withheld pending additional imaging.*

最容易错选的干扰项是选项B（肝静脉超声诊断Budd-Chiari综合征）——但即使Budd-Chiari在鉴别诊断之列，本题PMN计数已超过SBP诊断阈值，抗生素治疗不能因等待额外影像学检查而推迟。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a cirrhotic patient with ascites, peritoneal fluid PMN \>250/mm³ diagnoses SBP and mandates immediate empiric antibiotic therapy — do not wait for culture results.**

**肝硬化腹水患者腹水PMN \>250/mm³即可确诊SBP，必须立即开始经验性抗生素治疗——无需等待培养结果。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ALERT for SBP / 记忆钩 — SBP预警 "ALERT":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>A</strong>scites in a cirrhotic — required substrate for SBP to develop / 肝硬化腹水——SBP发生的必要基础<br />
• <strong>L</strong>eukocytes (PMN) &gt;250/mm³ — the one number that diagnoses and triggers treatment / 白细胞（PMN）&gt;250/mm³——诊断并触发治疗的关键数值<br />
• <strong>E</strong>nteric bacteria, especially E. coli — most common pathogen via translocation / 肠道细菌，尤其大肠杆菌——移位引起的最常见病原体<br />
• <strong>R</strong>x: 3rd-generation cephalosporins (cefotaxime) — empiric first-line, no culture needed first / 治疗：第三代头孢菌素（头孢噻肟）——经验性一线，无需先等培养<br />
• <strong>T</strong>ransfuse albumin IV — prevents hepatorenal syndrome, cuts risk from 33% to 10% / 静注白蛋白——预防肝肾综合征，将风险从33%降至10%</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Spontaneous Bacterial Peritonitis / 高频知识表 — 自发性细菌性腹膜炎

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic criteria<br />
诊断标准</td>
<td>PMN &gt;250/mm³ in ascitic fluid = SBP; culture sensitivity is only ~40%, so a positive culture is NOT required to diagnose or treat<br />
腹水PMN &gt;250/mm³ = SBP；培养敏感性仅约40%，阳性培养并非诊断或治疗的必要条件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common pathogens<br />
最常见病原体</td>
<td>E. coli (#1), Klebsiella pneumoniae, Streptococcus pneumoniae; infection is almost always monomicrobial — polymicrobial suggests secondary peritonitis<br />
大肠杆菌（最常见）、肺炎克雷伯菌、肺炎链球菌；感染几乎均为单一病原体——多种病原体混合提示继发性腹膜炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>IV cefotaxime 2 g q8h × 5 days; albumin 1.5 g/kg on day 1 and 1 g/kg on day 3 to prevent hepatorenal syndrome<br />
静注头孢噻肟2 g q8h × 5天；第1天白蛋白1.5 g/kg、第3天1 g/kg以预防肝肾综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary prophylaxis indications<br />
一级预防适应证</td>
<td>Cirrhotic patients with GI bleed (norfloxacin × 7 days) or ascitic protein &lt;1.5 g/dL + advanced cirrhosis (indefinite norfloxacin or TMP-SMX)<br />
肝硬化患者发生消化道出血（诺氟沙星×7天）或腹水蛋白&lt;1.5 g/dL合并晚期肝硬化（长期诺氟沙星或TMP-SMX）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secondary prophylaxis<br />
二级预防</td>
<td>Indefinite daily norfloxacin after first SBP episode; without prophylaxis, 1-year recurrence rate is ~70%<br />
首次SBP后长期每日服用诺氟沙星；无预防时1年内复发率约70%</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hepatorenal syndrome link<br />
与肝肾综合征的关联</td>
<td>SBP is the most common precipitant of hepatorenal syndrome (HRS) in cirrhosis; albumin infusion is protective by preventing systemic inflammation from worsening renal perfusion<br />
SBP是肝硬化中肝肾综合征最常见的诱因；白蛋白输注通过防止全身炎症加重肾灌注来起保护作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SAAG interpretation<br />
SAAG解读</td>
<td>SAAG = serum albumin − ascitic albumin; ≥1.1 indicates portal hypertension; SBP can artificially lower SAAG by raising ascitic protein from inflammation<br />
SAAG = 血清白蛋白 − 腹水白蛋白；≥1.1提示门静脉高压；SBP可因炎症升高腹水蛋白而人为降低SAAG</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Atypical SBP presentation:** SBP may present without fever or abdominal pain — any unexplained clinical deterioration (new encephalopathy, worsening renal function) in a cirrhotic with ascites warrants diagnostic paracentesis\
  **SBP不典型表现:** SBP可不伴发热或腹痛——肝硬化腹水患者出现任何不明原因的病情恶化（新发脑病、肾功能恶化）均应行诊断性腹腔穿刺

- **Culture-negative neutrocytic ascites (CNNA):** PMN \>250/mm³ with sterile cultures; treat identically to culture-positive SBP — the PMN threshold, not culture, drives management\
  **培养阴性中性粒细胞性腹水（CNNA）:** PMN \>250/mm³但培养无菌；治疗与培养阳性SBP完全相同——管理决策依据PMN阈值，而非培养结果

- **Secondary peritonitis red flags:** Polymicrobial culture, ascitic protein \>1 g/dL, glucose \<50 mg/dL, or LDH \> serum LDH should prompt imaging and surgical consultation for bowel perforation\
  **继发性腹膜炎危险信号:** 多种病原体培养、腹水蛋白\>1 g/dL、葡萄糖\<50 mg/dL或LDH\>血清LDH应立即行影像学检查并请外科会诊排除肠穿孔

- **Definitive management:** Liver transplantation is the only cure for end-stage cirrhosis; a history of SBP contributes to MELD score elevation and increases transplant priority\
  **根治性处理:** 肝移植是终末期肝硬化的唯一根治手段；SBP病史有助于MELD评分升高并提高移植优先级

# Question 97 — Chronic Myelogenous Leukemia / 慢性髓细胞白血病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>asymptomatic 62-year-old man</strong> comes for a routine health maintenance examination. Physical examination shows <strong>splenomegaly</strong>. Laboratory studies show: Hematocrit 42%, Leukocyte count <strong>46,000/mm³</strong> (segmented neutrophils 35%, bands 15%, basophils 1%, lymphocytes 16%, monocytes 5%, <strong>myeloblasts 1%</strong>, promyelocytes 2%, <strong>metamyelocytes 13%, myelocytes 12%</strong>), platelet count <strong>650,000/mm³</strong>. <strong>Leukocyte alkaline phosphatase activity is decreased.</strong> Examination of bone marrow shows many immature white blood cell precursors. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Agnogenic myeloid metaplasia<br />
B) Chronic myelogenous leukemia<br />
C) Chronic myelomonocytic leukemia<br />
D) Erythroleukemia<br />
E) Essential thrombocytosis<br />
F) Myelodysplasia<br />
G) Polycythemia vera</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Asymptomatic, incidental finding<br />
无症状，偶然发现</td>
<td>CML classically presents on routine labs in the chronic phase; absence of symptoms does not exclude malignancy<br />
CML慢性期经典表现为常规检查偶然发现；无症状不能排除恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Splenomegaly<br />
脾肿大</td>
<td>Extramedullary hematopoiesis causes splenomegaly in CML; also a feature of other myeloproliferative neoplasms<br />
髓外造血导致CML脾脏增大；也是其他骨髓增殖性肿瘤的特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>WBC 46,000/mm³ with full myeloid spectrum<br />
白细胞46,000/mm³，呈全系髓系谱</td>
<td>Hyperleukocytosis with cells at all maturation stages (blasts → mature neutrophils) is the hallmark of CML<br />
各成熟阶段细胞同时出现（原始细胞→成熟中性粒细胞）是CML标志性特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocyte alkaline phosphatase decreased<br />
白细胞碱性磷酸酶降低</td>
<td>Low LAP is pathognomonic for CML; distinguishes it from leukemoid reaction (LAP high) and myelofibrosis (LAP high)<br />
低LAP是CML的特征性表现；可与类白血病反应（LAP高）和骨髓纤维化（LAP高）鉴别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Platelet count 650,000/mm³<br />
血小板650,000/mm³</td>
<td>Thrombocytosis is common in CML from unregulated myeloproliferation; does not indicate essential thrombocytosis here<br />
血小板增多是CML骨髓不受控增殖的常见表现；此处不提示原发性血小板增多症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bone marrow: many immature WBC precursors<br />
骨髓：大量不成熟白细胞前体</td>
<td>Confirms myeloid hyperplasia at all stages; in CML the marrow is packed with granulocytes from blasts to mature cells<br />
证实各阶段髓系增生；CML骨髓中从原始细胞到成熟细胞的粒细胞均显著增多</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**CML** arises from the **Philadelphia chromosome** — a reciprocal translocation t(9;22)(q34;q11) that fuses the **BCR gene** on chromosome 22 with the **ABL1 gene** from chromosome 9, generating a constitutively active **BCR-ABL tyrosine kinase**:

**CML** 由**费城染色体**引起——9号与22号染色体发生相互易位t(9;22)(q34;q11)，将22号染色体上的**BCR基因**与9号染色体上的**ABL1基因**融合，产生持续激活的**BCR-ABL酪氨酸激酶**：

- BCR-ABL constitutively phosphorylates downstream targets (RAS, PI3K, STAT5), bypassing normal growth-factor control\
  BCR-ABL持续磷酸化下游靶点（RAS、PI3K、STAT5），绕过正常生长因子调控

- Drives expansion of myeloid progenitors at all differentiation stages → peripheral blood "myeloid spectrum" from blasts to mature segs\
  驱动各分化阶段髓系祖细胞扩增→外周血出现从原始细胞到成熟分叶粒细胞的"髓系谱"

- Malignant granulocytes remain well-differentiated and pliable → leukostasis is uncommon despite massive leukocytosis\
  恶性粒细胞保持良好分化且可变形→尽管白细胞极度增多，白细胞淤滞仍不常见

- LAP is decreased because BCR-ABL+ neutrophils are functionally abnormal and fail to upregulate alkaline phosphatase\
  LAP降低是因为BCR-ABL+中性粒细胞功能异常，无法正常上调碱性磷酸酶

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The CML peripheral smear looks like a bone marrow biopsy spilled into the blood — every stage of granulocyte maturation is represented simultaneously.

**解剖小窍门:** CML外周血涂片就像骨髓活检内容溢入血液——粒细胞成熟的每个阶段同时出现在外周血中。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Philadelphia Chromosome-Driven Myeloproliferation / 正确答案 (B) — 费城染色体驱动的骨髓增殖

**Chronic myelogenous leukemia (CML)** is a clonal myeloproliferative neoplasm defined by the BCR-ABL fusion oncogene, presenting with hyperleukocytosis, full myeloid left shift, splenomegaly, and pathognomonic low LAP:

**慢性髓细胞白血病（CML）** 是由BCR-ABL融合癌基因定义的克隆性骨髓增殖性肿瘤，表现为白细胞极度增多、全系髓系左移、脾肿大和特征性低LAP评分：

- Philadelphia chromosome t(9;22) identified by conventional cytogenetics or FISH; BCR-ABL fusion transcript detected by RT-PCR\
  费城染色体t(9;22)通过常规细胞遗传学或FISH检测；BCR-ABL融合转录本通过RT-PCR检测

- CBC shows all myeloid maturation stages simultaneously: blasts \< 10% (chronic phase), bands, metamyelocytes, myelocytes, and mature segs\
  全血细胞计数同时显示所有髓系成熟阶段：原始细胞\<10%（慢性期）、杆状、晚幼、中幼及成熟分叶粒细胞

- Basophilia (even mild) is characteristic; absolute basophilia increasing signals accelerated phase\
  嗜碱性粒细胞增多（即使轻度）为特征性表现；绝对嗜碱性粒细胞进行性增多提示进入加速期

- Three phases: chronic (blasts \< 10%) → accelerated (blasts 10–19%) → blast crisis (blasts ≥ 20%, resembles AML or ALL)\
  三期：慢性期（原始细胞\<10%）→加速期（原始细胞10-19%）→急变期（原始细胞≥20%，类似AML或ALL）

**Diagnosis:** Full myeloid spectrum + low LAP → confirm with Philadelphia chromosome (cytogenetics/FISH) or BCR-ABL PCR; molecular monitoring used to track treatment response

**诊断:** 全系髓系谱+低LAP→通过费城染色体（细胞遗传学/FISH）或BCR-ABL PCR确诊；分子检测用于追踪治疗反应

**Treatment:** Tyrosine kinase inhibitors (TKIs) — imatinib first-line; dasatinib or nilotinib as alternatives; allogeneic SCT reserved for TKI failure or blast crisis

**治疗:** 酪氨酸激酶抑制剂（TKI）——伊马替尼一线；达沙替尼或尼洛替尼备选；异基因造血干细胞移植用于TKI失败或急变期

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>

<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Agnogenic myeloid metaplasia<br />
A — 原发性骨髓纤维化</td>
<td>LAP is INCREASED, not decreased; bone marrow shows fibrosis with dry tap, not myeloid hyperplasia; teardrop RBCs on smear<br />
LAP升高而非降低；骨髓示纤维化（干抽），而非髓系增生；涂片可见泪滴形红细胞</td>
<td>LAP high; fibrotic marrow (dry tap); teardrop RBCs; leukoerythroblastic picture<br />
LAP高；骨髓纤维化（干抽）；泪滴形红细胞；幼红幼粒血象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Chronic myelogenous leukemia ✓<br />
B — 慢性髓细胞白血病 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — classic triad: asymptomatic hyperleukocytosis with full myeloid spectrum, low LAP, splenomegaly, confirmed by Ph1 chromosome<br />
正确——经典三联征：无症状白细胞极度增多伴全系髓系谱、低LAP、脾肿大，由费城染色体确诊</td>
<td>Philadelphia chromosome t(9;22); BCR-ABL; low LAP pathognomonic<br />
费城染色体t(9;22)；BCR-ABL；低LAP具有诊断特异性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Chronic myelomonocytic leukemia<br />
C — 慢性粒单核细胞白血病</td>
<td>Requires persistent monocytosis &gt; 1,000/mm³ as the dominant feature; this patient has only 5% monocytes without a monocytic predominance<br />
需要持续性单核细胞&gt;1,000/mm³为主要特征；本患者单核细胞仅5%，无单核细胞主导</td>
<td>Monocytosis is the defining feature; CMML is a mixed MDS/MPN disorder<br />
单核细胞增多为定义性特征；CMML是混合性MDS/MPN疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Erythroleukemia<br />
D — 红白血病</td>
<td>AML subtype (FAB M6) with proliferation of immature erythroid precursors; presents with anemia and leukopenia, not leukocytosis; acute course<br />
AML亚型（FAB M6），以不成熟红系前体增生为特征；表现为贫血和白细胞减少，而非白细胞增多；急性病程</td>
<td>Erythroid dysplasia + hyperplasia; anemia + leukopenia + thrombocytopenia; acute not chronic<br />
红系发育异常+增生；贫血+白细胞减少+血小板减少；急性非慢性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Essential thrombocytosis<br />
E — 原发性血小板增多症</td>
<td>Defined by isolated megakaryocyte proliferation and thrombocytosis; WBC is not markedly elevated and LAP is normal or high; bone marrow shows megakaryocyte hyperplasia only<br />
定义为孤立性巨核细胞增生和血小板增多；白细胞无显著升高，LAP正常或升高；骨髓仅示巨核细胞增生</td>
<td>Megakaryocyte proliferation on marrow biopsy (not WBC precursors); JAK2/CALR/MPL mutations<br />
骨髓活检示巨核细胞增生（非白细胞前体）；JAK2/CALR/MPL突变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Myelodysplasia<br />
F — 骨髓增生异常综合征</td>
<td>MDS features cytopenias and dysplastic (morphologically abnormal) cells, not hyperleukocytosis; bone marrow shows multi-lineage dysplasia, not myeloid hyperplasia<br />
MDS特征为血细胞减少和发育异常细胞，而非白细胞增多；骨髓示多系发育异常，而非髓系增生</td>
<td>Cytopenias + dysplasia; ring sideroblasts, pseudo-Pelger-Huët anomaly; not hyperleukocytosis<br />
血细胞减少+发育异常；环形铁粒幼红细胞、假Pelger-Huët异常；非白细胞增多</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>G — Polycythemia vera<br />
G — 真性红细胞增多症</td>
<td>PV is defined by erythrocytosis; this patient's Hct is 42% (normal for a male), making PV impossible; also driven by JAK2 V617F, not BCR-ABL<br />
PV定义为红细胞增多；本患者Hct 42%（男性正常值），故PV不可能；亦由JAK2 V617F驱动，而非BCR-ABL</td>
<td>Elevated Hct + JAK2 mutation; aquagenic pruritus; Hct 42% definitively excludes PV<br />
Hct升高+JAK2突变；洗澡后瘙痒；Hct 42%明确排除PV</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Agnogenic myeloid metaplasia (A) — both cause splenomegaly and immature myeloid cells in the blood, but the LAP score is the decisive differentiator: CML = LOW, primary myelofibrosis = HIGH.*

最容易混淆的干扰项是原发性骨髓纤维化（A）——两者均可引起脾肿大和外周血出现不成熟髓系细胞，但LAP评分是决定性鉴别指标：CML = 低，原发性骨髓纤维化 = 高。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**CML is an asymptomatic myeloproliferative neoplasm driven by the Philadelphia chromosome BCR-ABL fusion, characterized by hyperleukocytosis with a full myeloid spectrum, splenomegaly, thrombocytosis, and a pathognomonic low LAP score, treated with tyrosine kinase inhibitors.**

**CML是由费城染色体BCR-ABL融合驱动的无症状骨髓增殖性肿瘤，特征为白细胞极度增多伴全系髓系谱、脾肿大、血小板增多和特征性低LAP评分，以酪氨酸激酶抑制剂治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CML "SPILL" / 记忆钩 — CML 五要素 "SPILL":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>plenomegaly — massive spleen from extramedullary hematopoiesis / 脾肿大——髓外造血所致脾脏显著增大<br />
• <strong>P</strong>hiladelphia chromosome — t(9;22) BCR-ABL, the defining molecular lesion / 费城染色体——t(9;22) BCR-ABL，定义性分子病变<br />
• <strong>I</strong>matinib — first TKI that transformed CML from fatal to manageable chronic disease / 伊马替尼——将CML从致命转变为可控慢性病的首个TKI<br />
• <strong>L</strong>AP decreased — the classic lab: low in CML, high in leukemoid reactions and myelofibrosis / LAP降低——经典实验室指标：CML中低，类白血病反应和骨髓纤维化中高<br />
• <strong>L</strong>eukocytosis with full myeloid spectrum — peripheral blood shows every granulocyte stage simultaneously / 白细胞增多伴全系髓系谱——外周血同时出现各阶段粒细胞</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Chronic Myelogenous Leukemia / 高频知识表 — 慢性髓细胞白血病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Philadelphia chromosome<br />
费城染色体</td>
<td>Reciprocal translocation t(9;22)(q34;q11); present in &gt; 95% of CML; also seen in 20–30% of adult B-ALL (worse prognosis in ALL)<br />
相互易位t(9;22)(q34;q11)；见于&gt;95%的CML；也见于20–30%的成人B-ALL（ALL中预后更差）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BCR-ABL isoforms<br />
BCR-ABL亚型</td>
<td>p210 isoform in CML (larger fusion); p190 isoform in Ph+ ALL; p210 drives granulocytic/platelet proliferation<br />
CML中为p210亚型（较大融合蛋白）；Ph+ ALL中为p190亚型；p210驱动粒细胞/血小板增殖</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LAP score interpretation<br />
LAP评分解读</td>
<td>Low LAP = CML; High LAP = leukemoid reaction (infection/inflammation/PV/myelofibrosis); LAP is now largely replaced by BCR-ABL PCR<br />
低LAP = CML；高LAP = 类白血病反应（感染/炎症/PV/骨髓纤维化）；LAP现已基本被BCR-ABL PCR取代</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Three phases of CML<br />
CML三期</td>
<td>Chronic: blasts &lt; 10%, often asymptomatic → Accelerated: blasts 10–19%, worsening cytopenias, ↑basophils → Blast crisis: blasts ≥ 20%, AML-like (70%) or ALL-like (30%)<br />
慢性期：原始细胞&lt;10%，常无症状→加速期：原始细胞10–19%，进行性血细胞减少，嗜碱性粒细胞增多→急变期：原始细胞≥20%，类AML（70%）或类ALL（30%）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Imatinib mechanism and resistance<br />
伊马替尼机制与耐药</td>
<td>Competitive inhibitor of BCR-ABL ATP-binding site; T315I "gatekeeper" mutation causes resistance to all first/second-generation TKIs; ponatinib or asciminib used for T315I<br />
竞争性抑制BCR-ABL ATP结合位点；T315I"门卫"突变对所有一、二代TKI耐药；T315I使用泊那替尼或阿西米尼</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukemoid reaction vs CML<br />
类白血病反应与CML鉴别</td>
<td>Leukemoid: reactive (infection/stress), WBC typically &lt; 50,000, LAP HIGH, Ph1 negative, toxic granulation on smear; CML: LAP LOW, Ph1 positive, basophilia, no toxic changes<br />
类白血病反应：反应性（感染/应激），白细胞通常&lt;50,000，LAP高，Ph1阴性，涂片可见中毒颗粒；CML：LAP低，Ph1阳性，嗜碱性粒细胞增多，无中毒性改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Monitoring response to TKI<br />
TKI治疗反应监测</td>
<td>Hematologic response (CBC normalization, 3 months) → Cytogenetic response (Ph1 clearance by FISH, 6–12 months) → Molecular response (BCR-ABL PCR &lt; 0.1%, 12 months)<br />
血液学缓解（CBC正常化，3个月）→细胞遗传学缓解（FISH示Ph1清除，6–12个月）→分子学缓解（BCR-ABL PCR&lt;0.1%，12个月）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of hyperleukocytosis:** CML (LAP low, Ph1+, full myeloid spectrum) vs leukemoid reaction (LAP high, Ph1−, obvious infectious trigger) vs AML (blasts ≥ 20%, acute presentation, Auer rods possible)\
  **白细胞极度增多的鉴别:** CML（LAP低，Ph1+，全系髓系谱）vs 类白血病反应（LAP高，Ph1−，有明显感染诱因）vs AML（原始细胞≥20%，急性起病，可见Auer小体）

- **Blast crisis variant:** Myeloid blast crisis (70%) treated as de novo AML; lymphoid blast crisis (30%) treated with ALL-directed therapy (vincristine/prednisone/TKI); prognosis is poor for both\
  **急变期变式:** 髓系急变期（70%）按初发AML治疗；淋系急变期（30%）采用ALL方案（长春新碱/泼尼松/TKI）；两者预后均差

- **Key complication — leukostasis:** Rare in CML because malignant cells are pliable; more common in AML when blasts are rigid and occlude microvasculature → retinal, pulmonary, and CNS ischemia; leukapheresis may be needed acutely\
  **关键并发症——白细胞淤滞:** CML中少见（恶性细胞可变形）；AML中更常见，原始细胞僵硬堵塞微血管→视网膜、肺及CNS缺血；急性期可能需要白细胞单采

- **Exam trap — basophilia:** Even a mild absolute basophilia (as seen here: 1%) should raise suspicion for CML in the right clinical context; markedly increased basophilia (\> 20%) signals accelerated phase or impending blast crisis\
  **考试陷阱——嗜碱性粒细胞增多:** 即使轻度绝对嗜碱性粒细胞增多（如本题：1%）在正确临床背景下也应怀疑CML；嗜碱性粒细胞显著增多（\>20%）提示加速期或即将发生急变

# Question 98 — Vesicoureteral Reflux Workup After Febrile UTI / 发热性尿路感染后膀胱输尿管反流评估

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>5-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the office for a follow-up examination <strong>2 days after he was discharged from the hospital</strong> following an episode of <strong>pyelonephritis</strong>. Medications are cefixime and acetaminophen. He is at the 50th percentile for height and <strong>25th percentile for weight</strong>; BMI is at the 10th percentile. Temperature is 37.6°C (99.6°F), pulse is <strong>120/min</strong>, respirations are 22/min, and blood pressure is <strong>90/60 mm Hg</strong>. Physical examination shows no other abnormalities. Results of laboratory studies from his hospital admission showed a leukocyte count within the reference range and <strong>urine positive for leukocyte esterase</strong>; urine culture grew <strong>Klebsiella pneumoniae susceptible to cephalosporins</strong>. Kidney ultrasonography showed <strong>mild hydronephrosis</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Continuous antibiotic prophylaxis<br />
B) Kidney and bladder ultrasonography<br />
C) Renal scintigraphy using dimercaptosuccinic acid (DMSA)<br />
D) Repeat urine culture<br />
E) Voiding cystourethrography</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>5-year-old boy, first febrile UTI<br />
5岁男孩，首次发热性尿路感染</td>
<td>Age &lt;2 years and males are highest-risk groups for VUR; first febrile UTI mandates anatomic workup<br />
年龄&lt;2岁和男童是VUR高危人群；首次发热性UTI必须进行解剖学评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mild hydronephrosis on ultrasound<br />
超声示轻度肾积水</td>
<td>Hydronephrosis is a key VCUG trigger — suggests possible obstruction or retrograde reflux<br />
肾积水是VCUG的关键指征，提示可能存在梗阻或逆流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Klebsiella pneumoniae UTI<br />
克雷伯菌尿路感染</td>
<td>Gram-negative organisms in children warrant structural evaluation; not E. coli (most common)<br />
儿童革兰阴性菌感染需要结构性评估；非最常见的大肠埃希菌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-pyelonephritis follow-up<br />
肾盂肾炎后随访</td>
<td>Upper tract infection in a young child is a red flag for underlying anatomic anomaly<br />
幼儿上尿路感染是潜在解剖异常的警示信号</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Currently on cefixime (cephalosporin)<br />
目前使用头孢克肟（头孢菌素）</td>
<td>Appropriate treatment; focus should shift to identifying the underlying cause<br />
治疗方案合适；重点应转向查找潜在病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 10th percentile / weight 25th percentile<br />
BMI第10百分位/体重第25百分位</td>
<td>Subtle growth concern may reflect chronic renal disease from recurrent undetected infections<br />
轻度生长迟缓可能反映反复隐匿性感染所致慢性肾损害</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Vesicoureteral reflux (VUR)** is caused by **incompetence of the vesicoureteral junction (VUJ)**, which normally functions as a one-way valve preventing retrograde urine flow from the bladder into the ureters:

**膀胱输尿管反流（VUR）**由**膀胱输尿管连接部（VUJ）功能不全**引起，正常情况下该连接部作为单向阀防止尿液从膀胱逆流至输尿管：

- Normal VUJ: ureter traverses bladder wall at an oblique angle, creating a flap-valve mechanism\
  正常VUJ：输尿管斜行穿越膀胱壁，形成活瓣机制

- VUR: short intramural ureteral tunnel → VUJ fails to close during voiding → retrograde urine flow\
  VUR：膀胱壁内段输尿管过短→排尿时VUJ无法关闭→尿液逆流

- Retrograde flow carries bacteria from bladder to kidney → recurrent pyelonephritis → renal scarring\
  逆流将细菌从膀胱带至肾脏→反复肾盂肾炎→肾瘢痕形成

- Graded I–V by VCUG: Grade I (reflux into ureter only) to Grade V (massive reflux with tortuous ureter)\
  VCUG分级I–V级：I级（仅反流至输尿管）至V级（大量反流伴输尿管迂曲扩张）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The shorter the submucosal tunnel of the ureter within the bladder wall, the higher the grade of VUR and the less likely it is to resolve spontaneously.

**解剖小窍门:** 输尿管在膀胱壁内的黏膜下隧道越短，VUR分级越高，自行缓解的可能性越小。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Voiding Cystourethrography / 正确答案 (E) — 排尿性膀胱尿道造影

**Voiding cystourethrography (VCUG)** is the gold-standard test for diagnosing VUR and is indicated after a first febrile UTI when hydronephrosis is present on ultrasound:

**排尿性膀胱尿道造影（VCUG）**是诊断VUR的金标准，当超声发现肾积水时，首次发热性UTI后即有指征：

- Procedure: contrast instilled via urethral catheter → fluoroscopic imaging during bladder filling and voiding\
  操作：经尿道导管注入造影剂→在膀胱充盈和排尿过程中进行透视成像

- Detects VUR grade, laterality, and ureteral/renal pelvis anatomy\
  检测VUR分级、侧别及输尿管/肾盂解剖形态

- Also evaluates urethral anatomy (posterior urethral valves in boys — another cause of hydronephrosis)\
  同时评估尿道解剖（男童后尿道瓣膜——肾积水的另一病因）

- AAP 2011 guidelines: VCUG NOT recommended after first simple febrile UTI unless abnormal US\
  AAP 2011指南：首次简单发热性UTI后不常规推荐VCUG，除非超声异常

- This patient HAS hydronephrosis → VCUG is clearly indicated\
  本例患儿存在肾积水→VCUG明确有指征

**Diagnosis:** First febrile UTI + hydronephrosis on ultrasound = VCUG to evaluate for VUR and posterior urethral valves.

**诊断:** 首次发热性UTI + 超声肾积水 = 行VCUG评估VUR及后尿道瓣膜。

**Treatment:** VUR management depends on grade: low-grade (I–II) often resolves spontaneously; antibiotic prophylaxis for higher grades; surgical correction (ureteral reimplantation or endoscopic injection) for persistent high-grade VUR.

**治疗:** VUR处理取决于分级：低级别（I–II级）常自行缓解；较高级别予抗生素预防；持续性高级别VUR行手术矫正（输尿管再植或内镜注射治疗）。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Continuous antibiotic prophylaxis<br />
A — 持续抗生素预防</td>
<td>Premature — prophylaxis is given AFTER VUR is diagnosed, not before workup is complete<br />
为时过早——预防性抗生素在确诊VUR后给予，而非评估完成前</td>
<td>Must diagnose VUR first via VCUG before initiating prophylaxis<br />
必须先通过VCUG确诊VUR再开始预防治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Kidney and bladder ultrasonography<br />
B — 肾脏及膀胱超声</td>
<td>Already done — repeat US does not detect VUR; only shows anatomic abnormalities<br />
已完成检查——重复超声无法检测VUR，仅显示解剖异常</td>
<td>US cannot visualize retrograde flow; VCUG is needed for functional assessment<br />
超声无法显示逆流；需VCUG进行功能评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — DMSA renal scintigraphy<br />
C — DMSA肾核素显像</td>
<td>Detects existing renal scarring but NOT the cause (VUR); greater radiation, more expensive; not first-line<br />
检测已存在的肾瘢痕，但无法确定病因（VUR）；辐射剂量更大，费用更高；非一线检查</td>
<td>DMSA assesses sequelae (scarring), not etiology; VCUG identifies the underlying VUR<br />
DMSA评估后果（瘢痕），VCUG找出病因（VUR）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Repeat urine culture<br />
D — 重复尿培养</td>
<td>Not useful for identifying structural/functional abnormalities; cannot detect VUR<br />
无法识别结构或功能异常；不能检测VUR</td>
<td>Urine culture monitors infection status; anatomic workup requires imaging<br />
尿培养监测感染状态；解剖评估需要影像学检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Voiding cystourethrography ✓<br />
E — 排尿性膀胱尿道造影 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — gold-standard test for VUR; indicated by hydronephrosis on US after febrile UTI<br />
正确——VUR金标准检查；超声发现肾积水后发热性UTI的指征</td>
<td>Directly visualizes reflux grade and urethral anatomy (rules out PUV)<br />
直接显示反流分级及尿道解剖（排除后尿道瓣膜）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is Choice B (repeat ultrasound) — students may confuse "more imaging" with "better imaging," but US cannot detect VUR; only VCUG with contrast can demonstrate retrograde flow.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是B（重复超声）——考生可能混淆"更多影像学检查"与"更好的影像学检查"，但超声无法检测VUR；只有含造影剂的VCUG才能显示逆流。
