## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a child with a first febrile UTI plus hydronephrosis on ultrasound, VCUG is the mandatory next step to diagnose vesicoureteral reflux before deciding on prophylaxis or surgical management.**

**儿童首次发热性UTI合并超声肾积水时，VCUG是诊断膀胱输尿管反流的必要下一步，在决定预防性用药或手术处理前必须完成。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — The "HUNT" Rule for Pediatric UTI Workup / 记忆钩 — 儿童UTI检查"HUNT"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>ydronephrosis on US → <strong>H</strong>urry to get VCUG / 超声发现肾积水→立刻安排VCUG<br />
• <strong>U</strong>ltrasound first, always, after febrile UTI / 发热性UTI后超声永远是第一步<br />
• <strong>N</strong>ext step VCUG if US abnormal (hydro, scar, anomaly) / 超声异常（肾积水/瘢痕/异常）→下一步VCUG<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hen DMSA only if VUR confirmed to assess scarring / VCUG确认VUR后再用DMSA评估瘢痕</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Vesicoureteral Reflux (VUR) in Children / 高频知识表 — 儿童膀胱输尿管反流

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>VUR Grading (I–V)<br />
VUR分级（I–V级）</td>
<td>I: ureter only; II: ureter + renal pelvis (no dilation); III: mild dilation; IV: moderate dilation + blunted calyces; V: severe tortuous ureter + loss of papillary impressions<br />
I级：仅输尿管；II级：输尿管+肾盂（无扩张）；III级：轻度扩张；IV级：中度扩张+肾盏变钝；V级：重度迂曲+肾乳头印迹消失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>VCUG Indications (AAP 2011)<br />
VCUG指征（AAP 2011指南）</td>
<td>Febrile UTI + abnormal ultrasound (hydronephrosis, scarring, atypical findings); recurrent febrile UTIs; boys with any febrile UTI under age 2<br />
发热性UTI+超声异常（肾积水、瘢痕、不典型表现）；反复发热性UTI；2岁以下男童任何发热性UTI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>VUR Natural History<br />
VUR自然病程</td>
<td>Low-grade (I–III): ~80% resolve spontaneously by age 5; high-grade (IV–V): less likely to resolve, higher surgery rate<br />
低级别（I–III级）：约80%在5岁前自行缓解；高级别（IV–V级）：自行缓解可能性小，手术率高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Antibiotic Prophylaxis<br />
抗生素预防</td>
<td>TMP-SMX or nitrofurantoin low-dose daily; indicated for VUR (controversial — RIVUR trial showed modest benefit); NOT started before VUR diagnosis<br />
每日低剂量TMP-SMX或呋喃妥因；适用于VUR（有争议——RIVUR试验显示有限获益）；VUR确诊前不开始</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Posterior Urethral Valves (PUV)<br />
后尿道瓣膜（PUV）</td>
<td>Boys only; presents with hydronephrosis, poor urinary stream, recurrent UTI; VCUG shows dilated posterior urethra; treatment: endoscopic ablation<br />
仅见于男童；表现为肾积水、尿流细弱、反复UTI；VCUG示后尿道扩张；治疗：内镜消融</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DMSA Timing<br />
DMSA检查时机</td>
<td>Acute phase: detects pyelonephritis (photopenic defect); delayed (4–6 months post-infection): detects permanent scarring; NOT first-line for VUR diagnosis<br />
急性期：检测肾盂肾炎（光子缺损区）；延迟期（感染后4–6个月）：检测永久性瘢痕；非VUR诊断一线</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic Kidney Disease Risk<br />
慢性肾病风险</td>
<td>Recurrent pyelonephritis → bilateral renal scarring → reflux nephropathy → hypertension + CKD; accounts for 10–15% of pediatric ESRD<br />
反复肾盂肾炎→双侧肾瘢痕→反流性肾病→高血压+慢性肾病；占儿童终末期肾病的10–15%</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of pediatric hydronephrosis:** UPJ obstruction (most common cause), VUR, posterior urethral valves (boys), ureterocele, prune belly syndrome, physiologic (transient)\
  **儿童肾积水鉴别:** 肾盂输尿管连接处梗阻（最常见）、VUR、后尿道瓣膜（男童）、输尿管囊肿、梅干腹综合征、生理性（一过性）

- **Variant — when VCUG is NOT indicated:** First simple febrile UTI in girl \>2 years with normal ultrasound and good clinical response to treatment per 2011 AAP guidelines\
  **题目变式——VCUG无指征情形:** 根据2011年AAP指南，\>2岁女孩首次简单发热性UTI且超声正常、治疗反应良好时不常规行VCUG

- **Key complication of untreated VUR:** Reflux nephropathy — combination of renal scarring, hypertension, proteinuria, and progressive CKD; most dangerous consequence of missed VUR diagnosis in early childhood\
  **未治疗VUR的关键并发症:** 反流性肾病——肾瘢痕、高血压、蛋白尿和进行性慢性肾病的综合；幼儿期漏诊VUR最危险的后果

- **Mnemonic for VUR management ladder:** US → VCUG → Prophylaxis (if VUR+) → DMSA (assess scarring) → Surgery (if high-grade persistent)\
  **VUR管理阶梯记忆法:** 超声→VCUG→预防性用药（VUR阳性时）→DMSA（评估瘢痕）→手术（高级别持续性VUR）

# Question 99 — Anorexia Nervosa (Binge-Purging Type) with Hypokalemic Hypochloremic Metabolic Alkalosis / 神经性厌食症（暴食-清除型）伴低钾低氯代谢性碱中毒

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>16-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the emergency department immediately after she <strong>collapsed</strong> on her way to the bathroom at home. She has <strong>anorexia nervosa</strong> and has had an <strong>18-kg (40-lb) weight loss</strong> during the past 16 months. Menarche was at the age of 11 years, but her <strong>last menstrual period was 14 months ago</strong>. She does not drink alcohol or use illicit drugs. On arrival, she appears <strong>cachectic</strong>. She is 165 cm (5 ft 5 in) tall and weighs 36 kg (80 lb); <strong>BMI is 13 kg/m²</strong>. Her temperature is 36.4°C (97.6°F), <strong>pulse is 40/min</strong>, respirations are 18/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 85/55 mm Hg</strong>. Physical examination shows <strong>fine hair over the skin</strong>. An ECG shows <strong>ST-segment depression and an increased U wave</strong>. This patient is most likely to have which of the following sets of serum electrolyte findings?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely serum electrolyte panel?</strong></p>
<p>A) Na+ 125 mEq/L, K+ 3.2 mEq/L, Cl- 102 mEq/L, HCO3- 25 mEq/L<br />
B) Na+ 125 mEq/L, K+ 6.8 mEq/L, Cl- 102 mEq/L, HCO3- 27 mEq/L<br />
C) Na+ 140 mEq/L, K+ 2.3 mEq/L, Cl- 94 mEq/L, HCO3- 28 mEq/L<br />
D) Na+ 140 mEq/L, K+ 6.8 mEq/L, Cl- 94 mEq/L, HCO3- 28 mEq/L<br />
E) Na+ 155 mEq/L, K+ 3.2 mEq/L, Cl- 102 mEq/L, HCO3- 26 mEq/L</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Anorexia nervosa, collapsed going to bathroom<br />
神经性厌食症，去洗手间途中晕倒</td>
<td>"Going to bathroom" implies purging behavior (self-induced vomiting) → gastric HCl loss<br />
「去洗手间」暗示清除行为（自我诱导呕吐）→胃酸（HCl）丢失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 13 kg/m², 18-kg weight loss in 16 months<br />
BMI 13，16个月内体重减少18 kg</td>
<td>Severe malnutrition; BMI &lt;17 is the diagnostic threshold; drives systemic electrolyte and hormonal derangements<br />
严重营养不良；BMI&lt;17是诊断阈值；驱动全身电解质和激素紊乱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG: ST-segment depression + increased U wave<br />
心电图：ST段压低 + U波增高</td>
<td>Classic ECG signature of hypokalemia; U waves reflect delayed ventricular repolarization from K+ depletion<br />
低钾血症的典型心电图特征；U波反映K+耗竭导致的心室复极延迟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pulse 40/min, BP 85/55 mmHg<br />
脉搏40次/分，血压85/55 mmHg</td>
<td>Bradycardia + hypotension indicate hemodynamic instability from electrolyte-driven cardiac dysfunction<br />
心动过缓+低血压表明电解质驱动的心脏功能障碍所致血流动力学不稳定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Last menstrual period 14 months ago<br />
14个月前最后一次月经</td>
<td>Hypothalamic suppression from malnutrition → decreased GnRH → secondary amenorrhea<br />
营养不良导致下丘脑抑制→GnRH减少→继发性闭经</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fine hair over skin (lanugo)<br />
皮肤细毛（胎毛）</td>
<td>Lanugo is a thermoregulatory response to chronic hypothermia in severe malnutrition; confirms severe anorexia<br />
胎毛是严重营养不良时机体对慢性体温过低的体温调节反应；证实严重厌食症</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **binge-eating/purging subtype** of anorexia nervosa involves repeated self-induced vomiting that expels large volumes of **gastric HCl**. This triggers a predictable cascade of **acid-base and electrolyte disturbances** that are distinct from the restricting subtype:

**暴食-清除亚型**的神经性厌食症通过反复自我诱导呕吐排出大量**胃酸（HCl）**，引发可预测的**酸碱和电解质紊乱**级联反应，与限制型亚型截然不同：

- Loss of H+ ions → body retains HCO3- as compensation → **metabolic alkalosis** (HCO3- rises above 26 mEq/L)\
  H+离子丢失→机体代偿性保留HCO3-→**代谢性碱中毒**（HCO3-升高超过26 mEq/L）

- Direct loss of Cl- in gastric secretions → **hypochloremia** (Cl- falls below 98 mEq/L)\
  胃液中直接丢失Cl-→**低氯血症**（Cl-降至98 mEq/L以下）

- Gastric K+ loss + renal K+ wasting (alkalosis drives K+/H+ exchange in distal tubule) → **severe hypokalemia**\
  胃内K+丢失+碱中毒促使远端小管K+/H+交换增加→**严重低钾血症**

- Sodium balance is typically preserved; no significant hypo- or hypernatremia unless SIADH or severe volume depletion supervenes\
  钠平衡通常维持正常；除非并发SIADH或严重容量耗竭，否则无显著高低钠血症

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Vomiting loses acid (HCl) → alkalosis + hypokalemia + hypochloremia; diarrhea loses base (HCO3-) → acidosis + hypokalemia + hyperchloremia. Direction of acid-base change identifies the source of GI loss.

**解剖小窍门:** 呕吐丢失酸（HCl）→碱中毒+低钾+低氯；腹泻丢失碱（HCO3-）→酸中毒+低钾+高氯。酸碱变化方向可识别消化道丢失部位。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Hypokalemic Hypochloremic Metabolic Alkalosis / 正确答案 (C) — 低钾低氯代谢性碱中毒

**Hypokalemic hypochloremic metabolic alkalosis** is the hallmark electrolyte pattern of purging behavior; each value in Choice C maps directly to a specific mechanism of loss:

**低钾低氯代谢性碱中毒**是清除行为的标志性电解质模式；C选项中每个数值都直接对应一种特定的丢失机制：

- Na+ 140 mEq/L — normal; sodium homeostasis is maintained in typical purging anorexia\
  Na+ 140 mEq/L — 正常；典型清除型厌食症中钠稳态维持正常

- K+ 2.3 mEq/L — severely low; dual mechanism: gastric K+ loss + alkalosis-driven renal K+ wasting\
  K+ 2.3 mEq/L — 严重降低；双重机制：胃内K+丢失+碱中毒驱动的肾脏K+浪费

- Cl- 94 mEq/L — low; lost directly as HCl in every purging episode\
  Cl- 94 mEq/L — 降低；每次清除均以HCl形式直接丢失

- HCO3- 28 mEq/L — elevated; metabolic alkalosis from cumulative H+ depletion\
  HCO3- 28 mEq/L — 升高；H+累积耗竭导致代谢性碱中毒

**Diagnosis:** Anorexia nervosa binge-eating/purging type — confirmed by extreme low BMI (13), secondary amenorrhea, lanugo, bradycardia/hypotension, and ECG U waves with ST depression consistent with severe hypokalemia

**诊断:** 神经性厌食症暴食-清除型——通过极低BMI（13）、继发性闭经、胎毛、心动过缓/低血压及与严重低钾血症一致的心电图U波和ST段压低确认

**Treatment:** Gradual nutritional rehabilitation; IV fluid and electrolyte repletion (especially K+ — cautious IV replacement for K+ \<3.0); cardiac monitoring; psychiatric therapy (CBT); watch for refeeding syndrome (hypophosphatemia)

**治疗:** 渐进式营养康复；静脉补液和电解质补充（尤其K+——K+\<3.0时谨慎静脉补充）；心脏监测；心理治疗（CBT）；警惕再喂养综合征（低磷血症）

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Na+ 125, K+ 3.2, Cl- 102, HCO3- 25<br />
A — Na+ 125, K+ 3.2, Cl- 102, HCO3- 25</td>
<td>Hyponatremia (Na+ 125) is not typical of purging; K+ 3.2 is low-normal not hypokalemic; HCO3- 25 is normal (no alkalosis); Cl- 102 is normal (no hypochloremia)<br />
低钠血症（Na+ 125）不是清除型的典型表现；K+ 3.2为低正常值非低钾血症；HCO3- 25正常（无碱中毒）；Cl- 102正常（无低氯血症）</td>
<td>Purging → HCl loss → Cl- must fall and HCO3- must rise; all four electrolytes are wrong here<br />
清除→HCl丢失→Cl-必须降低，HCO3-必须升高；此选项四个电解质均错误</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Na+ 125, K+ 6.8, Cl- 102, HCO3- 27<br />
B — Na+ 125, K+ 6.8, Cl- 102, HCO3- 27</td>
<td>Hyperkalemia (K+ 6.8) is the opposite of what purging causes; hyponatremia also atypical; Cl- is not low<br />
高钾血症（K+ 6.8）与清除型效应相反；低钠血症也不典型；Cl-未降低</td>
<td>Hyperkalemia suggests Addison's disease or renal failure — not purging<br />
高钾血症提示Addison病或肾衰竭——而非清除行为</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Na+ 140, K+ 2.3, Cl- 94, HCO3- 28 ✓<br />
C — Na+ 140, K+ 2.3, Cl- 94, HCO3- 28 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — normal Na+, severe hypokalemia, hypochloremia, metabolic alkalosis: perfect match for binge-purging anorexia<br />
正确——正常Na+，严重低钾血症，低氯血症，代谢性碱中毒：与暴食-清除型厌食症完美匹配</td>
<td>ECG U waves confirm hypokalemia; low Cl- + high HCO3- confirm gastric HCl loss; normal Na+ fits typical purging<br />
心电图U波确认低钾血症；低Cl-+高HCO3-确认胃酸HCl丢失；正常Na+符合典型清除型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Na+ 140, K+ 6.8, Cl- 94, HCO3- 28<br />
D — Na+ 140, K+ 6.8, Cl- 94, HCO3- 28</td>
<td>Na+, Cl-, and HCO3- match the purging pattern perfectly, but K+ 6.8 is severe hyperkalemia — the exact opposite of what vomiting causes<br />
Na+、Cl-和HCO3-完全匹配清除型模式，但K+ 6.8为严重高钾血症——与呕吐导致的效果完全相反</td>
<td>The strongest distractor: ECG U waves are the deciding clue — U waves are hypokalemia, not hyperkalemia (which causes peaked T waves)<br />
最强干扰项：心电图U波是决定性线索——U波代表低钾血症，而非高钾血症（高钾血症表现为高尖T波）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Na+ 155, K+ 3.2, Cl- 102, HCO3- 26<br />
E — Na+ 155, K+ 3.2, Cl- 102, HCO3- 26</td>
<td>Hypernatremia (Na+ 155) suggests free water loss (diabetes insipidus, dehydration) not purging; K+ only mildly low; Cl- and HCO3- are essentially normal<br />
高钠血症（Na+ 155）提示自由水丢失（尿崩症、脱水）而非清除行为；K+仅轻度降低；Cl-和HCO3-基本正常</td>
<td>No acid-base signature of purging: absent hypochloremia and absent metabolic alkalosis rule this out<br />
无清除行为的酸碱特征：缺乏低氯血症和代谢性碱中毒排除此选项</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Choice D is the most dangerous distractor because it correctly identifies the acid-base disturbance (low Cl-, elevated HCO3-) but reverses K+ to hyperkalemia; the ECG finding of U waves — a hallmark of hypokalemia — is the single most important clue to reject it.*

D选项是最危险的干扰项，因为它正确识别了酸碱紊乱（低Cl-，HCO3-升高），但将K+逆转为高钾血症；心电图U波——低钾血症的标志性表现——是排除此选项的最重要单一线索。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In anorexia nervosa purging type, repeated vomiting expels gastric HCl, producing hypokalemia + hypochloremia + metabolic alkalosis with normal sodium, confirmed by ECG U waves and ST depression.**

**神经性厌食症清除型中，反复呕吐排出胃酸（HCl），产生低钾血症+低氯血症+代谢性碱中毒，钠浓度正常，心电图U波和ST段压低可确认。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PUKE for Purging Electrolytes / 记忆钩 — PUKE助记清除型电解质：</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>urging expels HCl → Hypochloremia (Cl- falls) / 清除（Purging）排出HCl → 低氯血症（Cl-降低）<br />
• <strong>U</strong> waves on ECG → Hypokalemia confirmed (not hyperkalemia!) / 心电图U波（U waves）→ 确认低钾血症（不是高钾！）<br />
• <strong>K</strong>+ depleted by gastric loss + renal wasting in alkalosis → K↓ / K+因胃丢失+碱中毒肾脏浪费而耗竭 → K↓<br />
• <strong>E</strong>levated HCO3- → Metabolic alkalosis (H+ lost, base retained) / HCO3-升高（Elevated）→ 代谢性碱中毒（H+丢失，碱保留）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Anorexia Nervosa: Complications & Electrolyte Physiology / 高频知识表 — 神经性厌食症：并发症与电解质生理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ECG changes in hypokalemia<br />
低钾血症心电图改变</td>
<td>U waves (most characteristic), ST depression, T wave flattening or inversion, prolonged QU interval; K+ &lt;2.5 → risk of ventricular fibrillation<br />
U波（最具特征性），ST段压低，T波低平或倒置，QU间期延长；K+&lt;2.5→室颤风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dual mechanism of hypokalemia in purging<br />
清除型低钾血症的双重机制</td>
<td>(1) Direct K+ loss in vomitus; (2) Metabolic alkalosis drives K+/H+ exchange in renal distal tubule → K+ wasted in urine<br />
（1）呕吐物中直接K+丢失；（2）代谢性碱中毒驱动肾远端小管K+/H+交换→K+随尿丢失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lanugo (fine body hair)<br />
胎毛（细体毛）</td>
<td>Thermoregulatory response to severe malnutrition and loss of subcutaneous fat; resolves with weight restoration; also seen in premature neonates<br />
严重营养不良和皮下脂肪丢失的体温调节反应；体重恢复后消退；也见于早产儿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypothalamic amenorrhea mechanism<br />
下丘脑性闭经机制</td>
<td>Malnutrition → ↓leptin → ↓GnRH → ↓LH/FSH → anovulation → secondary amenorrhea + bone density loss (osteoporosis risk requiring DXA scan)<br />
营养不良→瘦素↓→GnRH↓→LH/FSH↓→无排卵→继发性闭经+骨密度丢失（需DXA扫描评估骨质疏松风险）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Refeeding syndrome<br />
再喂养综合征</td>
<td>Rapid refeeding shifts phosphate intracellularly (insulin surge) → severe hypophosphatemia → cardiac/respiratory failure, seizures; prevented by slow caloric reintroduction and phosphate supplementation<br />
快速再喂养使磷酸盐向细胞内转移（胰岛素激增）→严重低磷血症→心脏/呼吸衰竭，癫痫发作；通过缓慢热量再引入和补磷预防</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Russell's sign and dental erosion<br />
Russell征和牙齿侵蚀</td>
<td>Calluses/scars on dorsal hand knuckles from contact with incisors during self-induced vomiting; dental enamel erosion on palatal surfaces from chronic gastric acid exposure<br />
自我诱导呕吐时手背指关节与门牙接触形成老茧/瘢痕；腭侧牙面因长期胃酸暴露导致牙釉质侵蚀</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anorexia restricting vs. purging type electrolytes<br />
厌食症限制型vs清除型电解质</td>
<td>Restricting type: malnutrition → relatively preserved electrolytes, mainly hypokalemia from poor intake; Purging type: vomiting → HCl loss → hypokalemia + hypochloremia + metabolic alkalosis (more severe)<br />
限制型：营养不良→电解质相对保留，主要因摄入不足导致低钾血症；清除型：呕吐→HCl丢失→低钾+低氯+代谢性碱中毒（更严重）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of secondary amenorrhea:** Pregnancy (always exclude first with hCG), hypothalamic amenorrhea (anorexia, excessive exercise, stress), hyperprolactinemia (check prolactin), primary ovarian insufficiency (↑FSH), thyroid dysfunction\
  **继发性闭经鉴别:** 妊娠（首先用hCG排除），下丘脑性闭经（厌食症、过度运动、压力），高催乳素血症（检查催乳素），原发性卵巢功能不全（FSH↑），甲状腺功能障碍

- **Key complication — fatal arrhythmia:** K+ 2.3 + HR 40 + QT-prolonging metabolic alkalosis creates a perfect storm for ventricular fibrillation; this patient needs continuous cardiac monitoring and IV K+ replacement before any other intervention\
  **关键并发症——致死性心律失常:** K+ 2.3+HR 40+代谢性碱中毒延长QT构成室颤的完美风暴；此患者在任何其他干预前需持续心脏监测和静脉K+补充

- **Variant — bulimia nervosa vs. anorexia purging type:** Both share identical electrolyte pattern (hypokalemia + hypochloremia + metabolic alkalosis); key distinction is BMI — bulimia nervosa patients have normal or near-normal BMI (≥18.5) while anorexia purging type have BMI \<17\
  **题目变式——神经性贪食症vs厌食症清除型:** 两者共享相同电解质模式（低钾+低氯+代谢性碱中毒）；关键区别是BMI——神经性贪食症患者BMI正常或接近正常（≥18.5），而厌食症清除型BMI\<17

- **Cause of death in anorexia nervosa:** Cardiac arrhythmia (hypokalemia + QT prolongation → torsades de pointes) and suicide are the two leading causes; anorexia nervosa carries the highest mortality rate of any psychiatric disorder (~10% at 10 years)\
  **厌食症死亡原因:** 心律失常（低钾血症+QT延长→尖端扭转型室速）和自杀是两大主要死因；神经性厌食症是所有精神疾病中死亡率最高的（10年约10%）

# Question 100 — ABO Hemolytic Disease of the Newborn / ABO 新生儿溶血病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>20-hour-old female newborn</strong> was noted to have jaundice <strong>1 hour ago</strong>. She was born at term to a <strong>29-year-old woman, gravida 2, para 2</strong>, following an uncomplicated pregnancy and spontaneous vaginal delivery. The mother emigrated from <strong>Ethiopia</strong> 2 years ago. She received routine prenatal care. Examination of the patient shows <strong>jaundice to the level of the umbilicus</strong>. There is <strong>conjunctival icterus</strong>. No other abnormalities are noted. The maternal blood group is <strong>O, Rh-positive</strong>. Results of laboratory studies, including the patient's blood group, are pending. Which of the following laboratory findings is most likely to be decreased in this patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following laboratory findings is most likely to be decreased in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Hematocrit<br />
B) Leukocyte count<br />
C) Platelet count<br />
D) Serum direct bilirubin concentration<br />
E) Serum indirect bilirubin concentration</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>20-hour-old newborn with jaundice<br />
20小时龄新生儿出现黄疸</td>
<td>Jaundice within first 24 hours of life is always pathological — physiological jaundice begins on day 2–3<br />
生后24小时内出现黄疸始终为病理性——生理性黄疸始于生后第2-3天</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Jaundice to umbilicus + conjunctival icterus<br />
黄疸至脐部 + 结膜黄染</td>
<td>Kramer zone 2 involvement plus scleral icterus indicates significant hyperbilirubinemia requiring workup<br />
Kramer II区受累加巩膜黄染提示显著高胆红素血症，需要积极评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Maternal blood group O, Rh-positive<br />
母亲血型 O，Rh 阳性</td>
<td>Group O mothers naturally harbor IgG anti-A and anti-B antibodies capable of crossing the placenta<br />
O型血母亲天然携带 IgG 型抗-A 和抗-B 抗体，可穿越胎盘</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gravida 2, para 2<br />
孕2产2</td>
<td>Multiparous; unlike Rh incompatibility, ABO incompatibility can affect even the first pregnancy because anti-A/B IgG already exists<br />
经产妇；与Rh不合不同，ABO不合因抗-A/B IgG已天然存在，甚至可累及第一胎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mother emigrated from Ethiopia<br />
母亲来自埃塞俄比亚</td>
<td>G6PD deficiency is highly prevalent in sub-Saharan Africa — a potential contributing factor for neonatal hemolysis, though ABO incompatibility is the primary etiology here<br />
撒哈拉以南非洲地区G6PD缺乏症高发——可能的辅助溶血因素，但此题主因为ABO不合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Question asks what is DECREASED<br />
题目问哪项指标"降低"</td>
<td>Hemolysis → RBC destruction → decreased hematocrit; bilirubin fractions are elevated, not decreased<br />
溶血 → 红细胞破坏 → 血细胞比容降低；各胆红素组分均升高，而非降低</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**ABO incompatibility** occurs when a **type O mother** carries a fetus with **blood group A, B, or AB**. Because type O individuals naturally develop **IgG anti-A and anti-B antibodies** through environmental exposure to bacterial polysaccharides, no prior sensitizing pregnancy is required:

**ABO不合**发生于**O型血母亲**孕育**A型、B型或AB型**胎儿时。由于O型血个体因环境中细菌多糖暴露已自然产生**IgG型抗-A和抗-B抗体**，无需前次妊娠致敏：

- IgG anti-A/B antibodies cross the placenta → bind to fetal/neonatal RBC surface antigens\
  IgG型抗-A/B抗体穿越胎盘 → 结合至胎儿/新生儿红细胞表面抗原

- Antibody-coated RBCs are phagocytosed by splenic macrophages → extravascular hemolysis\
  抗体包被的红细胞被脾脏巨噬细胞吞噬 → 血管外溶血

- Heme catabolism generates unconjugated (indirect) bilirubin, which accumulates because the neonatal liver lacks sufficient UDP-glucuronosyltransferase\
  血红素分解产生非结合（间接）胆红素，因新生儿肝脏UDP-葡萄糖醛酸转移酶不足而蓄积

- Net result: hematocrit falls (hemolytic anemia) + indirect bilirubin rises (pathological jaundice)\
  最终结果：血细胞比容下降（溶血性贫血）+ 间接胆红素升高（病理性黄疸）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The placenta selectively transports IgG (~150 kDa) via FcRn receptors but excludes IgM (~900 kDa); this is why only IgG-class alloantibodies cause hemolytic disease of the newborn.

**解剖小窍门:** 胎盘通过FcRn受体选择性转运IgG（约150 kDa），而排斥IgM（约900 kDa）；这正是只有IgG类同种抗体才能引起新生儿溶血病的原因。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Decreased Hematocrit due to Hemolytic Anemia / 正确答案 (A) — 溶血性贫血所致血细胞比容降低

**Hematocrit** is decreased because maternal IgG anti-A/B antibodies cross the placenta and destroy neonatal red blood cells through extravascular hemolysis, reducing total RBC mass:

**血细胞比容**降低，因母体IgG型抗-A/B抗体穿越胎盘，通过血管外溶血途径破坏新生儿红细胞，导致红细胞总量减少：

- IgG anti-A/B opsonizes neonatal RBCs → splenic macrophage engulfment and destruction\
  IgG抗-A/B调理新生儿红细胞 → 脾脏巨噬细胞吞噬与破坏

- RBC mass decreases → hematocrit falls → hemolytic anemia\
  红细胞总量减少 → 血细胞比容下降 → 溶血性贫血

- Peripheral smear classically shows spherocytes and polychromasia (reticulocytosis)\
  外周血涂片经典表现为球形红细胞和多染性红细胞（网织红细胞增多）

- Direct Coombs (DAT) test is positive but may be only weakly positive in ABO incompatibility compared to Rh incompatibility\
  直接抗球蛋白试验（DAT）阳性，但ABO不合时常为弱阳性，弱于Rh不合

**Diagnosis:** Suspected in a neonate born to a type O mother presenting with pathological jaundice within 24 hours and hemolytic anemia; confirmed by neonatal blood typing, positive DAT, and elevated indirect bilirubin.

**诊断:** 对O型血母亲所生新生儿，若24小时内出现病理性黄疸合并溶血性贫血，即应高度怀疑；通过新生儿血型、DAT阳性及间接胆红素升高确诊。

**Treatment:** Phototherapy (blue light 450–490 nm) converts indirect bilirubin to water-soluble photoisomers; exchange transfusion reserved for severe or rapidly rising bilirubin levels unresponsive to phototherapy.

**治疗:** 光疗（蓝光450-490 nm）将间接胆红素转化为水溶性光异构体；对光疗无效的重度或快速上升性高胆红素血症行换血治疗。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Hematocrit ✓<br />
A — 血细胞比容 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — maternal IgG anti-A/B destroys neonatal RBCs via extravascular hemolysis, directly reducing RBC mass and hematocrit<br />
正确——母体IgG抗-A/B通过血管外溶血破坏新生儿红细胞，直接降低红细胞总量及血细胞比容</td>
<td>Hemolytic anemia is the cardinal pathophysiologic consequence of ABO incompatibility<br />
溶血性贫血是ABO不合最核心的病理生理结果</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Leukocyte count<br />
B — 白细胞计数</td>
<td>Anti-A/B antibodies target red blood cell surface antigens, not leukocyte surface antigens; WBC count is unaffected by ABO incompatibility<br />
抗-A/B抗体靶向红细胞表面抗原，而非白细胞表面抗原；ABO不合不影响白细胞计数</td>
<td>ABO blood group antigens are expressed on RBCs; leukocytes are not targeted by these antibodies<br />
ABO血型抗原表达于红细胞；白细胞不被这些抗体靶向</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Platelet count<br />
C — 血小板计数</td>
<td>Anti-A/B antibodies do not target platelets; platelet count is not decreased in ABO hemolytic disease<br />
抗-A/B抗体不靶向血小板；ABO溶血病不降低血小板计数</td>
<td>Neonatal thrombocytopenia suggests immune thrombocytopenia (anti-HPA antibodies) or DIC, not ABO incompatibility<br />
新生儿血小板减少提示免疫性血小板减少症（抗HPA抗体）或DIC，而非ABO不合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Serum direct bilirubin concentration<br />
D — 血清直接胆红素浓度</td>
<td>Direct (conjugated) bilirubin is not decreased — hemolysis primarily raises indirect bilirubin; direct bilirubin may be mildly elevated or normal<br />
直接（结合）胆红素不会降低——溶血以升高间接胆红素为主；直接胆红素可轻度升高或正常</td>
<td>The question asks what is DECREASED; bilirubin fractions rise (not fall) with hemolysis<br />
题目问哪项指标"降低"；溶血时胆红素各组分升高（而非降低）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Serum indirect bilirubin concentration<br />
E — 血清间接胆红素浓度</td>
<td>Indirect (unconjugated) bilirubin is markedly INCREASED — it is the direct cause of the visible jaundice in this neonate and the primary risk factor for kernicterus<br />
间接（非结合）胆红素显著升高——它正是该新生儿可见黄疸的直接原因，也是核黄疸的主要风险因素</td>
<td>Indirect bilirubin predominates because the immature neonatal liver cannot conjugate bilirubin at sufficient rates<br />
以间接胆红素升高为主，因不成熟的新生儿肝脏结合能力不足</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous trap is E — candidates may see "jaundice" and infer bilirubin is somehow consumed or decreased, but the clinical finding of jaundice is itself direct evidence that indirect bilirubin is elevated.*

最危险的陷阱是选项E——考生可能看到"黄疸"后误认为胆红素被"消耗"而降低，但黄疸这一临床表现本身就是间接胆红素升高的直接证据。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — ABO Incompatibility vs. Rh(D) Incompatibility / ABO不合与Rh(D)不合的鉴别对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>ABO Incompatibility</strong><br />
<strong>ABO不合</strong></th>
<th><strong>Rh(D) Incompatibility</strong><br />
<strong>Rh(D)不合</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Maternal blood type<br />
母亲血型</td>
<td>Group O — natural IgG anti-A and anti-B<br />
O型血——天然含IgG型抗-A和抗-B</td>
<td>Rh-negative — acquired IgG anti-D after sensitization<br />
Rh阴性——致敏后产生IgG型抗-D</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First pregnancy affected?<br />
第一胎是否受累</td>
<td>Yes — pre-existing IgG antibodies require no prior sensitization<br />
是——已存在IgG抗体，无需前次致敏</td>
<td>Rarely — requires prior RBC exposure (miscarriage, amniocentesis, delivery)<br />
少见——需前次红细胞暴露（流产、羊穿、分娩等）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Severity<br />
严重程度</td>
<td>Mild to moderate; hydrops fetalis is rare<br />
轻至中度；胎儿水肿罕见</td>
<td>Can be severe; classic cause of hydrops fetalis<br />
可重度；胎儿水肿的经典病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Direct Coombs (DAT)<br />
直接抗球蛋白试验</td>
<td>Weakly positive or sometimes negative<br />
弱阳性，有时阴性</td>
<td>Strongly positive<br />
强阳性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peripheral smear<br />
外周血涂片</td>
<td>Spherocytes, polychromasia<br />
球形红细胞、多染性</td>
<td>Nucleated RBCs, polychromasia<br />
有核红细胞、多染性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prevention<br />
预防措施</td>
<td>None — anti-A/B are natural antibodies<br />
无——抗-A/B为天然抗体，无法预防</td>
<td>RhoGAM (anti-D Ig) at 28 weeks and within 72 hours postpartum<br />
孕28周及产后72小时内注射RhoGAM（抗D免疫球蛋白）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A type O mother's IgG anti-A/B antibodies cross the placenta, destroy neonatal RBCs causing hemolytic anemia (decreased hematocrit), and release indirect bilirubin causing pathological jaundice within 24 hours of birth.**

**O型血母亲的IgG型抗-A/B抗体穿越胎盘，破坏新生儿红细胞引起溶血性贫血（血细胞比容降低），并释放间接胆红素，导致生后24小时内出现病理性黄疸。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — OHIO Rule for ABO Incompatibility / 记忆钩 — ABO不合"OHIO"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>O</strong>-type mother — only group O has both IgG anti-A and anti-B naturally / O型血母亲——只有O型血天然同时含IgG抗-A和抗-B<br />
• <strong>H</strong>emolysis of neonatal RBCs — hematocrit falls, indirect bilirubin rises / 新生儿红细胞溶血——血细胞比容下降，间接胆红素升高<br />
• <strong>I</strong>gG crosses placenta — IgM cannot (molecular weight too large at ~900 kDa) / IgG穿越胎盘——IgM不能穿越（分子量约900 kDa，过大）<br />
• <strong>O</strong>nset within 24 hours — always pathological, never physiological / 24小时内发病——始终为病理性黄疸，绝非生理性</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Neonatal Jaundice and ABO Hemolytic Disease / 高频知识表 — 新生儿黄疸与ABO溶血病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Pathological vs. physiological neonatal jaundice<br />
病理性与生理性新生儿黄疸的区别</td>
<td>Pathological: onset &lt;24 hours, rise &gt;5 mg/dL/day, or bilirubin above phototherapy threshold; causes include ABO/Rh incompatibility, G6PD deficiency, sepsis, TORCH<br />
病理性：&lt;24小时发病，每日升速&gt;5 mg/dL，或超光疗阈值；病因含ABO/Rh不合、G6PD缺乏、败血症、TORCH感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ABO incompatibility diagnosis<br />
ABO不合的诊断</td>
<td>Type O mother + neonatal blood type A/B/AB + hemolytic anemia + early jaundice; DAT may be weakly positive; peripheral smear shows spherocytes<br />
O型血母亲 + 新生儿血型A/B/AB + 溶血性贫血 + 早发黄疸；DAT可弱阳性；外周血涂片见球形红细胞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Indirect vs. direct bilirubin in hemolysis<br />
溶血时间接与直接胆红素的变化</td>
<td>Hemolysis releases heme → heme oxygenase → biliverdin → unconjugated bilirubin; immature neonatal UGT1A1 cannot conjugate rapidly → indirect fraction predominates<br />
溶血释放血红素 → 血红素加氧酶 → 胆绿素 → 非结合胆红素；新生儿UGT1A1不成熟 → 以间接组分为主</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Kernicterus (bilirubin encephalopathy)<br />
核黄疸（胆红素脑病）</td>
<td>Indirect bilirubin is lipid-soluble → crosses blood-brain barrier → deposits in basal ganglia and brainstem → acute: hypotonia, poor feeding, high-pitched cry → chronic: choreoathetosis, sensorineural hearing loss, intellectual disability<br />
间接胆红素脂溶性 → 穿越血脑屏障 → 沉积于基底节和脑干 → 急性期：肌张力低、喂养困难、高调哭声 → 慢性期：手足徐动症、感音神经性耳聋、智力残障</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Phototherapy mechanism<br />
光疗机制</td>
<td>Blue-green light (450–490 nm) isomerizes insoluble 4Z,15Z-bilirubin to water-soluble lumirubin and 4Z,15E-bilirubin, excreted in bile and urine without hepatic conjugation<br />
蓝绿光（450-490 nm）将不溶性4Z,15Z-胆红素异构化为水溶性腊光胆红素和4Z,15E-胆红素，无需肝脏结合即可经胆汁和尿液排泄</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>G6PD deficiency and neonatal jaundice<br />
G6PD缺乏症与新生儿黄疸</td>
<td>X-linked; prevalent in sub-Saharan Africa, Mediterranean, Southeast Asia; oxidative stress (sepsis, naphthalene, fava beans) triggers hemolysis; can co-exist with ABO incompatibility<br />
X染色体连锁遗传；常见于撒哈拉以南非洲、地中海和东南亚地区；氧化应激（败血症、萘、蚕豆）触发溶血；可与ABO不合并存</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of jaundice within 24 hours of birth:** ABO incompatibility, Rh incompatibility, G6PD deficiency, hereditary spherocytosis, pyruvate kinase deficiency, congenital TORCH infection\
  **生后24小时内黄疸的鉴别诊断:** ABO不合、Rh不合、G6PD缺乏症、遗传性球形红细胞增多症、丙酮酸激酶缺乏症、先天性TORCH感染

- **Key variant — Ethiopian heritage as a G6PD clue:** If the question emphasized specific triggers (naphthalene mothballs, oxidant drugs) rather than maternal blood type O, G6PD deficiency would become the primary diagnosis; here the O blood type makes ABO incompatibility the lead\
  **题目变式——埃塞俄比亚血统作为G6PD线索:** 若题目强调特定触发因素（萘丸、氧化性药物）而非母亲O型血，G6PD缺乏症应作为首要诊断；此题因O型血线索，ABO不合为优先考虑

- **Key complication — hydrops fetalis:** Unlike Rh incompatibility, ABO incompatibility rarely causes hydrops fetalis; if a question describes fetal ascites or skin edema in the setting of ABO incompatibility, suspect co-existing parvovirus B19 or Rh incompatibility\
  **关键并发症——胎儿水肿:** 与Rh不合不同，ABO不合极少引起胎儿水肿；若题目描述ABO不合背景下出现胎儿腹水或皮肤水肿，应怀疑合并细小病毒B19感染或Rh不合

- **Mnemonic — Why RhoGAM does NOT prevent ABO incompatibility:** RhoGAM contains anti-D immunoglobulin only; it neutralizes D-antigen exposure on Rh-negative mothers but has zero effect on naturally occurring IgG anti-A/B antibodies present in all type O mothers\
  **助记——为何RhoGAM不能预防ABO不合:** RhoGAM仅含抗D免疫球蛋白；它中和Rh阴性母亲的D抗原暴露，对所有O型血母亲天然存在的IgG抗-A/B抗体完全无效
